Gopālabhaṭṭa Haribhaktivilāsa 

gaurava-vilasa

hari-bhakti-vilāsaḥ prathamo vilāsaḥ

atha maṅgalācaraṇam

caitanya-devaṃ bhagavantam āśraye
śrī-vaiṣṇavānāṃ pramude'ñjasā likhan ।
āvaśyakaṃ karma vicārya sādhubhiḥ
sārdhaṃ samāhṛtya samasta-śāstrataḥ ।।

bhakter vilāsāṃś cinute prabodhā-
nandasya śiṣyo bhagavat-priyasya ।
gopāla-bhaṭṭo raghunātha-dāsaṃ
santoṣayan rūpa-sanātanau ca ।।

mathurā-nātha-pādābja-prema-bhakti-vilāsataḥ ।
jātaṃ bhakti-vilāsākhyaṃ tad-bhaktāḥ śīlayantv imam ।।

jīyāsur ātyantika-bhakti-niṣṭhāḥ śrī-vaiṣṇavā māthura-maṇḍale'tra ।
kāśīśvaraḥ kṛṣṇa-vane cakāstu śrī-kṛṣṇa-dāsaś ca sa-lokanāthaḥ ।।

tatra lekhya-pratijñā

ādau sa-kāraṇaṃ lekhyaṃ śrī-gurv-āśrayaṇaṃ tataḥ ।
guruḥ śiṣyaḥ parīkṣādir bhagavān manavo asya ca ।।

mantrādhikārī siddhy-ādi-śodhanaṃ mantra-saṃskriyāḥ ।
dīkṣā nityaṃ brāhma-kāle śubhotthānaṃ pavitratā ।
prātaḥ smṛtyādi kṛṣṇasya vādyādaiś ca prabodhanam ।।

nirmālyottāraṇādy-ādau maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ ।
maitrādi-kṛtyaṃ śaucācamanaṃ dantasya dhāvanam ।।
snānaṃ tāntrika-sandhyādi deva-sadmādi-saṃskriyā ।।
tulasyādyāhṛtir geha-snānam uṣṇodakādikam ।
vastraṃ pīṭhaṃ cordhva-puṇḍraṃ śrī-gopī-candanādikam ।।

cakrādi-mudrā mālā ca gṛha-sandhyārcanaṃ guroḥ ।
māhātmyaṃ cātha kṛṣṇasya dvāra-veśmāntarārcanam ।।

pūjārthāsanam arghyādi-sthāpanaṃ vighna-vāraṇam ।
śrī-gurv-ādi-natir bhūta-śuddhiḥ prāṇa-viśodhanam ।।

nyāsa-mudrā-pañcakaṃ ca kṛṣṇa-dhyānāntarārcane ।
pūjā padāni śrī-mūrti-śālagrāma-śilās tathā ।।

dvārakodbhava-cakrāṇi śuddhayaḥ pīṭha-pūjanam ।
āvāhanādi tan-mudrā āsanādi-samarpaṇam ।।

snapanaṃ śaṅkha-ghaṇṭādi-vādyaṃ nāma-sahasrakam ।
purāṇa-pāṭho vasanam upavītaṃ vibhūṣaṇam ।।

gandhaḥ śrī-tulasī-kāṣṭha-candanaṃ kusumāni ca ।
patrāṇi tulasī cāṅgopāṅgāvaraṇa-pūjanam ।।

dhūpo dīpaś ca naivedyaṃ pānaṃ homo bali-kriyā ।
avagaṇḍūṣādyāsyavāso divya-gandhādikaṃ punaḥ ।।

rājopacārā gītādi mahā-nīrājanaṃ tathā ।
śaṅkhādi-vādanaṃ sāmbu-śaṅkha-nīrājanaṃ stutiḥ ।।

natiḥ pradakṣiṇā karmādy-arpaṇaṃ japa yācane ।
āgaḥ-kṣamāpaṇaṃ nānāgāṃsi nirmālya-dhāraṇam ।।

śaṅkhāmbu-tīrthaṃ tulasī-pūjā tan-mṛttikādi ca ।
dhātrī-snāna-niṣedhasya kālo vṛtter upārjanam ।।

madhyāhne vaiśa-devādi-śrāddhaṃ cānarpyam acyute ।
vinārcām aśane doṣās tathānarpita-bhojane ।।

naivedya-bhakṣaṇaṃ santaḥ sat-saṅgo asad-asaṅgatiḥ ।
asad-gatir vaiṣṇavopahāsa-nindādi-duṣphalam ।।

satāṃ bhaktir viṣṇu-śāstraṃ śrīmad-bhāgavataṃ tathā ।
līlā-kathā ca bhagavad-dharmāḥ sāyaṃ nija-kriyāḥ ।।

karma-pāta-parīhāras trikālārcā viśeṣataḥ ।
naktaṃ kṛtyānyatho pūjā-phala-siddhy-ādi-darśanam ।।

viṣṇv-artha-dānaṃ vividhopacārā nyūna-pūraṇam ।
śayanaṃ mahimārcāyāḥ śrīman-nāmnas tathādbhutaḥ ।।

nāmāparādhā bhaktiś ca premāthāśrayaṇādayaḥ ।
pakṣeṣv ekādaśī sāṅgā śrī-dvādaśy-aṣṭakaṃ mahat ।।

kṛtyāni mārga-śīrṣādi-māseṣu dvādśeṣv api ।
puraścaraṇa-kṛtyāni mantraṃ siddhasya lakṣaṇam ।।

mūrtyāvirbhāvanaṃ mūrti-pratiṣṭhā kṛṣṇa-mandiram ।
jīrṇoddhṛtiḥ śrī-tulasī-vivāho ananya-karma ca ।।

tatra śrī-gurūpasatti-kāraṇam

kṛpayā kṛṣṇa-devasya tad-bhakta-jana-saṅgataḥ ।
bhakter māhātmyam ākarṇya tām icchan sad-guruṃ bhajet ।।

atrānubhūyate nityaṃ duḥkha-śreṇī paratra ca ।
duḥsahā śrūyate śāstrāt titīrṣed api tāṃ sudhīḥ ।।

tathā coktam ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ]- 
labdhvā su-durlabham idaṃ bahu-sambhavānte
mānuṣyam artha-dam anityam apīha dhīraḥ ।
tūrṇaṃ yateta na pated anu-mṛtyu yāvan
niḥśreyasāya viṣayaḥ khalu sarvataḥ syāt ।।

svayaṃ śrī-bhagavatā ca [bhp ]- 
nṛ-deham ādyaṃ su-labhaṃ su-durlabhaṃ
plavaṃ su-kalpaṃ guru-karṇa-dhāram ।
mayānukūlena nabhasvateritaṃ
pumān bhavābdhiṃ na taret sa ātma-hā ।।

atha śrī-gurūpasattiḥ

tatraiva śrī-prabuddha-yogeśvaroktau [bhp ]-
tasmād guruṃ prapadyeta jijñāsuḥ śreya uttamam ।
śābde pare ca niṣṇātaṃ brahmaṇy upaśamāśrayam ।।

svayaṃ śrī-bhagavad-uktau [bhp ]- mad-abhijñaṃ guruṃ śāntam upāsīta mad-ātmakam ।।

krama-dīpikāyāṃ ca 
vipraṃ pradhvasta-kāma-prabhṛti-ripu-ghaṭaṃ nirmalāṅgaṃ gariṣṭhāṃ
bhaktiṃ kṛṣṇāṅghri-paṅkeruha-yugala-rajorāgiṇīm udvahantam ।
vettāraṃ veda-śāstāgama-vimala-pathāṃ sammataṃ satsu dāntaṃ
vidyāṃ yaḥ saṃvivitsuḥ pravaṇa-tanu-manā deśikaṃ saṃśrayeta ।।

śrutāv api [muṇḍu chāu ] -
tad-vijñānārthaṃ sa gurum evābhigacchet samit-pāṇiḥ śrotriyaṃ brahma-niṣṭham ।
ācāryavān puruṣo veda ।।

atha gurūpasatti-nityatā

śrī-bhāgavate daśama-skandhe śruti-stutau [bhp ] 
vijita-hṛṣīka-vāyubhir adānta-manas tura-gaṃ
ya iha yatanti yantum ati-lolam upāya-khidaḥ ।
vyasana-śatānvitāḥ samavahāya guroś caraṇaṃ
vaṇija ivāja santy akṛta-karṇa-dharā jaladhau ।।

śrutau ca [kaṭhu ]-
naiṣā tarkeṇa matir āpaneyā
proktānyenaiva sujñānāya preṣṭha ।।

atha viśeṣataḥ śrī-guror lakṣaṇāni

mantra-muktāvalyām -
avadātānvayaḥ śuddhaḥ svocitācāra-tat-paraḥ ।
āśramī krodha-rahito vedavit sarva-śāstravit ।।

śraddhāvān anasūyaś ca priya-vāk priya-darśanaḥ ।
śuciḥ suveśas taruṇaḥ sarva-bhūta-hite rataḥ ।।

dhīmān anuddhata-matiḥ pūrṇo ahantā vimarśakaḥ ।
sa-guṇo arcāsu kṛtadhīḥ kṛtajñaḥ śiṣya-vatsalaḥ ।।

nigrahānugrahe śakto homa-mantra-parāyaṇaḥ ।
ūhāpoha-prakāra-jñaḥ śuddhātmā yaḥ kṛpālayaḥ ।
ity ādi-lakṣaṇair yukto guruḥ syād garimā-nidhiḥ ।।

agastya-saṃhitāyāṃ ca 
devatopāsakaḥ śānto viṣayeṣv api niḥspṛhaḥ ।
adhyātmavid brahma-vādī veda-śāstrārtha-kovidaḥ ।।

uddhartuṃ caiva saṃhartuṃ samartho brāhmaṇottamaḥ ।
tattvajño yantra-mantrāṇāṃ marma-bhettā rahasyavit ।।

puraścaraṇa-kṛd dhoma-mantra-siddhaḥ prayogavit ।
tapasvī satya-vādī ca gṛhastho gurur ucyate ।।

viṣṇu-smṛtau 
paricaryā-yaśo-lābha-lipsuḥ śiṣyād gurur nahi ।
kṛpā-sindhuḥ susampūrṇaḥ sarva-sattvopakārakaḥ ।।

niḥspṛhaḥ sarvataḥ siddhaḥ sarva-vidyā-viśāradaḥ ।
sarva-saṃśaya-saṃchettā nālaso gurur āhṛtaḥ ।।

śrī-nārada-pañcarātre śrī-bhagavan-nārada-saṃvāde -
brāhmaṇaḥ sarva-kāla-jñaḥ kuryāt sarveṣv anugraham ।
tad-abhāvād dvija-śreṣṭhaḥ śāntātmā bhagavan-mayaḥ ।।

bhāvitātmā ca sarvajñaḥ śāstrajñaḥ sat-kriyā-paraḥ ।
siddhi-trayam āyukta ācāryatve'bhiṣecitaḥ ।।

kṣatra-viṭ-śūdra-jātīnāṃ kṣatriyo anugrahe kṣamaḥ ।
kṣatriyasyāpi ca guror bhāvād īdṛśo yadi ।।

vaiśyaḥ syāt tena kāryaś ca dvaye nityam anugrahaḥ ।
sajātīyena śūdreṇa tādṛśena mahā-mate ।
anugrahābhiṣekau ca kāryau śūdrasya sarvadā ।।

kiṃ ca -
varṇottam'tha ca gurau sati yā viśrute'pi ca ।
svadeśato athat vānyatra nedaṃ kāryaṃ śubhārthinā ।।

vidyamāne tu yaḥ kuryāt yatra tatra viparyayam ।
tasyehāmutra nāśaḥ syāt tasmāc chāstroktam ācaret ।।
kṣatra-viṭ-śūdra-jātīyaḥ prātilomyaṃ na dīkṣayet ।।
pādme ca [padmap ]-
mahā-bhāgavataḥ śreṣṭho brāhmaṇo vai gurur nṛṇām ।
sarveṣām eva lokānām asau pūjyo yathā hariḥ ।।

mahākūla-prasūto api sarva-yajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ ।
sahasra-śākhādhyāyī ca na guruḥ syād avaiṣṇavaḥ ।।

iti

gṛhīta-viṣṇu-dīkṣāko viṣṇu-pūjā-paro naraḥ ।
vaiṣṇavo abhihito abhijñair itaro asmād avaiṣṇavaḥ ।।

tattva-sāgare-
bahvāśī dīrgha-sūtrī ca viṣayādiṣu lolupaḥ ।
hetu-vāda-rato duṣṭo avāg-vādī guṇa-nindakaḥ ।।

aromā bahu-romā ca ninditāśrama-sevakaḥ ।
kāla-danto asitauṣṭhaś ca durgandhi-śvāsa-vāhakaḥ ।।

duṣṭa-lakṣaṇa-sampanno yadyapi svayam īśvaraḥ ।
bahu-pratigrhāsakta ācāryaḥ śrī-kṣayāvahaḥ ।।

atha śiṣya-lakṣaṇāni

mantra-muktāvalyām-
śiṣyaḥ śuddhānvayaḥ śrīmān vinītaḥ priya-darśanaḥ ।
satya-vāk puṇya-carito adabhra-dhīr dambha-varjitaḥ ।।

kāma-krodha-parityāgī bhaktaś ca guru-pādayoḥ ।
devatā-pravaṇaḥ kāya-mano-vāgbhir divā-niśam ।।

nīrujo nirjitāśeṣa-pātakaḥ śraddhyānvitaḥ ।
dvija-deva-pitṝṇāṃ ca nityam arcā-parāyaṇaḥ ।।

yuvā viniyatāśeṣa-karaṇaḥ karuṇālayaḥ ।
ity ādi-lakṣaṇair yuktaḥ śiṣyo dīkṣādhikāravān ।।

ekādaśa-skandhe ca [bhp ] 
amāny amatsaro dakṣo nirmamo dṛṭha-sauhṛdaḥ ।
asatvaro artha-jijñāsur anasūyur amogha-vāk ।।

athāpekṣyāḥ

agastya-saṃhitāyām-
alasā malināḥ kliṣṭā dāmbhikāḥ kṛpaṇās tathā ।
daridrā rogiṇo ruṣṭā rāgiṇo bhoga-lālasāḥ ।।

asūyā-matsara-grastāḥ śaṭhāḥ paruṣa-vādinaḥ ।
anyāyopārjita-dhanāḥ para-dāra-ratāś ca ye ।।

viduṣāṃ vairiṇaś caiva ajñāḥ paṇḍita-māninaḥ ।
bhraṣṭa-vratāś ca ye kaṣṭa-vṛttayaḥ piśunāḥ khalāḥ ।।

bahv-āśinaḥ krūra-ceṣṭā durātmanaś ca nindita ।
ity evam ādayo apy anye pāpiṣṭhāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ ।।

akṛtyebhyo anivāryāś ca guru-śikṣā-sahiṣṇavaḥ ।
evambhūtāḥ parityājyāḥ śiṣyatve nopakalpitāḥ ।।

yady ete hy upakalperan devatākrośa-bhājanāḥ ।
bhavantīha dardrās te putra-dāra-vivarjitāḥ ।।
nārakāś caiva dehānte tiryañcaḥ prabhavanti te ।।
hayaśīrṣa-pañcarātre-
jaiminiḥ sugataś caiva nāstiko nagna eva ca ।
kapilaś cākṣapādaś ca ṣaḍ ete hetu-vādinaḥ ।।

etan-matānusāreṇa vartante ye narādhamāḥ ।
te hetuvādinaḥ proktās tebhyas tantraṃ na dāpayet ।।

iti

tayoḥ parīkṣā cānyo anyam ekābdaṃ saha-vāsataḥ ।
vyavahāra-svabhāvānubhavenaivābhijāyate ।।

atha parīkṣaṇam

mantra-muktāvalyāṃ-
tayor vatsara-vāsena jñātānyonya-svabhāvayoḥ ।
gurutā śiṣyatā ceti nānyathaiveti niścayaḥ ।।

śrutiś ca- nāsaṃvatsara-vāsine deyāt ।।

sāra-saṅgrahe'pi- sad-guruḥ svāśritaṃ śiṣyaṃ varṣm ekaṃ parīkṣayet ।।

rājñi cāmātyajā doṣāḥ patnī-pāpaṃ sva-bhartari ।
tathā śiṣyārjitaṃ pāpaṃ guruḥ prāpnoti niścitam ।।

krama-dīpikāyāṃ tu 
santoṣayed akuṭilādretarāntarātmā
taṃ svair dhanaiś ca vapuṣāpy anukūlavāṇyā ।
abda-trayaṅkamalanābhadhiyā'tidhīras
tuṣṭe vivakṣatu gurāv atha mantra-dīkṣām ।।

atha viśeṣataḥ śrī-guru-sevā-vidhiḥ

kaurme śrī-vyāsa-gītāyām-
udakumbhaṃ kuśān puṣpaṃ samidho asyāharet sadā ।
mārjanaṃ lepanaṃ nityam aṅgānāṃ vāsasāṃ caret ।।

nāsya nirmālya-śayanaṃ pādukopāsanahāv api ।
ākrāmed āsanaṃ chyāyām āsandīṃ vā kadācana ।।
sādhayed danta-kāṣṭhādīn kṛtyaṃ cāsmai nivedayeet ।।
anāpṛcchya na gantavyaṃ bhavet priya-hite rasaḥ ।
na pādau sārayed asya sannidhāne kadācana ।।

jṛmbhā-hāsyādikaṃ caiva kaṇṭha-prāvaraṇaṃ tathā ।
varjayet sannidhau nityam athāsphoṭanam eva ca ।।

kiṃ ca-
śreyas tu guruvad vṛttir nityam eva samācaret ।
guru-putreṣu dāreṣu guroś caiva sva-bandhuṣu ।।

utsādanaṃ vai gātrāṇāṃ snāpanocchiṣṭa-bhojane ।
na kuryād guru-putrasya pādayoḥ śaucam eva ca ।।

guruvat paripūjyāś ca sa-varṇā guru-yoṣitaḥ ।
asavarṇās tu sampūjyāḥ pratyutthānābhivādanaiḥ ।।

abhyañjanaṃ snāpanaṃ ca gātrotsādanam eva ca ।
guru-patnyā ca kāryāṇi keśānāṃ ca prasādhanam ।।

devy-āgame śrī-śivoktau-
guru-śayyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pāduke pāda-pīṭhakam ।
snānodakaṃ tathā chāyāṃ laṅghayen na kadācana ।।

guror agre pṛthak-pūjām advaitaṃ ca parityajet ।
dīkṣāṃ vyākhyāṃ prabhutvaṃ ca guror agre vivarjayet ।।

śrī-nāradoktau-
yatra yatra guruṃ paśyet tatra tatra kṛtāñjali ।
praṇamet daṇḍavad bhūmau chinna-mūla iva drumaḥ ।।

guror vākyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pādukopānahau tathā ।
vastraṃ chāyāṃ tathā śiṣyo laṅghayen na kadācana ।।

śrī-manu-smṛtau- 
nodāhared guror nāma parokṣam api kevalam ।
na caivāsyānukurvīta gati-bhāṣaṇa-ceṣṭitam ।।

guror gurau sannihite guruvad dhṛtim ācaret ।
na cāvisṛṣṭo guruṇā svān gurūn abhivādayet ।।

śrī-nārada-pañcarātre-
yathā tathā yatra tatra na gṛhṇīyāc ca kevalam ।
abhaktyā na guror nāma gṛhṇīyāc ca yatātmavān ।।

praṇavaḥ śrīs tato nāma viṣṇu-śabdād anantaram ।
pāda-śabda-sametaṃ ca nata-mūrdhāñjalī-yutaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
na tam ājñāpayen mohāt tasyājñāṃ na ca laṅghayet ।
nānivedya guroḥ kiñcid bhoktavyaṃ vā guros tathā ।।

anyatra ca-
āyāntam agrato gacched gacchantaṃ tam anuvrajet ।
āsane śayane vāpi na tiṣṭhed agrato guroḥ ।।

yat kiñcid anna-pānādi priyaṃ dravyaṃ manoramam ।
samarpya gurave paścāt svayaṃ bhuñjīta pratyaham ।।

śrī-viṣṇu-smṛtau-
na guror apriyaṃ kuryāt tāḍitaḥ pīḍito api vā ।
nāvamanyeta tad-vākyaṃ nāpriyaṃ hi samācaret ।।

ācāryasya priyaṃ kuryāt prāṇair api dhanair api ।
karmaṇā manasā vācā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।

śrī-nārada-pañcarātre -
yo vakti nyāya-rahitam anyāyena śṛṇoti yaḥ ।
tāv ubhau narakaṃ ghoraṃ vrajataḥ kālam akṣayam ।।

vaiṣṇava-tantre -
trāyasva bho jagannātha guro saṃsāra-vahninā ।
dagdhaṃ māṃ kāla-daṣṭaṃ ca tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।

iti

tatra śrī-vāsudevasya sarva-deva-śiromaṇeḥ ।
pādāmbujaika-bhāg eva dīkṣā grāhyā manīṣibhiḥ ।।

prathama-skandhe [bhp ] - 
sattvaṃ rajas tama iti prakṛter guṇās tair
yuktaḥ parama-puruṣa eka ihāsya dhatte ।
sthity-ādaye hari-viriñci-hareti saṃjñāḥ
śreyāṃsi tatra khalu sattva-tanor nṝṇāṃ syuḥ ।।

kiṃ ca [bhp ] - 
athāpi yat-pāda-nakhāvasṛṣṭaṃ
jagad viriñcopahṛtārhaṇāmbhaḥ ।
seśaṃ punāty anyatamo mukundāt
ko nāma loke bhagavat-padārthaḥ ।।

śrī-daśama-skandhe [bhp ] -
tan niśamyātha munayo vismitā mukta-saṃśayāḥ ।
bhūyāṃsaṃ śraddadhur viṣṇuṃ yataḥ śāntir yato abhayam ।।

pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye yama-brāhmaṇa-saṃvāde [padmap ] 
vyāmohāya carācarasya jagatas te te purāṇāgamās
tāṃ tām eva hi devatāṃ paramikāṃ jalpantu kalpāvadhi ।
siddhānte punar eka eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ samastāgama-
vyāpāreṣu vivecana-vyatikaraṃ nīteṣu niścīyate ।।

nārasiṃhe -
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyam utkṣipya bhujam ucyate ।
vedāc chāstraṃ paraṃ nāsti na devaḥ keśavāt paraḥ ।।

yataḥ pādme -
arir mitraṃ viṣṃ pathyam adharmo dharmatāṃ vrajet ।
suprasanne hṛṣīkeśe viparīte viparyayaḥ ।।

tatraiva śrī-bhagavad-vākyam-
man-nimittaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpam api dharmāya kalpate ।
mām anādṛtya dharmo api pāpaṃ syān mat-prabhāvataḥ ।।

ataevoktaṃ skānde śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde -
vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo anyaṃ devam upāsate ।
sva-mātaraṃ parityajya śvapacīṃ vandate hi saḥ ।।

tatraivānyatra -
vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo anyaṃ devam upāsate ।
tyaktvāmṛtaṃ sa mūḍhātmā bhuṅkte halāhalaṃ viṣam ।।

mahābhārate -
yas tu viṣṇuṃ parityajya mohād anyam upāsate ।
sa hema-rāśim utsṛjya pāṃśu-rāśiṃ jighṛkṣati ।।

anādṛtya tu yo viṣṇum anya-devaṃ samāśrayet ।
gaṅgāmbhasaḥ sa tṛṣṇārto mṛga-tṛṣṇāṃ pradhāvati ।।

pañcarātre -
yo mohād viṣṇum anyena hīna-devena durmatiḥ ।
sādhāraṇaṃ sakṛd brūte so antyajo nāntyajo antyajaḥ ।।

vaiṣṇava-tantre -
na labheyuḥ punar bhaktiṃ harer aikāntikīṃ jaṅāḥ ।
ekāgra-manasaś cāpi viṣṇu-sāmānya-darśinaḥ ।।

anyatra ca -
yas tu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ brahma-rudrādi-daivataiḥ ।
samatvenaiva vīkṣeta sa pāṣaṇḍī bhaved dhruvam ।।

iti

sahasra-nāma-stotrādau ślokaughāḥ santi cedṛśāḥ ।
viśeṣataḥ sattva-niṣṭhaiḥ sevoy viṣṇur na cāparaḥ ।।

tathā ca śrī-hari-vaṃśe śiva-vākyam -
harir eva sadārādhyo bhavadbhiḥ sattva-saṃsthitaiḥ ।
viṣṇu-mantraṃ sadā viprāḥ paṭhadhvaṃ dhyāta keśavam ।।

iti

īdṛṅ-māhātmya-vākyeṣu saṅgṛhīteṣu sarvataḥ ।
grantha-bāhulya-doṣaḥ syāl likhyante'pekṣitāni tat ।।

atha śrī-vaiṣṇava-mantra-māhātmyam

āgame-
mantrān śrī-mantra-rājādīn vaiṣṇavān gurv-anugrahāt ।
sarvaiśvaryaṃ japan prāpya yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।।

puṇyaṃ varṣa-sahasrair yaiḥ kṛtaṃ suvipulaṃ tapaḥ ।
japanti vaiṣṇavān mantrān narās te loka-pāvanāḥ ।।

vaiṣṇave ca-
prajapan vaiṣṇavān mantrān yaṃ yaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā ।
padā vā saṃspṛśet sadyo mucyate'sau mahā-bhayāt ।।

iti

likhyate viṣṇu-mantrāṇāṃ mahimātha viśeṣataḥ ।
tātparyataḥ śrī-gopāla-mantra-māhātmya-puṣṭaye ।।

tatra dvādaśākṣarāṣṭākṣarayor māhātmyam

padma-purāṇe devadūta-vikuṇḍala-saṃvāde-
sāṅgaṃ sa-mudraṃ sa-nyāsaṃ sa-ṛṣi-daivatam ।
sa-dīkṣā-vidhi sa-dhyānaṃ sa-yantraṃ dvādaśākṣaram ।।

aṣṭākṣaraṃ ca mantreśaṃ ye japanti narottamāḥ ।
tān dṛṣṭvā brahmahā śudhyete yato viṣṇavaḥ svayam ।।

śaṅkhinaś cakriṇo bhūtvā brahmāyur vana-mālinaḥ ।
vasanti vaiṣṇave loke viṣṇu-rūpeṇa te narāḥ ।।

tatraiva dvādaśākṣarayas caturtha-skandhe [bhp ] 
japaś ca paramo guhyaḥ śrūyatāṃ me nṛpātmaja ।
yaṃ sapta-rātraṃ prapaṭhan pumān paśyati khecarān ।।

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ]
gatvā gatvā nivartante candra-sūryādayo grahāḥ ।
adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣara-cintakāḥ ।।

aṣṭākṣarasya, yathā nārada-pañcarātre-
trayo vedāḥ ṣaḍ-aṅgāni chandāṃsi vividhāḥ surāḥ ।
sarvam aṣṭākṣarāntaḥsthaṃ yac cānyad api vāṅ-mayam ।।

sarva-vedānta-sārārthaṃ saṃsārārṇava-tāraṇaḥ ।
gatir aṣṭākṣaro nṝṇāṃ na punar bhava-kāṅkṣiṇām ।।

yatrāṣṭākṣara-saṃsiddho mahā-bhāgo mahīyate ।
na tatra sañcariṣyanti vyādhi-durbhikṣa-taskarāḥ ।।

deva-dānava-gandharvāḥ siddha-vidyādharādayaḥ ।
praṇamanti mahātmānam aṣṭākṣara-vidaṃ naram ।।

vyaktaṃ hi bhagavān eva sākṣān nārāyaṇaḥ svayam ।
aṣṭākṣara-svarūpeṇa mukheṣu parivartate ।।

pādmottara-khaṇḍe [padmap ] 
evam aṣṭākṣaro mantro jñeyaḥ sarvārtha-sādhakaḥ ।
sarva-duḥkha-haraḥ śrīmān sarva-mantrātmakaḥ śubhaḥ ।।

liṅga-purāṇe-
kim anyair bahubhir mantraiḥ kim anyair bahubhir vrataiḥ ।
namo nārāyaṇeti mantraḥ sarvārtha-sādhakaḥ ।।

tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu namo nārāyaṇeti yaḥ ।
japet sa yāti viprendra viṣṇu-lokaṃ sa-bāndhavaḥ ।।

bhaviṣya-purāṇe-
aṣṭākṣaro mahā-mantraḥ sarva-pāpa-haraḥ paraḥ ।
sarveṣāṃ viṣṇu-mantrāṇāṃ rājatve parikīrtitaḥ ।।

śrī-śuka-vyāsa-saṃvāde ca-
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārtha-sādhakaḥ ।
bhaktānāṃ japatāṃ tāta svarga-mokṣa-phala-pradaḥ ।।

eṣa eva paro mokṣa eṣa svarga udāhṛtaḥ ।
sarva-veda-rahasyebhyaḥ sāra eṣa samuddhṛtaḥ ।।

viṣṇunā vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu hitāya manunā purā ।
kīrtitaḥ sarva-pāpaghnaḥ sarva-kāma-pradāyakaḥ ।।

nārāyaṇāya nama ity ayam eva satyaṃ
saṃsāra-ghora-viṣa-saṃharaṇāya mantraḥ ।
śṛṇvantu satya-matayo muditās tarāgā
uccais tarām upadiśāmy aham ūrdhva-bāhuḥ ।।

bhūtvordhva-bāhur adyāhaṃ satya-pūrvaṃ bravīmi vaḥ ।
he putra-śiṣyāḥ śṛṇuta na mantro aṣṭākṣarāt paraḥ ।।

ataevoktaṃ gāruḍe-
āsīno vā śayāno vā tiṣṭhāno yatra tatra vā ।
namo nārāyaṇeti mantraika-śaraṇo bhavet ।।

tāpanī-śrutiṣu [nṛsiṃhatu ] devā ha vai prajāpatim abruvann ānuṣṭubhasya mantra-rājasya nārasiṃhasya phalaṃ no brūhi bhagava iti sa hovāca prajāpatirya etaṃ mantra-rājaṃ nārasiṃham ānuṣṭubhaṃ nityam adhīte so agni-pūto bhavati sa vāyu-pūto bhavati sa āditya-pūto bhavati sa soma-pūto bhavati sa satya-pūto bhavati sa brahma-pūto bhavati sa viṣṇu-pūto bhavati sa rudra-pūto bhavati sa sarva-pūto bhavati sa sarva-pūto bhavati ।।

tatraivānte [nṛsiṃhatu ]- anupanīta-śatam ekam ekenopanītena tat-samam । upanīta-śatam ekam ekena gṛhasthena tat-samam । gṛhastha-śatam ekam ekena vānaprasthena tat samaṃ । vānaprastha-śatam ekam ekena yatinā tat samaṃ । yatīnāṃ tu śataṃ pūrṇam ekam ekena rudra-jāpakena tat-samam । rudra-jāpaka-śatam ekam ekena atharva-śiraḥ-śikhādhyāpakena tat-samam ।

tad vā etat paramaṃ dhāma mantra-rājādhyāpakasya yatra na sūryas tapati yatra na vāyur vāti yatra na candramā bhāti yatra na nakṣatrāṇi bhānti yatra nāgnir dahati yatra na mṛtyuḥ praviśati yatra na duḥkhaṃ sadānandaṃ paramānandaṃ śāntaṃ śāśvataṃ sadā-śivaṃ brahmādi-vanditaṃ yogi-dhyeyaṃ paramaṃ padaṃ yatra gatvā na nivartante yoginaḥ । tad etad ṛcābhyuktam । tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ । divīva cakṣur ātatam । tad viprāso vipanyavo jāgṛvāṃsaḥ samindhate । viṣṇor yat paramaṃ padam ।।

atha śrī-rāma-mantrāṇāṃ māhātmyam

agastya-saṃhitāyām -
sarveṣu mantra-vargeṣu śreṣṭhaṃ vaiṣṇavam ucyate ।
gāṇapatyeṣu śaiveṣu śākta-saureṣv abhīṣṭadam ।।

vaiṣṇaveṣv api mantreṣu rāma-mantrāḥ phalādhikāḥ ।
gāṇapaty-ādi-mantrebhyaḥ koṭi-koṭi-guṇādhikāḥ ।।

vinaiva dīkṣāṃ viprendra puraścaryāṃ vinaiva hi ।
vinaiva nyāsa-vidhinā japa-mātreṇa siddhidāḥ ।।

mantreṣv aṣṭasv anāyāsa-phalado ayaṃ ṣaḍ-akṣaraḥ ।
ṣaḍ-akṣaro ayaṃ mantras tu mahāghaugha-nivāraṇaḥ ।।

mantra-rāja iti proktaḥ sarveṣām uttamottamaḥ ।
dainandinaṃ tu duritaṃ pakṣa-māsa-rtu-varṣajam ।।

sarvaṃ dahati niḥśeṣaṃ tūlācalam ivānalaḥ ।
brahma-hatyā-sahasrāṇi jñānājñāna-kṛtāni ca ।।

svarṇas teyasurāpāna-guru-talpa-yutāni ca ।
koṭi-koṭi-sahasrāṇi hyupapāpāni yāny api ।
sarvāṇy api praṇaśyanti rāma-mantrānukīrtanāt ।।

tāpanī-śrutiṣu ca - ya etat-tārakaṃ brāhmaṇo nityam adhīte, sa pāpmānaṃ tarati, sa mṛtyuṃ tarati, sa bhrū-hatyāṃ tarati, sa sarva-hatyāṃ tarati, sa saṃsāraṃ tarati, sa sarvaṃ tarati, sa vimuktāśrito bhavati, so amṛtatvaṃ ca gacchati ।।

atha gopāla-deva-mantra-māhātmyam

mantrās tu kṛṣṇa-devasya sākṣād bhagavato hareḥ ।
sarvāvatāra-bījasya sarvato vīryavattamāḥ ।।

tathā ca bṛhad-gautamīye śrī-govinda-vṛndāvanākhye -
sarveṣāṃ mantra-varyāṇāṃ śreṣṭho vaiṣṇava ucyate ।
viśeṣāt kṛṣṇa-manavo bhoga-mokṣaika-sādhanam ।।

yasya yasya ca mantrasya yo yo devas tathā punaḥ ।
abhedāt tan-manūnāṃ ca devatā saiva bhāṣyate ।।

kṛṣṇa eva paraṃ brahma saccidānanda-vigrahaḥ ।
smṛti-mātreṇa teṣāṃ vai bhukti-mukti-phala-pradaḥ ।।

iti

tatrāpi bhagavattāṃ svāṃ tanvato gopa-līlayā ।
tasya śreṣṭhatamā mantrās teṣv apy aṣṭādaśākṣaraḥ ।।

tāpanī-śrutiṣu oṃ munayo ha vai brahmāṇam ūcuḥ । kaḥ paramo devaḥ । kuto mṛtyur bibheti । kasya jñānenākhilaṃ jñātaṃ bhavati । kenedaṃ viśvaṃ saṃsaratīti । tān u hovāca brāhmaṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vai paramaṃ daivatam । govindān mṛtyur bibheti । gopī-jana-vallabha-jñānenākhilaṃ jñātaṃ bhavati । svāhayedaṃ saṃsaratīti । tam u hocuḥ । kaḥ kṛṣṇo govindaḥ ko asau gopī-jana-vallabhaḥ kaḥ kā svāheti । tān uvāca brāhmaṇaḥ pāpa-karṣaṇo go-bhūmi-veda-vidito veditā gopī-janāvidyā-kalā-prerakas tan-māyā ceti । sakalaṃ paraṃ brahmaiva tat । yo dhyāyati rasati bhajati so amṛto bhavati so amṛto bhavatīti । te hocuḥ kiṃ tad-rūpaṃ kiṃ rasanaṃ kathaṃ vāho tad-bhajanaṃ । tat sarvaṃ vividiṣatām ākhyāhīti । tad u hovāca hairaṇyaḥ gopa-veśam abhrābhaṃ taruṇaṃ kalpa-drumāśritam ।।

kiṃ ca, tatraivāgre bhaktir asya bhajanam । tad ihāmutropādhi-nairāsyenaivāmuṣmin manaḥ-kalpanam । etad eva ca naiṣkarmyam ।

kṛṣṇaṃ taṃ viprā bahudhā yajanti
govindaṃ santaṃ bahudhārādhayanti ।
gopījana-vallabho bhuvanāni dadhre
svāhāśrito jagad ejayjat sva-retāḥ ।।

vāyur yathaiko bhuvanaṃ praviṣṭo
janye janye pañca-rūpo babhūva ।
kṛṣṇas tathaiko api jagad-dhitārthaṃ
śabdenāsau pañca-pado vibhāti ।।

iti 

kiṃ ca tatraivopāsana-vidhi-kathanānantaram -

eko vaśī sarvagaḥ kṛṣṇa īḍya
eko api san bahudhā yo vibhāti ।
taṃ pīṭhasthaṃ ye'nubhajanti dhīrās
teṣāṃ sukhaṃ śāśvataṃ netareṣām ।।

nityo nityānāṃ cetanaś cetanānām
eko bahūnāṃ yo vidadhāti kāmān ।
taṃ pīṭhagaṃ ye'nubhajanti dhīrās
teṣāṃ siddhiḥ śāśvatī netareṣām ।।

etad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ ye
nitya-muktāḥ saṃyajante na kāmān ।
teṣām asau gopa-rūpaḥ prayatnāt
prakāśayed ātma-padaṃ tadaiva ।।

yo brahmāṇaṃ vidadhāti pūrvaṃ
yo vidyās tasmai gopāyati sma kṛṣṇaḥ ।
taṃ ha daivam ātma-buddhi-prakāśaṃ
mumukṣur vai śaraṇam anuvrajeta ।।

oṃkāreṇāntaritaṃ ye japanti
govindasya pañcapadaṃ manum ।
teṣām asau darśayed ātma-rūpaṃ
tasmān mumukṣur abhyasen nitya-śāntyai ।।

tasmād anye pañcapadād abhūvan
govindasya manavo mānavānām ।
daśārṇādyās te'pi saṅkrandanādyair
abhyasyante bhūti-kāmair yathāvat ।।

kiṃ ca tatraiva tad u hovāca brāhmaṇo asāv anavarataṃ me dhyātaḥ stutaḥ parārdhānte so abudhyata । gopa-veśo me puruṣaḥ purastād āvirbabhūva । tataḥ praṇatena mayā'nukūlena hṛdā mahyam aṣṭādaśārṇaṃ svarūpaṃ sṛṣṭaye dattvāntarhitaḥ । punaḥ sisṛkṣā me prādurabhūt । teṣv akṣareṣu bhaviṣyaj-jagad-rūpaṃ prakāśayat । tad iha kād āpo । lāt pṛthivī । īto agniḥ । bindor induḥ । tan-nādād arka iti klīṃ-kārād asṛjam । kṛṣṇād ākāśaṃ yad vāyur ity uttarāt surabhiṃ vidyāṃ prādurakārṣam । tad-uttarāt tad-uttarāt strī-pumādi cedaṃ sakalam idaṃ iti ।।

tathā ca gautamīya-tantre -
klīṃ-kārād asṛjad viśvam iti prāha śruteḥ śiraḥ ।
la-kārāt pṛthivī jātā ka-kārāj jala-sambhavaḥ ।।

ī-kārād vahnir utpanno nādād āyur ajāyata ।
bindor ākāśa-sambhūtir iti bhūtātmako manuḥ ।।

svā-śabdena ca kṣetrajño heti cit-prakṛtiḥ parā ।
tayor aikya-samudbhūtir mukha-veṣṭana-varṇakaḥ ।।
ataeva hi viśvasya layaḥ svāhārṇake bhavet ।।
punaś ca sā śrutiḥ etasyaiva yajanena candra-dhvajo gata-moham ātmānaṃ vedayitvā oṃkārāntarālakaṃ manum āvartayat saṅga-rahito abhyānayat । tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ । divīva cakṣur ātatam । tasmād enaṃ nityam abhyaset ।।

ity ādi

tatraivāgre 
yasya pūrva-padād bhūmir dvitīyāt salilodbhavaḥ ।
tṛtīyāt teja udbhūtaṃ caturthād gandha-vāhanaḥ ।।

pañcamād ambarotpattis tam evaikaṃ samabhyaset ।
candra-dhvajo agamad viṣṇuḥ paramaṃ padam avyayam ।।

tato viśuddhaṃ vimalaṃ
viśokam aśeṣa-lobhādi-nirasta-saṅgam ।
yat tat padaṃ pañca-padaṃ tad eva
sa vāsudevo na yato anyad asti ।।
tam ekaṃ govindaṃ sac-cid-ānanda-vigraham pañca-padaṃ vṛndāvana-sura-bhūruha-talāsīnaṃ satataṃ sa-marud-gaṇo ahaṃ paramayā stutyā toṣayāmi ।।
iti

kiṃ ca stuty-anantaram amuṃ pañcapadaṃ mantram āvartayed yaḥ sa yāty anāyāsataḥ kevalaṃ tat padaṃ tat । anejad ekaṃ manaso javīyo naitad devā āpnuvan pūrvam arśāt ।।
tasmāt kṛṣṇa eva paro devas taṃ dhyāyet taṃ raset taṃ yajed iti oṃ tat sad iti ।।
trailokya-saṃmohana-tantre ca, devīṃ prati śrī-mahādevoktāṣṭādaśākṣara-prasaṅga eva -
dharmārtha-kāma-mokṣāṇām īśvaro jagad-īśvaraḥ ।
santi tasya mahābhāgā avatārāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ madhye'vatārāṇāṃ bālatvam atidurlabham ।
amānuṣāṇi karmāṇi tāni tāni kṛtāni ca ।।

śāpānugraha-kartṛtve yena sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
tasya matnraṃ pravakṣyāmi sāṅgopāṅgam anuttamam ।।

yasya vijñāna-mātreṇa naraḥ sarvajñatām iyāt ।
putrārthī putram āpnoti dharmārthī labhate dhanam ।।

sarva-śāstrārtha-pārajño bhavaty eva na saṃśayaḥ ।
trailokyaṃ ca vaśīkuryāt vyākulīkurute jagat ।।

mohayet sakalaṃ so api mārayet sakalān ripūn ।
bahunā kim ihoktena mumukṣur mokṣam āpnuyāt ।।

yathā cintāmaṇiḥ śreṣṭho yathā gauś ca yathā satī ।
yathā dvijo yathā gaṅgā tathāsau mantra uttamaḥ ।।

yathāvad akhila-śreṣṭhaṃ yathā śāstraṃ tu vaiṣṇavam ।
yathā susaṃskṛtā vāṇī tathāsau mantra uttamaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca 
ato mayā sureśāni pratyahaṃ japyate manuḥ ।
naitena sadṛśaḥ kaścid jagaty asmin caracare ।।

sanatkumāra-kalpe'pi -
gopāla-viṣayā mantrās trayastriṃśat prabhedataḥ ।
teṣu sarveṣu mantreṣu mantra-rājam imaṃ śṛṇu ।।

suprasannam imaṃ mantraṃ tantre sammohanāhvaye ।
gopanīyas tvayā mantro yatnena muni-puṅgava ।।

anena mantra-rājena mahendratvaṃ purandaraḥ ।
jagāma deva-deveśo viṣṇunā dattam añjasā ।।

durvāsasaḥ purā śāpād asaubhāgyena pīḍitaḥ ।
sa eva subhagavatvaṃ vai tenaiva punar āptavān ।।

bahunā kim ihoktena puraścaraṇa-sādhanaiḥ ।
vināpi japa-mātreṇa labhate sarvam īpsitam ।।

prabhuṃ śrī-kṛṣṇa-caitanyaṃ taṃ nato asmi gurūttamam ।
kathañcid āśrayād yasya prākṛto apy uttamo bhavet ।।

athādhikāra-nirṇayaḥ

tāntrikeṣu ca mantreṣu dīkṣāyāṃ yoṣitām api ।
sādhvīnām adhikāro asti śūdrādīnāṃ ca sad-dhiyām ।।

tathā ca smṛty-artha-sāre pādme ca vaiśākha-māhātmye [padmap ] śrī-nāradāmbarīṣa-saṃvāde -

āgamoktena mārgeṇa strī-śūdrair api pūjanam ।
kartavyaṃ śraddhayā viṣṇoś cintayitvā patiṃ hṛdi ।।

śūdrāṇāṃ caiva bhavati nāmnā vai devatārcanam ।
sarve apy āgama-mārgeṇa kuryur vedānukāriṇā ।।

strīṇām apy adhikāro asti viṣṇor ārādhanādiṣu ।
pati-priya-ratānāṃ ca śrutir eṣā sanātanī ।।

agastya-saṃhitāyāṃ śrī-rāma-mantra-rājam uddiśya -
śucivratatamāḥ śūdrā dhārmikā dvija-sevakāḥ ।
striyaḥ pati-vratāś cānye pratilomānulomajāḥ
lokāś cāṇḍāla-paryantāḥ sarve'py atrādhikāriṇaḥ ।।

iti

guruś ca siddha-sādhyādi-mantra-dāne vicārayet ।
sva-kulāny akulatvaṃ ca bāla-prauḍhatvam eva ca ।।

strī-puṃ-napuṃsakatvaṃ ca rāśi-nakṣatra-melanam ।
supta-prabodha-kālaṃ ca tathā ṛṇa-dhanādikam ।।

atha siddha-sādhyādi-śodhanam

saradā-tilake -
prāk pratyag agrā rekhāḥ syuḥ pañca yāmyottarāgragāḥ ।
tāvatyaś ca catuṣkoṣṭha-catuṣkaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhavet ।।

indv-agni-rudra-nava-netra-yugena dikṣu
ṛtv-aṣṭa-ṣaḍaśa-caturdaśa-bhautikeṣu ।
pātāla-pañcadaśa-vahni-himāṃśu-koṣṭhe
varṇāṃl likhel lipi-bhavān kramaśas tu dhīmān ।।

janma-rkṣākṣa-ratau yāvan-mantrādimākṣaram ।
caturbhiḥ koṣṭhakais tv ekam iti koṣṭha-catuṣṭaye ।।

punaḥ koṣṭhaka-koṣṭheṣu savyato janmabhākṣarāt ।
siddha-sādhya-susiddhārikramāj jñeyā vicakṣṇaiḥ ।।

siddhaḥ sidhyati kālena sādhyas tu japa-homataḥ ।
susiddho graha-mātreṇa arir mūla-nikṛntanaḥ ।।

siddha-siddho yathoktena dvi-guṇāt siddha-sādhakaḥ ।
siddha-susiddho ardha-japāt siddhārir hanti bāndhavān ।।

sādhya-siddho dviguṇikaḥ sādhya-sādhyo hy anarthakaḥ ।
tat-susiddhas triguṇitāt sādhyārir hanti gotrajān ।।

susiddha-siddhordha-japāt tat-sādhyas tu guṇādhikāt ।
tat-susiddho grahād eva susiddhāriḥ sva-gotrahā ।।

ari-siddhaḥ sutān hanyād ari-sādhyas tu kanyakāḥ ।
tat-susiddhas tu patnī-ghnas tad-arir hanti sādhakam ।।

tathā ca tantre, asya ca mantra-viśeṣe'pavādaḥ -
nṛsiṃhārka-varāhāṇāṃ prāsāda-praṇavasya ca ।
vaidikasya ca mantrasya siddhādīn naiva śodhayet ।।

svapna-labdhe striyā datte mālā-mantre ca try-akṣare ।
ekākṣare tathā mantre siddhādīn naiva śodhayet ।।

sva-kulāny akulatvādi vijñeyaṃ cāgamāntarāt ।
na vistara-bhayād atra vyarthatvād api likhyate ।।

śrīmad-gopāla-devasya sarvaiśvarya-pradarśinaḥ ।
tādṛk-śaktiṣu mantreṣu nahi kiñcid vicāryate ।।

tathā ca krama-dīpikāyām sarveṣu varṇeṣu tathāśrameṣu 
nārīṣu nānāhvaya-janmabheṣu
dātā phalānām abhivāñchitānāṃ
drāg eva gopālaka-mantra eṣaḥ ।।

trailokya-saṃmohana-tantre ca, aṣṭādaśākṣara-mantram adhikṛtya śrī-śivenoktam -
na cātra śātravā doṣā narṇasvādi-vicāraṇā ।
ṛkṣa-rāśi-vicāro vā na kartavyo manau priye ।।

kecic chinnāś ca ruddhāś ca kecin mada-samuddhatāḥ ।
malināḥ stambhitāḥ kecit kīlitā dūṣitā api ।
etair doṣair yuto nāyaṃ yatas tribhunottamaḥ ।।

iti 
sāmānyataś ca yathā bṛhad-gautamīye -
atha kṛṣṇa-manūn vakṣye dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa-phala-pradān ।
yān vai vijñāya munayo lebhire muktim añjasā ।।

gṛhasthā vanagāś caiva yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ ।
striyaḥ śūdrādayaś caiva sarve yatrādhikāriṇaḥ ।।

nātra cintyo ari-śuddhyādir nāri-mitrādi-lakṣaṇam ।
na vā prayāsa-bāhulyaṃ sādhane na pariśramaḥ ।।

ajñāna-tūla-rāśeś ca analaḥ kṣaṇa-mātrataḥ ।
siddha-sādhya-susiddhāri-rūpā nātra vicāraṇā ।।

sarveṣāṃ siddha-mantrāṇāṃ yato brahmākṣaro manuḥ ।
prajāpatir avāpāgryaṃ deva-rājyaṃ śacīpatiḥ ।
avāpus tridaśāḥ svargaṃ vāgīśatvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ।।

ity ādi

tatraivāntare -
viṣṇu-bhaktyā viśeṣeṇa kiṃ na sidhyati bhūtale ।
kīṭādi-brahma-paryantaṃ govindānugrahān mune ।।

sarva-sampatti-nilayāḥ sarvatrāpy akutobhayāḥ ।
ity ādi kathitaṃ kiñcin māhātmyaṃ vo munīśvarāḥ ।।

ākāśe tārakā yadvat sindhoḥ saikata-sṛṣṭivat ।
etad-vijñāna-mātreṇa labhen muktiṃ caturvidhām ।।

etad-anyeṣu mantreṣu doṣāḥ santi pare ca ye ।
tad-arthaṃ mantra-saṃskārā lipyante tantrato daśa ।।

saradā-tilake -
jananaṃ jīvanaṃ ceti tāḍanaṃ rodhanaṃ tathā ।
athābhiṣeko vimalīkaraṇāpyāyane punaḥ ।
tarpaṇaṃ dīpanaṃ guptir daśaitā mantra-saṃskriyāḥ ।।

mantrāṇāṃ mātṛkā-madhyād uddhāro jananaṃ smṛtam ।
praṇavāntaritān kṛtvā mantra-varṇān japet sudhīḥ ।।

etaj jīvanam ity āhur mantra-tantra-viśāradāḥ ।
manor varṇān samālikhya tāḍayec candanāmbhasā ।।

pratyekaṃ vāyunā mantrī tāḍanaṃ tad udāhṛtam ।
vilikhya mantraṃ taṃ mantrī prasūnaiḥ kara-vīrajaiḥ ।।

tan-mantrākṣara-saṅkhyātair hanyād yat tena rodhanam ।
svatantrokta-vidhānena mantrī mantrārṇa-saṅkhyayā ।।

aśvattha-pallavair mantram abhiṣiñced viśuddhaye ।
saṃcintya manasā mantraṃ yotir mantreṇa nirdahet ।।

mantre mūla-trayaṃ mantrī vimalīkaraṇaṃ tv idam ।
tāra-vyomāgni-manu-yuga-daṇḍī jyotir manur mataḥ ।
kuśodakena japtena pratyarṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ manoḥ ।।

tena mantreṇa vidhivad etad āpyāyanaṃ smṛtam ।
mantreṇa vāriṇā yantre tarpaṇaṃ tarpaṇaṃ smṛtam ।।

tāra-māyā-ramā-yogo manor dīpanam ucyate ।
japyamānasya mantrasya gopanaṃ tv aprakāśanam ।।

balitvāt kṛṣṇa-mantrāṇāṃ saṃskārāpekṣaṇaṃ nahi ।
sāmānyoddeśa-mātreṇa tathāpy etad udīritam ।।

iti śrī-gopāla-bhaṭṭa-vilikhite śrī-bhagavad-bhakti-vilāse gauravo nāma prathamo vilāsaḥ

daiksika-vilasa

dvitīyo vilāsaḥ daikṣikaḥ

taṃ śrīmat-kṛṣṇa-caitanyaṃ vande jagad-gurum ।
yasyānukampayā śvāpi mahābdhiṃ santaret sukham ।।

atha dīkṣā-vidhiḥ

dīkṣā-vidhir likhyate'trānusṛtya krama-dīpikām ।
vinā dīkṣāṃ hi pūjāyāṃ nādhikāro asti karhicit ।।

āgame 
dvijānām anupetānāṃ sva-karmādhyayanādiṣu ।
yathādhikāro nāstīha syāc copanayanād anu ।।

tathātrādīkṣitānāṃ tu mantradevārcanādiṣu ।
nādhikāro asty ataḥ kuryād ātmānaṃ śivasaṃstutam ।।

skānde kārttika-prasaṅge śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde 
te narāḥ paśavo loke kiṃ teṣāṃ jīvane phalam ।
yair na labdhā harer dīkṣā nārcito vā janārdanaḥ ।।

tatraiva śrī-rukmāṅgada-mohinī-saṃvāde, viṣṇu-yāmale ca -
adikṣitasya vāmoru kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ nirarthakam ।
paśu-yonim avāpnoti dīkṣā-virahito janaḥ ।।

viśeṣato viṣṇu-yāmale -
snehād vā lobhato vāpi yo gṛhṇīyād adīkṣayā ।
tasmin gurau sa-śiṣye tu devatā-śāpa āpatet ।।

viṣṇu-rahasye ca -
avijñāya vidhānoktaṃ hari-pūjā-vidhi-kriyām ।
kurvan bhaktyā samāpnoti śata-bhāgaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

divyaṃ jñānaṃ yato dadyāt kuryāt pāpasya saṅkṣayam ।
tasmād dīkṣeti sā proktā deśikais tattvakovidaiḥ ।।

ato guruṃ praṇamyaivaṃ sarvasvaṃ vinivedya ca ।
gṛhṇīyād vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ dīkṣāpūrvaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

skānde tatraiva śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde -
tapasvinaḥ karma-niṣṭhāḥ śreṣṭhās te vai narā bhuvi ।
prāptā yais tu harer dīkṣā sarva-duḥkha-vimocinī ।।

tantra-sāgare ca 
yathā kāñcanatāṃ yāti kāṃsyaṃ rasavidhānataḥ ।
tathā dīkṣāvidhānena dvijatvaṃ jāyate nṛṇām ।।

atha dīkṣā-kālaḥ tatra māsa-śuddhiḥ

āgame -
mantra-svīkaraṇaṃ caitre bahu-duḥha-phala-pradam ।
vaiśākhe ratna-lābhaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam ।।

āṣāḍhe bandhu-nāśāya śrāvaṇe tu bhayāvaham ।
prajā-hānir bhādrapade sarvatra śubham āśvine ।।

kārttike dhana-vṛddhiḥ syān mārgaśīrṣe śubha-pradam ।
pauṣe tu jñāna-hāniḥ syān māghe medhāvi-vardhanam ।
phālgune sarva-vaśyatvam ācāryaiḥ parikīrtitam ।।

kvacic ca -
samṛddhiḥ śrāvaṇe nūnaṃ jñānaṃ syāt kārttike tathā ।
phālgune'pi samṛddhiḥ syān malamāsaṃ parityajet ।।

gautamīye-
mantrārambhas tu caitre syāt samasta-puruṣārthadaḥ ।
vaiśākhe ratna-lābhaḥ syāt jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam ।।

āṣāḍhe bandhu-nāśaḥ syāt pūrṇāyuḥ śrāvaṇe bhavet ।
prajā-nāśo bhaved bhādre āśvine ratna-sañcayaḥ ।।

kārttike mantra-siddhiḥ syāt mārga-śīrṣe tathā bhavet ।
pauṣe tu śatru-pīḍā syāt māghe medhā-vivardhanam ।
phālgune sarva-kāmāḥ syur mala-māsaṃ parityajet ।।

skānde tatraiva śrī-rukmāṅgada-mohinī-saṃvāde-
kārttike tu kṛtā dīkṣā nṝṇāṃ janma-nikṛntanī ।
tasmāt sarva-prayatnena dīkṣāṃ kurvīta kārttike ।।

śrīmad-gopāla-mantrāṇāṃ dīkṣāyāṃ tu na duṣyati ।
caitra-māse yad uktā tad dīkṣā tatraiva deśikaiḥ ।।

atha bāra-śuddhiḥ
ravau gurau tathā some kartavyaṃ budha-śukrayoḥ ।।
atha nakṣatra-śuddhiḥ

nārada-tantre-
rohiṇī śravaṇārdrā ca dhaniṣṭhā cottarātrayaḥ ।
puṣyaṃ śatabhiṣaś caiva dīkṣā-nakṣatram ucyate ।।

kvacic ca-
aśvinī-rohiṇī-svāti-viśākhā-hastabheṣu ca ।
jyeṣṭhottarātrayeṣv eva kuryān mantrābhiṣecanam ।।

atha tithi-śuddhiḥ

sāra-saṅgrahe-
dvitīyā pañcamī caiva ṣaṣṭhī caiva viśeṣataḥ ।
dvādaśyām api kartavyaṃ trayodaśyām athāpi ca ।।

kvacic ca-
pūrṇimā pañcamī caiva dvitīyā saptamī tathā ।
trayodaśī ca daśamī praśastā sarva-kāmadā ।।

iti

evaṃ śuddhe dine śukla-pakṣe śukra-gurūdaye ।
sal-lagne candra-tārānukūle dīkṣā praśasyate ।।

athātrāpavādaḥ 

rudra-yāmale-
sat-tīrthe'rka-vidhu-grāse tantu-dāmana-parvaṇoḥ ।
mantra-dīkṣāṃ prakurvīta māsa-rkṣādi na śodhayet ।।

sulagna-candra-tārādi-balam atra sadaiva hi ।
labdho atra mantor dīrghāyuḥ-sampat-santati-vardhanaḥ ।।

sūrya-grahaṇa-kālena samāno nāsti kaścana ।
yatra yad yat kṛtaṃ sarvam ananta-phaladaṃ bhavet ।
na māsa-tithi-vārādi-śodhanaṃ sūrya-parvaṇi ।।

tattva-sāgare ca-
durlabhe sad-gurūṇāṃ ca sakṛt saṅga upasthite ।
tad-anujñā yadā labdhā sa dīkṣāvasaro mahān ।।

grāme vā yadi vāraṇye kṣetre vā divase niśi ।
āgacchati gurur daivād yadā dīkṣā tadājñayā ।।

yadaivecchā tadā dīkṣā guror ājñānurūpataḥ ।
na tīrthaṃ na vrataṃ homo na snānaṃ na japa-kriyā ।
dīkṣāyāḥ karaṇaṃ kintu svecchā-prāpte tu sad-gurau ।।

atha maṇḍapa-nirmāṇa-vidhiḥ

kriyāvatyādi-bhedena bhaved dīkṣā caturvidhā ।
tatra kriyāvatī dīkṣā saṅkṣepeṇaiva likhyate ।।

bhūmiṃ saṃskṛtya tasyāṅ cārcayitvā vāstu-devatāḥ ।
sapta-hasta-mitaṃ kuryān maṇḍapaṃ ramya-vedikam ।।

aṣṭa-dhvajaṃ caturdhāraṃ kṣīra-pādapa-toraṇam । triguṇīkṛta-sūtrāḍhyaṃ kuśamālābhiveṣṭitam ।।

atha kuṇḍa-nirmāṇa-vidhiḥ

tasmiṃś ca diśi kauveryāṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ trimekhalam ।
kuṇḍe kuryāc caturviṃśaty-aṅguli-pramitaṃ budhah ।।

khātaṃ trimekhalocchrāya-sahitaṃ tāvad ācaret ।
tasmāt khātād bahiḥ kuryāt kaṇṭham ekāṅgulaṃ dhruvam ।।

tatrādy-mekhalocchrāya-vistārau catur-aṅgulau ।
try-aṅgulau tau dvitīyāyās tṛtīyāyā yugāṅgulau ।।

yoniṃ ca paścime bhāge mekhalā-tritayopari ।
ṣaḍ-aṅgulāṃ ca vistāre dairghye ca dvādaśāṅgulām ।।

ekāṅgulāṃ tathocchrāye madhye chidra-samanvitām ।
gadādharākṛtiṃ kuryād vidhivan mekhalānvitām ।।
śatārdha-home kuṇḍaṃ syād ūrdhva-muṣṭi-karonmitam ।।
śata-home'ratni-mātram sahasre pāṇinā mitam ।
lakṣe caturbhir hastaiś ca koṭau tair aṣṭabhir mitam ।
caturasraṃ kuṇḍa-khātaṃ kurvītādhaś ca tādṛśam ।।

homas tv adhika-saṅkhākaḥ kuṇḍe vai nyūna-saṅkhyayā ।
kṛte kāryo na c anyūna-saṅkhyākaḥ saṅkhayādhike ।।

yathāvidhy eva kartavyaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatnena dhīmatā ।
anyathā bahavo doṣā bhaveyur bahu-duḥkhadāḥ ।।

tad uktaṃ tāntrikaiḥ-
evaṃ lakṣaṇa-saṃyuktaṃ kuṇḍam iṣṭa-phala-pradam ।
aneka-doṣadaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatra nyūnādhikām bhavet ।।

tasmāt samyak parīkṣyaiva kartavyaṃ śubham icchatā ।
hasta-mātraṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vā saṃkṣipte homa-karmaṇi ।।

hārītenāpi -
vistārādhikya-hīnatve alpāyur jāyate dhruvam ।
khātādhikye bhaved yogī hīne tu dhana-saṃkṣayaḥ ।
kuṇḍe vakre ca santāpo maraṇaṃ chinna-mekhale ।।

śokas tu mekhalonatve tadādhikye paśu-kṣayaḥ ।
bhāryā-nāśo yoni-hīne kaṇṭha-hīne śubha-kṣayaḥ ।।

aṅguli-parimāṇaṃ coktam-
tiryag-yavodarāṇyaṣṭāv ūrdhvā vā brīhayas trayaḥ ।
jñeyam aṅguli-mānaṃ tu madhyamā madhya-parvaṇā ।।

iti

viśeṣo apekṣito anyatra srak-sruva-prakriyādikaḥ ।
jñeyo granthāntarāt so atrādhikya-bhītyā na likhyate ।।

atha dīkṣā-maṇḍala-vidhiḥ

athokṣite pañca-gavyair gandhāmbhobhiś ca maṇḍape ।
yathāvidhi likhed dīkṣā-maṇḍalaṃ vedikopari ।।

tan-madhye cāṣṭapatrābjaṃ bahir vṛtta-trayaṃ tataḥ ।
tato rāśīṃs tataḥ pīṭhaṃ catuṣpāda-samanvitam ।।

tasmād bahiś caturdikṣu likhed vīthī-catuṣṭayam ।
śobhāpaśobhā-koṇāḍhyaṃ tato dvāra-catuṣṭayam ।।

atha dīkṣāṅga-pūjā

prātaḥ-kṛtyaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā yathā-sthānaṃ nyaset tataḥ ।
śaṅkhaṃ pūjopacārāṃś ca puro-lekhya-prakārataḥ ।।

tatrādau kumbha-sthāpana-vidhiḥ

gurūn gaṇeśaṃ cābhyarcya pīṭha-pūjāṃ vidhāya ca ।
padma-madhye nyaset śālīṃs taṇḍulāṃś ca kuśāṃs tathā ।।

vahner daśa-kalā yādivarṇādyāś ca kuśopari ।
nyasyābhyarcya japaṃs tāraṃ nyaset kumbhaṃ yathoditam ।।

tāś coktāḥ-
dhūmrārcir uṣmā jvalanī jvālinī visphuliṅinī ।
suśrīḥ surūpā kapilā havya-kavyavahe api ।।

iti

kādyaṣṭhāntair yutā bhādyair ḍāntaiś cārṇair vilomagaiḥ ।
sūryasya ca kalāḥ kumbhe dvādaśa nyasya pūjayet ।।

adhunā tasmin kuṇḍe sūrya-kalānāṃ nyāsādikaṃ likhati-kādyair iti । kakārādyaiṣ ṭha-kārāntair arṇair varṇair yutā dvādaśāpi kalāḥ । ca-kāraḥ samuccaye । bha-kārādyair ḍa-kārāntair varṇair api yutāḥ । nanu, bha-kārādīnāṃ dvādaśa-varṇānāṃ ḍa-kārāntatā kathaṃ syāt ? krameṇa kṣa-kārāntatā-prāptes tatrāha-vilomagaiḥ vyutkrama-prāptaiḥ । ayam arthaḥ-anuloma-paṭhita-ka-kārādyaikaikam akṣaraṃ pratiloma-paṭhita-bha-kārādy-ekaikākṣareṇa sahitam ādau sūrya-kalāsu saṃyojya nyāsādikaṃ kuryād iti । prayogaś ca kaṃ bhaṃ tapanyai nama ity ādi ।।

tāś coktāḥ-
tapanī tāpanī dhūmrā bhrāmarī jvālinī ruciḥ ।
suṣumṇā bhogadā viśvā bodhinī dhāriṇī kṣamā ।।

iti

kubmhāntar nikṣipen mūla-mantreṇa kusumaṃ sitam ।
sākṣataṃ sasitaṃ svarṇaṃ sa-ratnaṃ ca kuśāṃs tathā ।।

tataś cokta-prakāreṇādhāra-rūpam agniṃ kumbha-rūpaṃ sūryaṃ ca vicintya kumbhasya tasya antar madhye śukla-kusumādikaṃ kṣipet । sa-sitaṃ sa-śarkaram । tad uktam- 
prottolayitvā tan-madhye śukla-puṣpaṃ sitā-yutam ।
svarṇaṃ ratnaṃ ca kūrcaṃ ca mūlenaiva vinikṣipet ।।

iti yac ca mūla-granthārthād adhikaṃ kiṃcil likhate, tat pūrva-gatasya yathoditam ity asyānuvartanād iti jñeyam ।।

kumbhaṃ ca vidhinā tīrthāmbunā śuddhena pūrayet ।
jale cendukulā nyasya sasvarāḥ ṣoḍaśārcayet ।।

tāś coktāḥ-
amṛtā mānadā pūṣā tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭī ratir dhṛtiḥ ।
śaśinī candrikā kāntir jyotsnā śrīḥ prītir aṅgadā ।
pūrṇā pūrṇāmṛtā ca ।।

iti

śuddhāmbu-pūrite śaṅkhe kṣiptvā gandhāṣṭakaṃ kalāḥ ।
āvāhya sarvās tāḥ prāṇa-pratiṣṭhām ācaret kramāt ।।

gandhāṣṭakaṃ coktam-
uśīraṃ kuṅkumaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bālakaṃ cāgurur murā ।
jaṭā-māṃsī candanaṃ cetīṣṭaṃ gandhāṣṭakaṃ hareḥ ।।

iti

kaiścic candana-karpūrāguru-kuṅkuma-rocanāḥ ।
kakkola-kapi-māṃsyaś ca gandhāṣṭakam idaṃ matam ।।

tathaivākārajā varṇaiḥ kādibhir daśabhir daśa ।
ukārajāṣṭakārādyaiḥ pa-kārādyair ma-kāra-jāḥ ।।

catasro bindujāḥ ṣādyaiś caturbhir nāda-jāḥ kalāḥ ।
svaraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhir yuktā nyasec chaṅkhe ca ṣoḍaśa ।।

tāś coktāḥ-
sṛṣṭir ṛddhiḥ smṛtir medhā kāntir lakṣmīr dhṛitḥ sthirā ।
sthitiḥ siddhir akārotthāḥ kalā daśa samīritaḥ ।।

jarā ca pālinī śāntir aiśvarī rati-kāmike ।
varadā hlādinī prītir dīrghā cokāra-jāḥ kalāḥ ।।

tīkṣṇā raudrā bhayā nidrā tantīr kṣut krodhanī kriyā ।
utkārī caiva mṛtyuś ca makārākṣarajāḥ kalāḥ ।।

nivṛttiś ca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntis tathaiva ca ।
indhikā dīpikā caiva recikā mocikā parā ।।

sūkṣmā sūkṣmāmṛtā jñānājñānā cāpy āyanī tathā ।
vyāpinī vyoma-rūpā ca anantā nāda-sambhavāḥ ।।

iti 
nyāsaṃ kalānāṃ sarvāsāṃ kuryād ekaikaśaḥ kramāt ।
nāmoccārya caturthāntaṃ tat-tad-varṇair namo antakam ।।

pūrvaṃ prāṇa-pratiṣṭhāyās tāsām āvāhanāt param ।
ṛcaḥ pañca yathā-sthānaṃ paṭhet tāś cārcayet kalāḥ ।।

haṃśaḥ śuciṣad ity ādau pratad viṣṇus tataḥ param ।
tryambakaṃ tat savitur viṣṇur yonim iti kramāt ।।

tac ca śaṅkhodakaṃ kumbhe mūla-mantreṇa nikṣipet ।
pidadhyāt tan mukhaṃ śakra-vallī-cūtādi-pallavaiḥ ।।

śarāvenātha puṣpādi-yuktenācchādya tat punaḥ ।
saṃveṣṭya vastra-yugmena tataḥ kumbhaṃ ca maṇḍayet ।।

atha kumbhe śrī-bhagavat-pūjā-vidhiḥ

tasminn āvāhya kalase paraṃ tejo yathā-vidhi ।
sakalīkṛtya cācāryaḥ pūjayed āsanādibhiḥ ।।

sakalīkaraṇaṃ coktam- devatāṅge ṣaḍ-aṅgānāṃ nyāsaḥ syāt sakalī-kṛtiḥ ।।

kecic cāhuḥ kara-nyāsau vinākhilaiḥ ।
nyāsais tat-tejasaḥ sāṅgīkaraṇaṃ sakalīkṛtaḥ ।।

evaṃ ca kumbhe taṃ sāṅgopāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ prabhum ।
agrato lekhya-vidhinārcayed bhojyārpaṇāvadhi ।।

naivedyārpaṇataḥ paścān maṇḍalasya ca sarvataḥ ।
sa-dīpān paiṣṭikān nyasyet sa-bījāṅkura-bhājanāt ।।

atha dīkṣā-homa-vidhiḥ

tato dīkṣāṅga-homārthaṃ kuṇḍalasya ca sarvataḥ ।
saṃmārjya darbha-mārjanyā yathā-vidhy upalepayet ।।

vikīrya sarṣapāṃs tatra gavyaiḥ samprokṣya pañcabhiḥ ।
madhye sampūjayed vāstu-puruṣaṃ dikṣu tat-patīn ।।

śoṣaṇādīni kuṇḍasya kṛtvā prokṣya kuśāmbubhiḥ ।
ullikhya cāsmin yony-ādi-sahitaṃ maṇḍalaṃ likhet ।।

śrī-bījaṃ madhya-yonau ca vilikhyābhukṣya pūjayet ।
nidhāya tatra puṣpādi-viṣṭaraṃ sādhu kalpayet ।।

tatra lakṣmī-mṛtyu-snānāṃ viṣṇuṃ cāvāhya pūjayet ।
tāmrādi-pātreṇānīyāgrato agniṃ sthāpayec chubhram ।।

gandhādināgnim abhyarcya viṣṇoḥ sakrīḍataḥ śriyā ।
reto-rūpaṃ vicintyāmuṃ kuṇḍaṃ tāreṇa cārcayet ।।

vaiśvānareti mantreṇācchācyāgniṃ taṃ sad-indhanaiḥ ।
cit-piṅgaleti prajvālyopatiṣṭhed agnim ity amum ।।

jihvā nyasyet sapta tsminn apy aṅgeṣv aṅga-devatāḥ ।
ṣaṭsu ṣaṭ nyasya mūrtīś ca nyasyāṣṭābhyarcayec ca tāḥ ।।

sapta-jihvāś coktāḥ-
hiraṇyā gaganā raktā tathā kṛṣṇā ca suprabhā ।
bahu-rūpāti-rūpā ca sapta jihvā vasor imāḥ ।।

athāṅga-devatāḥ

sahasrārciḥ svasti-pūrṇa uttiṣṭha-puruṣas tathā ।
dhūma-vyāpī sapta-jihvo dhanurdhara iti smṛtaḥ ।।

aṣṭa-mūrtayaś ca

jāta-vedāḥ sapta-jihvo havya-vāhana eva ca ।
aśvodaraja-saṃjñaś ca tathā vaiśvānaro aparaḥ ।
kaumāra-tejāś ca tathā viśvadeva-mukhāhvayau ।।

iti

tato vahniṃ paristīrya saṃskṛtājyaṃ yathā-vidhi ।
hutvā ca vyāhṛtīḥ paścāt trīn vārān juhuyāt punaḥ ।।

tato asya garbhadhānādīn vivhāntān yathākramam ।
saṃskārān ācared ukta-mantreṇāṣṭāhutais tathā ।।

itthaṃ hi saṃskṛte vahnau pīṭham abhyarcya tatra ca ।
devam āvāhya gandhādi-dīpānta-vidhinārcayet ।।

taṃ cāgniṃ deva-rasanāṃ saṃkalpyāṣṭottaraṃ budhaḥ ।
sahasraṃ juhuyāt sarpiḥ-śarkarā-pāyasair yutaiḥ ।।

hutvājyenātha mahatī-vyāhṛtīr vidhinā kṛtī ।
graharkṣa-karaṇādibhyo baliṃ dadyād yathoditam ।।

atha homa-dravyādi-parimāṇam

karṣa-mātraṃ ghṛtaṃ home śukti-mātraṃ payaḥ smṛtam ।
uktāni pañca-gavyāni tat-samāni manīṣibhiḥ ।।

tat-samaṃ madhu-dugdhānnam akṣa-mātram udāhṛtam ।
dadhi prasṛti-mātraṃ syāt lājāḥ syuḥ muṣṭi-saṃmitāḥ ।।

। ity ādi ।

atha natvāmbu-pānārthaṃ pradāyācamanāni ca ।
ātmārpaṇāntam abhyarcya lekhyena vidhinācaret ।।

atha guru-śiṣya-niyamādiḥ

vrata-sthaṃ vāg-yataṃ śiṣyaṃ praveśyātha yathā-vidhi ।
tad-dehe mātṛkāṃ sāṅgāṃ nyasyāthopadiśec ca tām ।।

devaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ kumbha-gataṃ cānusmaran guruḥ ।
japtvāṣṭottara-sāhasraṃ śayīta prāśya kiṃcana ।।

darbhoparyajine tvaiṇe niviṣṭo mātṛkāṃ smaran ।
guruṃ ca śiṣyo nidrāṇaṃ tāṃ śayīta japan vratī ।।

iti pūrva-dina-kṛtyam ।

atha tad-dina-kṛtyāni

prātaḥ-kṛtyaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā kumbhaṃ cābhyarcya pūrvavat ।
hutvā dattvā baliṃ karmānyat kuryāt svārpaṇāvadhi ।।

saṃhāra-mudrayā kṛṣṇe saṃyojyāvṛtti-devatāḥ ।
tam cāmṛta-mayaṃ dhyātvā svasmiṃś cāgniṃ vilāpayet ।।

dhvaja-toraṇa-dik-kumbha-maṇḍapādy-adhidevatāḥ ।
sarvā vibhāvya cid-rūpāḥ kumbhe saṃyojya pūjayet ।।

ato guruṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca viṣvaksenaṃ ca pūjayet ।
udvāsya kalasaṃ spṛṣṭvā śatam aṣṭottaraṃ japet ।।

kṛtopavāsaḥ śiṣyo athat prātaḥ-kṛtyaṃ vidhāya saḥ ।
śukla-vastraḥ suveśaḥ san viprān dravyeṇa toṣayet ।।

guruṃ ca bhagavad-dṛṣṭyā parikramya praṇamya ca ।
dattvoktāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ tasmai sva-śarīraṃ samarpayet ।।

atha dīkṣāṅga-pūjā

tathā ca daśama-skandhe [bhp ] -
iyad eva hi sac-chiṣyaiḥ kartavyaṃ guru-niṣkṛtam ।
yad vai viśuddha-bhāvena sarvārthātmārpaṇaṃ gurau ।।

athābhiṣecana-vidhiḥ

yāgālayād uttarasyām āśāyāṃ snāna-maṇḍape ।
pīṭhe niveśya taṃ śiṣyaṃ kārayec choṣaṇādikam ।।

pīṭha-nyāsāntam akhilaṃ mātṛkānyāsa-pūrvakam ।
nyāsaṃ śiṣya-tanau kṛtvā pīṭha-mantreṇa pūjayet ।।

sad-ūrvākṣata-puṣpāṃ ca mūrdhni śiṣyasya rocanām ।
nidhāya kalasaṃ tasyāntike vādyādinā nayet ।।

śrī-kṛṣṇam atha samprārthya guruḥ kumbhasya vāsasā ।
nīrājya śiṣyaṃ tan-mūrdhni nyaset tat-pallavādikam ।।

tad uktam-
vidhivat kumbham uddhṛtya tan-mukhasthān sura-drumān ।
śiśoḥ śirasi vinyasya mātṛkāṃ manasā japet ।।

tataḥ kumbhāmbhasā śiṣyaṃ prokṣya trir mūla-mantrataḥ ।
viprāśīr maṅgalodghoṣair abhiṣiñcen manūn paṭhan ।।

athābhiṣeka-mantrāḥ

vaśiṣṭha-saṃhitāyām-
surās tvām abhiṣiñcyaṃ tu brahma-viṣṇu-maheśvarāḥ ।
vāsudevo jagannāthas tathā saṅkarṣaṇo vibhuḥ ।।

pradyumnaś cāniruddhaś ca bhavantu vibhavāya te ।
ākhaṇḍalo agnir bhagavān yamo vai nirṛtis tathā ।।

varuṇaḥ pavanaś caiva dhanādhyakṣas tathā śivaḥ ।
brahmaṇā sahitā hy ete dik-pālāḥ pāntu vaḥ sadā ।।

kīrtir lakṣmīr dhṛtir medhā puṣṭiḥ śraddhā kriyā gatiḥ ।
buddhir lajjā vapuḥ śāntir māyā nidrā ca bhāvanā ।।

etās tvām abhiṣiñcantu rāhuḥ ketuś ca pūjitāḥ ।
deva-dānava-gandharvā yakṣa-rākṣasa-pannagāḥ ।।

ṛṣayo munayo gāvo deva-mātara eva ca ।
deva-patnyo dhruvā nāgā daityā apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।।

astrāṇi sarva-śastrāṇi rājāno vāhanāni ca ।
auṣadhāni ca ratnāni kālasyāvayavāś ca ye ।।

saritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailās tīrthāni jaladā nadāḥ ।
ete tvām abhiṣiñcantu dharma-kāmārtha-siddhaye ।।

atha mantra-kathana-vidhiḥ

paridhāyāṃśuke śiṣya ācānto yāga-maṇḍape ।
gatvā bhaktyā guruṃ natvā guror āsīta dakṣiṇe ।।

guruḥ samarpya gandhādīn puruṣāhāra-saṃmitam ।
nivedya pāyasaṃ kṛṣṇe kuryāt puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ ।।

sāmpradāyika-mudrādi-bhūṣitaṃ taṃ kṛtāñjalim ।
pañcāṅga-pramukhair nyāsaiḥ kuryāt śrī-kṛṣṇa-sāc-chiśum ।।

nyasya pāṇi-talaṃ mūrdhni tasya karṇe ca dakṣiṇe ।
ṛṣy-ādi-yuktaṃ vidhavan mantraṃ vāra-trayaṃ vadet ।।

dīrgha-mantraṃ ca śiṣyasya yāvad āgrahaṇaṃ paṭhet ।
guru-daivata-mantraikyaṃ śiṣyas taṃ bhāvayan paṭhet ।।

sākṣataṃ gurur ādāya vāri śiṣyasya dakṣiṇe ।
kare'rpayed vadan mantro ayaṃ samo astv āvayor iti ।।

svasmāj jyotirmayīṃ vidyāṃ gacchantīṃ bhāvayed guruḥ ।
āgatāṃ bhāvayec chiṣyo dhanyo asmīti viśeṣataḥ ।।

mahā-prasādaṃ śiṣyāya dattvā tat-pāyasaṃ guruḥ ।
nidadhyād akṣatān mūrdhni tasya yacchan śubhāśiṣam ।।

guruṇā kṛpayā dattaṃ śiṣyaś cāvāpya taṃ manum ।
aṣṭottara-śataṃ japtvā samayān śṛṇuyāt tataḥ ।।

atha samayāḥ

śrī-nārada-pañcarātre-
sva-mantro nopadeṣṭavyo vaktavyaś ca na saṃsadi ।
gopanīyaṃ tathā śāstraṃ rakṣaṇīyaṃ śarīravat ।।

vaiṣṇavānāṃ parā bhaktir ācāryāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
pūjanaṃ ca yathā-śakti tān āpannāṃś ca pālayet ।।

prāptam āyatanād viṣṇoḥ śirasāṃ praṇato vahet ।
nikṣiped ambhasi tato na pated avanau yathā ।।

soma-sūryāntarasthaṃ ca gavāśvatthāgni-madhyagam ।
bhāvayed daivataṃ viṣṇuṃ guru-vipra-śarīragam ।।

yatra yatra parivādo mātsaryāc chrūyate guroḥ ।
tatra tatra na vastavyaṃ niryāyāt saṃsmaran harim ।।

yaiḥ kṛtā ca guror nindā vibhoḥ śāstrasya nārada ।
nāpi taiḥ saha vastavyaṃ vaktavyaṃ vā kathañcana ।।

pradakṣiṇe prayāṇe ca pradāne ca viśeṣataḥ ।
prabhāte ca pravāse ca sva-mantraṃ bahuśaḥ smaret ।।

svapne vākṣi-samakṣaṃ vā āścaryam atiharṣadam ।
akasmād yadi jāyeta na khyātavyaṃ guror vinā ।।

pañcarātrāntare-
samayāṃś ca pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepāt pañcarātrakāt ।
na bhakṣayen matsya-māṃsaṃ kūrma-śūkarakāṃs tathā ।।

kāṃsya-pātre na bhuñjīta na plakṣa-baṭa-patrayoḥ ।
devāgāre na niṣṭhīvet kṣutaṃ cātra vivarjayet ।
na sopānatka-caraṇaḥ praviśed antaraṃ kvacit ।।

ekādaśyāṃ na cāśnīyāt pakṣayor ubhayor api ।
jāgaraṃ niśi kurvīta viśeṣāc cārcayed vibhum ।।

sammohana-tantre ca-
gopayed devatām iṣṭāṃ gopayed gurum ātmanaḥ ।
gopayec ca nijaṃ mantraṃ gopayen nija-mālikām ।।

iti

catur-yuk-śata-saṅkhyeṣu prāg guroḥ samayeṣu ca ।
śiṣyeṇāṅgīkṛteṣv eva dīkṣā kaiścana manyate ।।

tathā ca viṣṇu-yāmale-
guruḥ parīkṣayec chiṣyaṃ saṃvatsaram atandritaḥ ।
niyamān vihitān varjyān śrāvayec ca catuḥśatam ।।

brāhme muhūrta utthānaṃ mahā-viṣṇoḥ prabodhanam ।
nīrājanaṃ ca vādyena prātaḥ-snānaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

viśuddhāhata-yug vastra-dhāraṇaṃ devatārcanam ।
gopī-candana-mṛtsnāyāḥ sarvadā corddhva-puṇḍrakam ।।

pañcāyudhānāṃ vidhṛtiś caraṇāmṛta-sevanam ।
tulasī-maṇi-mālādi-bhūṣā-dhāraṇam anvaham ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-pūjā pratimāsu ca bhaktitaḥ ।
nirmālya-tulasī-bhakṣas tulasya-vacayo vidheḥ ।।

vidhinā tāntrikī sandhyā śikhā-bandho hi karmaṇi ।
viṣṇu-pādodakenaiva pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇa-kriyā ।
mahārājopacāraiś ca śaktyāṃ sampūjanaṃ hareḥ ।।

viṣṇu-bhakty-avirodhena nitya-naimittikī kriyā ।
bhūta-śuddhy-ādi-karaṇaṃ nyāsāḥ sarve yathā-vidhi ।।

navīna-phala-puṣpāder bhaktitaḥ saṃnivedanam ।
tulasī-pūjanaṃ nityaṃ śrī-bhāgavata-pūjanam ।।

tri-kālaṃ viṣṇu-pūjā ca purāṇa-śrutir anvaham ।
viṣṇor niveditānāṃ vai vastrādīnāṃ ca dhāraṇam ।।

sarveṣāṃ puṇya-kāryāṇāṃ svāmi-dṛṣṭyā pravartanam ।
gurv-ājñā-grahaṇaṃ tatra viśvāso guruṇodite ।।

yathā-sva-mudrā-racanaṃ gīta-nṛtyādi bhaktitaḥ ।
śaṅkhādi-dhvani-māṅgalya-līlādy-abhinayo hareḥ ।
nitya-homa-vidhānaṃ ca bali-dānaṃ yathā-vidhi ।।

sādhūnāṃ svāgataṃ pūjā śeṣa-naivedya-bhojanam ।
tāmbūla-śeṣa-grahaṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaiḥ saha saṅgamaḥ ।।

viśiṣṭa-dharma-jijñāsā daśamyādi-dina-traye ।
vrate niyamataḥ svāsthyaṃ santoṣo yena kena vai ।।

parvayātrādi-karaṇaṃ vāsarāṣṭaka-sad-vidhiḥ ।
viṣṇoḥ sarvartu-caryā ca mahārājopacārataḥ ।।

sarveṣāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vratānāṃ paripālanam ।
gurāv īśvara-bhāvaś ca tulasī-saṅgrahaḥ sadā ।।
śayanādy-upacāraś ca rāmādīnāṃ ca cintanam ।।
sandhyayoḥ śayanaṃ naiva na śaucaṃ mṛttikāṃ vinā ।
tiṣṭhatācamanaṃ naiva tathā gurvāsanāsanam ।।

gurv-agre pāda-vistāra-cchāyāyā laṅghanaṃ guroḥ ।
śaktau snāna-kriyā-hānir devatārcana-lopanam ।।

devatānāṃ gurūṇāṃ ca pratyutthānādya-bhāvanam ।
guroḥ purastāt pāṇḍityaṃ prauḍha-pāda-kriyā tathā ।।

amantra-tilakācāmo nīlī-vastra-vidhāraṇam ।
abhaktaiḥ saha maitry-ādi asac-chāstra-parigrahaḥ ।
tuccha-saṅga-sukhāsaktir madya-māṃsa-niṣevaṇam ।।

mādakauṣadha-sevā ca masurādy-anna-bhojanam ।
śākaṃ tumbī kalañjādi tathābhaktānna-saṅgrahaḥ ।
avaiṣṇava-vratārambhas tathā japyam avaiṣṇavam ।।

abhicārādi-karaṇaṃ śaktyā gauṇopacārakam ।
śokādi-pāravaśyaṃ ca dig-viddhaikādaśī-vratam ।।

śuklākṛṣṇāvibhedaś cāsad-vyāpāro vrate tathā ।
śaktau phalādi-bhuktiś ca śrāddhaṃ caikādaśī-dine ।।

dvādaśyāṃ ca divā-svāpas tulasyāvacayas tathā ।
tatra viṣṇor divā-snānaṃ śrāddhaṃ hary-aniveditaiḥ ।।

vṛddhāv atulasī-śrāddhaṃ tathā śrāddham avaiṣṇavam ।
caraṇāmṛta-pāne'pi śuddhy-arthācamana-kriyā ।।

kāṣṭhāsanopaviṣṭena vāsudevasya pūjanam ।
pūjā-kāle'sad-ālāpaḥ kara-vīrādi-pūjanam ।।

āyasaṃ dhūpa-pātrādi tiryak-puṇḍraṃ pramādataḥ ।
pūjā cāsaṃskṛtair dravyais tathā cañcala-cittataḥ ।।

eka-hasta-praṇāmādi akāle svāmi-darśanam ।
paryuṣitādi-duṣṭānām annādīnāṃ nivedanam ।।

saṅkhyāṃ vinā mantra-japas tathā mantra-prakāśanam ।
sadā śaktyāṃ mukhya-lopo gauṇakāla-parigrahaḥ ।।

prasādāgrahaṇaṃ viṣṇor varjayed vaiṣṇavaḥ sadā ।
catuḥ-śataṃ vidhīn etān niṣedhān śrāvayed guruḥ ।।

aṅgīkāre kṛte bāḍhaṃ tan-nīrājana-pūrvakam ।
deva-pūjāṃ kārayitvā dakṣa-karṇe mantraṃ japet ।।

iti

tataś cotthāya pūrṇātmā daṇḍavat praṇamed gurum ।
tat-pāda-paṅkajaṃ śiṣyaḥ pratiṣṭhāpya sva-mūrdhani ।।

atha nyāsān guruḥ svasmin kṛtvāntar-yajanaṃ tathā ।
sāṣṭaṃ sahasraṃ tan-mantraṃ sva-śakty-akṣataye japet ।।

śiṣyaḥ kumbhādi tat sarvaṃ dravam anyac ca śaktitaḥ ।
dattvābhyarcya guruṃ natvā viprān saṃpūjya bhojayet ।।

śrī-guror brāhmaṇānāṃ ca śubhāśīrbhiḥ samedhitaḥ ।
tān anujñāpya gurvādīn bhuñjīta saha bandhubhiḥ ।।

iti dīkṣā-vidhānena yo mantraṃ labhate guroḥ ।
sa bhāgyavān cirañjīvī kṛta-kṛtyaś ca jāyate ।।

tathā ca saṃmohana-tantre śrī-śivomā-saṃvāde-
evaṃ yaḥ kurute martyaḥ kare tasya vibhūtayaḥ ।
ataḥ paraṃ mahā-bhāge nānyat karmāsti bhūtale ।
yasyācaraṇa-mātreṇa sākṣāt kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati ।।

prāyaḥ prapañca-sārādāv ukto ayaṃ tāntriko vidhiḥ ।
dīkṣāyā likhyate divyo vidhiḥ paurāṇiko adhunā ।।

atha varāha-purāṇokta-dīkṣā-vidhiḥ

idānīṃ śṛṇu me devi pañca-pātaka-nāśanam ।
yajanaṃ deva-devasya viṣṇoḥ putra-vasu-pradam ।।

iha janmani dāridrya-vyādhi-kuṣṭhādi-pīḍitaḥ ।
alakṣmīvān aputras tu yo bhavet puruṣo bhuvi ।
tasya sadyo bhavel lakṣmīr āyur vittaṃ sutāḥ sukham ।।

dṛṣṭvā tu maṇḍale devi devaṃ devyā samanvitam ।
nārāyaṇaṃ paraṃ devaṃ yaḥ paśyati vidhānataḥ ।।

pūjitaṃ nava-nābhe tu ṣoḍaśābja-dale tathā ।
ācārya-darśitaṃ devaṃ mantra-mūrtim ayonijam ।।

kārttike māsi śuddhāyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।
sarvāsu ca yajed devaṃ dvādaśīṣu vidhānataḥ ।।

saṅkrāntau ca mahābhāge candra-sūrya-grahe'pi vā ।
yaḥ paśyati hariṃ devaṃ pūjitaṃ guruṇā śubhe ।
tasya sadyo bhavet tuṣṭiḥ pāpa-dhvaṃso apy aśeṣataḥ ।।
sa sāmānyo hi devānāṃ bhavatīti na saṃśayaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇa-kṣatriya-viśāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca parīkṣaṇam ।
saṃvatsaraṃ guruḥ kuryāj jāti-śauca-kriyādibhiḥ ।।

upasannāṃs tato jñātvā hṛdayenāvadhārayet ।
te'pi bhaktimato jñātvā ātmanaḥ parameśvaram ।
saṃvatsaraṃ guror bhaktiṃ kuryur viṣṇāv ivācalām ।।
saṃvatsaraṃ tataḥ pūrṇe guruṃ caiva prasādayet ।।
bhagavaṃs tvat-prasādena saṃsārārṇava-tāraṇam ।
icchāmas tv aihikīṃ lakṣmīṃ viśeṣeṇa tapodhana ।।

evam abhyarthya medhāvī guruṃ viṣṇum ivāgrataḥ ।
abhyarcya tad-anujñāto daśamyāṃ kārttikasya tu ।।

kṣīra-vṛkṣa-samudbhūtaṃ mantritaṃ parameṣṭhinā ।
bhakṣayitvā śayītorvyāṃ devadevasya sannidhau ।।

svapnān dṛṣṭvā guror agre śrāvayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
tataḥ śubhāśubhaṃ tadvad ālapet paramo guruḥ ।
ekādaśyām upoṣyātha snātvā devālayaṃ vrajet ।।

guruś ca maṇḍalaṃ bhūmau kalptāyāṃ tu vartayet ।
lakṣaṇair vividhair bhūmiṃ lakṣayitvā vidhānataḥ ।।

ṣoḍaśāraṃ likhec cakraṃ nava-nābham athāpi vā ।
aṣṭa-patram atho vāpi likhitvā darśayed budhaḥ ।।

netra-bandhaṃ prakurvīta sita-vastreṇa yatnataḥ ।
varṇānukramataḥ śiṣyān purṣpa-hastān praveśayet ।।

nava-nābhaṃ yadā kuryān maṇḍalaṃ varṇakair budhaḥ ।
tadānīṃ pūrvato devam indram aindryāṃ tu pūjayet ।।

loka-pālam athāgneyyām agniṃ sampūjayed dvijaḥ ।
yamaṃ tad anu yāmyāyāṃ nairṛtyāṃ nirṛtiṃ nyaset ।
vāruṇyāṃ varuṇaṃ caiva vāyavyāṃ pavanaṃ yajet ।।

dhanadaṃ cottare nyasya rudram aiśāna-gocare ।
sampūjyaivaṃ vidhānena dik-patreṣu viśeṣataḥ ।
adhaḥ-patre tathā viṣṇum arcayet parameśvaram ।।

pūrva-patre balaṃ pūjya pradyumnaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā ।
aniruddhaṃ tathā pūjya paścime cottare tathā ।
pūjayed vāsudevaṃ tu sarva-pātaka-śāntidam ।।

aiśānyāṃ vinyasec chaṅkham āgneyyāṃ cakram eva ca ।
saumyāyāṃ tu gadā pūjyā vāyavyāṃ padmam eva ca ।।

nairṛtyāṃ muṣalaṃ pūjyaṃ dakṣiṇe garuḍaṃ tathā ।
vāmato vinyasel lakṣmīṃ devadevasya buddhimān ।।

dhanuś caiva ca khaḍgaṃ ca devasya purato nyaset ।
śrīvatsaṃ kaustubhaṃ caiva devasya purato arcayet ।।

evaṃ pūjya yathā-nyāyaṃ devadevaṃ janārdanam ।
diṅ-maṇḍale ca vinyasya cāṣṭau kumbhān vidhānataḥ ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ kalasaṃ caiva navamaṃ tatra kalpayet ।।

snāpayen mukti-kāmāṃs tu vaiṣṇavena ghaṭena tu ।
śrī-kāmān snāpayet tadvad aindreṇātha ghaṭena tu ।।

jaya-pratāpa-kāmāṃs tu āgneyenābhiṣecayet ।
mṛtyuñjaya-vidhānena yāmyena snāpanaṃ tathā ।।

duṣṭa-pradhvaṃsnāyālaṃ nairṛtena vidhīyate ।
śāntaye vāruṇyenātha pāpa-nāśāya vāyavam ।।

dravya-sampatti-kāmasya kauvareṇa vidhīyate ।
raudreṇa jñāna-hetus tu loka-pāla-ghaṭās tv ime ।।

ekaikena naraḥ snātaḥ sarva-pāpa-varjitaḥ ।
bhaved avyāhata-jñānaḥ śrīmāṃś ca puruṣaḥ sadā ।।

kiṃ punar navabhiḥ snāto naraḥ pātaka-varjitaḥ ।
jāyate viṣṇu-sadṛśaḥ sadyo rājāthavā punaḥ ।।

athavā dikṣu sarvāsu yathā-saṅkhyena lokapān ।
pūjayet sva-sva-nāmnā tu ṣaḍ-bhinnena vidhānataḥ ।।

evaṃ sampūjya devāṃs tu loka-pālān prasanna-dhīḥ ।
paścāt parīkṣitān śiṣyān baddha-netrān praveśayet ।।

āgneya-dhāraṇā-dagdhān vāyunā vidhūtāṃs tataḥ ।
somenāpy āyitān paścāc chrāvayen niyamān budhaḥ ।।

na ninded abrāhmaṇān devān viṣṇuṃ brāhmaṇam eva ca ।
rudram ādiyam agniṃ ca loka-pālān grahāṃs tathā ।
vandeta vaiṣṇavaṃ cāpi puruṣaṃ pūrva-dīkṣitam ।।

evaṃ tu samayān śrāvya paścād dhomaṃ tu kārayet ।
tattvāni śiṣya-deheṣu vinyasya ca viśodhayet ।।
oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarva-rūpiṇe huṃ svāhā ।।
ṣoḍaśākṣara-mantreṇa homayej jvalitānalaḥ ।
garbhādhānādikāś caiva kriyāḥ sarvāś ca kārayet ।।

tribhis tribhir āhutibhir devadevasya sannidhau ।
tato apanīya dṛg-bandhaṃ puraḥ śiṣyaṃ niveśya ca ।
prāyaḥ pūrvokta-vidhinā mantraṃ tasmai gurur diśet ।।

homānte dīkṣitaḥ paścād dāpayed guru-dakṣiṇām ।
hasty-aśva-ratna-kaṭakaṃ hema-grāmādikaṃ nṛpaḥ ।।

dāpayed gurave prājño madhyamo madhyamāṃ tathā ।
dāpayed itaro yugmaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ yathā-vidhi ।।

evaṃ kṛte tu yat puṇyaṃ māhātmyaṃ jāyate dhare ।
tad aśakyaṃ tu gaditum api varṣa-śatair api ।।

dīkṣitātmā guror bhūtvā vārāhaṃ śṛṇuyād yadi ।
tena vedāḥ purāṇāni sarve mantrāḥ susaṅgrahāḥ ।।

japtāḥ syuḥ puṣkare tīrthe prayāge sindhu-sāgare ।
devahūte kurukṣetre vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

graheṇa viṣuve caiva yat phalaṃ japatāṃ bhavet ।
tat phalaṃ dviguṇaṃ tasya dīkṣito yaḥ śṛṇoti ca ।।

devā api tapaḥ kṛtvā dhyāyanti ca vadanti ca ।
kadā me bhārate varṣe janma syād bhūta-dhāriṇi ।।

dīkṣitāś ca bhaviṣyāmo vārāhaṃ śṛṇumaḥ kadā ।
vārāhaṃ ṣoḍaśātmānaṃ yuktā dehe kadācana ।
paśyāmaḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ yad gatvā na punar bhavet ।।

evaṃ jalpanti vibudhā manasā cintayanti ca ।
vārāha-yāgaṃ kārttikyāṃ kadā drakṣyāmahe dhare ।।

eṣa te vidhir uddiṣṭo mayā te bhūta-dhāriṇi ।
deva-gandharva-yakṣāṇāṃ sarvathā durlabho hy asau ।।

evaṃ yo vetti tattvena yaś ca paśyati maṇḍalam ।
yaś cemaṃ śṛṇuyād devi sarve muktā iti śrutiḥ ।।

atha saṅkṣipta-dīkṣā

saṅkṣiptaś cātha dīkṣāyā vidhir eṣa vilikhyate ।
mukhya-kalpe hy aśaktasya janasya syād dhitāya ca ।।

su-muhūrte'tha samprāpte sarvatobhadra-maṇḍale ।
nūtanaṃ gandha-puṣpādi-maṇḍitaṃ kalasaṃ nyaset ।।

vastrāvṛtaṃ payaḥ pūrṇaṃ pañca-pallava-saṃyutam ।
sarvauṣadhi-pañca-ratna-mṛtsnā-saptaka-garbhitam ।।

mṛttikāś ca saptoktāḥ-
aśva-sthānād gaja-sthānād valmīkāc ca catuṣpathāt ।
rāja-dvārāc ca goṣṭhāc ca nadyāḥ kūlān mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

iti

kṛṣṇam abhyarcya taṃ kumbhaṃ kuśa-kūrcena deśikaḥ ।
deya-mantreṇa sāṣṭaṃ tu sahasram abhimantrayet ।।

tad-adbhiḥ pūrvavac chiṣyam abhiṣicya diśen manum ।
śiṣyo arcayed guruṃ bhaktyā yathā-śakti dvijān api ।।

athopadeśas tattva-sāgare-
atrāpy aśaktaḥ kaścic ced abjam abhyarcya sākṣatam ।
tad-ambhasābhiṣicyāṣṭa vārān mūlena ke karam ।।

nidhāyāmuṃ japet karṇe upadeśeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
candra-sūrya-grahe tīrthe siddha-kṣetre śivālaye ।
mantra-mātra-prakathanam upadeśaḥ sa ucyate ।।

tatra tatraiva viśeṣaḥ śrī-nārada-pañcarātre ।
vitta-lobhād vimuktasya svalpa-vittasya dehinaḥ ।
saṃsāra-bhaya-bhītasya viṣṇu-bhaktasya tattvataḥ ।।

agnāv ājyānvite bījaiḥ salilaiḥ kevalaiś ca vā ।
dravya-hīnasya kurvīta vacasānugrahaṃ guruḥ ।।

yaḥ samaḥ sarva-bhūteṣu virāgo vīta-matsaraḥ ।
jitendriyaḥ śucir dakṣaḥ sarvāṅgāvayavānvitaḥ ।।

karmaṇā manasā vācā bhīte cābhayadaḥ sadā ।
sama-buddhi-padaṃ prāptas tatrāpi bhagavan-mayaḥ ।।

pañca-kāla-paraś caiva pañcarātrārthavit tathā ।
viṣṇu-tattvaṃ parijñāya ekaṃ cāneka-bhedagam ।
vīkṣayen medinīṃ sarvāṃ kiṃ punaś copasannatān ।।

atha mantra-dāna-māhātmyam

skānde brahma-nārada-saṃvāde -
iha kīrtiṃ vadānyatvaṃ prajā-vṛddhiṃ dhanaṃ sukham ।
vidyā-dānena labhate sāttviko nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

yathā surāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ paramaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।
tathaiva sarva-dānānāṃ vidyā-dānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam ।।

yāvac ca pātakaṃ tena kṛtaṃ janma-śatair api ।
tat sarvaṃ nāśam āpnoti vidyā-dānena dehinām ।।

vidyā-dānāt paraṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।
yena dattena cāpnoti śivaṃ parama-kāraṇam ।।

iti śrī-gopāla-bhaṭṭa-vilikhite śrī-bhagavad-bhakti-vilāse daikṣiko nāma dvitīyo vilāsaḥ ।

sauciya-vilasa

tṛtīya-vilāsaḥ śaucīyaḥ

vande'nantādbhutaiśvaryaṃ śrī-caitanyaṃ mahāprabhum ।
nīco api yat-prasādāt syāt sadācāra-pravartakaḥ ।।

puṃso gṛhīta-dīkṣasya śrī-kṛṣṇaṃ pūjayiṣyataḥ ।
ācāro likhyate kṛtyaṃ śruti-smṛty-anusārataḥ ।।

atha dīkṣitasya pūjāyā nityatā

labdhvā mantraṃ tu yo nityaṃ nārcayen mantra-devatām ।
sarva-karma-phalaṃ tasyāniṣṭaṃ yacchati devatā ।।

atha sad-ācāraḥ

na kiñcit kasyacit sidhyet sad-ācāraṃ vinā yataḥ ।
tasmād avaśyaṃ sarvatra sad-ācāro hy apekṣyate ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ] -
vaṛṇāśramācaravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān ।
viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyat tat-toṣa-kāraṇam ।।

atha sad-ācārasya nityatā

mārkaṇḍeya-purāṇe śrīmad-ālasālarka-saṃvāde-
gṛhasthena sadā kāryam ācāra-paripālanam ।
na hy ācāra-vihīnasya sukham atra paratra ca ।।

yajña-dāna-tapāṃsīha puruṣasya na bhūtaye ।
bhavanti yaḥ sadācāraṃ samullaṅghya pravartate ।।

bhaviṣyottare ca śrī-kṛṣṇa-yudhiṣṭhira-saṃvāde- 
ācāra-hīnaṃ na punanti vedāḥ
yadyapy adhītāḥ saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥ ।
chandāṃsy enaṃ mṛtyu-kāle tyajanti
nīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jāta-pakṣāḥ ।।

kapālasthaṃ yathā toyaṃ śvadṛtau vā yathā payaḥ ।
duṣṭaṃ syāt sthāna-doṣeṇa vṛtta-hīne tathāśubham ।
ācāra-rahito rājan neha nāmutra nindati ।।

iti

lekhyena smaraṇādīnāṃ nityatvenaiva setsyati ।
smaraṇādy-ātmakasyāpi sad-ācārasya nityatā ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe tatraiva gṛhi-dharma-prasaṅge - sad-ācāravatā puṃsā jitau lokāv ubhāv api ।।

sādhavaḥ kṣīṇa-doṣās tu sac-chabdaḥ sādhu-vācakaḥ ।
teṣām ācaraṇaṃ yat tu sad-ācāraḥ sa ucyate ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe skandāgastya-saṃvāde-
anadhyayana-śīlaṃ ca sad-ācāra-vilaṅghinam ।
sālasyaṃ ca durannādaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ bādhate'ntakaḥ ।।

tato abhyaset prayatnena sad-ācāraṃ sadā dvijaḥ ।
tīrthāny apy abhilaṣyanti sad-ācāra-samāgamam ।।

bhaviṣyottare ca tatraiva-
ācāra-prabhavo dharmaḥ santaś cācāra-lakṣaṇāḥ ।
sādhūnāṃ ca yathā vṛttaṃ sa sad-ācāra iṣyate ।।

tasmāt kuryāt sad-ācāraṃ ya icched gatim ātmanaḥ ।
sarva-lakṣaṇa-hīno api samucācāravān nṛpa ।
śraddadhāno anasūyaś ca sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt ।।

kiṃ ca-
ācāra eva dharmasya mūlaṃ rājan kulasya ca ।
ācārād vicyuto jantur na kulīno na dhārmikaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
ācāro bhūti-janana ācāraḥ kīrti-vardhanaḥ ।
ācārād vardhate hy āyur ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam ।।

ācāra eva nṛpa-puṅgava sevyamāno
dharmārtha-kāma-phalado bhaviteha puṃsām ।
tasmāt sadaiva viduṣāvahitena rājan
śāstrodito hy anudinaṃ paripālanīyaḥ ।।

atha tatra nitya-kṛtyāni

brāhme muhūrta utthāya kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kīrtayan ।
prakṣālya pāṇi-pādau ca danta-dhāvanam ācaret ।।

ācamya vasanaṃ rātres tyaktvānyat paridhāya ca ।
punar ācamane kuryāl lekhyena vidhināgrataḥ ।।

athecchan paramāṃ śuddhiṃ mūrdhni dhyātvā guroḥ padau ।
stutvā ca kīrtayan kṛṣṇaṃ smaraṃś caitad udīrayet ।।

atha prātaḥ-smaraṇa-kīrtane

jayati jana-nivāso devakī-janma-vādo
yadu-vara-pariṣat svair dorbhir asyann adharmam ।
sthira-cara-vṛjina-ghnaḥ su-smita- śrī-mukhena
vraja-pura-vanitānāṃ vardhayan kāma-devam ।।

[bhp ]

smṛte sakala-kalyāṇa-bhājanaṃ yatra jāyate ।
puruṣas tam ajaṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim ।।

vidagdha-gopāla-vilāsinīnāṃ
sambhoga-cihnāṅkita-sarva-gātram ।
pavitram āmnāya-girām agamyaṃ
brahma prapadye nava-nīta-cauram ।।

daśama-skandhe [bhp ] - 
udgāyatīnām aravinda-locanaṃ
vrajāṅganānāṃ divam aspṛśad dhvaniḥ ।
dadhnaś ca nirmanthana-śabda-miśrito
nirasyate yena diśām amaṅgalam ।।

iti

paṭhet punaś ca sādhūnāṃ sampradāyānusārataḥ ।
catuḥślokīm imāṃ sarva-doṣa-śāntyai śubhāptaye ।।

prātaḥ smarāmi bhava-bhīti-mahārti-śāntyai
nārāyaṇaṃ garuḍa-vāhanam abja-nābham ।
grāhābhibhūta-vara-vāri-vāraṇa-mukti-hetuṃ
cakrāyudhaṃ taruṇa-vārija-patra-netram ।।

prātar namāmi manasā vacasā ca mūrdhnā
pādāravinda-yugalaṃ paramasya puṃsaḥ ।
nārāyaṇasya narakārṇava-tāraṇasya
pārāyaṇa-pravaṇa-vipra-parāyaṇasya ।।

prātar bhajāmi bhajatām abhayaṅkaraṃ taṃ
prāk sarva-janma-kṛta-pāpa-bhayāvahatyai ।
yo grāha-vaktra-patitāṅghri-gajendra-ghora-
śoka-praṇāśam akarod dhṛta-śaṅkha-cakraḥ ।।

śloka-trayam idaṃ puṇyaṃ prātaḥ prātaḥ paṭhet tu yaḥ ।
loka-traya-gurus tasmai dadyād ātma-padaṃ hariḥ ।।

iti

tad etal likhitaṃ kutra kutracid vyavahārataḥ ।
kintu svābhīṣṭa-rūpādi śrī-kṛṣṇasya vicintayet ।।

itthaṃ vidadhyād bhagavat-kīrtana-smaraṇādikam ।
sarva-tīrthābhiṣekaṃ vai bahir antarviśodhanam ।।

tathā ca skānde skandaṃ prati śrī-śivoktau-
sakṛn nārāyaṇaety uktvā pumān kalpa-śata-trayam ।
gaṅgādi-sarva-tīrtheṣu snāto bhavati putraka ।।

anyatra ca-
śayanād utthito yas tu kīrtayen madhusūdanam ।
kīrtanāt tasya pāpasya nāśam āyāty aśeṣataḥ ।।

iti

māhātmyaṃ kīrtanasyāgre lekhyaṃ mukhya-prasaṅgataḥ ।
smaraṇasya tu māhātmyam adhunā likhyate kiyat ।।

tatrādau tasya nityatā

pādme bṛhat-sahasra-nāmni stotre -
smartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit ।
sarve vidhi-niṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ ।।

skānde kārttika-prasaṅge śrīmad-agastyoktau-
sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sa mohaḥ sa ca vibhramaḥ ।
yan-muhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe ca śrī-dhruva-carite-
iyam eva parā hānir upasargo ayam eva ca ।
abhāgyaṃ paramaṃ caitad vāsudevaṃ na yat smaret ।।

ye muhūrtāḥ kṣaṇā ye ca yāḥ kāṣṭhā ye nimeṣakāḥ ।
ṛte viṣṇu-smṛter yātās teṣu muṣṭo yamena saḥ ।।

iti 
nityatve'py asya māhātmyaṃ vicitra-phala-dānataḥ ।
jñeyaṃ śāstroditaṃ darśa-pūrṇamāsādivad budhaiḥ ।।

atha smaraṇa-māhātmyam tatra sarva-tīrtha-snānādhikatvam

uktaṃ ca smārtair api-
māntraṃ pārthivam āgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyam eva ca ।
vāruṇaṃ mānasaṃ ceti snānaṃ sapta-vidhaṃ smṛtam ।।

śaṃ na āpas tu vai māntraṃ mṛd-ālambhaṃ tu pārthivam ।
bhasmanā snānam āgneyaṃ snānaṃ gorajasānilam ।।

ātape sati yā vṛṣṭir divyaṃ snānaṃ tad ucyate ।
bahir nadyādiṣu snānaṃ vāruṇaṃ procyate budhaiḥ ।
dhyānaṃ yan manasā viṣṇor mānasaṃ tat prakīrtanam ।।

kiṃ ca-
asāmarthyena kāyasya kāla-deśādy-apekṣayā ।
tulya-phalāni sarvāṇi syur ity āha parāśaraḥ ।।

snānānāṃ mānasaṃ snānaṃ manv-ādyaiḥ paramaṃ smṛtam ।
kṛtena yena mucyante gṛhasthā api vai dvijāḥ ।।

parama-śodhaktavam 
gāruḍe śrī-nāradoktau, viṣṇu-dharme ca pulasytyoktau -
apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthāṃ gato api vā ।
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ ।।

yadyapy upahataḥ pāpair manasāyanta-dustaraiḥ ।
tathāpi saṃsmaran viṣṇuṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ ।।

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ] -
prāyaścittāny aśeṣāṇi tapaḥ karmātmakāni vai ।
yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇāṃ kṛṣṇānusmaraṇaṃ param ।।

kṛte pāpe'nutāpo vai yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate ।
prāyaścittaṃ tu tasyaikaṃ hari-saṃsmaraṇaṃ param ।।

kiṃ ca [vip ] -
kali-kalmaṣam atyugraṃ narakārti-pradaṃ nṝṇām ।
prayāti vilayaṃ sadyaḥ sakṛd yatrānusaṃsmṛte ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye [ṇārp ] śukra-bali-saṃvāde -
harir harati pāpāni duṣṭa-cittair api smṛtaḥ ।
anicchayāpi saṃspṛṣṭo dahaty eva hi pāvakaḥ ।।

tatraiva [ṇārp ] prāyaścitta-prasaṅgānte
mahā-pātaka-yukto vā yukto vā sarva-pātakaiḥ ।
sa vai vimucyate sadyo yasya viṣṇu-paraṃ manaḥ ।।

brahma-vaivarte -
karmaṇā manasā vācā yaḥ kṛtaḥ pāpa-sañcayaḥ ।
so apy aśeṣaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti smṛtvā kṛṣṇāṅghra-paṅkajam ।।

ataevoktaṃ skānde kārttika-prasaṅge śrī-parāśareṇa -
yama-mārgaṃ mahā-ghoraṃ narakāṃś ca yamaṃ tathā ।
svapne'pi na naraḥ paśyed yaḥ smared garuḍadhvajam ।।

ṣaṣṭha-skandhe [bhp ] śrī-śukena - 
sakṛn manaḥ kṛṣṇa-padāravindayor
niveśitaṃ tad-guṇa-rāgi yair iha ।
na te yamaṃ pāśa-bhṛtaś ca tad-bhaṭān
svapne api paśyanti hi cīrṇa-niṣkṛtāḥ ।।

sarvāpad-vimocakatvam

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ] śrī-prahlādoktau - 
dantā gajānāṃ kulśāgra-niṣṭhurāḥ
śīrṇā yad ete na balaṃ mamaitat ।
mahā-vipat-pāta-vināśano ayaṃ
janārdanānusmaraṇānubhāvaḥ ।।

vāmana-purāṇe ca -
viṣṭayo vyatipātāś ca ye'nye durnīti-sambhavāḥ ।
te sarve smaraṇād viṣṇor nāśam āyānty upadravāḥ ।।

pādme māgha-māhātmye deva-dyuti-stutau -
yasya smaraṇa-mātreṇa na moho na ca durgatiḥ ।
na rogo na ca duḥkhāni tam anantaṃ namāmy aham ।।

durvāsanonmūlanatvam 
dvādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] -
yathā hemni sthito vahnir durvarṇaṃ hanti dhātu-jam ।
evam ātma-gato viṣṇur yoginām aśubhāśayam ।।

sarva-maṅgala-kāritvam

pāṇḍava-gītāyām-
lābhas teṣāṃ jayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ ।
yeṣām indīvara-śyāmo hṛdayastha-janārdanaḥ ।।

sarva-sat-karma-phaladatvam skānde kārttika-prasaṅge'gastyoktau- 
deveṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu caiva
dāneṣu tīrtheṣu vrateṣu caiva ।
iṣṭeṣu pūrteṣu ca yat pradiṣṭaṃ
nṝṇāṃ smṛte tat-phalam acyute ca ।।

karma-sādguṇya-kāritvam

bṛhan-nāradīye [ṇārp] -
nyūnātiriktatā siddhā kalau vedokta-karmaṇām ।
hari-saṃsmaraṇam evātra sampūrṇa-phala-dāyakam ।।

smṛtau ca-
pramādāt kurvatāṃ karma pracyavetādhvareṣu yat ।
smaraṇād eva tad viṣṇoḥ sampūrṇaṃ syād iti śrutiḥ ।।

sarva-karmādhikatvam

bṛhan-nāradīye kali-prasaṅge [ṇārp] -
tulā-puruṣa-dānānāṃ rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ ।
phalaṃ viṣṇoḥ smṛti-samaṃ na jātu dvija-sattama ।।

dvādaśa-skandhe [bhp ]- 
vidyā-tapaḥ-prāṇa-nirodha-maitrī
tīrthābhiṣeka-vrata-dāna-japyaiḥ ।
nātyanta-śuddhiṃ labhate antar-ātmā
yathā hṛdi-sthe bhagavaty anante ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ] hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prati śrī-prahlādoktau - 
bhayaṃ bhayānām apahāriṇi sthite
manasy anante mama kutra tiṣṭhati ।
yasmin smṛte janma-jarodbhavāni
bhayāni sarvāṇy apayānti tāta ।।

tatraivānyatra [vip ] -
viṣṇu-saṃsmaraṇāt kṣīṇa-samasta-kleśa-saṃcayaḥ ।
muktiṃ prayāti svargāptis tasya vighno anumīyate ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye [ṇārp ] - 
varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ purāṇaṃ
nija-prabhā-bhāvita-sarva-lokam ।
saṅkalpitārtha-pradam ādi-devaṃ
smṛtvā vrajen mukti-padaṃ manuṣyaḥ ।।

skānde-
yasya smaraṇa-mātreṇa janma-saṃsāra-bandhanāt ।
vimucyate namas tasmai viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave ।।

tatraiva kārttika-prasaṅge śrī-parāśaroktau-
tadaiva puruṣo mukto janma-duḥkha-jarādibhiḥ ।
bhaktyā tu parayā nūnaṃ yadaiva smarate harim ।।

bhagavat-prasādanam

bṛhan-nāradīye [ṇārp ] 
yena kenāpy upāyena smṛto nārāyaṇo avyayaḥ ।
api pātaka-yuktasya prasannaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ ।।

śrī-vaikuṇṭha-loka-prāpakatvam vāmana-purāṇe- 
anādy-anantam ajarāmaraṃ hariṃ
ye saṃsmaranty aharahar niyataṃ narā bhuvi ।
tat sarvagaṃ brahma paraṃ purāṇaṃ
te yānti vaiṣṇava-padaṃ dhurvam avyayaṃ ca ।।

pādme deva-dūta-vikuṇḍala-saṃvāde yamasya dūtānuśāsane-
smaranti ye sakṛd bhūtāḥ prasaṅgenāpi keśavam ।
te vidhvastākhilāghaughā yanti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।।

brahma-purāṇe viṣṇu-rahasye -
śāṭhyenāpi narā nityaṃ ye smaranti janārdanam ।
te api yānti tanuṃ tyaktvā viṣṇulokam anāmayam ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare-
nirāśīr nirmamo yas tu viṣṇor dhyāna-paro bhavet ।
tat-padaṃ samavāpnoti yatra gatvā na śocati ।।

sārūpya-prāpaṇam

kāśī-khaṇḍe śrī-bindumādhava-prasaṅge agni-bindu-stutau- 
ye tvāṃ trivikrama sadā hṛdi śīlayanti
kādambinī-rucir arociṣam ambujākṣa ।
saudāminī-vilasitāṃśuka-vīta-mūrte
te'pi spṛśanti tava kāntim acintya-rūpām ।।

śrī-bhagavad-gītāsu [ṅītā ] -
anta-kāle ca mām eva smaran muktvā kalevaram ।
yaḥ prayāti sa mad-bhāvaṃ yāti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ ।।

daśama-skandhe [bhp ] pṛthukopākhyāne -
smarataḥ pāda-kamalam ātmānam api yacchati ।
kiṃ nv artha-kāmān bhajato nāty-abhīṣṭān jagad-guruḥ ।।

vaiṣṇave-
vāsudeve mano yasya japa-homārcanādiṣu ।
tasyāntarāyo maitreya devendratvādi sat-phalam ।।

gāruḍe-
mahatas tapaso mūlaṃ prasavaḥ puṇya-santateḥ ।
jīvitasya phalaṃ svādu niyataṃ smaraṇaṃ hareḥ ।।

dvitīya-skandhe [bhp ] -
etāvān sāṅkhya-yogābhyāṃ sva-dharma-pariniṣṭhayā ।
janma-lābhaḥ paraḥ puṃsām ante nārāyaṇa-smṛtiḥ ।।

ataeva jarāsandha-niruddha-nṛpa-vargaiḥ prārthitaṃ daśama-skandhe [bhp ] -
taṃ naḥ samādiśopāyaṃ yena te caraṇābjayoḥ ।
smṛtir yathā na viramed api saṃsaratām iha ।।

śrī-nāradenāpi [bhp ] 
dṛṣṭaṃ tavāṅghri-yugalaṃ janatāpavargaṃ
brahmādibhir hṛdi vicintyam agādha-bodhaiḥ ।
saṃsāra-kūpa-patitottaraṇāvalambaṃ
dhyāyaṃś carāmy anugṛhāṇa yathā smṛtiḥ syāt ।।

iti 
kṛṣṇa-smaraṇa-māhātmya-mahābdhir dustaro dhiyā ।
yo yiyāsati tat-pāraṃ sa hi caitanya-vañcitaḥ ।।

tataḥ pādodakaṃ kiñcit prāk pītvā tulasī-dalaiḥ ।
gṛhītenācaret tena svamūrdhany abhiṣecanam ।।

athādau śrī-guruṃ natvā śrī-kṛṣṇasya padābjayoḥ ।
kiñcid vijñāpayan sarvasva-kṛtyāny arpayen namet ।।

atha prātaḥ praṇāmaḥ

vāmana-purāṇe -
sarva-maṅgala-maṅgalyaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ śivam ।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya sarva-karmāṇi kārayet ।।

atha vijñāpanam

viṣṇu-dharmottare -
yad-utsavādikaṃ karma tat tvayā prerito hare ।
kariṣyāmi tvayā jñeyam iti vijñāpanaṃ mama ।।

prātaḥ prabodhito viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśena yat tvayā ।
yad yat kārayasīśāna tat karomi tavājñayā ।।

trailokya-caitanyamayādi-deva
śrī-nātha viṣṇo bhavad-ājñayaiva ।
prātaḥ samutthāya tava priyārthaṃ
saṃsāra-yātrām anuvartayiṣye ।।

saṃsāra-yātrām anuvartamānaṃ
tvad-ājñayā śrī-nṛhare'ntarātman ।
spardhātiraskāra-kali-pramāda-
bhayāni mā mābhibhavantu bhūman ।।

jānāmi dharmaṃ na ca me pravṛttir
jānāmy adharmaṃ na ca me nivṛttiḥ ।
tvayā hṛṣīkeśa hṛdi sthitena
yathā niyukto asmi tathā karomi ।।

atha praṇāma-vākyāni

mahābhārate -
namo brahmaṇya-devāya go-brāhmaṇa-hitāya ca ।
jagad-dhitāya kṛṣṇāya govindāya namo namaḥ ।।

garuḍa-purāṇe- 
asura-vibudha-siddhair jñāyate yasya nāntaḥ
sakala-munibhir antaś cintyate yo viśuddhaḥ ।
nikhila-hṛdi niviṣṭo vetti yaḥ sarva-sākṣī
tam ajam amṛtam īśaṃ vāsudevaṃ nato asmi ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ??]
yajñibhir yajña-puruṣo vāsudevaś ca sātvataḥ ।
vedānta-vedibhir viṣṇuḥ procyate yo nato asmi tam ।।

evaṃ vijñāpayan dhyāyan kīrtayaṃś ca yathāvidhi ।
praṇāmānācarec chaktyā catuḥ-saṅkhyāvarān budhaḥ ।।

śrī-gopī-candanenordhva-puṇḍraṃ kṛtvā yathā-vidhi ।
āsīta prāṅ-mukho bhūtvā śuddha-sthāne śubhāsane ।।

tathā ca nāradīya-pañcarātre-
nirgatyācamya vidhivat praviśya ca punaḥ sudhīḥ ।
āsane prāṅ-mukho bhūtvā vihite copaviśya vai ।।

sampradāyānusāreṇa bhūta-śuddhiṃ vidhāya ca ।
prāṇāyāmāṃś ca vidhivat kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyet yathoditam ।।

tathā coktam-
upapātakeṣu sarveṣu pātakeṣu mahatsu ca ।
praviśya rajanī-pādaṃ viṣṇu-dhyānaṃ samācaret ।।

vaihāyasa-pañcarātre ca-
tathaiva rātri-śeṣaṃ tu kālaṃ sūryodayāvadhi ।
kartavyaṃ sajapaṃ dhyānaṃ nityam ārādhakena vai ।।

vibhajya pañcadhā rātriṃ śeṣe devārcanādikam ।
japaṃ homaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ nityaṃ kurvīta sādhakaḥ ।।

ataeva viṣṇu-smṛtau- rātres tu paścime yāme muhūrtau brāhmya ucyate ।।

iti 
pādodapānādīnāṃ ca sa vidhir mahimāgrataḥ ।
lekhyo adhunā tu dhyānasya sa saṅkṣepeṇa likhyate ।।

tāpanīya-śrutiṣu [ṅṭū ] -
sat-puṇḍarīka-nayanaṃ meghābhaṃ vaidyutāmbaram ।
dvi-bhujaṃ jñāna-mudrāḍhyaṃ vana-mālinam īśvaram ।।

gopa-gopī-gavāvītaṃ sura-druma-talāśritam ।
dviyālaṅkaraṇopetaṃ ratna-paṅkaja-madhyagam ।।

kālindī-jala-kallola-saṅgi-māruta-sevitam ।
cintayaṃś cetasā kṛṣṇaṃ mukto bhavati saṃsṛteḥ ।।

mṛtyuñjaya-saṃhitānusārodita-sāradā-tilake ca -
smared vṛndāvane ramye mohayantam anāratam ।
govindaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ gopa-kanyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।

ātmano vadanāmbhoja-preritākṣi-madhu-vratāḥ ।
kāma-bāṇena vivaśāś ciram āśleṣeṇotsukāḥ ।।

muktāhāra-lasat-pīnottuṅgastana-bharānatāḥ ।
srasta-dhammilla-vasanā mada-skhalita-bhāṣaṇāḥ ।।

danta-paṅkti-prabhodbhāsi-spandamānādharāñcitāḥ ।
vilobhayantīr vividhair vibhramair bhāva-garbhitaiḥ ।।

phullendīvara-kāntim indu-vadanaṃ barhāvataṃsa-priyaṃ
śrī-vatsāṅkam udāra-kaustubha-dharaṃ pītāmbaraṃ sundaram ।
gopīnāṃ nayanotpalārcita-tanuṃ go-gopa-saṅghāvṛtaṃ
govindaṃ kala-veṇu-vādana-paraṃ divyāṅga-bhūṣaṃ bhaje ।।

iti 
śrī-gautamīya-tantrādau tad-dhyānaṃ prathitaṃ param ।
agrato atrāpi saṃlekhyaṃ yad iṣṭaṃ tatra tad bhajet ।।

bṛhat-śātātāpa-smṛtau-
pakṣopavāsād yat pāpaṃ puruṣasya praṇaśyati ।
prāṇāyāma-śatenaiva yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām ।।

prāṇāyāma-sahasreṇa yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām ।
kṣaṇa-mātreṇa tat pāpaṃ harer dhyānāt praṇaśyati ।।

viṣṇu-dharme-
sarva-pāpa-prasakto api dhyāyan nimiṣam acyutam ।
bhūtas tapasvī bhavati paṅkti-pāvana-pāvanaḥ ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe ca-
dhyāyen nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānādiṣu ca karmasu ।
prāyaścittaṃ hi sarvasya duṣkṛtasyeti niścitam ।।

kali-doṣa-haratvam

bṛhan-nāradīye kali-prasaṅge [ṇārp ] -
samasta-jagad-ādhāraṃ paramārtha-svarūpiṇam ।
ghore kali-yuge prāpte viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati ।।

sarva-dharmādhikāritvam

skānde kārttika-māhātmye agastyoktau-
kintv asya bahubhis tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tasya bahubhir vrataiḥ ।
yo nityaṃ dhyāyate devaṃ nārāyaṇam ananya-dhīḥ ।।

mokṣa-pradatvam

bṛhan-nāradīye kali-prasaṅge [ṇārp ] - 
ye mānavā vigata-rāga-parāvara-jñā
nārāyaṇaṃ sura-guruṃ satataṃ smaranti ।
dhyānena tena hata kilbiṣa-cetanās te
mātuḥ payodhara-rasaṃ na punaḥ pibanti ।।

śrī-vaikuṇṭha-prāpakatvam 
skānde śrī-brahmoktau-
muhūrtam api yo dhyāyen nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ ।
so api sad-gatim āpnoti kiṃ punas tat-parāyaṇaḥ ।।

pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye yama-brāhmaṇa-saṃvāde [padmap ]
dhyāyanti puruṣaṃ divyam acyutaṃ ye smaranti ca ।
labhante te'cyuta-sthānaṃ śrutir eṣā purātanī ।।

sārūpya-prāpaṇam

ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] - 
vaireṇa yaṃ nṛpatayaḥ śiśupāla-pauṇḍra-
śālvādayo gati-vilāsa-vilokanādyaiḥ ।
dhyāyanta ākṛta-dhiyaḥ śayanāsanādau
tat-sāmyam āpur anurakta-dhiyāṃ punaḥ kim ।।

svataḥ parama-phalatvam

caturtha-skandhe [bhp ] śrī-pṛthūktau - 
bhajanty atha tvām ata eva sādhavo
vyudasta-māyā-guṇa-vibhramodayam ।
bhavat-padānusmaraṇād ṛte satāṃ
nimittam anyad bhagavan na vidmahe ।।

skanda-purāṇe brahmoktau ca -
āloḍya sarva-śāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ ।
idame eva suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā ।।

ataevoktaṃ hāyaśīrṣa-pañcarātre nārāyaṇa-vyūha-stave -
ye tyakta-loka-dharmārthā viṣṇu-bhakti-vaśaṃ gatāḥ ।
dhyāyanti paramātmānaṃ tebhyo apīha namo namaḥ ।।

iti

smaraṇe yat tan māhātmyaṃ tad-dhyāne'py akhilaṃ viduḥ ।
bhedaḥ kalpyeta sāmānya-viśeṣābhyāṃ tayoḥ kiyān ।।

atha śrī-bhagavat-prabodhanam

tato devālaye gatvā ghaṇṭādy-udghoṣa-pūrvakam ।
prabodhya stutibhiḥ kṛṣṇaṃ nīrājyaṃ prārthayed idam ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe [bhp ] - 
so asāv adabhra-karuṇo bhagavān vivṛddha-
prema-smitena nayanāmburuhaṃ vijṛmbhan ।
utthāya viśva-vijayāya ca no viṣādaṃ
mādhvyā girāpanayatāt puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ ।।

deva-prapannārtihara prasādaṃ kuru keśava ।
avalokana-dānena bhūyo māṃ pārayācyuta ।।

iti 
devālayaṃ praviśyātha stotrāṇīṣṭāni kīrtayan ।
kṛṣṇasya tulasī-varjaṃ nirmālyam apasārayet ।।

atha nirmālyottāraṇam

atri-smṛtau-
prātaḥ-kāle sadā kuryān nirmālyottāraṇaṃ budhaḥ ।
tṛṣitāḥ paśavo baddhāḥ kanyakā ca rajasvalā ।
devatā ca sanirmālyā hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam ।।

nārasiṃhe śrī-yamoktau-
deva-mālyāpanayanaṃ devāgāre samūhanam ।
snāpanaṃ sarva-devānāṃ go-pradāna-samaṃ smṛtam ।।

nārada-pañcarātre- 
yaḥ prātar utthāya vidhāya nityaṃ
nirmālyam īśasya nirākaroti ।
na tasya duḥkhaṃ na daridratā ca
nākāla-mṛtyur na ca roga-mātram ।।

aruṇodaya-velāyāṃ nirmālyaṃ śalyatāṃ vrajet ।
prātas tu syān mahāśalyaṃ ghaṭikā-mātra-yogataḥ ।।

atiśalyaṃ vijānīyāt tato vajra-prahāravat ।
aruṇodaya-velāyāṃ śalyaṃ tat kṣamate hariḥ ।।

ghaṭikāyām atikrāntau kṣudraṃ pātakam āvahet ।
muhūrte samatikrānte pūrṇaṃ pātakam ucyate ।।

atipātakam ev syāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye ।
muhūrta-tritaye pūrṇe mahā-pātakam ucyate ।।

tataḥ paraṃ brahma-vadho mahā-pātaka-pañcakam ।
prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte prāyaścittaṃ tato na hi ।।

nirmālyasya vilambe tu prāyaścittam athocyate ।
atikrānte muhūrtārdhe sahasraṃ japam ācaret ।।

pūrṇe muhūrte sañjāte sahasraṃ sārdham ucyate ।
sahasra-dvitīyaṃ kuryāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye ।।

muhūrta-tritaye'tīte ayutaṃ japam ācaret ।
prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte puraścaraṇam ucyate ।
prahare samatikrānte prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate ।।

atha śrī-mukha-prakṣālanam

śrī-hastāṅghri-mukhāmbhoja-kṣālanāya ca tad-gṛhe ।
gaṇḍūṣāṇi jalair dattvā danta-kāṣṭhaṃ samarpayet ।।

jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā pāduke śuddha-mṛttikām ।
salilaṃ ca punar dadyād vāso api mukha-mārjanam ।।

tataḥ śrī-tulasīṃ puṇyām arpayet bhagavat-priyām ।
tan-māhātmyaṃ ca tan-mukhya-prasaṅge lekhyam agrataḥ ।।

atha danta-kāṣṭhārpaṇa-māhātmyam

viṣṇu-dharmottare-
danta-kāṣṭha-pradānena danta-saubhāgyam ṛcchati ।
jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā virogas tv abhijāyate ।।

pādukāyāḥ pradānena gatim iṣṭām avāpnuyāt ।
mṛd-bhāga-dānād devasya bhūmim āpnoty anuttamām ।।

atha maṅgala-nīrājanam

paṭhitvātha priyān ślokān mahā-vāditra-nisvanaiḥ ।
prabhor nīrājanaṃ kuryān maṅgalākhyaṃ jagad-dhitam ।।

nīrājanaṃ tv idaṃ sarvaiḥ kartavyaṃ śuci-vigrahaiḥ ।
parama-śraddhayotthāya draṣṭavyaṃ ca sadā naraiḥ ।।

strīṇāṃ puṃsāṃ ca sarveṣām etat sarveṣṭa-pūrakam ।
samasta-dainya-dāridrya-duritādy-upaśānti-kṛt ।।

atha prātaḥ-snānārthodyamaḥ

tato aruṇodayasyānte snānārthaṃ niḥsared bahiḥ ।
kīrtayan kṛṣṇa-nāmāni tīrthaṃ gacched anantaram ।।

tathā ca śukra-smṛtau-
brāhme muhūrte cotthāya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ ।
svastikādy-āsanaṃ baddhvā dhyātvā kṛṣṇa-pādāmbujam ।।

tato nirgatya nilayānnāmānīmāni kīrtayet ।
śrī-vāsudevāniruddha-pradyumnādhokṣajācyuta ।
śrī-kṛṣṇānanta govinda saṅkarṣaṇa namo astu te ।।

gatvā tīrthādikaṃ tatra nikṣipya snāna-sādhanam ।
vidhinācarya maitry-ādi-kṛtyaṃ śaucaṃ vidhāya ca ।
ācamya khāni saṃmārjya snānaṃ kuryāt yathocitam ।।

atha maitryādi-kṛtya-vidhiḥ

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ] aurva-sagara-saṃvāde gṛhi-dharma-kathane-
tataḥ kalye samutthāya kuryān mūtraṃ nareśvara ।
nairṛtyām iṣu-vikṣepam atītyādhikaṃ gṛhāt ।।

dūrādāvasathān mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca samutsṛjet ।
pādāv asecanocchiṣṭe prakṣipen na gṛhāṅgaṇe ।।

ātma-cchāyāṃ taroś chāyāṃ go-sūryāgny-anilāṃs tathā ।
guruṃ dvijādīṃś ca budho na meheta kadācana ।।

na kṛṣṭe śasya-madhye vā go-vraje jana-saṃsadi ।
na vartmani na nady-ādi-tīrtheṣu puruṣarṣabha ।।

nāpsu naivāmbhasas tīre na śmaśāne samācaret ।
utsargaṃ vai purīṣasya mūtrasya ca visarjanam ।।
