udaṅmukho divotsargaṃ viparīta-mukho niśi ।
kurvītānāpadi prājño mūtrotsargaṃ ca pārthiva ।।

tṛṇair ācchādya vasudhāṃ vastra-prāvṛta-mastakaḥ ।
tiṣṭhen nāticiraṃ tatra naiva kiñcid udīrayet ।।

tathā kaurme vyāsa-gītāyām-
nidhāya dakṣiṇe karṇe brahma-sūtram udaṅmukhaḥ ।
antardhāpya mahīṃ kāṣṭhaiḥ patrair loṣṭrais tṛṇena vā ।।

prāvṛtya tu śiraḥ kuryād vin-mūtrasya visarjanam ।
na caivābhimukhaḥ strīṇāṃ guru-brāhmaṇayor gavām ।
na deva-devālayor nāpām api kadācana ।।

nadīṃ jyotīṃṣi vīkṣitvā na vāyv-agni-mukho api vā ।
prayādityaṃ pratyanalaṃ pratisomaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

kāśī-kāṇḍe śrī-skandāgastya-saṃvāde-
tataś cāvaśyakaṃ kartuṃ nairṛtīṃ diśam āśrayet ।
grāmād dhanuḥ-śataṃ gacchen nagarāc ca caturguṇam ।।

karṇopavīty-udag-vaktro divase sandhyayor api ।
vin-mūtre visṛjen maunī niśāyāṃ dakṣiṇā-mukhaḥ ।।

nālokayed diśo bhāgān jyotiś cakraṃ nabho amalam ।
vāmena pāṇinā śiśnaṃ dhṛtvottiṣṭhet prayatnavān ।।

tatraivāgre-
na mūtraṃ go-vraje kuryān na valmīke na bhasmani ।
na garteṣu sa-sattveṣu na tiṣṭhan na vrajann api ।।

yathā-sukha-mukho rātrau divā chāyāndhakārayoḥ ।
bhītiṣu prāṇa-bādhāyāṃ kuryān mala-visarjanam ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe [bhp ] tatraiva-
valmīka-mūṣikotkhātāṃ mṛdaṃ nāntar-jalāt tathā ।
śaucāvaśiṣṭāṃ gehāc ca na dadyāl lepa-sambhavām ।।

antaḥprāṇyavapannāṃ ca halotkhātāṃ ca pārthiva ।
parityajen mṛdaś caitāḥ sakalāḥ śauca-sādhane ।।

ekā liṅge gude tisras daśa vāma-kare nṛpa ।
hasta-dvaye saptānyā mṛdaḥ śaucopapādikāḥ ।।

yama-smṛtau- tisras tu pādayor deyāḥ śuddhi-kāmena nityaśaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca- tisras tu mṛttikā deyāḥ kṛtvā tu nakha-śodhanam ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe ca tatraiva-
guhye dadyān mṛdaṃ caikāṃ pāyau pañcāmbu-sāntarāḥ ।
daśa vāma-kare cāpi sapta pāṇi-dvaye mṛdaḥ ।।

ekaikāṃ pādayor dadyāt tisraḥ pāṇyor mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
itthaṃ śaucaṃ gṛhī kuryād gandha-lepa-kṣayāvadhi ।।

kramād dviguṇam etat tu brahmacaryādiṣu triṣu ।
divā vihita-śaucāc ca rātrāv ardhaṃ samācaret ।।

rujārdhaṃ ca tad-ardhaṃ ca pathi caurādi-pīḍite ।
tad-ardha-yoṣitāṃ cāpi svāsthye nyūnaṃ na kārayet ।
ārdra-dhātrī-phalonmānā mṛdaḥ śauce prakīrtitāḥ ।।

śaṅkha-smṛtau- mṛttikā tu samuddiṣṭā triparvī pūryate yayā ।।

dakṣa-smṛtau-
ardha-prasṛti-mātrā tu prathamā mṛttikā smṛtā ।
dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā ca tad-ardhaṃ parikīrtitā ।।

atha kevala-mūtrotsarge

dakṣaḥ- ekā liṅge tu savye trir ubhayor mṛd-dvayaṃ smṛtam ।।

brāhme-
pādayor dve gṛhītvā ca suprakṣālita-pāṇinā ।
ācamya tu tataḥ śuddhaḥ smṛtvā viṣṇuṃ sanātanam ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe [bhp ] tatraiva-
acchenāgandha-phenena jalenābudbudena ca ।
ācāmeta mṛdaṃ bhūyas tathā dadyāt samāhitaḥ ।।

niṣpāditāṅghri-śaucas tu pāpāv abhyukṣya vai punaḥ ।
triḥ pibet salilaṃ tena tathā dviḥ parimārjayet ।।

śīrṣaṇyāni tataḥ khāni mūrdhānaṃ ca mṛdā labhet ।
bāhū nābhiṃ ca toyena hṛdayaṃ cāpi saṃspṛśet ।।

atra ca viśeṣo dakṣeṇoktaḥ-
prakṣālya hastau pādau ca triḥ pibed ambu vīkṣitam ।
saṃvṛttāṅguṣṭha-mūlena dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham ।।

saṃhatya tisṛbhiḥ pūrvam āsyam evam upaspṛśet ।
aṅguṣṭhena pradeśinyā ghrāṇaṃ paścād anantaram ।।

aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu cakṣuḥ-śrotre punaḥ punaḥ ।
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayor nābhiṃ hṛdayaṃ tu talena vai ।
sarvābhis tu śiraḥ paścād bāhū cāgreṇa saṃspṛśet ।।

tathā kāśī-khaṇḍe tatraiva-
prāg āsya udagāsyo vā sūpaviṣṭaḥ śucau bhuvi ।
upaspṛśed vihīnāyāṃ tuṣāṅgārāsthi-bhasmabhiḥ ।।

anuṣṇābhir aphenābhir adbhir hṛdgābhir atvaraḥ ।
brāhmaṇo brahma-tīrthena dṛṣṭi-pūtanābhir ācamet ।।

kaṇṭha-gābhir nṛpaḥ śudhyet tālugābhis tathorujaḥ ।
strī-śūdrāvāsyasaṃsparśa-mātreṇāpi visudhyataḥ ।।

yājñavalkya-smṛtau-
pāda-kṣālana-śeṣeṇa nācāmet vāriṇā dvijaḥ ।
yady ācamet srāvayitvā bhūmau baudhāyano abravīt ।।

bharadvāja-smṛtau-
pāṇinā dakṣiṇenaiva saṃhatāṅgulinācamet ।
muktāṅguṣṭhaka-niṣṭhena naka-spṛṣṭā apas tyajet ।।

kaurme ca vyāsa-gītāyām-
bhuktvā pītvā ca suptvā ca snātvā rathyopasarpaṇe ।
auṣṭhau vilomakau spṛṣṭvā vāso viparidhāya ca ।।

reto-mūtra-purīṣāṇām utsarge'nṛta-bhāṣaṇe ।
ṣthīvitvādhyayanārambhe kāśa-śvāsāgame tathā ।।

catvaraṃ vā śmaśānaṃ vā samabhyasya dvijottamaḥ ।
sandhyor ubhayos tadvad ācānto apy ācamet punaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
śiraḥ prāvṛtya kaṇṭhaṃ vā muktakaccha-śikho api vā ।
akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucam ācānto apy aśucir bhavet ।।

sopānatkau jalastho vā noṣṇīṣī cācamed budhaḥ ।
na caiva varṣa-dhārābhir hastocchiṣṭe tathā budhaḥ ।।

naika-hastārpiutta-jalair vinā sūtreṇa vā punaḥ ।
na pādukāsana-stho vā bahir jānur athāpi vā ।।

atha vaiṣṇavācamanam

triḥ-pāne keśavaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ mādhavam apy atha ।
prakṣālane dvayoḥ pāṇyor govindaṃ viṣṇum apy ubhau ।।
madhusūdanam ekaṃ ca mārjane'nyaṃ trivikramam ।।unmārjane'py adharayor vāmana-śrīdharāv ubhau ।।
prakṣālane punaḥ pāṇyor hṛṣīkeśaṃ ca pādayoḥ ।
padmanābhaṃ prokṣaṇe tu mūrdhno dāmodaraṃ tataḥ ।।

vāsudevaṃ mukhe saṅkarṣaṇaṃ pradyumnam ity ubhau ।
nāsayor netra-yugale'niruddhaṃ puruṣottamam ।
adhokṣajaṃ nṛsiṃhaṃ ca karṇayor nābhito acyutam ।।

janārdanaṃ ca hṛdaye upendraṃ mastake tataḥ ।
dakṣiṇe tu hariṃ bāhau vāme kṛṣṇaṃ yathāvidhi ।
namo anantaṃ ca caturthy-antam ācāmet kramato japan ।।

aśaktaḥ kevalam dakṣaṃ spṛśet karṇaṃ tathā ca vāk ।
kurvītālabhanaṃ vāpi dakṣiṇa-śravaṇasya vai ।।

atha danta-dhāvana-vidhiḥ

tatra kātyāyanaḥ-
utthāya netraṃ prakṣālya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ ।
parijapya ca mantreṇa bhakṣayed danta-dhāvanam ।।

mantraś cāyam-
āyur balaṃ yaśo varcaḥ prajā paśu-vasūni ca ।
brahma prajñāṃ ca medhāṃ ca tvaṃ no dhehi vanaspate ।।

tasya nityatā

kāśī-khaṇḍe-
atho mukha-viśuddhy-arthaṃ gṛhṇīyād danta-dhāvanam ।
ācānto apy aśucir yasmād akṛtvā danta-dhāvanam ।।

vārāhe ca-
danta-kāṣṭham akhāditvā yas tu mām upasarpati ।
sarva-kāla-kṛtaṃ karma tena caikena naśyati ।।

atha danta-kāṣṭha-niṣiddha-dināni

manuḥ-
caturdaśy-aṣṭamī-darśa-paurṇamāsy-arka-saṅkramaḥ ।
eṣu strī-taila-māṃsāni danta-kāṣṭhāni varjayet ।।

saṃvartakaḥ-
ādye tithau navamyāṃ ca kṣaye candramasas tathā ।
ādity-vāre śaure ca varjayed danta-dhāvanam ।।

kātyāyanaḥ-
pratipad-darśa-ṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
dantānāṃ kāṣṭha-saṃyogo dahaty āsaptamaṃ kulam ।।

vṛddha-vaśiṣṭhaḥ-
upavāse tathā śrāddhena khāded danta-dhāvanam ।
dantānāṃ kāṣṭha-saṃyogo hanti sapta-kulāni vai ।।

anyatra ca-
pratipad-dara-ṣaṣṭhīṣu navamy-ekādaśī-ravau ।
dantānāṃ kāṣṭha-saṃyogo hanti puṇyaṃ purā-kṛtam ।।

atha tatra pratinidhiḥ
dinaeṣv eteṣu kāṣṭhair hi dantānāṃ dhāvanasya tu ।
niṣiddhatvāt tṛṇaiḥ kuryāt tathā kāṣṭhetaraiś ca tat ।।

tathā ca vyāsaḥ-
pratipad-darśa-ṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ danta-dhāvanam ।
parṇair anyatra kāṣṭhaiś ca jīvollekhhaḥ sadaiva hi ।।

paiṭhīnasiḥ-
alābhe ca niṣedhe vā kāṣṭhānāṃ danta-dhāvanam ।
parṇādinā viśuddhena jihvollekhaḥ sadaiva hi ।।

atha tatraivāpavādaḥ

kāṣṭhaiḥ pratipad-ādau yan niṣiddhaṃ danta-dhāvanam ।
tṛṇa-parṇais tu tat kuryād amām ekādaśīṃ vinā ।।

ata eva vyāsasya vacanāntaram-
alābhe danta-kāṣṭhānāṃ niṣiddhāyāṃ tathā tithau ।
apāṃ dvādaśa-gaṇḍūṣair vidadhyād danta-dhāvanam ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe tatraiva-
mukhe paryuṣite yasmād bhaved aśuci-bhāg naraḥ ।
tataḥ kuryāt prayatnena śuddhy-arthaṃ danta-dhāvanam ।।

upavāse'pi no duṣyed danta-dhāvanam añjanam ।
gandhālaṅkāra-sad-vastra-puṣpa-mālānulepanam ।।

atha danta-kāṣṭhāni

smṛtau-
sarva kaṇṭakinaḥ puṇyāḥ āyurdāḥ kṣīriṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
kaṭu-tikta-kaṣāyāś ca balārogya-sukha-pradāḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
palāśānāṃ danta-kāṣṭhaṃ pāduke caiva varjayet ।
varjayec ca prayatnena baṭaṃ vāśvattham eva ca ।।

kaurme śrī-vyāsa-gītāyām-
madhyāṅguli-samasthaulyaṃ dvādaśāṅgula-sammitam ।
sa-tvacaṃ danta-kāṣṭhaṃ yat tad-agre na tu dhārayet ।।

kṣīri-vṛkṣa-samudbhūtaṃ mālatī-sambhavaṃ śubham ।
apāmārgaṃ ca bilvaṃ vā kara-vīraṃ viśeṣatah ।।

varjayitvā ninitāni gṛhītvaikaṃ yathoditam ।
parihṛtya dinaṃ pāpaṃ bhakṣayed vai vidhānavit ।।

na pāṭayet danta-kāṣṭhaṃ nāṅguly-agreṇa dhārayet ।
prakṣālya bhuktvā taj jahyāt śucau deśe samāhitaḥ ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe ca tatraiva-
kaniṣṭhāgra-parīṇāhaṃ sa-tvacaṃ nirvraṇaṃ ṛjum ।
dvādaśāṅgula-mānaṃ ca sārdraṃ syād danta-dhāvanam ।
jihvollekhanikām vāpi kuryāc cāpākṛtiṃ śubhām ।।

rāmārcana-candrikāyām ca- 
dantollekho vitastyā bhavati parimitād annam ity ādi-mantrāt
prātaḥ kṣīry-ādi-kāṣṭhād vaṭa-khadira-palāśair vinārkāmra-bilvaiḥ ।
bhuktvā gaṇḍūṣa-ṣaṭkaṃ dvir api kuśam ṛte deśinīm aṅgulībhir
nandābhūtāṣṭa-parvaṇy api na khalu navamy-arka-saṅkrānti-pāte ।।

atha keśa-prasādhanādiḥ

tataś cācamya vidhivat kṛtvā keśa-prasādhanam ।
smṛtvā praṇava-gāyatryau nibadhnīyāc chikhāṃ dvijaḥ ।।

tathā coktaṃ-
na dakṣiṇā-mukho nordhvaṃ kuryāt keśa-prasādhanam ।
smṛtvoṅkāraṃ ca gāyatrīṃ nibadhnīyāc cikhāntataḥ ।।

atha snānam

viṣṇu-purāṇe [bhp ] tatraiva-
nadī-nada-taḍāgeṣu deva-khāta-jaleṣu ca ।
nitya-kriyārthaṃ snāyīta giri-prasravaṇeṣu ca ।।

kūpeṣūddhṛta-toyena snānaṃ kurvīta vā bhuvi ।
snāyītoddhṛta-toyena athavā bhuvy asambhave ।।

atha snāna-nityatā

tatra kātyāyanaḥ-
yathāhani tathā prātar nityaṃ snāyād anāturaḥ ।
atyanta-malinaḥ kāyo nava-cchidra-samanvitaḥ ।
sravat eva divā-rātrau prātaḥ-snānaṃ viśodhanam ।।

dakṣaḥ-
prātar madhyāhnayoḥ snānaṃ vānaprastha-gṛhasthayoḥ ।
yates tri-savanaṃ snānaṃ sakṛt tu brahmacāriṇaḥ ।।
sarve cāpi sakṛt kuryur aśaktau codakaṃ vinā ।।
kiṃ ca-
aśiraskaṃ bhavet snānam aśaktau karmiṇāṃ sadā ।
ārdreṇa vāsasā vāpi pāṇinā vāpi mārjanam ।।

śaṅkhaś ca- asnātas tu pumān nārho japādi-havanādiṣu ।।

kaurme vyāsa-gītāyām-
prātaḥ-snānaṃ vinā puṃsāṃ pāpitvaṃ karmasu smṛtam ।
home jape viśeṣeṇa tasmāt snānaṃ samācaret ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe-
prasveda-lālasādyāklinno nidrādhīno yato naraḥ ।
prātaḥ-snānāt tato arhaḥ syān mantra-stotra-japādiṣu ।।

pādme ca devahūti-vikuṇḍala-saṃvāde [padmap ] 
snānaṃ vinā tu yo bhuṅkte malāśī sa sadā naraḥ ।
asnāyino aśuces tasya vimukhāḥ pitṛ-devatāḥ ।।

snāna-hīno naraḥ pāpaḥ snāna-hīno naro aśuciḥ ।
asnāyī narakaṃ bhuṅkte puṃs-kīṭādiṣu jāyate ।।

atha snāna-māhātmyam

mahābhārate udyoga-parvaṇi śrī-viduroktau- 
guṇā daśa snāna-śīlaṃ bhajante
balaṃ rūpaṃ svara-varṇa-praśuddhiḥ ।
sparśaś ca gandhaś ca viśuddhatā ca
śrīḥ saukumāryaṃ pravarāś ca nāryaḥ ।।

pādme ca tatraiva-
yāmyaṃ hi yātanā-duḥkhaṃ nitya-snāyī na paśyati ।
nitya-snānena pūyante api pāpa-kṛto narāḥ ।।

prātaḥ-snānaṃ hared vaiśya bāhyābhyantarajaṃ malam ।
prātaḥ-snānena niṣpāpo naro na nirayaṃ vrajet ।।

ye punaḥ srotasi snānam ācarantīha parvaṇi ।
tenaiva narakaṃ yānti na jāyante kuyoniṣu ।।

duḥsvapnā duṣṭa-cintāś ca bandhyā bhavanti sarvadā ।
prātaḥ-snānena śuddhānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ viśāṃ vara ।।

atri-smṛtau-
snāne manaḥ-prasādaḥ syād devā abhimukhāḥ sadā ।
saubhāgyaṃ śrīḥ sukhaṃ puṣṭiḥ puṇyaṃ vidyā yaśo dhṛtiḥ ।।

mahā-pāpāny alakṣmīṃ ca duritaṃ durvicintitam ।
śoka-duḥkhādi harate prātaḥ-snānaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

kaurme tatraiva-
prātaḥ-snānaṃ praśaṃsanti dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa-karaṃ hi tat ।
prātaḥ-snānena pāpāni pūyante nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe ca-
prātaḥ-snānāt yataḥ śudhyet kāyo ayaṃ malinaḥ sadā ।
chidrito navabhiś chidraiḥ sravaty eva divā-niśam ।।

utsāha-medhā-saubhāgya-rūpa-sampat-pravartakam ।
manaḥ-prasannatā-hetuḥ prātaḥ-snānaṃ praśasyate ।।

prātaḥ prātas tu yat snānaṃ saṃjāte cāruṇodvaye ।
prājāpatya-samaṃ prāhus tan mahāgha-vighātakṛt ।।

prātaḥ-snānaṃ haret pāpam alakṣmīṃ glānim eva ca ।
aśucitvaṃ ca duḥsvapnaṃ tuṣṭiṃ puṣṭiṃ prayacchati ।।

nopasarpanti vai duṣṭāḥ prātaḥ-snāyi-janaṃ kvacit ।
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa-phalaṃ tasmāt prātaḥ-snānaṃ samācaret ।।

snāna-mātraṃ tathā prātaḥ-snānaṃ cātra niyojitam ।
yadyapy anyo anya-milite pṛthag jñeye tathāpy amū ।।

atha snāna-vidhiḥ

atha tīrtha-gatas tatra dhauta-vastraṃ kuśāṃs tathā ।
mṛttikāṃ ca taṭe nyasya snāyāt sva-sva-vidhānataḥ ।।

adhautena tu vastreṇa nitya-naimittikīṃ kriyām ।
kurvan na phalam āpnoti kṛtā cen niṣphalā bhavet ।।

dhautāṅghri-pāṇir ācāntaḥ kṛtvā saṅkalpam ādarāt ।
gaṅgādi-smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tīrthāyārghyaṃ samarpayet ।।

sāgara-svana-nirghoṣa-daṇḍa-hastāsurāntaka ।
jagat-sraṣṭar jagan-mardin namāmi tvāṃ sureśvara ।।

imaṃ mantraṃ samuccārya tīrtha-snānaṃ samācaret ।
anyathā tat-phalasyārdhaṃ tīrtheśo harati svayam ।।

natvātha tīrthaṃ snānārtham anujñāṃ prārthayed imām ।
devadeva jagannātha śaṅkha-cakra-gadādhara ।
dehi viṣṇo mamānujñāṃ tava tīrtha-niṣevaṇe ।।

iti 
vidhivan mṛdam ādāya tīrtha-toye praviśya ca ।
pravāhābhimukho nadyāṃ syād anyatrārka-sammukhaḥ ।।

dig-bandhaṃ vidhinācarya tīrthāni parikalpya ca ।
āvāhayed bhagavatīṃ gaṅgām āditya-maṇḍalāt ।।

darbha-pāṇiḥ kṛta-prāṇāyāmaḥ kṛṣṇa-padāmbujam ।
dhyātvā tan-nāma saṅkīrtya nimajjet puṇya-vāriṇi ।।

ācamya mūla-mantraṃ ca sa-prāṇāyāmakaṃ japan ।
kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyan jale bhūyo nimajjya snānam ācaret ।।

kṛtvāgha-marṣaṇāntaṃ ca nāmabhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ ।
tatra dvādaśadhā toye nimajjya snānam ācaret ।।

tatra viśeṣaḥ

śrī-nārada-pañcarātre-
prasiddheṣu ca tīrtheṣu yady anyasyābhidhāṃ smaret ।
snātakaṃ taṃ tu tat tīrtham abhiśapya kṣaṇād vrajet ।।

iti iti vaidika-tāntrika-miśrito vidhiḥ ।

pādme vaiśākhya-māhātmye [padmap ] śrī-nāradāmbarīṣa-saṃvāde -
evam uccārya tat-tīrthe pādau prakṣālya vāg yataḥ ।
smaran nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānaṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ ।।

tīrthaṃ prakalpayed dhīmān mūla-mantram imaṃ paṭhan ।
auṃ namo nārāyaṇāya mūla-mantra udāhṛtaḥ ।।

darbha-pāṇis tu vidhivad ācāntaḥ praṇato bhuvi ।
catur-hasta-samāyuktaṃ caturasraṃ samantataḥ ।।

prakalpyāvāhayed gaṅgāṃ mantreṇānena mānavaḥ ।
viṣṇu-pāda-prasūtāsi vaiṣṇavī viṣṇu-devatā ।
trāhi nas tvenasas tasmād ājanma-maraṇāntikāt ।।

। ityādi ।

sapta-vārābhijaptena kara-sampuṭa-yojite ।
mūrdhni kṛtvā jalaṃ bhūpaś catur vā pañca sapta vā ।
snānaṃ kṛtvā mṛdā tadvad āmantrya tu vidhānataḥ ।।

aśva-krānte ratha-krānte viṣṇu-krānte vasundhare ।
mṛttike hara me pāpaṃ yan mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।।

uddhṛtāsi varāheṇa viṣṇunā śata-bāhunā ।
namas te sarva-lokānāṃ prabhavāraṇi suvrate ।।

iti 
guroḥ sannihitasyātha pitroś ca caraṇodakaiḥ ।
viprāṇāṃ ca padāmbhodhiḥ kuryān mūrdhany abhiṣecanam ।।

tathā ca pādme- guroḥ pādodakaṃ putra tīrtha-koṭi-phala-pradam ।।

kiṃ ca-
vipra-pādodaka-klinnaṃ yasya tiṣṭhati vai śiraḥ ।
tasya bhāgīrathī-snānam ahany ahani jāyate ।।

tathā gautamīya-tantre-
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni tāni tīrthāni sāgare ।
sa-sāgarāṇi tīrthāni pāde viprasya dakṣiṇe ।।

iti 
śaṅkhe vasanti sarvāṇi tīrthāni ca viśeṣataḥ ।
śaṅkhena mūla-mantreṇābhiṣekaṃ punar ācaret ।।

tathaiva tulasī-miśra-śālagrāma-śilāmbhasā ।
abhiṣekaṃ vidadhyāc ca pītvā tat kiṃcid agrataḥ ।।

tad uktaṃ gautamīya-tantre-
śālagrāma-śilā-toyaṃ tulasī-gandha-miśritam ।
kṛtvā śaṅkhe bhrāmayaṃs triḥ prakṣipen nija-mūrdhani ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-toyam apītvā yas tu mastake ।
prekṣepaṇaṃ prakurvīta brahmahā sa nigadyate ।।

viṣṇu-pādodakān pūrvaṃ vipra-pādodakaṃ pibet ।
viruddham ācaran mohād brahmahā sa nigadyate ।।

śrī-caraṇāmṛta-dhāraṇa-mantraḥ

akāla-mṛtyu-haraṇaṃ sarva-vyādhi-vināśanam ।
viṣṇoḥ pādodakaṃ pītvā śirasā dhārayāmy aham ।।

iti 
lekhyo agrye kṛṣṇa-pādābja-tīrtha-dhāraṇa-pānayoḥ ।
mahimātra tu tat-tīrthenābhiṣekasya likhyate ।।

atha śrī-caraṇodakābhiṣeka-māhātmyam

padma-purāṇe [ ]-
sa snātaḥ sarva-tīrtheṣu sarva-yajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ ।
śālagrāma-śilā-toyair yo abhiṣekaṃ samācaret ।।

gaṅgā godāvarī revā nadyo mukti-pradās tu yāḥ ।
nivasanti satīrthās tāḥ śālagrāma-śilā-jale ।।

koṭi-tīrtha-sahasrais tu sevitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam ।
tīrthaṃ yadi bhavet puṇyaṃ śālagrāma-śilodbhavam ।।

tatraiva śrī-gautamāmbarīṣa-saṃvāde-
yeṣāṃ dhautāni gātrāṇi hareḥ pādodakena vai ।
ambarīṣa kule teṣāṃ dāso asmi vaśagaḥ sadā ।।

rājante tāni tāvac ca tīrthāni bhuvana-traye ।
yāvan na prāpyate toyaṃ śālagrāmābhiṣekajam ।।

skānde kārttika-māhātmye-
gṛhe'pi vasatas tasya gaṅgā-snānaṃ dine dine ।
śālagrāma-śilā-toyair yo abiṣiñcati mānavaḥ ।।

tatraivānyatra ca-
yāni kāni ca tīrthāni brahmādyā devatās tathā ।
viṣṇu-pādodakasyaite kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।।

śālagrāmodbhvao devo devo dvāravatī-bhavaḥ ।
ubhayoḥ snāna-toyena brahma-hatyā nivartate ।।

kiṃ ca-
sa vai cāvabhṛta-snātaḥ sa ca gaṅgā-jalāplutaḥ ।
viṣṇu-pādodakaṃ kṛtvā śaṅkheyaḥ snāti mānavaḥ ।।

śrī-nṛsiṃha-purāṇe- 
gaṅgā-prayāga-gaya-naimiṣa-puṣkarāṇi
puṇyāni yāni kuru-jāṅgala-yāmunāni ।
kālena tīrtha-salilāni punanti pāpaṃ
pādodakaṃ bhagavataḥ prapunāti sadyaḥ ।।

smṛtau ca-
tri-rātri-phaladā nadyo yāḥ kāścid asamudragāḥ ।
samudragāś ca pakṣasya māsasya saritāṃ patiḥ ।।

ṣaṇ-māsa-phaladā godā vatsarasya tu jāhnavī ।
pādodakaṃ bhagavato dvādaśābda-phala-pradam ।।

tan-nityatā

garuḍa-purāṇe- 
jalaṃ ca yeṣāṃ tulasī-vimiśritaṃ
pādodakaṃ cakra-śilā-samudbhavam ।
nityaṃ trisandhyaṃ plavate na gātraṃ
khagendra te dharma-bahiṣkṛtā narāḥ ।।

iti 
tato jalāñjalīn kṣiptvā mūrdhni trīn kumbha-mudrayā ।
mūlenāthāviśeṣeṇa kuryād devādi-tarpaṇam ।।

atha sāmānyato devādi-tarpaṇam

tac ca vaidikeṣu prasiddham eva- brahmādayo ye devās tān devān tarpayāmi । bhūr-devāṃs tarpayāmi । bhuvar-devāṃs tarpayāmi । svar-devāṃs tarpayāmi । bhūr-bhuvaḥ-svar-devāṃs tarpayāmi ।।

। ity ādi ।

ācāmyāṅgāni saṃmārjya snāna-vastrāṇya-vāsasā ।
paridhāyāṃśuke śukle niviśyācamanaṃ caret ।।

vidhivat tilakaṃ kṛtvā punaś cācamya vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
vidhāya vaidikīṃ sandhyām athopāsīta tāntrikīm ।।

atha vaidikī sandhyā

kaurme tatraiva-
prāk-kuleṣu tataḥ sthitvā darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ ।
prāṇāyāma-trayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyet sandhyām iti śrutiḥ ।।

manu-smṛtau -
brāhmaṇāḥ śāktikāḥ sarve na śaivā na ca vaiṣṇavāḥ ।
yata upāsate devīṃ gāyatrīṃ veda-mātaram ।।

yā ca sandhyā jagat-sūtir māyātītā hi niṣkalā ।
aiśvarī kevalā śaktis tattva-traya-samudbhavā ।।

dhyātvārka-maṇḍala-gatāṃ sāvitrīṃ tāṃ japed budhaḥ ।
prāṅ-mukhaḥ satataṃ vipraḥ sandhyopāsanam ācaret ।।

kiṃ ca-
sahasra-paramāṃ nityaṃ śata-madhyāṃ daśāvarām ।
sāvitrīṃ vai japed vidvān prāṅ-mukhaḥ prayataḥ sthitaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
sandhyā-hīno aśucir nityam anarhaḥ sarva-karmasu ।
yad anyat kurute kiñcin na tasya phalam apnuyāt ।।

yo anyatra kurute yatnaṃ dharma-kārye dvijottamaḥ ।
vihāya sandhyā-praṇatiṃ sa yāti narakāyutam ।।

ananya-cetasaḥ śāntā brāhmaṇā veda-pāragāḥ ।
upāsya vidhivat sandhyāṃ prāptāḥ pūrve parāṃ gatim ।।

atha tāntrikī sandhyā

tataḥ sampūjya salile nijāṃ śrī-mantra-devatām ।
tarpayed vidhinā tasya tathivāvaraṇāni ca ।।

tathā ca bodhāyana-smṛtau-
haviṣāgnau jale puṣpair dhyānena hṛdaye harim ।
arcanti sūrayo nityaṃ japena ravi-maṇḍale ।।

pādme ca tatraiva- sūrye cābhyarhaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ salile salilādibhiḥ ।।

atha tad-vidhiḥ

mūla-mantram athoccārya dhyāyan kṛṣṇāṅghri-paṅkaje ।
śrī-kṛṣṇaṃ tarpayāmīti triḥ samyak tarpayet kṛtī ।।

dhyānoddiṣṭa-svarūpāya sūrya-maṇḍala-vartine ।
kṛṣṇāya kāma-gāyatryā dadyād arghyam anantaram ।।

atha kāma-gāyatrī

śrī-sanat-kumāra-kalpe-
ādau manmatham uddhṛtya kāma-deva-padaṃ vadet ।
āyānte vidmahe puṣpa-bāṇāyeti padaṃ vadet ।
dhīmahīti tathoktvātha tan no anaṅgaḥ pracodayāt ।।

iti 
athārka-maṇḍale kṛṣṇaṃ dhyātvaitāṃ daśadhā japet ।
kṣamasveti tam udvāsya dadyād arghyaṃ vivasvate ।।

vidhis tāntirka-sandhyāyā jale'rcāyāś ca kaścana ।
yo anyo manyeta so apy atra tad-viśeṣāya likhyate ।।

atha matāntara-tāntrika-sandhyā-vidhiḥ

ādau dakṣiṇa-hastena gṛhṇīyād vāri vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
tato hṛdaya-mantreṇa vāma-pāṇi-tale'rpayet ।।

tad-aṅgulī-viniryātāmbhaḥ-kaṇair dakṣa-pāṇinā ।
mastake netra-mantreṇa kuryāt samprokṣaṇaṃ tataḥ ।।

śiṣṭaṃ tac cāstra-mantreṇādāyāmbho dakṣa-pāṇinā ।
adhaḥ kṣipet punaś caivam iti vāra-catuṣṭayam ।।

punar hṛdaya-mantreṇādāyāmbho dakṣa-pāṇinā ।
nāsā-puṭena vāmenāghrāyānyena visarjayet ।।

athāmbho añjalim ādāya sūrya-maṇḍala-vartine ।
arghyaṃ gopāla-gāyatryā kṛṣṇāya trir nivedayet ।।

sā coktā

brūyād gopījanaṃ ṅe'ntaṃ vidmahe ity ataḥ param ।
punar gopī-janaṃ tadvad dhīmahīti tataḥ param ।
tan naḥ kṛṣṇa iti prānte prapūrvaṃ codayād iti ।।

mūrdhni nyaset tad-aṅgāni lalāṭe netrayor dvayoḥ ।
bhujayoḥ pādayoś caiva sarvāṅgeṣu tathā kramāt ।।

tāni coktāni-
pañcabhiś ca tirbhiś caiva pañcabhiś ca tribhiḥ punaḥ ।
caturbhiś ca caturbhiś ca kuryād aṅgāni varṇakiḥ ।।

iti 
rāsa-krīḍā-rataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dhyātvā cāditya-maṇḍale ।
tat-sammukhotkṣipta-bhujo gāyatrīṃ tāṃ japet kṣaṇam ।।

atha tatra jale śrī-bhagavat-pūjā-vidhiḥ

aṅga-nyāsaṃ sva-mantreṇa kṛtvāthābjaṃ jalāntare ।
sañcintya pīṭha-mantreṇa tarpayec ca sakṛt sakṛt ।।

tasmiṃś ca kṛṣṇam āvāhya sakalīkṛtya mānasān ।
pañcopacārāt dattvāpsu dhenu-mudrāṃ pradarśayet ।।

taj-jalaṃ cāmṛtaṃ dhyātvā sva-mantreṇābhimantrya ca ।
aṣṭottara-śataṃ kṛṣṇottamāṅge tarpayet kṛtī ।।

tataś ca mūla-mantreṇa vārān vai pañca-viṃśatim ।
abhijaptenodakenācamanaṃ vidhinā caret ।।

atha viśeṣato devādi-tarpaṇam

pādme [; tatraiva-
brahmāṇaṃ tarpayet pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ prajāpatīn ।
devā yakṣās tathā nāgā gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।।

krūrāḥ sarpāḥ suparṇāś ca taravo jambhakādayaḥ ।
vidyādharā jaladharās tathaivākāśa-gāminaḥ ।।

nirādhārāś ca ye jīvā pāpa-dharma-ratāś ca ye ।
teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā ।।

kṛtopavīto devebhyo nivītī ca bhavet tataḥ ।
manuṣyāṃs tarpayed bhaktyā ṛṣi-putrān ṛṣīṃs tathā ।।

sanakaś ca sanandaś ca tṛtīyaś ca sanātanaḥ ।
kapilaś cāsuriś caiva voḍhuḥ pañca-śikhas tathā ।
sarve te tṛptim āyāntu mad-dattenāmbunā sadā ।।

marīcim atry-aṅgirasau pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ।
pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ nāradam eva ca ।
deva-brahma-ṛṣīn sarvāṃs tarpayet sākṣatodakaiḥ ।।

apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvāsavyaṃ jānu ca bhūtale ।
agniṣv āttās tathā saumyā bahiṣmantas tathoṣmapāḥ ।।

kavyānalau barhiṣadas tathā caivājyapāḥ punaḥ ।
tarpayet pitṛ-bhaktyā ca sa-tilokdaka-candanaiḥ ।।

yamāya dharma-rājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca ।
vaivasvatāya kālāya sarva-bhūtākṣayāya ca ।।

auḍumbarāya dadhnāya nīlāya parameṣṭhine ।
vṛkodarāya citrāya citra-guptāya vai namaḥ ।।
darbha-pāṇiḥ suprayataḥ pitṝn svān tarpayet tataḥ ।।
pitrādīn nāma-gotreṇa tathā mātā-mahān api ।
santarpya vidhinā sarvān imaṃ mantram udīrayet ।।

ye'bāndhavā bāndhavā vā ye'nya-janmani bāndhavāḥ ।
te tṛptim akhilāṃ yāntu ye cāsmat-toya-kāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।।

iti 
sandhyopāsanataḥ pūrvaṃ kecid devādi-tarpaṇam ।
manyante sakṛd evedaṃ purāṇoktānusārataḥ ।।

tathā ca pādme, snāne mṛd-grahaṇānantaram-
evaṃ snātvā tataḥ paścād ācamya suvidhānataḥ ।
utthāya vāsasī śukle śuddhe tu paridhāya vai ।
tatas tu tarpaṇaṃ kuryāt trailokyāpyāyanāya vai ।।

ata eva śrī-rāmārcana-candrikāyām-
niṣpīḍayitvā vastraṃ tu paścāt sandhyāṃ samācaret ।
anyathā kurute yas tu snānaṃ tasyāphalaṃ bhavet ।।

kiṃ ca-
vastraṃ triguṇitaṃ yas tu niṣpīḍayati mūḍha-dhīḥ ।
vṛthā snānaṃ bhavet tasya niṣpīḍayati cāmbuni ।।

kāśī-kāṇḍe-
api sarva-nadī-toyair mṛt-kūṭaiś cātha go-rasaiḥ ।
āpātam ācarec chaucaṃ bhāva-duṣṭo na śuddhi-bhāk ।।

naktaṃ dinaṃ nimajjyāpsu kaivartāḥ kim u pāvanāḥ ।
śataśo api tathā snātā na śuddhā bhāva-dūṣitāḥ ।।

pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye śrī-nāradāmbarīṣa-saṃvāde- 
puṇyena gāṅgena jalena kāle
deśe'pi yaḥ snāna-paro api bhūpa ।
ājanmato bhāva-hato api dātā na
śuddhyatīty eva mataṃ mamaitat ।।

prajvālya vahniṃ ghṛta-taila-siktaṃ
pradakṣiṇāvarta-śikhaṃ sva-kāle ।
praviśya dagdhaḥ kila bhāva-duṣṭo
na svargam āpnoti phalaṃ na cānyat ।।

ataeva bhaviṣyottare-
yasya hastau ca pādau ca vāṅ manaś ca susaṃyatam ।
vidyā-tapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrtha-phalam āpnuyāt ।।

aśraddadhānaḥ pāpātmā nāstiko acchinna-saṃśayaḥ ।
hetu-niṣṭhaś ca pañcaite na tīrtha-phala-bhāginaḥ ।।

iti śrī-gopāla-bhaṭṭa-vilikhite śrī-bhagavad-bhakti-vilāse śaucīyo nāma tṛtīyo vilāsaḥ ।

vaisnavalamkara-vilasa

caturtho vilāsaḥ śrī-vaiṣṇavālaṅkāraḥ

snātvā śrī-kṛṣṇa-caitanya-nāma-tīrthottame sakṛt ।
nityāśuciḥ śucīndraḥ san sva-dharmaṃ vaktum arhati ।।

atha sva-gṛham āgacched ādau natveṣṭa-devatām ।
gurūn jyeṣṭhāṃś ca puṣpaidhaḥ-kuśāmbhodhāraketarān ।।

tathā ca śrī-nṛsiṃha-purāṇe-
jale devaṃ namaskṛtya tato gacched gṛhaṃ pumān ।
pauruṣeṇa tu sūktena tato viṣṇuṃ samarcayet ।।

atha śrī-bhagavan-mandira-saṃskāraḥ

mandiraṃ mārjayed viṣṇor vidhāyācamanādikam ।
kṛṣṇaṃ paśyan kīrtayaṃś ca dāsyenātmānam arpayet ।।

śuddhaṃ gomayam ādāya tato mṛtsnāṃ jalaṃ tathā ।
bhaktyā tat parito limped abhukṣec ca tad-aṅganam ।।

tathā ca navama-skandhe [bhp ] śrīmad-ambarīṣopākhyāne sa vai manaḥ kṛṣṇa-padāravindayor 
vacāṃsi vaikuṇṭha-guṇānuvarṇane
karau harer mandira-mārjanādiṣu
śrutiṃ cakārācyuta-sat-kathodaye ।।

ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] śrī-bhagavad-uddhava-saṃvāde bhagavad-dharma-kathane -
sammārjanopalepābhyāṃ seka-maṇḍala-vartanaiḥ ।
gṛha-śuśrūṣaṇaṃ mahyaṃ dāsavad yad amāyayā ।।

atha tatra saṃmārjana-māhātmyam

śrī-nṛsiṃha-purāṇe -
narasiṃha-gṛhe nityaṃ yaṃ sammārjanam ācaret ।
samasta-pāpa-nirmukto viṣṇu-loke sa modate ।।

śrī-viṣṇu-dharmottare-
saṃmārjanaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt puruṣaḥ keśavālaye ।
rajas-tamobhyāṃ nirmuktaḥ sa bhaven nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

pāṃśūnāṃ yāvatāṃ rājan kuryāt saṃmārjanaṃ naraḥ tāvanty abdāni sa sukhī nākam āsādya modate ।।

śrī-vārāhe-
yāvatkāni prahārāṇi bhūmi-saṃmārjane daduḥ ।
tāvad-varṣa-sahasrāṇi śāka-dvīpe mahīyate ।।

jāyate mama bhaktaś ca sarva-dharma-samanvitaḥ ।
śucir bhāgavataḥ śuddho hy aparādha-vivarjitaḥ ।।

tato bhuktvā sarva-bhogān tīrtvā saṃsāra-sāgaram ।
śāka-dvīpāt paribhraṣṭaḥ svarga-lokaṃ sa gacchati ।।

nandanaṃ vanam āśritya modate cāpsaraiḥ saha ।
nandanāc ca paribhraṣṭo mama karma-vyavasthitaḥ ।
sarva-saṅgāt parityajya mama lokaṃ tu gacchati ।।

athopalepana-māhātmyam

tatraiva-
go-mayaṃ gṛhya vai bhūmiṃ mama veśmopalepayet ।
yāvatas tu padāṃs tatra samantād upalepayet ।
tāvad-varṣa-sahasrāṇi mad-bhakto jāyate tathā ।।

samīpe yadi vā dūre yaś cālayati gomayam ।
yāvat tasya padāgrāṇi tāvat svarge mahīyate ।।

śālmalau tat-paribhraṣṭo rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ।
mad-bhaktaś caiva jāyate sarva-śāstra-viśāradaḥ ।।

yaś cālepayate bhūmiṃ go-mayena dṛḍha-vrataḥ ।
tasya dṛṣṭvānulepaṃ tu mama tuṣṭiḥ prajāyate ।।

goś ca yasyāḥ purīṣeṇa kriyate bhūmi-lepanam ।
ekenaiva tu lepena go-yonyā vipramucyate ।।

sthānopalepane bhūme salilaṃ yo dadāti me ।
tasya puṇyaṃ mahā-bhāge śṛṇu tattvena niṣkalam ।।

yāvanti jala-bindūni lipyamānasya sundari ।
tāvad-varṣa-sahasrāṇi svarga-loke mahīyate ।।

yāvanto bindavaḥ kecit pānīyasya vasundhare ।
tāvad varṣa-sahasrāṇi krauñca-dvīpe mahīyate ।।

krauñca-dvīpāt paribhraṣṭaḥ sarva-dharma-parāyaṇaḥ ।
sarva-saṅgān parityajya mama lokaṃ ca gacchati ।।

śrī-viṣṇu-dharmottare-
kṛtvopalepanaṃ viṣṇor naras tv āyatane sadā ।
go-mayena śubhān lokān ayatnād eva gacchati ।।

hasta-pramāṇaṃ bhū-bhāgam upalipya narādhipa ।
deva-rāmā-śataṃ nāke labhate satataṃ naraḥ ।।

nārasiṃhe-
go-mayena mṛdā toyair yaḥ kuryād upalepanam ।
cāndrāyaṇa-phalaṃ prāpya viṣṇu-loke mahīyate ।।

tatraiva śrī-dharma-rājasya dūtānuśāsane-
saṃmārjanaṃ yaḥ kurute gomayenopalepanam ।
karoti bhavane viṣṇos tyājyaṃ teṣāṃ kula-trayam ।।

athābhukṣaṇa-māhātmyam

śrī-viṣṇu-dharmottare-
abhyukṣaṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt pānīyena surālaye ।
sa śānta-tāpo bhavati nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।

abhyukṣaṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryād deva-devājire naraḥ ।
sarva-pāpa-vinirmukto vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute ।।

sarvato-bhadra-padmādīn abhijñaḥ svastikāni ca ।
viracayya vicitrāṇi maṇḍayed dhari-mandiram ।।

tathā ca nārasiṃhe-
saṃmārjanopalepābhyāṃ raṅga-padmādi-śobhanam ।
kuryāt sthānaṃ mahā-viṣṇoḥ sojjvalāṅgaṃ mudānvitaḥ ।।

atha maṇḍala-māhātmyam

skanda-purāṇe kārttika-prasaṅge-
agamya-gamane pāpam abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe ।
sarvaṃ tan-nāśam āpnoti maṇḍayitvā harer gṛham ।।

aṇu-mātraṃ tu yaḥ kuryān maṇḍalaṃ keśavāgrataḥ ।
mṛdā dhātu-vikāraiś ca divi kalpa-śataṃ vaset ।।

śālagrāma-śilāgre tu yaḥ kuryāt svastikaṃ śubham ।
kārttike tu viśeṣeṇa punāty āsaptamaṃ kulam ।।

maṇḍalaṃ kurute nityaṃ yā nārī keśavāgrataḥ ।
sapta-janmāni vaidhavyaṃ na prāpnoti kadācana ।।

gṛhītvā go-mayaṃ yā tu maṇḍalaṃ keśavāgrataḥ ।
bhartur viyogaṃ nāpnoti santateś ca dhanasya ca ।।

prāṅgaṇaṃ varṇakopetaṃ svastikaiś ca samanvitam ।
devasya kurute yas tu krīḍate bhuvana-traye ।।

nāradīye-
mṛdā dhātu-vikārair vā varṇakair gomayena vā ।
viṣṇu-loke'tha tatra rathaiḥ sa-spṛhaṃ vīkṣyate sukhī ।।

hari-bhakti-sudhodaye-
upalipyālayaṃ viṣṇoś citrayitvātha varṇakaiḥ ।
viṣṇu-loke'tha tatrasthaiḥ sa-spṛhaṃ vīkṣyate sukhī ।।

atha svastika-lakṣaṇam

āgame-
vidig-gata-catuṣkāṇi bhittvā ṣoḍaśadhā sudhīḥ ।
mārjayet svastikākāraṃ śveta-pītāruṇāsitaiḥ ।।

tatra ca pañcarātra-vacanam-
rajāṃsi pañca-varṇāni maṇḍalārthaṃ hi kārayet ।
śāli-taṇḍula-cūrṇena śuklaṃ vā yava-sambhavam ।।

rakta-kuṅkuma-sindūra-gairikādi-samudbhavam ।
hari-tālodbhavaṃ pītaṃ rajanī-sambhavaṃ kvacit ।
kṛṣṇaṃ dagdhair harid-yavair harit-pītair vimiśritam ।।

atha tatra dhvaja-patākādy-āropaṇam

tato dhvaja-patākādi vinyasya hari-mandire ।
vicitraṃ bhūṣayet tac ca bhagavad-bhaktimān naraḥ ।।

atha dhvarāropaṇa-māhātmyam

dhvajam āropayed yas tu prāsādopari bhaktitaḥ ।
tasya brahma-pade vāsaḥ krīḍate brahmaṇā saha ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye -
yaḥ kuryād viṣṇu-bhavane dhvajāropaṇam uttamam ।
saṃpūjyate viriñcy-ādyaiḥ kim anyair bahu-bhāṣitaiḥ ।।

tatraivāgre ca [ṇārp ]-
paṭo dhvajasya viprendra yāvac calati vāyunā ।
tāvanti pāpa-jālāni naśyanty eva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

mahā-pātaka-yukto vā yukto vā sarva-pātakaiḥ ।
dhvajaṃ viṣṇu-gṛhe kṛtvā mucyate sarva-pātakaiḥ ।।

āropitaṃ dhvajaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye'bhinandanti dhārmikāḥ ।
te'pi sarve pramucyante mahā-pātaka-koṭibhiḥ ।।

।iti।

evaṃ bṛhan-nāradīye khyātaṃ yac cānyad adbhutam ।
dhvajāropaṇa-māhātmyaṃ tad draṣṭavyam ihākhilam ।।

atha patādāropaṇa-māhātmyam

dvārakā-māhātmye-
kṛṣṇālayaṃ yaḥ kurute patākābhiś ca śobhitam ।
sadaiva tasya loke tu vāsas tasya na cānyataḥ ।।

viṣṇudharmottare-
patākāṃ ca śubhāṃ dattvā tathā keśava-veśmani ।
vāyu-lokam avāpnoti bahūn abda-gaṇān dvijaḥ ।।

dodhūyate yathā sā tu vāyunā keśavālaye ।
tathā tasyāpi sakalaṃ dehāt pāpaṃ vidhūyate ।।

atha vandana-mālā-kadalī-stambhāropaṇa-māhātmyam

dvārakā-māhātmye tatraiva-
bhūpa vandana-mālāṃ tu kurute kṛṣṇa-veśmani ।
devakanyāvṛtair lakṣaiḥ sevyate sura-nāyakaiḥ ।।

yaḥ kuryāt kṛṣṇa-bhavanaṃ kadalī-stambha-śobhitam ।
nandate cāpsaro-yuktaḥ svāgataṃ tasya deva-rāṭ ।।

atha pīṭha-pātra-vastrādi-saṃskāraḥ

tatra tāmrādi-pātraṃ yat prabhor vastrādikaṃ ca yat ।
pīṭhādikaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ yathoktaṃ ca viśodhayet ।।

tatra pīṭhasya saṃskāraḥ

nārasiṃhe-
pāda-pīṭhaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya bilva-patreṇa dharṣayet ।
uṣṇāmbunā ca prakṣālya sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

atha taijasādi-pātrāṇāṃ saṃskāraḥ

mārkaṇḍeya-purāṇe-
uḍumbarāṇām amlena kṣāreṇa trapu-sīsayoḥ ।
bhasmāmbubhiś ca kāmsyānāṃ śuddhiḥ plāvo dravasya ca ।।

vāyu-purāṇe ca-
maṇi-vajra-pravālānāṃ muktā-śaṅkhopalasya ca ।
siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena tila-kalkena vā punaḥ ।।

brāhme-
suvarṇa-rūpya-śaṅkhāśma-śukti-ratna-mayāni ca ।
kāṃsyāyas-tāmra-raityāni trapu-sīsa-mayāni ca ।।

nirlepāni tu śudhyanti kevalenodakena tu ।
śūdrocchiṣṭhāni śodhyāni tridhā kṣārāmla-vāribhiḥ ।।

।iti।

atiduṣṭaṃ tu pātrādi viśodhyātithya-karmaṇe ।
yuñjyāt tat-parivartāya prabhu-karmāntarāya vā ।।

etasya parivartena prabhave'nyat samarpayet ।
ity ayaṃ sarvato loke sadācāro virājate ।।

manuḥ -
tāmrāyaḥ-kāṃsya-raityānāṃ trapuṇaḥ sīsakasya ca ।
śaucaṃ yathārhaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣārāmlodaka-vāribhiḥ ।।

śaṅkhaḥ-
amlodakena tāmrasya sīsasya trapuṇas tathā ।
kṣāreṇa śuddhiṃ kāṃsyasya lauhasya ca vinirdiśet ।।

kiṃ ca-
sūtikocchiṣṭha-bhāṇḍasya surādy-upahatasya ca ।
triḥ-sapta-mārjanāc chuddhir na tu kāṃsyasya tāpanam ।।

anyatra ca-
tāmram amlena śudhyena na cedāmiṣa-lepanam ।
āmiṣeṇa tu yal liptaṃ punar dāhena śudhyanti ।।

brāhme-
sūtikā-śava-viṇ-mūtra-rajaḥsvala-hatāni ca ।
prakṣeptavyāni tāny agnau yac ca yāvat sahed api ।।

ata eva devalaḥ-
lohānāṃ dahanāc chuddhir bhasmanā gomayena vā ।
dahanāt khananād vāpi śailānām ambhasāpi vā ।।

kāṣṭhānāṃ takṣaṇāc chuddhir mṛd-gomaya-jalair api ।
mṛṇ-mayānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ dahanāc chuddhir iṣyate ।।

manuḥ -
madyair mūtraiḥ purīṣair vā ṣṭhīvanaih pūyaśoṇitaiḥ ।
saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śuddhyeta punaḥpākena mṛn-mayam ।।

vṛddha-śātātapaḥ-
saṃhatānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ yad ekam upahanyate ।
tasyaivaṃ śodhanaṃ proktaṃ sāmānya-dravya-śuddhi-kṛt ।।

atha vastrādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥ

tatra śaṅkhaḥ-
tāntavaṃ malinaṃ pūrvam adbhiḥ kṣāraiś ca śodhayet ।
aṃśubhiḥ śoṣayitvā vā vāyunā vā samāharet ।।

ūrṇā-paṭṭāṃśuka-kṣauma-dukūlāvika-carmaṇām ।
alpāśauce bhavec chuddhiḥ śoṣaṇa-prokṣaṇādibhiḥ ।।

tāny evāmedhya-liptāni nenijyād gaura-sarṣapaiḥ ।
dhānya-kalkaiḥ parṇa-kalkaiḥ rasaiś ca phala-balkalaiḥ ।।

tulikādy-upadhānāni puṣpa-ratnāmbarāṇi ca ।
śodhayitvātape kiṃcit karair unmārjayen muhuḥ ।।

paścāc ca vāriṇā prokṣya śucīty evam udāharet ।
tāny apy atimalāktāni yathāvat pariśodhayet ।।

śātātapaḥ-
kusumbha-kuṅkumāraktās tathā lākṣā-rasena ca ।
prakṣālanena śudhyanti caṇḍāla-sparśane tathā ।।

yamaḥ-
kṛṣṇājinānāṃ vātaiś ca bālānāṃ mṛdbhir ambhasā ।
gomūtreṇāsthi-dantānāṃ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaura-sarṣapaiḥ ।।

śaṅkhaḥ-
siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena danta-śṛṅga-mayasya ca ।
go-bālaiḥ phala-pātrāṇām asthnāṃ syāc chṛṅgavat tathā ।।

kiṃ ca-
niryāsānāṃ guḍānāṃ ca lavaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca ।
kusumbha-kusumānāṃ ca ūrṇākārpāsayos tathā ।
prokṣaṇāt kathitā śuddhir ity āha bhagavān yamaḥ ।।

manuḥ [ ]
adbhis tu prokṣaṇaṃ śaucaṃ bahūnāṃ dhānya-vāsasām ।
prakṣālanena tv alpānām adbhiḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate ।।

cailavat-carmaṇāṃ śuddhir vaidalānāṃ tathā-eva ca ।
śāka-mūla-phalānāṃ ca dhānyavat-śuddhir iṣyate ।।

prokṣaṇāt tṛṇa-kāṣṭhaṃ ca palālaṃ caiva śudhyati ।
mārjana-upāñjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛt-mayam ।।

kiṃ ca [manu ]-
yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktād gandho lepaś ca tat-kṛtaḥ ।
tāvan mṛd-vāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu ।।

bṛhaspatiḥ-
vastra-vaidala-carmādeḥ śuddhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ smṛtam ।
atiduṣṭasya tan-mātraṃ tyajec chittvā tu śuddhaye ।।

viṣṇuḥ-
mṛt-parṇa-tṛṇa-kāṣṭhānāṃ śvāsthi-cāṇḍāla-vāyasaiḥ ।
sparśane vihitaṃ śaucaṃ soma-sūryāṃśu-mārutaiḥ ।।

baudhāyanaḥ-
āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ nāvaḥ panthās tṛṇāni ca ।
mārutārkeṇa śudhyanti pakveṣṭa-racitāni ca ।।

atha dhānyādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥ

tatra baudhāyanaḥ-
vrīhayaḥ prokṣaṇād adbhiḥ śāka-mūla-phalāni ca ।
tan-mātrasyāpahārād vā nistuṣīkaraṇena ca ।।

śaṅkhaḥ-
śrapaṇaṃ ghṛta-tailānāṃ plāvanaṃ go-rasasya ca ।
bhāṇḍāni plāvayed adbhiḥ śāka-mūla-phalāni ca ।।

brāhme- drava-dravyāṇi bhūrīṇi pariplāvyāni cāmbhasā ।।

śasyāni vrīhayaś caiva śāka-mūla-phalāni ca ।
tyaktvā tu dūṣitaṃ bhāgaṃ plāvyāny atha jalena tu ।।

bṛhaspatiḥ-
tāpanaṃ ghṛta-tailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya ca ।
tan-mātram uddhṛtaṃ śudhyet kaṭhinaṃ tu payodadhi ।।

avilīnaṃ tathā sarpir vilīnaṃ śrapaṇena tu ।
ādhāra-doṣe tu nayet pātrāt pātrāntaraṃ dravam ।।

ghṛtaṃ ca pāyasaṃ kṣīraṃ tathaikṣava-raso guḍaḥ ।
śūdra-bhāṇḍa-sthitaṃ takraṃ tathā madhu na duṣyati ।।

kiṃ ca manuḥ -
ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭo dravya-hastaḥ kathaṃ cana ।
anidhāyaiva tad dravyam ācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt ।।

।iti।

anye'pi śuddhi-vidhayo dravyāṇāṃ smṛti-śāstrataḥ ।
apekṣyā vaiṣṇavair jñeyās tat-tad-vistāraṇair alam ।।

atha pūjārtha-tulasī-puṣpādy-āharaṇam

praṇamyātha mahā-viṣṇuṃ prārthyānujñāṃ tu vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
samāharet śrī-tulasīṃ puṣpādi ca yathoditam ।।

yac ca hārīta-vacanam-
snānaṃ kṛtvā tu ye kecit puṣpaṃ gṛhṇanti vai dvijāḥ ।
devatās tan na gṛhṇanti bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat ।।

।iti।

tac ca madhyāhna-snāna-viṣayam, yata uktaṃ pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye-
asnātvā tulasīṃ chittvā devārthaṃ pitṛ-karmaṇi ।
tat sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ yāti pañcagavyena śudhyati ।।

atha gṛha-snāna-vidhiḥ

sva-gṛhe vācaran snānaṃ prakṣālyāṅghrī karau tathā ।
ācamyāyamya ca prāṇān kṛta-nyāso hariṃ smaret ।।

tato gaṅādikaṃ smṛtvā tulasī-miśritair jalaiḥ ।
pūrṇe pātre samastāni tīrthāny āvāhayet kṛtī ।।

āvāhana-mantraś cāyam-
gaṅge ca yamune caiva godāvari sarasvati ।
narmade sindhu kāveri jale'smin sannidhiṃ kuru ।।

।iti ।।

athavā jāhnavīm eva sarva-tīrtha-mayīṃ budhaḥ ।
āvāhayed dvādaśabhir nāmabhir jala-bhājane ।।

dvādaśa-nāmāni-
nalinī nandinī sītā mālinī ca mahāpagā ।
viṣṇu-pādārghya-sambhūtā gaṅgā tripatha-gāminī ।
bhāgīrathī bhogavatī jāhnavī tridaśeśvarī ।।

padma-purāṇe ca vaiśākha-māhātmye-
nandinīty eva te nāma vedeṣu nalinīti ca ।
dakṣā pṛthvī ca vihagā viśva-gāthā śiva-priyā ।।

vidyādharī mahā-devī tathā loka-prasādinī ।
kṣemaṃkarī jāhnavī ca śāntā śānti-pradāyinī ।।

athācamya guruṃ smṛtānujñāṃ prārthya ca pūrvavat ।
kṛṣṇa-pādābjato gaṅgāṃ patantīṃ mūrdhni cintayet ।।

tathā coktaṃ śrī-nārada-pañcarātre-
svasthitaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ mantra-mūrtiṃ prabhuṃ smaret ।
anantāditya-saṅkāśaṃ vāsudevaṃ caturbhujam ।।

śaṅkha-cakra-gadā-padmadharaṃ pītāmbarāvṛtam ।
śyāmalaṃ śānta-vadanaṃ prasannaṃ varadekṣaṇam ।।

divya-candana-liptāṅgaṃ cārahāsa-mukhāmbujam ।
aneka-ratna-saṃchanna-jvalan-makara-kuṇḍalam ।।

vanamālā-parivṛtaṃ nāradādibhir arcitam ।
keyūra-valayopetaṃ suvarṇa-mukuṭojjvalam ।
sarvāṅga-sundaraṃ devaṃ sarvābharaṇa-bhūṣitam ।।

tat-pāda-paṅkajād dhārāṃ nipatantīṃ sva-mūrdhani ।
cintayed brahma-randhreṇa praviśantīṃ svakāṃ tanum ।
tayā saṃkṣālayet sarvam antar-deha-gataṃ malam ।।

tat-kṣaṇād virajā mantrī jāyate sphaṭikopamaḥ ।
idaṃ snānāntaraṃ māntrāt sahasram adhikaṃ smṛtam ।।

।iti।

sakṛn nārāyaṇety ādi vacanaṃ tatra kīrtayet ।
snāna-kāle tu tan-nāma saṃsmarec ca mahāprabhum ।।

tathā ca kūrma-purāṇe-
āpo nārāyaṇodbhūtās tā evāsyāyanaṃ yathaḥ ।
tasmān nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snāna-kāle smared budhaḥ ।।

।iti।

snāyād uṣṇodakenāpi śakto apy āmalakais tathā ।
tilais tailaiś ca saṃvarjya pratiṣiddha-dināni tu ।।

athoṣṇodaka-snānam

ṣaṭ-triṃśan-mate-
āpaḥ svabhāvato medhyā viśeṣād agni-yogataḥ ।
tena santaḥ praśaṃsanti snānam uṣṇena vāriṇā ।।

yamaś ca-
āpaḥ svayaṃ sadā pūtā vahni-taptā viśeṣataḥ ।
tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu uṣṇāmbhaḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam ।।

yac coktaṃ śaṅkhena-
snātasya vahni-taptena tathaivātapa-vāriṇā ।
śarīra-śuddhir vijñeyā na tu snāna-phalaṃ bhavet ।।

।iti।

tat tu kāmya-naimittika-viṣayam । ata evoktaṃ gargeṇa- 
kuryān naimittikaṃ snānaṃ śītādbhiḥ kāmyam eva ca ।
nityaṃ yādṛcchikaṃ caiva yathāruci samācaret ।।

atha tatra niṣiddha-dināni

tatra yamaḥ-
putra-janmani saṅkrāntau grahaṇe candra-sūryayoḥ ।
aspṛśya-sparśane caiva na snāyād uṣṇa-vāriṇā ।।

vṛddha-manuḥ-
paurṇamāsyāṃ tathā darśe yaḥ snāyād uṣṇa-vāriṇā ।
sa gohatyā-kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prāpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ ।।

athāmalaka-snānam

tatra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ-
tuṣyaty āmalakair viṣṇur ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
śrī-kāmaḥ sarvadā snānaṃ kurvītāmalakair naraḥ ।।

saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ nīlīvastraṃ na dhārayet ।
na cāpy āmalakaṃ snāyān na kuryāt kalahaṃ naraḥ ।।

bhṛguḥ-
amāṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ saptamīṃ ca navamīṃ ca trayodaśīm ।
saṅkrāntau ravi-vāre ca snāna-mālakais tyajet ।।

yājñavalkyaḥ-
dhātrī-phalair amāvasyā-saptamī-navamīṣu ca ।
yaḥ snāyāt tasya hīyante tejaś cāyurdhanaṃ sutāḥ ।।

atha tila-snānam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ- sarva-kālaṃ tilaiḥ snānaṃ punar vyāso abravīn muniḥ ।।

ṣaṭtriṃśan-mate-
tathā saptamy-amāvasyā-saṅkrānti-grahaṇeṣu ca ।
dhana-putra-kalatrārthī tila-spṛṣṭaṃ na saṃspṛśet ।।

atha taila-snānam

tatraiva- ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tailam anāyuṣyaṃ caturthīṣv api ca parvasu ।।

yogī-yājñavalkyaḥ-
daśamyāṃ tailam apṛṣṭvā yaḥ snāyād avicakṣaṇaḥ ।
catvāri tasya naśyanti āyuḥ prajñā yaśodhanam ।।

mohāt pratipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ kuhūṃ riktātithiṃ tathā ।
tailenābhyañjayed yas tu caturbhiḥ parihīyate ।।

pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ saptamyāṃ ravi-saṅkrame ।
dvādaśyāṃ saptamīṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ taila-sparśaṃ vivarjayet ।।

anyac ca-
saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ navamyāṃ pratipady api ।
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃm amāvasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

kiṃ ca- snāne vā yadi vāsnāne pakka-tailaṃ na duṣyati ।।

kiṃ ca atri-smṛtau-
tailābhyukto ghṛtābhyakto viṇ-mūtre kurute dvijaḥ ।
aho-rātroṣito bhūtvā pañca-gavyena śudhyati ।।

athāṅgam alam uttārya snātvā vidhivad ācaret ।
nāsālagnena culukodakenaivāgha-marṣaṇam ।।

tato gurv-ādi-pādodaiḥ prāgvat kṛtvābhiṣecanam ।
kāryo abhiṣekaḥ śaṅkhena tulasī-miśritair jalaiḥ ।।

atha tulasī-jalābhiṣeka-māhatmyam

gāruḍe-
mārjayaty abhiṣeke tu tulasyā vaiṣṇavo naraḥ ।
sarva-tīrtha-mayaṃ dehaṃ tat-kṣaṇāt dvija jāyate ।।

tulasī-dalaja-snāne ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
mucyate sarva-pāpebhyo yadyapi brahmahā bhavet ।।

tan-mūla-mṛttikābhyaṅgaṃ kṛtvā snāti dine dine ।
daśāśvamedhāvabhṛtaṃ labhate snāna-jaṃ phalam ।।

tulasī-dala-saṃmiśraṃ toyaṃ gaṅgā-samaṃ viduḥ ।
yo vahec chirasā nityaṃ dhṛtā bhavati jāhnavī ।।

pādodakaṃ tāmra-pātre kṛtvā sa-tulasī-dalam ।
śaṅkhaṃ kṛtvābhiṣiñceta mūlenaiva sva-mūrdhani ।।

tan-māhātmye coktaṃ pādme kārttika-māhātmye-
dvārakā-cakra-saṃyukta-śālagrāma-śilā-jalam ।
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu nikṣiptaṃ snānārthaṃ tāmra-bhājane ।
tulasī-dala-saṃyuktaṃ brahma-hatyā-vināśanam ।।

।iti।

snāna-śāṭītareṇaiva vāsasāmbhāṃsi gātrataḥ ।
saṃmārjya vāsasī dadhyāt paridhānottarīyake ।।

atha vastra-dhāraṇa-vidhiḥ 
tatrātriḥ-
adhautaṃ kāru-dhautaṃ vā paredyu-dhautam eva vā ।
kāṣāyaṃ malinaṃ vastraṃ kaupīnaṃ ca parityajet ।।

na cārdram eva vasanaṃ paridadhyāt kadācana ।।
nagno malina-vastraḥ syāt nagnaś cārdha-paṭas tathā ।
nagno dviguṇa-vastraḥ syān nagno rakta-paṭas tathā ।।

nagnaś ca syūta-vastraḥ syān nagnaḥ snigdha-paṭas tathā ।
dvikaccho anuttarīyaś ca nagnaś cāvastra eva ca ।।

śrautaṃ smārtaṃ tathā karma na nagnaś cintayed api ।
mohāt kurvann adho gacchet tad bhaved āsuraṃ smṛtam ।।

japa-homopavāseṣu dhauta-vastra-dharo bhavet ।
alaṅkṛtaḥ śucir maunī śrāddhādau ca jitendriyaḥ ।।

gobhilaḥ- eka-vastro na bhuñjīta na kuryād devanārcanam ।।

trailokya-sammohana-pañcarātre- śukla-vāso bhaven nityaṃ raktaṃ caiva vivarjayet ।।

aṅgirāḥ-
śaucaṃ sahasra-romāṇāṃ vāyv-agny-arkendu-raśmibhiḥ ।
retaḥ-spṛṣṭaṃ śava-spṛṣṭam āvikaṃ naiva duṣyati ।।

anyatra ca-
chinnaṃ vā sandhitaṃ dagdhm āvikaṃ na praduṣyati ।
āvikena tu vastreṇa mānavaḥ śrāddham ācaret ।
gayā-śrāddha-samaṃ proktaṃ pitṛbhyo dattam akṣayam ।।

na kuryāt sandhitaṃ vastraṃ deva-karmaṇi bhūmipa ।
na dagdhaṃ na ca vai chinnaṃ pārakyaṃ na tu dhārayet ।।

kāka-viṣṭhā-samaṃ hy uktam avidhautaṃ ca yad bhavet ।
rajakād āhṛtaṃ yac ca na tad vastraṃ bhavec chuci ।।

kīṭa-spṛṣṭaṃ tu yad vastraṃ purīṣaṃ yena kāritam ।
mūtraṃ vā maithunaṃ vāpi tad vastraṃ parivarjayet ।।

āvikaṃ tu sadā vastraṃ pavitraṃ rāja-sattama ।
pitṛ-deva-manuṣyāṇāṃ kriyāyāṃ ca praśasyate ।।

dhautādhautaṃ tathā dagdhaṃ sandhitaṃ rajakāhṛtam ।
śukra-mūtra-rakta-liptaṃ tathāpi paramaṃ śuci ।।

agnir āvika-vastraṃ ca brahmaṇāś ca tathā kuśāḥ ।
caturṇāṃ na kṛto doṣo brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।।

kiṃ cānyatra-
dhārayed vāsasī śuddhe paridhānottarīyake ।
acchinna-sudaśe śukle ācāmet pīṭha-saṃsthitaḥ ।।

atha pīṭham

bahvṛca-pariśiṣṭe-
yatīnām āsanaṃ śuklaṃ kūrmākāraṃ tu kārayet ।
anyeṣāṃ tu catuṣpādaṃ caturasraṃ tu kārayet ।।

go-śakṛn-mayaṃ bhinnaṃ tathā palāśa-paippalam ।
loha-baddhaṃ sadaivārkaṃ varjayed āsanaṃ budhaḥ ।।

athāsana-vidhiḥ 
tatraiva-
dānam ācamanaṃ homaṃ bhojanaṃ devatārcanam ।
prauḍha-pādo na kurvīta svādhyāyaṃ caiva tarpaṇam ।।

āsanārūḍha-pādas tu jānunor vātha jaṅghayoḥ ।
kṛtāvaskthiko yas tu prauḍha-pādaḥ sa ucyate ।।

।iti।

tato bhūmi-gatāṅghriḥ san niviśyācamya darbha-bhṛt ।
ūrdhva-puṇḍrādikaṃ kuryāt śrī-gopī-candanādinā ।।

tatrādāv anulepena bhagavac-caraṇābjayoḥ ।
nirmālyena prasādena sarvāṇy aṅgāni mārjayet ।।

tad uktaṃ brāhme śrī-bhagavatā-
śālagrāma-śilā-lagnaṃ candanaṃ dhārayet sadā ।
sarvāṅgeṣu mahā-śuddhi-siddhaye kamalāsana ।।

।iti।

tato dvādaśabhiḥ kuryān nāmabhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ ।
dvādaśāṅgeṣu vidhivad ūrdhva-puṇḍrāṇi vaiṣṇavaḥ ।।

atha dvādaśa-tilaka-vidhiḥ

padma-purāṇe uttara-khaṇḍe -
lalāṭe keśavaṃ dhyāyen nārāyaṇam athodare ।
vakṣaḥ-sthale mādhavaṃ tu govindaṃ kaṇṭha-kūpake ।।

viṣṇuṃ ca dakṣiṇe kukṣau bāhau ca madhusūdanam ।
trivikramaṃ kandhare tu vāmanaṃ vāma-pārśvake ।।

śrīdharaṃ vāma-bāhau tu hṛṣīkeśaṃ tu kandhare ।
pṛṣṭhe tu padmanābhaṃ ca kaṭyāṃ dāmodaraṃ nyaset ।।
tat-prakṣālana-toyaṃ tu vāsudeveti mūrdhani ।।
kiṃ ca -
ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe tu sarveṣāṃ prathamaṃ smṛtam ।
lalāṭādi-krameṇaiva dhāraṇaṃ tu vidhīyate ।।

।iti।

evaṃ nyāsaṃ samācarya sampradāyānusārataḥ ।
nyaset kirīṭa-mantraṃ ca mūrdhni sarvārtha-siddhaye ।।

atha kirīṭa-mantraḥ
oṃ śrī-kirīṭa-keyūra-hāra-makara-kuṇḍala-cakra-śaṅkha-gadā-padma-hasta-pītāmbara-dhara śrīvatsāṅkita-vakṣaḥ-sthala śrī-bhūmi-sahita-svātma-jyotir dīpti-karāya sahasrāditya-tejase namo namaḥ ।।
।iti।

athordhva-puṇḍra-nityatā

pādme śrī-bhagavad-uktau-
mat-priyārthaṃ śubhārthaṃ vā rakṣārthe caturānana ।
mat-pūjā-homa-kāle ca sāyaṃ prātaḥ samāhitaḥ ।
mad-bhakto dhārayen nityam ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ bhayāpaham ।।

tatraiva śrī-nāradoktau-
yajño dānaṃ tapo homaḥ svādhyāyaḥ pitṛ-tarpaṇam ।
vyarthaṃ bhavati tat sarvam ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam ।।

tatraivottara-khaṇḍe-
ūrdhva-puṇḍrair vihīnas tu kiṃcit karma karoti yaḥ ।
iṣṭāpūrtādikaṃ sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ ।।

ūrdhva-puṇḍrair vihīnas tu sandhyā-karmādikaṃ caret ।
tat sarvaṃ rākṣasaṃ nityaṃ narakaṃ cādhigacchati ।।

anyac ca-
ūrdhva-puṇḍre tri-puṇḍraṃ yaḥ kurute narādhamaḥ ।
bhaṅktvā viṣṇu-gṛhaṃ puṇḍraṃ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam ।।

ata eva pādme śrī-nāradoktau-
yac charīraṃ manuṣyāṇām ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam ।
draṣṭavyaṃ naiva tat tāvat śmaśāna-sadṛśaṃ bhavet ।।

padma-purāṇe-
ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ mṛdā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate ।
sa cāṇḍālo api śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

skānde-
tiryak-puṇḍraṃ na kurvīta samprāpte maraṇe'pi ca ।
naivānyan nāma ca brūyāt pumān nārārāyaṇād ṛte ।।

dhārayed viṣṇu-nirmālyaṃ dhūpa-śeṣaṃ vilepanam ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ kārayet puṇḍraṃ gopī-candana-sambhavam ।।

tatraiva kārttika-prasaṅge-
yasyordhva-puṇḍraṃ dṛśyeta lalāṭe no narasya hi ।
tad-darśanaṃ na kartavyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūryaṃ nirīkṣayet ।।

anyatrāpi-
vaiṣṇavānāṃ brāhmaṇānām ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ vidhīyate ।
anyeṣāṃ tu tri-puṇḍraṃ syād iti brahma-vido viduḥ ।।

tripuṇḍraṃ yasya viprasya ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ na dṛśyate ।
taṃ spṛṣṭvāpy athavā dṛṣṭvā sa-celaṃ snānam ācaret ।।

ūrdhva-puṇḍre na kurvīta vaiṣṇavānāṃ tripuṇḍrakam ।
kṛta-tri-puṇḍra-martyasya kriyā na prītaye hareḥ ।।

ataevottara-khaṇḍe-
aśvattha-patra-saṅkāśo veṇu-patrākṛtis tathā ।
padma-kuṭmala-saṅkāśo mohanaṃ tritayaṃ smṛtam ।।

athordhva-puṇḍra-māhātmyam

skānde kārttika-prasaṅge-
ūrdhva-puṇḍro mṛdā śubhro lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate ।
caṇḍālo api viśuddhātmā yāti braham sanātanam ।।

ūrdhva-puṇḍre sthitā lakṣmīr ūrdhva-puṇḍre sthitaṃ yaśaḥ ।
ūrdhva-puṇḍre sthitā muktir ūrdhva-puṇḍre sthito hariḥ ।।

padma-purāṇe-
ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ mudā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate ।
sa cāṇḍālo api śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tatraivottara-khaṇḍe śivomā-saṃvāde -
ūrdhva-puṇḍrasya madhye tu viśāle sumanohare ।
lakṣmyā sārdhaṃ samāsīno deva-devo janārdanaḥ ।।

tasmād yasya śarīre tu ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ dhṛto bhavet ।
tasya dehaṃ bhagavato vimalaṃ mandiraṃ śubham ।।

ūrdhva-puṇḍra-dharo vipraḥ sarva-lokeṣu pūjitaḥ ।
vimāna-varam āruhya yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।।

ūrdhva-puṇḍra-dharaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।
namaskṛtvāthavā bhaktyā sarva-dāna-phalaṃ labhet ।।

ūrdhva-puṇḍra-dharaṃ vipraṃ yaḥ śrāddhe bhojayiṣyati ।
ākalpa-koṭi-pitaras tasya tṛptā na saṃśayaḥ ।।

ūrdhva-puṇḍra-dharo yas tu kuryāc chrāddhaṃ śubhānane ।
kalpa-koṭi-sahasrāṇi gayā-śrāddha-phalaṃ labhet ।।

yajña-dāna-tapaś-caryā-japa-homādikaṃ ca yat ।
ūrdhva-puṇḍra-dharaḥ kuryāt tasya puṇyam anantakam ।।

śrī-brahmāṇḍa-purāṇe-
aśucir vāpya nācāro manasā pāpam ācaran ।
śucir eva bhaven nityam ūrdhva-puṇḍrāṅkito naraḥ ।।

tatraiva śrī-bhagavad-vacanam-
ūrdhva-pūṇḍra-dharo martyo mriyate yatra kutracit ।
śvapāko api vimānastho mama loke mahīyate ।।

ūrdhva-pūṇḍra-dharo martyo gṛhe yasyānnam aśnute ।
tadā viṃśat-kulaṃ tasya narakād uddharāmy ahaṃ ।।

athohva-pūṇḍra-irmāṇa-vidhiḥ

śrī-brahmāṇḍa-purāṇe-
vīkṣyādarśe jale vāpi yo vidadhyāt prayatnataḥ ।
ūrdhva-pūṇḍraṃ mahā-bhāga sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।

daśāṅgula-pramāṇaṃ tu uttamottamam ucyate ।
navāṅgulaṃ madhyamaṃ syād aṣṭāṅgulam ataḥ param ।।
etair aṅguli-bhedais tu kārayen na nakhaiḥ spṛśet ।।
padma-purāṇe uttara-khaṇḍe tatraiva [ ] -
ekāntino mahā-bhāgāḥ sarva-bhūta-hite ratāḥ ।
sāntarālaṃ prakurvīran puṇḍraṃ hari-padākṛtim ।।

śyāmaṃ śānti-karaṃ proktaṃ raktaṃ vaśya-karaṃ tathā ।
śrī-karaṃ pītam ity āhuḥ śvetaṃ mokṣa-karaṃ śubham ।।

vartulaṃ tiryag achidraṃ hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ tataṃ tanum ।
vakraṃ virūpaṃ baddhāgraṃ chinna-mūlaṃ pada-cyutam ।।

aśubhaṃ rūkṣam āsaktaṃ tathā nāṅguli-kalpitam ।
vigandham avasahyaṃ ca puṇḍram āhur anarthakam ।।

ārabhya nāsikā-mūlaṃ lalāṭāntaṃ likhen mṛdā ।
nāsikāyās trayo bhāgā nāsā-mūlaṃ pracakṣyate ।।
samārabhya bhruvor madhyam antarālaṃ prakalpayet ।।
tatraiva [ ]
nirantarālaṃ yaḥ kuryād ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ dvijādhamaḥ ।
sa hi tatra sthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ śriyaṃ caiva vyapohati ।।

acchidram ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ tu ye kurvanti dvijādhamāḥ ।
teṣāṃ lalāṭe satataṃ śunaḥ pādo na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tasmāc chidrānvitaṃ puṇḍraṃ daṇḍākāraṃ suśobhanam ।
viprāṇāṃ satataṃ kāryaṃ strīṇāṃ ca śubha-darśane ।।

hari-mandira-lakṣaṇam

nāsādi-keśa-prayantam ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ suśobhanam ।
madhye chidra-samāyuktaṃ tad vidyād harimandiram ।।

vāma-pārśve sthito brahmā dakṣiṇe ca sadā-śivaḥ ।
madhye viṣṇuṃ vijānīyāt tasmān madhyaṃ na lepayet ।।

vāyu-purāṇe sevāparādhe-
adhṛtvā cordhva-puṇḍraṃ ca hareḥ pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ ।
tiryak-puṇḍra-dharo yas tu yajed devaṃ janārdanam ।।

accidreṇordhva-puṇḍreṇa bhasmanā tiryag-aṅginā ।
adhṛtvā śaṅkha-cakre ca cety ādinā doṣa uktaḥ ।।

śrutiś ca, yajurvedasya hiraṇya-keśaurya-śakhāyām- 
hareḥ padākrāntim ātmani dhārayati yaḥ ।
sa parasya priyo bhavati sa puṇyavān ।
madhye chidram ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ
yo dhārayati sa muktibhāg bhavati ।।

।iti।

tilaka-racanāṅguli-niyamaḥ

smṛtiḥ-
anāmikā kāmadoktā madhyam āyuskarī bhavet ।
aṅguṣṭhaḥ puṣṭidaḥ proktas tarjanī mokṣa-dāyinī ।।

athordhva-puṇḍra-mṛttikāḥ

padma-purāṇe tatraiva-
parvatāgre nadī-tīre bilva-mūle jalāśaye ।
sindhu-tīre ca valmīke hari-kṣetre viśeṣataḥ ।।

viṣṇoḥ snānodakaṃ yatra pravāhayati nityaśaḥ ।
puṇḍrāṇāṃ dhāraṇārthāya gṛhṇīyāt tatra mṛttikām ।।

śrī-raṅge veṅkaṭādrau ca śrī-kūrme dvārake śubhe ।
prayāge nārasiṃhādrau vārāhe tulasī-vane ।।

gṛhītvā mṛttikāṃ bhaktyā viṣṇu-pāda-jalaiḥ saha ।
dhṛtvā puṇḍrāṇi cāṅgeṣu viṣṇu-sāyujyam āpnuyāt ।।

tatraiva- yat tu divyaṃ hari-kṣetre tasyaiva mṛdam āharet ।।

uktaṃ ca pādme śrī-nāradena-
brahmaghno vātha go-ghno vā haitukaḥ sarva-pāpa-kṛt ।
gopī-candana-samparkāt pūto bhavati tat-kṣaṇāt ।।

gopī-candana-khaṇḍaṃ tu yo dadātii hi vaiṣṇave ।
kulam ekottaraṃ tena sambhavet tāritaṃ śatam ।।

skanda-purāṇe-
śaṅkha-cakrāṅkita-tanuḥ śirasā mañjarī-dharaḥ ।
gopī-candana-liptāṅgo dṛṣṭaś cet tad aghaṃ kṛtaḥ ।।

gopī-mṛt-tulasī śaṅkhaḥ śālagrāmaḥ sacakrakaḥ ।
gṛhe'pi yasya pañcaite tasya pāpa-bhayaṃ kutaḥ ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe ca śrī-yamena-
śrīkhaṇḍe kva sa āmodaḥ svarovarṇaḥ kva tādṛśaḥ ।
tat pāvitryaṃ kva vai tīrthe śrī-gopī-candane yathā ।।

atha gopīcandanordhva-puṇḍra-māhātmyam

uktaṃ ca garuḍa-purāṇe nāradena- 
yo mṛttikāṃ dvāravatī-samudbhavāṃ
kare samādāya lalāṭa-paṭṭake ।
karoti nityaṃ tv atha cordhva-puṇḍraṃ
kriyā-phalaṃ koṭi-guṇaṃ sadā bhavet ।।

kriyā-vihīnaṃ yadi mantra-hīnaṃ
śraddhā-vihīnaṃ yadi kāla-varjitam ।
kṛtvā lalāṭe yadi gopī-candanaṃ
prāpnoti tat karma-phalaṃ sadā kṣayam ।।

gopī-candana-sambhavaṃ suruciraṃ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dvijo
nityaṃ dhārayate yadi dvija-pate rātrau divā sarvadā ।
yat puṇyaṃ kuru-jāṅgale ravi-grahe mādhyāṃ prayāge tathā
tat prāpnoti khagendra viṣṇu-sadane santiṣṭhate devavat ।।

yasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati gopīcandanaṃ
bhaktyā lalāṭe manujo bibharti ।
tasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati sarvadā hariḥ
śraddhānvitaḥ kaṃsahā vihaṅgama ।।

yo dhārayet kṛṣṇa-purī-samudbhavāṃ
sadā pavitrāṃ kali-kilbiṣāpahām ।
nityaṃ lalāṭe hari-mantra-saṃyutāṃ
yamaṃ na paśyed yadi pāpa-saṃvṛtaḥ ।।

yasyānta-kāle khaga gopī-candanaṃ
bāhvor lalāṭe hṛdi mastake ca ।
prayāti lokaṃ kamalālayaṃ prabhor
go-bāla-ghātī yadi brahma-hā bhavet ।।

grahā na pīḍanti na rakṣasāṃ gaṇāḥ
yakṣāḥ piśācoraga-bhūta-dānavāḥ ।
lalāṭa-paṭṭe khaga gopī-candanaṃ
santiṣṭhate yasya hareḥ prasādataḥ ।।

padma-purāṇe śrī-gotamena-
ambarīṣa mahāghasya kṣayārthe kuru vīkṣaṇam ।
lalāṭe yaiḥ kṛtaṃ nityaṃ gopī-candana-puṇḍrakam ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe ca śrī-yamena-
dūtāḥ śṛṇuta yad-bhālaṃ gopī-candana-lāñchitam ।
jvalad-indhanavat so api tyājyo dūre prayatnataḥ ।।

।iti।

atha tasyopari śrīmat-tulasī-mūla-mṛtsnayā ।
tatraiva vaiṣṇavaiḥ kāryam ūrdhva-puṇḍraṃ manoharam ।।

atha śrī-tulasī-mūla-mṛttikā-puṇḍra-māhātmyam

tan-mṛdaṃ gṛhya yaiḥ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dhāritaṃ naraiḥ ।
pramāṇakaṃ kṛtaṃ tais tu mokṣāya gamanaṃ prati ।।

tatraiva ca kārttika-māhātmye brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
tulasī-mṛttikā-puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate ।
dehaṃ na spṛśati pāpaṃ kriyamāṇas tu nārada ।।

garuḍa-purāṇe-
tulasī-mṛttikā-puṇḍraṃ yaḥ karoti dine dine ।
tasyāvalokanāt pāpaṃ yāti varṣa-kṛtaṃ nṛṇām ।।

।iti।

tasyopariṣṭhād bhagavan-nirmālyam anulepanam ।
tathaiva dhāryam evaṃ hi trividhaṃ tilakaṃ smṛtam ।।

tato nārāyaṇīṃ mudrāṃ dhārayet prītaye hareḥ ।
matsya-kūrmādi-cihnāni cakrādīny āyudhāni ca ।।

atha mudrā-dhāraṇa-nityatā

smṛtau-
aṅkitaḥ śaṅkha-cakrābhyām ubhayor bāhu-mūlayoḥ ।
samarcayed dhariṃ nityaṃ nānyathā pūjanaṃ bhavet ।।

āditya-purāṇe-
śaṅkha-cakrordhva-puṇḍrādi-rahitaṃ brāhmaṇādhamam ।
gardabhaṃ tu samāropya rājā rāṣṭrāt pravāsayet ।।

gāruḍe śrī-bhagavad-uktau-
sarva-karmādhikāraś ca śucīnām eva coditaḥ ।
śucitvaṃ ca vijānīyān madīyāyudha-dhāraṇāt ।।

pādme cottara-khaṇḍe-
śaṅkha-cakrādibhiś cihnair vipraḥ priyatamair hareḥ ।
rahitaḥ sarva-dharmebhyaḥ pracyuto narakaṃ vrajet ।।

śrutau ca yajuḥ-kaṭha-śākhāyām- 
dhṛtordhva-puṇḍraḥ kuta-cakra-dhārī
viṣṇuṃ paraṃ dhyāyati yo mahātmā ।
svareṇa mantreṇa sadā hṛdi sthitaṃ
parātparaṃ yan mahato mahāntam ।।

atharvaṇi ca- 
ebhir vayam urukramasya cihnair
aṅkitā loke subhagā bhavema ।
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ
ye gacchanti lāṅchitāḥ ।।

। ity ādi ।

ataeva brahma-purāṇe
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sammānaṃ na karoti yaḥ ।
dvādaśābdārjitaṃ puṇyaṃ cāphalayopagacchati ।।

atha mudrā-dhāraṇa-māhātmyam

skānde śrī-sanat-kumāra-mārkaṇḍeya-saṃvāde-
yo viṣṇu-bhakto viprendra śaṅkha-cakrādi-cihnitaḥ ।
sa yāti viṣṇu-lokaṃ vai dāha-pralaya-varjitam ।।

tatra vāntyatra ca-
nārāyaṇāyudhair nityaṃ cihnitaṃ yasya vigraham ।
pāpa-koṭi-yuktasya tasya kiṃ kurute yamaḥ ।।

śaṅkhoddhāre tu yat proktaṃ vasatāṃ varṣa-koṭibhiḥ ।
tat phalaṃ likhite śaṅkhe pratyahaṃ dakṣiṇe bhuje ।।

yat phalaṃ puṣkare nityaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa-darśane ।
śaṅkhopari kṛte padme tat phalaṃ samavāpnuyāt ।।

vāme bhuje gadā yasya likhitā dṛśyate kalau ।
gadādharo gayā-puṇyaṃ pratyahaṃ tasya yacchati ।।

yac cānanda-pure proktaṃ cakra-svāmī-samīpataḥ ।
gadādhollikhite cakre tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇa-darśane ।।

śrī-bhagavad-uktau-
yaḥ punaḥ kali-kāle tu mat-purī-sambhavāṃ mṛdam ।
matsya-kūrmādikāṃ cihnaṃ gṛhītvā kurute naraḥ ।।

dehe tasya praviṣṭo ahaṃ jānantu tridaśottamāḥ ।
tasya me nāntaraṃ kiṃcit kartavyaṃ śreya icchatā ।।

mamāvatāra-cihnāni dṛśyante yasya vigrahe ।
martyair martyo na vijñeyaḥ sa nūnaṃ māmakī tanūḥ ।।

pāpaṃ sukṛta-rūpaṃ tu jāyate tasya dehinaḥ ।
mamāyudhāni tasyāṅge likhitāni kalau yuge ।।

ubhābhyām api cihnābhyāṃ yo aṅkito matsya-mudrayā ।
kūrmayāpi svakaṃ tejo nikṣiptaṃ tasya vigrahe ।।

śaṅkhaṃ ca padmaṃ ca gadāṃ rathāṅgaṃ
matsyaṃ ca kūrmaṃ racitaṃ sva-dehe ।
karoti nityaṃ sukṛtasya vṛddhiṃ
pāpa-kṣayaṃ janma-śatārjitasya ।।

tatraiva śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
kṛṣṇa-śastrāṅka-kavacaṃ durbhedyaṃ deva-dānavaiḥ ।
adṛśyaṃ sarva-bhūtānāṃ śatrūṇāṃ rakṣasām api ।।

lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī durgā sāvitrī hari-vallabhā ।
nityaṃ tasya vased dehe yasya śaṅkhāṅkitā tanuḥ ।।

gaṅgā gayā kurukṣetraṃ prayāgaṃ puṣkarādi ca ।
nityaṃ tasya sadā tiṣṭhed yasya padāṅkitaṃ vapuḥ ।।

yasya kaumodakī-cihnaṃ bhuje vāme kali-priya ।
pratyahaṃ tatra draṣṭavyo gaṅgā-sāgara-saṅgamaḥ ।।

savye kare gadādhastad rathāṅgaṃ tiṣṭhate yadi ।
kṛṣṇena sahitaṃ tatra trailokyaṃ sa-carācaram ।।

trayo agnayas trayo devā viṣṇos trīṇi padāni ca ।
nivasanti sadā yasya yasya dehe sudarśanam ।।

kiṃ ca-
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitā mudrā yasya nārāyaṇī kare ।
ūrdhva-lokādhikārī ca sa jñeyas tridaśāṃ patiḥ ।।

kṛṣṇa-mudrā-prayuktas tu daivaṃ pitryaṃ karoti yaḥ ।
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ pratyahaṃ cākṣayaṃ bhavet ।।

pīḍayanti na tatraiva grahā ṛkṣāṇi rāśayaḥ ।
aṣṭākṣarāṅkitā mudrā yasya dhātumayī kare ।।

vārāhe śrī-sanat-kumāroktau-
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dehaṃ gopī-candana-mṛtsnayā ।
prayāgādiṣu tīrtheṣu sa gatvā kiṃ kariṣyati ।।

yadā yasya prapaśyeta dehaṃ śaṅkhādi-cihnitam ।
tadā tasya jagat-svāmī tuṣṭo harati pātakam ।।

bhavate yasya dehe tu aho-rātraṃ dine dine ।
śaṅkha-cakra-gadā-padmaṃ likhitaṃ so acyutaḥ svayam ।।

nārāyaṇāyudhair yuktaṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ kalau yuge ।
kurute puṇya-karmāṇi meru-tulyāni tāni vai ।।

śaṅkhādināṅkito bhaktyā śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kurute dvija ।
vidhi-hīnaṃ tu sampūrṇaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu gayā-samam ।।

yathāgnir dahate kāṣṭhaṃ vāyunā prerito bhṛśam ।
tathā dahyanti pāpāni dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇāyudhāni vai ।।

brāhmye śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
viṣṇu-nāmāṅkitāṃ mudrām aṣṭākṣara-samanvitām ।
śaṅkhādikāyudhādikair yuktāṃ svarṇa-rūpya-mayīm api ।।

dhatte bhāgavato yas tu kalikāle viśeṣataḥ ।
prahlādasya samo kṣeyo nānyathā kala-vallabha ।।

kiṃ ca-
śaṅkhāṅkita-tanur vipro bhuṅkte yasya ca veśmani ।
tad-annaṃ svayam aśnāti pitṛbhiḥ saha keśavaḥ ।।

kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkito yas tu śmaśāne mriyate yadi ।
prayāge yā gatiḥ proktā sā gatis tasya nārada ।।

kṛṣṇāyudhaiḥ kalau nityaṃ maṇḍitaṃ yasya vigraham ।
tatrāśrayaṃ prakurvanti vivadhā vāsavādayaḥ ।।

yaḥ karoti hareḥ pūjāṃ kṛṣṇa-śastrāṅkito naraḥ ।
aparādha-sahasrāṇi nityaṃ harati keśavaḥ ।।

kṛtvā kāṣṭha-mayaṃ bimbaṃ kṛṣṇa-śastrais tu cihnitam ।
yo hy aṅkayati cātmānaṃ tat-samo nāsti vaiṣṇavaḥ ।।

pāṣaṇḍa-patita-vrātyair nāstikālāpa-pātakaiḥ ।
na lipyate kali-kṛtaiḥ kṛṣṇa-śastrāṅkito naraḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
aṣṭākṣarāṅkitā mudrā yasya dhātumayī bhavet ।
śaṅkha-padmādibhir yuktā pūjyate'sau surāsuraiḥ ।।

dhṛtā nārāyaṇī mudrā prahlādena purā kṛte ।
vibhīṣaṇena balinā dhruveṇa ca śukena ca ।।

māndhātṛṇāmbarīṣeṇa mārkaṇḍa-pramukhair dvijaiḥ ।
śaṅkhādi-cihnitaiḥ śastrair dehe kṛtvā kalipriya ।
ārādhya keśavāt prāptaṃ samīhita-phalaṃ mahat ।।

kiṃ ca-
gopī-candana-mṛtsnāyā likhitaṃ yasya vigrahe ।
śaṅkha-padmādi-cakraṃ vā tasya dehe vased dhariḥ ।।

tatraiva śrī-sanat-kumāroktau-
yasya nārāyaṇī mudrā dehaṃ śaṅkhādi-cihnitam ।
dhātrī-phala-kṛtā mālā tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhavā ।।

dvādaśākṣara-mantrais tu niyuktāni kalevare ।
āyudhāni ca viprasya mat-samaḥ sa ca vaiṣṇavaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
yasya nārāyaṇī mudrā dehe śaṅkhādi cihnitā ।
sarvāṅgaṃ cihnitaṃ yasya sastrair nārāyaṇodbhavaiḥ ।
praveśo nāsti pāpasya kavacaṃ tasya vaiṣṇavam ।।

anyatra ca-
ebhir bhāgavataiś cihnaiḥ kali-kāle dvijātayaḥ ।
bhavanti martya-loke te śāpānugraha-kārakāḥ ।।

atha mudrā-dhāraṇa-vidhiḥ

gautamīye-
cakraṃ ca dakṣiṇe bāhau śaṅkhaṃ vāme'pi dakṣiṇe ।
gadāṃ vāme gadādhastāt punaś cakraṃ ca dhārayet ।।

śaṅkhopari tathā padmaṃ punaḥ padmaṃ ca dakṣiṇe ।
khaḍgaṃ vakṣasi cāpaṃ ca sa-śaraṃ śīrṣṇi dhārayet ।।

iti pañcāyudhāny ādau dhārayed vaiṣṇavo janaḥ ।
matsyaṃ ca dakṣiṇe haste kūrmaṃ vāma-kare tathā ।।

tathā coktaṃ -
dakṣiṇe tu bhuje vipro vibhṛṣād vai sudarśanam ।
matsyaṃ padmaṃ cāpare'tha śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ gadās tathā ।।

।iti।

sāmpradāyika-śiṣṭānām ācārāc ca yathāruci ।
śaṅkha-cakrādi-cihnāni sarveṣv aṅgeṣu dhārayet ।।
bhaktyā nijeṣṭa-devasya dhārayel lakṣaṇāny api ।।cakra-śaṅkhau ca dhāryate saṃmiśrāv eva kaiścana ।।
śrī-gopī-candanenaivaṃ cakrādīni budho anvaham ।
dhārayec chayanādau tu taptāni kila tāni hi ।।

atha cakrādīnāṃ lakṣaṇāni

dvādaśāraṃ tu ṣaṭ-koṇaṃ valayatraya-saṃyutam ।
cakraṃ syād dakṣiṇāvartaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca śrī-hareḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

gadā-padmādikaṃ loka-siddham eva mataṃ budhaiḥ ।
mudrā vā bhagavan-nāmāṅkitā vāṣṭākṣarādibhiḥ ।।

atha mālādi-dhāraṇam

tataḥ kṛṣṇārpitā mālā dhārayet tulasī-dalaiḥ ।
padmākṣais tulasī-kāṣṭhaiḥ phalair dhātryāś ca nirmitāḥ ।।

dhārayet tulasī-kāṣṭha-bhūṣaṇāni ca vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
mastake karṇayor bāhvoḥ karayoś ca yathā-ruci ।।

atha mālā-dhāraṇa-vidhiḥ

skānde-
sannivedyaiva haraye tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhavām ।
mālāṃ paścāt svayaṃ dhatte sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

haraye nārpayed yas tu tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhavām ।
mālāṃ dhatte svayaṃ mūḍhaḥ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam ।।

kṣālitāṃ pañca-gavyena mūla-mantreṇa mantritām ।
gāyatryā cāṣta kṛtvā vai mantritāṃ dhūpayec ca tām ।
vidhivat parayā bhaktyā sadyo-jātena pūjayet ।।

tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhūte māle kṛṣṇa-jana-priye ।
bibharmi tvām ahaṃ kaṇṭhe kuru māṃ kṛṣṇa-vallabham ।।

yathā tvaṃ vallabhā viṣṇor nityaṃ viṣṇu-jana-priyā ।
tathā māṃ kuru deveśi nityaṃ viṣṇu-jana-priyam ।।

dāne lā-dhātur uddiṣṭo lāsi māṃ hari-vallabhe ।
bhaktebhyaś ca samastebhyas tena mālā nigadyase ।।

evaṃ samprārthya vidhivan mālāṃ kṛṣṇa-gale'rpitām ।
dhārayed vaiṣṇavo yo vai sa gacched vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।।

tatraiva kārttika-prasaṅge-
dhātrī-phala-kṛtāṃ mālāṃ kaṇṭhasthāṃ yo vahen na hi ।
vaiṣṇavo na sa vijñeyo viṣṇu-pūjā-rato yadi ।।

gāruḍe-
dhārayanti na ye mālāṃ haitukāḥ pāpa-buddhayaḥ ।
narakān na nivartante dagdhāḥ kopāgninā hareḥ ।।

ata eva skānde-
na jahyāt tulasī-mālāṃ dhātrī-mālāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
mahā-pātaka-saṃhantrīṃ dharma-kāmārtha-dāyinīm ।।

atha mālā-dhāraṇa-māhātmyam

agastya-saṃhitāyām-
nirmālya-tulasī-mālā-yukto yaś cārcayed dharim ।
yad yat karoti tat sarvam ananta-phaladaṃ bhavet ।।

nāradīye- 
ye kaṇṭha-lagna-tulasī-nalinākṣa-mālā
ye vā lalāṭa-phalke lasad ūrdhva-puṇḍrāḥ ।
ye bāhu-mūla-paricihnita-śaṅkha-cakrās
te vaiṣṇavā bhuvanam āśu pavitrayanti ।।

kiṃ ca- 
bhuja-yugam api cihnair aṅkitaṃ yasya viṣṇoḥ
parama-puruṣa-nāmnāṃ kīrtanaṃ yasya vāci ।
ṛjutaram api puṇḍraṃ mastake yasya kaṇṭhe
sarasija-maṇi-mālā yasya tasyāsmi dāsaḥ ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare śrī-bhagavad-uktau-
tulasī-kāṣṭha-mālāṃ ca kaṇṭha-sthāṃ vahate tu yaḥ ।
apy aśauco apy anācāro mām evaiti na saṃśayaḥ ।।

skānde-
dhātrī-phala-kṛtā mālā tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhavā ।
dṛśyate yasya dehe tu sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

tulasī-dalajāṃ mālāṃ kaṇṭhasthāṃ vahate tu yaḥ ।
viṣṇūttīrṇā viśeṣeṇa sa namasyo divaukasām ।।

tulasī-dalajā mālā dhātrī-phala-kṛtāpi ca ।
dadāti pāpināṃ muktiṃ kiṃ punar viṣṇu-sevinām ।।

tatraiva kārttika-prasaṅge-
yaḥ punas tulasī-mālāṃ kṛtvā kaṇṭhe janārdanam ।
pūjayet puṇyam āpnoti pratipuṣpaṃ gavāyutam ।।

yāval luṭhati kaṇṭha-sthā dhātrī-mālā narasya hi ।
tāvat tasya śarīre tu prītyā luṭhati keśavaḥ ।।

spṛśec ca yāni lomāni dhātrī-mālā kalau nṛṇām ।
tāvad varṣa-sahasrāṇi vasate keśavālaye ।।

yāvad dināni vahate dhātrī-mālāṃ kalau naraḥ ।
tāvad-yuga-sahasrāṇi vaikuṇṭhe vasatir bhavet ।।

mālā-yugmaṃ vahed yas tu dhātrī-tulasi-saṃbhavam ।
vahate kaṇṭha-deśe tu kalpa-koṭi-ṃ divaṃ vaset ।।

gāruḍe ca mārkaṇḍeyoktau-
tulasī-dalajāṃ mālāṃ kṛṣṇottīrṇā vahet tu yaḥ ।
patre patre'śvamedhānāṃ daśānāṃ labhate phalam ।।

tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhūtāṃ yo mālāṃ vahate naraḥ ।
phalaṃ yacchati daitāriḥ pratyahaṃ dvārakodbhavam ।।

nivedya viṣṇave mālāṃ tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhavam ।
vahate yo naro bhaktyā tasya vai nāsti pātakam ।।

sadā prītamanās tasya kṛṣṇa devakī-nandanaḥ ।
tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhūtāṃ yo mālāṃ vahate naraḥ ।
prāyaścittaṃ na tasyāsti nāśaucaṃ tasya vigrahe ।।

tulasī-kāṣṭha-sambhūtāṃ śiraso yasya bhūṣaṇam ।
bāhvoḥ kare ca martyasya dehe tasya sadā hariḥ ।।

tulasī-kāṣṭha-mālābhir bhūṣitaḥ puṇyam ācaret ।
pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca kṛtaṃ koṭi-guṇaṃ kalau ।।

tulasī-kāṣṭha-mālāṃ tu preta-rājasya dūtakāḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā naśyanti dūreṇa vātoddhūtaṃ yathā dalam ।।

tulasī-kāṣṭha-mālābhir bhūṣito bhramate yadi ।
duḥsvapnaṃ durnimittaṃ ca na bhayaṃ śastrajaṃ kvacit ।।

atha gṛhe sandhyopāsana-vidhiḥ

sandhyopāsty-ādikaṃ karma tataḥ kuryāt yathā-vidhi ।
kṛṣṇa-pādodakenaiva tatra devādi-tarpaṇam ।।

śirasā viṣṇu-nirmālyaṃ pādodenāpi tarpaṇam ।
pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca vaiṣṇavais tu samaṃ matam ।।

sandhyopāstau ca vaśiṣṭha-vacanam-
gṛhe tv eka-guṇā sandhyā goṣṭhe daśa-guṇā smṛtā ।
śata-sāhasrikā nadyām anantā viṣṇu-sannidhau ।।

atha śrī-guru-pūjā

pūjayiṣyaṃs tataḥ kṛṣṇam ādau sannihitaṃ gurum ।
praṇamya pūjayed bhaktyā dattvā kiṃcid upāayanam ।।

smṛti-mahārṇave-
rikta-pāṇir na paśyeta rājānaṃ bhiṣajaṃ gurum ।
nopāyana-karaḥ putraṃ śiṣyaṃ bhṛtyaṃ nirīkṣayet ।।

kiṃ ca, śrī-bhagavad-uktau-
prathamaṃ tu guruṃ pūjya tataś caiva mamārcanam ।
kurvan siddhim avāpnoti hy anyathā niṣphalaṃ bhavet ।।

śrī-nāradena ca-
gurau sannihite yas tu pūjayed anyam agrataḥ ।
sa durgatim avāpnoti pūjanaṃ tasya niṣphalam ।।

śrutiṣu [śvetu ]
yasya deve parā bhaktiḥ yathā deve tathā gurau ।
tasyaite kathitā hy arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ ।।

ekādaśa-skandhe śrī-bhagavad-uktau-
ācāryaṃ māṃ vijānīyān nāvamanyeta karhicit ।
na martya-buddhyāsūyeta sarva-deva-mayo guruḥ ।।

daśama-skandhe [bhp ] ca 
nāham ijyā-prajātibhyāṃ tapasopaśamena ca ।
tuṣyeyaṃ sarva-bhūtātmā guru-śuśrūṣayā yathā ।।

saptama-skandhe [bhp ]-
yasya sākṣād bhagavati jñāna-dīpa-prade gurau ।
martyāsad-dhīḥ śrutaṃ tasya sarvaṃ kuñjara-śaucavat ।।

anyatrāpi-
sādhakasya gurau bhaktiṃ mandīkurvanti devatāḥ ।
yan no atītya vrajed viṣṇuṃ śiṣyo bhaktyā gurau dhruvan ।।

manu-smṛtau -
ajño bhavati vai bālaḥ pitā bhavati mantradaḥ ।
ajñaṃ hi bālam ity āhuḥ pitety eva tu mantradam ।।

kiṃ ca-
gurur brahmā gurur viṣṇur gurur devo maheśvaraḥ ।
gurur eva paraṃ brahma tasmāt sampūjayet sadā ।।

vāmana-kalpe-
yo mantraḥ sa guruḥ sākṣāt yo guruḥ sa hariḥ smṛtaḥ ।
gurur yasya bhavet tuṣṭas tasya tuṣṭo hariḥ svayam ।
guroḥ samāsane naiva na caivoccāsane vaset ।।

viṣṇu-rahasye-
tasmāt sarva-prayatnena yathā-vidhi tathā gurum ।
abhedenārcayet yas tu sa mukti-phalam āpnuyāt ।।

viṣṇu-dharme śrī-bhāgavate ca hariścandrasya-
guru-suśrūṣaṇaṃ nāma sarva-dharmottamottamam ।
tasmād dharmāt paro dharmaḥ pavitraṃ naiva vidyate ।।

kāma-krodhādikaṃ yad yad ātmano aniṣṭa-kāraṇam ।
etat sarvaṃ gurau bhaktyā puruṣo hy añjasā jayet ।।

pādme-
pitur ādhikya-bhāvena ye'rcayanti guruṃ sadā ।
bhavanty atithayo loke brahmaṇas te viśāṃ vara ।।

tatraiva devahūti-stutau-
bhaktir yathā harau me'sti tadvan niṣṭhā gurau yadi ।
mamāsti tena satyena svaṃ darśayatu me hariḥ ।।

aditya-purāṇe-
avidyo vā sa-vidyo vā gurur eva janārdanaḥ ।
mārgastho vāpy amārga-stho gurur eva sadā gatiḥ ।।

anyatra ca-
harau ruṣṭe gurus trātā gurau ruṣṭe na kaścana ।
tasmāt sarva-prayatnena gurum eva prasādayet ।।

brahma-vaivarte-
api ghnantaḥ śapanto vā viruddhā api ye krudhāḥ ।
guravaḥ pūjanīyās te gṛhaṃ natvā nayeta tān ।।

tat ślāghyaṃ janma dhanyaṃ tat dinaṃ puṇyātha naḍikā ।
yasyāṃ guruṃ praṇamate samupāsya tu bhaktitaḥ ।।

upadeṣṭāram āmnāya-gataṃ pariharanti ye ।
tān mṛtān api kravyādāḥ kṛtaghnān nopabhuñjate ।।

bodhaḥ kaluṣitas tena daurātmyaṃ prakaṭīkṛtam ।
gurur yena parityaktas tena tyaktaḥ purā hariḥ ।।

anyatra ca -
pratipadya guruṃ yas tu mohād vipratipadyate ।
sa kalpa-koṭiṃ narake pacyate puruṣādhamaḥ ।।

pañcarātre 
avaiṣṇavopadiṣṭena mantreṇa nirayaṃ vrajet ।
punaś ca vidhinā samyag grāhayed vaiṣṇavād guroḥ ।।

agastya-saṃhitāyāṃ 
ye gurv-ājñāṃ na kurvanti pāpiṣṭhāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ ।
na teṣāṃ naraka-kleśa-nistāro muni-sattama ।।

yaiḥ śiṣyaiḥ śaśvad ārādhyā guravo hy avamānitāḥ ।
putra-mitra-kalatrādi-sampadbhyaḥ pracyutā hi te ।।

adhikṣipya guruṃ mohāt paruṣaṃ pravadanti ye ।
śūkaratvaṃ bhavaty eva teṣāṃ janma-śateṣv api ।।

ye guru-drohiṇo mūḍhāḥ satataṃ pāpa-kāriṇaḥ ।
teṣāṃ ca yāvat sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ ।।

ataḥ prāg gurum abhyarcya kṛṣṇa-bhāvena buddhimān ।
try-avarān asamān kuryāt praṇāmān daṇḍa-pātavat ।।

ata eva kaurme śrī-vyāsa-gītāyām-
vyatyasta pāṇinā kāryam upasaṅgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ ।
savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇaḥ ।।

।iti।

atha śrī-guru-pādānāṃ prāpyānujñāṃ ca sādhakaḥ ।
prāk saṃskṛtaṃ harer gehaṃ pravekṣyan pāduke tyajet ।।

tathā cāpastamba-
agny-āgāre gavāṃ goṣṭhe deva-brāhmaṇa-sannidhau ।
jape bhojana-kāle ca pāduke parivarjayet ।।

।iti।

tataḥ śrī-bhagavat-pūjā-mandirasyāṅganaṃ gataḥ ।
prakṣālya hastau pādau ca dvi-rācamanam ācaret ।।

tathā ca mārkaṇḍeye-
devārcanādi-kāryāṇi tathā gurv-abhivādanam ।
kurvīta samyag ācamya tadvad eva bhuji-kriyām ।।

।iti।

iti śrī-gopāla-bhaṭṭa-vilikhite śrī-bhagavad-bhakti-vilāse śrī-vaiṣṇavālaṅkāro nāma caturtho vilāsaḥ

adhisthanika-vilasa

pañcama-vilāsaḥ ādhiṣṭhānikaḥ

śrī-caitanya-prabhuṃ vande bālo api yad-anugrahāt ।
taren nānā-mata-grāha-vyāptaṃ pūjā-kramārṇavam ।।

sanātanaḥ śrī-caitanyāya namaḥ । bālo ajñaḥ । pakṣe śiśuḥ । nānā-vidha-matāny eva grāhas tair vyāptam । pūjāyāḥ kramo vidhiḥ । vidhy-anukramo vā sa evārṇavas tam hbhvc 

śrīmad-gopāla-devasyāṣṭādaśākṣara-yantrataḥ ।
likhyate'rcā-vidhir gūḍhaḥ krama-dīpikayekṣitaḥ ।।

sanātanaḥ aṣṭādaśākṣara-mantreṇa yo arcā-vidhiḥ pūjā-prakāraḥ sa likhyate । yadyapi daśākṣarādināpi pūjā-vidhau bhedo nāsti, tathāpi nyāsādi-bhedāpekṣayā, tathā likhitam । gūḍho api krama-dīpikayā śrī-keśavācārya-viracitayā īkṣitaḥ darśitaḥ san । ataḥ krama-dīpikoktānusāreṇa lekhya iti bhāvaḥ hbhvc 

āgamoktena mārgeṇa bhagavān brāhmaṇair api ।
sadaiva pūjyo ato lekhyaḥ prāya āgamiko vidhiḥ ।।

tathā ca viṣṇu-yāmale-
kṛte śruty-ukta-mārgaḥ syāt tretāyāṃ smṛti-bhāvitaḥ ।
dvāpare tu purāṇoktaḥ kalāv āgama-sambhavaḥ ।।

aśuddhāḥ śūdrākalpā hi brāhmaṇāḥ kali-sambhavāḥ ।
teṣām āgama-mārgeṇa śuddhir na śrauta-vartmanā ।।

sanātanaḥ teṣām āgama-mārgeṇa śrauta-vartmanety anena tair api āgamika-vidhinaiva pūjā kāryeti bhāvaḥ । tathā caikādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] nānā-tantra-vidhānena kalāv api tathā śṛṇu iti । tatra śrīdhara-svāmi-pādāḥ-nānā-tantra-vidhāneneti kalau tantra-mārgasya prādhānyaṃ darśayati iti hbhvc 

atha dvāra-pūjā

śrī-kṛṣṇa-dvāra-devebhyo dattvā pādyādikaṃ tataḥ ।
gandha-puṣpair arcayet tān yathā-sthānaṃ yathā-kramam ।।

sanātanaḥ tān śrī-kṛṣṇa-dvāra-devān, praṇavādi-caturthy-antaṃ deva-nāma namo antakam ity agre lekhyatvād atraivaṃ prayogaḥ-śrī-kṛṣṇa-dvāra-devatābhyo namaḥ । anena mantreṇa pādyārdhyādikaṃ dattvā gandhādibhiḥ punar viśeṣeṇa pūjayed ity arthaḥ । evam agre'pi sa-parivārebhyaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa-pārṣadebhyo namaḥ ity ādi prayogo draṣṭavyaḥ hbhvc 

dvārāgre sa-parīvārān bhū-pīṭhe kṛṣṇa-pārṣadān ।
tad-agre garuḍaṃ dvārasyordhve dvāra-śriyaṃ yajet ।।

prāg-dvārobhaya-pārśve tu yajec caṇḍa-pracaṇḍakau ।
dvāre ca dakṣiṇe dhātṛ-vidhātārau ca paścime ।।

jayaṃ ca vijayaṃ caiva balaṃ prabalam uttare ।
dvandva-śastv evam abhyarcya dehalyāṃ vāstu-puruṣam ।।

sanātanaḥ evaṃ sāmānyena sarveṣām eva pūjā-vidhir likhitaḥ । idānīṃ yathā-sthānaṃ yathā-kramam iti yal likhitaṃ, tad eva vivicya likhati-dvārāgra iti dvārābhyām । tatrāpy ādau dvārasyāgre yat bhū-rūpaṃ pīṭhaṃ, tatra samasta-parivārānvitān śrī-kṛṣṇa-pārṣadān yajet pūjayet । anantaraṃ tasya dvārasyāgre garuḍaṃ । yadyapi dvāra-śriyo arcanaṃ prabalārcanānantaram eva krama-dīpikāyām uktam, tathāpi iṣṭveti kṭvā-pratyayena caṇḍādi-pūjātaḥ pūrva-kāla eveti bodhitam । tathaivaa sad-ācārāt । kiṃ ca, dvandva ity agre likhanāt, caṇḍa-pracaṇḍābhyāṃ namaḥ ity evaṃ yugmatvena prayogo jñeyaḥ hbhvc 

dvārāntaḥ-pārśvayor gaṅgāṃ yamunāṃ ca tato arcayet ।
tat-pārśvayoḥ śaṅkha-nidhiṃ tathā padma-nidhiṃ yajet ।।

sanātanaḥ dvārasyāntaḥ abhyantare tat-pārśva-dvaye tayor gaṅgā-yamunayoḥ pārśva-dvaye hbhvc 

gaṇeśaṃ mandirasyāgni-koṇe durgāṃ ca nairṛte ।
vāṇīṃ vāyavya aiśāne kṣetrapālaṃ tathārcayet ।।
sanātanaḥ āgneye koṇe gaṇeśam arcayet । tathā coktaṃ krama-dīpikāyām -
parivārārāḥ kṛtāḥ sarve punaḥ śrī-viṣṇu-pārṣadāḥ ।
dvārāgrābali-pīṭhe'rcyāḥ pakṣīndraś ca tad-agrataḥ ।।

caṇḍa-pracaṇḍau prāg dhātṛ-vidhātārau ca dakṣiṇe ।
jayaḥ sa-vijayaḥ paścād balaḥ prabala uttare ।।

ūrdhve dvāra-śriyaṃ ceṣṭvā dvāry etān yugmaśo arcayet ।
pūjyo vāstu-pumāṃs tatra tatra dvāḥ-pītha-madhyataḥ ।।

dvārāntaḥ-pārśvayor arcyā gaṅgā ca yamunā nadī ।
koṇeṣu vighnaṃ durgāṃ ca vāṇīṃ kṣetre samarcayet ।।

iti

dvāḥ-śākhām āśrayan vāmāṃ saṅkocyāṅgāni dehalīm ।
aspṛṣṭvā praviśed veśma nyasyan prāg dakṣiṇaṃ padam ।।

sanātanaḥ vāmāṃ sva-vāma-bhāga-vartinīṃ dvāra-śākhāṃ āśrayan īṣat spṛṣad nijāṅgāni saṃkocya dehalīm aspṛṣṭvā na laṅghayitvety arthaḥ । dakṣiṇaṃ padaṃ prāk ādau nyasyan । dakṣiṇa-pāda-nyāsa-krameṇety arthaḥ । veśma śrī-bhagavan-mandiraṃ harer gehaṃ pravekṣyann iti pūrva-likhanāt । praviśet tan-madhyaṃ śanaiḥ pūjako gacchet hbhvc 

tathā ca sāradā-tilake-
kiṃcit spṛśan vāma-śākhāṃ dehalīṃ laṅghayan guruḥ ।
aṅgaṃ saṅkocayann antaḥ praviśed dakṣiṇāṅghriṇā ।।

sanātanaḥ gurur iti dīkṣā-vidhānoktaḥ hbhvc 

atha gṛha-praveśa-māhātmyam

tan-māhātmyaṃ ca hari-bhakti-sudhodaye-
praviśann ālayaṃ viṣṇor arcanārthaṃ subhaktimān ।
na bhūyaḥ praviśan mātuḥ kukṣi-kārā-gṛhaṃ sudhīḥ ।।

atha gṛhāntaḥ-pūjā

nairṛte vāstu-puruṣaṃ brahmāṇam api pūjayet ।
āsanastho yajet tāṃs tān anyatra bhagavad-gṛhāt ।।

tat-pūjāmantraś coktaḥ-
praṇavādi-caturthy-antaṃ deva-nāma namo antakam ।
pūjā-mantram idaṃ proktaṃ sarvatrārcana-karmaṇi ।।

iti

atha kṛṣṇāgratas tiṣṭhan kṛtvā dig-bandhanaṃ kṣipet ।
puṣpākṣatān samastāsu dikṣu tatrokta-mantrataḥ ।।

atha pūjārthāsanam

tataś cāsana-mantreṇābhimantryābhyarcya cāsanam ।
tasminn upaviśet padmāsanena svastikena vā ।।

tatra kṛṣṇārcakaḥ prāyo divase prāṅ-mukho bhavet ।
udaṅmukho rajanyāṃ tu sthira-mūrtiś ca sammukhaḥ ।।

tatra ca ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ]- āsīnaḥ prāg udag-vārcet sthirāyāntv atha sammukhaḥ ।।

athāsana-mantraḥ

āsana-mantrasya meru-pṛṣṭha ṛṣiḥ sutalaṃ chandaḥ ।
kūrmo devatā āsanābhimantreṇa viniyogaḥ ।।

pṛthvi tvayā dhṛtā lokā devi tvaṃ viṣṇunā dhṛtā ।
tvaṃ ca dhāraya māṃ nityaṃ pavitraṃ kuru cāsanam ।।

athāsana-vidhiḥ

nārada-pañcarātre- vaṃśāśma-dāru-dharaṇī-tṛṇa-pallava-nirmitam । varjayed āsanaṃ vidvān dāridrya-vyādhi-duḥkhadam । kṛṣṇājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā nānyad āsanam iṣyate ।।

anyatra ca-
kṛṣṇājinaṃ vyāghra-carma kauṣeyaṃ vetra-nirmitam ।
vastrājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā kalpayed āsanaṃ mṛdu ।।

atha viśeṣata āsana-doṣa-vidhiḥ

nārada-pañcarātre-
vaṃśād āhur daridratvaṃ pāṣāṇe vyādhi-sambhavam ।
dharaṇyāṃ duḥkha-sambhūtiṃ daurbhāgyaṃ dāravāsane ।।

tṛṇāsane yaśo-hāniṃ pallave citta-vibhramam ।
darbhāsane vyādhi-nāśaṃ kambalaṃ duḥkha-mocanam ।।

kiṃ ca, śrī-bhagavad-gītāsu [ṅītā ]-
śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ ।
nātyucchritaṃ nātinīcaṃ cailājina-kuśottaram ।।

iti

yathokatam upaviśyātha sampradāyānusārataḥ ।
śaṅkhādi-pūjā-sambhārān nyaset tat-tat-padeṣu tān ।।

atha pātrāsādanam

svasya vāmāgrataḥ śaṅkhaṃ sādhāraṃ sthāpayed budhaḥ ।
tatraivārdhyādi-pātrāṇi nyasyec ca dvāri bhāgaśaḥ ।।

tulasī-gandha-puṣpādi-bhājanāni ca dakṣiṇe ।
vāme ca sthāpayet pārśve kalasaṃ pūrṇam ambhasā ।।

dakṣiṇe ghṛta-dīpaṃ ca taila-dīpaṃ ca vāmataḥ ।
sambhārānaparān nyaset sva-dṛṣṭi-viṣaye pade ।
kara-prakṣālanārthaṃ ca pātram ekaṃ sva-pṛṣṭhataḥ ।।

atha pātrāṇi tan-māhātmyaṃ ca

devī-purāṇe-
nānā-vicitra-rūpāṇi puṇḍarīkākṛtīni ca ।
śaṅkha-nīlotpalābhāni pātrāṇi parikalpayet ।।

ratnādi-racitāny eva kāñcī-mūla-yutāni ca ।
yathā-śobhaṃ yathā-lābhaṃ tathā pātrāṇi kārayet ।।

kiṃ ca-
haṃsa-pātreṇa sarvāṇi cepsitāni labhen mune ।
arghyaṃ dattvā tathā raupyeṇāyu-rājyaṃ śubhaṃ bhavet ।
tāmra-pātreṇa saubhāgyaṃ dharmaṃ mṛṇ-maya-sambhavam ।।

vārāhe-
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ kāṃsyaṃ yena dīyate bhājanam ।
tān sarvān samparityajya tāmraṃ tu mama rocate ।।

pavitrāṇāṃ pavitraṃ yo maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam ।
viśuddhānāṃ śuciṃ caiva tāmraṃ saṃsāra-mokṣaṇam ।।

dīkṣitānāṃ viśuddhānāṃ mama karma-parāyaṇaḥ ।
sadā tāmreṇa kartavyam evaṃ bhūmi mama priyam ।।

iti

kecic ca tāmra-pātreṣu gavyāder yoga-doṣataḥ ।
tāmrātiriktam icchanti madhuparkasya bhājanam ।।

tathaiva śaṅkham evārdhya-pātram icchanti kecana ।
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu pānīyaṃ sa-puṣpaṃ salilākṣatam ।
arghyaṃ dadāti devasyety evaṃ skānde'bhidhānataḥ ।।

atha maṅgala-ghaṭa-sthāpanam

maṅgalārthaṃ ca kalasaṃ sajalaṃ karakānvitam ।
phalādi-sahitaṃ divyaṃ nyased bhagavato agrataḥ ।।

tathā ca skānde-
kumbhaṃ sa-karakaṃ divyaṃ phala-karpūra-saṃyutam ।
nyased arcana-kāle tu kṛṣṇasyātīva vallabham ।।

iti

kiṃ ca-
sanīraṃ ca sa-karpūraṃ kumbhaṃ kṛṣṇāya yo nyaset ।
kalpaṃ tasya na pāpekṣāṃ kurvanti prapitāmahāḥ ।।

athārghyādi-pātrāṇi

prakṣiped arghya-pātre tu gandha-puṣpākṣatān yavān ।
kuśāgra-tila-dūrvāś ca siddhārthān api sādhakaḥ ।
kecic cātra jalādīni dravyāṇy aṣṭau vadanti hi ।।

yata uktaṃ bhaviṣye-
āpaḥ kṣīraṃ kuśāgrāṇi dadhy-akṣata-tilas tathā ।
yavāḥ siddhārthakāś caivam arghyo aṣṭāṅgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

pādya-pātre ca kamalaṃ dūrvā śyāmākam eva ca ।
nikṣiped viṣṇu-patrīṃ cety evaṃ dravya-catuṣṭayam ।।

tathaivācamanīyārthaṃ pātre dravya-trayaṃ budhaḥ ।
jātī-phalaṃ lavaṅgaṃ ca kakkolam api nikṣipet ।।

madhuparkīya-pātre ca gavyaṃ dadhi payo ghṛtam ।
madhu-khaṇḍam apīty evaṃ nikṣiped dravya-pañcakam ।।
kecit trīṇy eva pātre'smin dravyāṇīcchanti sādhavaḥ ।।
yata uktaṃ śrī-viṣṇu-dharme- ghṛtaṃ dadhi tathā kṣaudraṃ madhuparko vidhīyate ।।

ādi-vārāhe ca-
dadhi-sarpir madhu-samaṃ pātre auḍumbare mama ।
madhunas tu alābhe tu guḍena saha miśrayet ।।

ghṛtasyālābhe suśroṇi lājaiś ca saha miśrayet ।
tathā dadhno apy alābhe tu kṣīreṇa saha miśrayet ।।

teṣām abhāve puṣpādi tat-tad-bhāvanayā kṣipet ।
nāradas tv āha vimalenodakenaiva pūryate ।।

mūlena pātreṇaikena maṣṭakṛtvo abhimantrayet ।
kuryāc ca teṣāṃ pātrāṇāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ cakra-mudrayā ।।

pūjām ārabhamāṇo hi yathoktāsanam āsthitaḥ ।
paṭhen maṅgala-śāntiṃ tāṃ yārcane sammatā satām ।।

atha maṅgala-śāntiḥ

oṃ bhadraṃ karṇebhiḥ śṛṇuyāma devā
bhadraṃ paśyemākṣabhir yajatrā ।
sthirair aṅgais tuṣṭuvāṃsas tanubhir
vyaśema deva-hitaṃ yad āyuḥ ।।

svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ । svasti naḥ pūṣā viśvadevāḥ । svasti nas tārkṣo ariṣṭanemiḥ । svasti no bṛhaspatir dadhātu ।।

iti

paṭhan, oṃ śāntiḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa-pāda-padmārādhaneṣu śāntir bhavatu ।।

iti

atha vighna-nivāraṇam

apasarpantu te bhūtā ye bhūtā bhuvi saṃsthitāḥ ।
ye bhūtā vighna-kartāras te naśyantu śivājñayā ।।

ity udīryāstra-mantreṇa vāma-pādasya pārṣṇinā ।
ghātais tribhir budho vighnān bhaumān sarvān nivārayet ।।

āntarīkṣāṃś ca tenaivordhvordhva-tāla-trayeṇa hi ।
nirasyotsārayed divyān māntriko divya-dṛṣṭitaḥ ।।

śrī-gurv-ādi-natiḥ

tataḥ kṛtāñjalir vāme śrī-guruṃ paramaṃ gurum ।
parameṣṭhi-guruṃ ceti named guru-paramparām ।।

gaṇeśaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge durgām agre'tha pṛṣṭhataḥ ।
kṣetrapālaṃ named bhaktyā madhye cātmeṣṭa-daivatam ।।

tataś cāstreṇa saṃśodhya karau kurvīta tena hi ।
tāla-trayaṃ diśāṃ bandham agni-prākāram eva ca ।।

atha bhūta-śuddhiḥ

śarīrākāra-bhūtānāṃ bhūtānāṃ yad viśodhanam ।
avyaya-brahma-samparkād bhūta-śuddhir iyaṃ matā ।।

bhūta-śuddhiṃ vinā kartur japa-homādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।
bhavanti niṣphalāḥ sarvā yathā-vidhy apy aniṣṭhitāḥ ।।

tat-prakāraś ca

kara-kacchapikāṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ buddhyā hṛd-abjataḥ ।
śiraḥ-sahasra-patrābje paramātmani yojayet ।
pṛthivyādīni tattvāni tasmin līnāni bhāvayet ।।

vāma-hastaṃ tathottānam adho dakṣiṇa-bandhitam ।
kara-kacchapikā mudrā bhūta-śuddhau prakīrtitā ।।

dehaṃ saṃśoṣya dagdhvedam āplāvyāmṛta-varṣataḥ ।
utpādya draḍhayitvāsu-pratiṣṭhāṃ vidhinācaret ।।

ātmānam evaṃ saṃśodhya nītvā kṛṣṇārcanārhatām ।
vātsalyād dhṛd-gataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ yaṣṭuṃ hṛt punar ānayet ।।

tathā ca trailokya-saṃmohana-tantre-
nābhistha-vāyunā dehaṃ sa-pāpaṃ śodhayed budhaḥ ।
vahninā hṛdaya-sthena dahet tac ca kalevaram ।।

sahasrāre mahāpadme lalāṭa-sthe sthitaṃ vidhum ।
sampūrṇa-maṇḍalaṃ śuddhaṃ cintayed amṛtātmakam ।।

tasmād galita-dhārābhiḥ plāvayed bhasmasād budhaḥ ।
ābhir varṇamayībhiś ca pañca-bhūtātmakaṃ vapuḥ ।
pūrvavad bhāvayed devīm ।।

। ity ādi ।

kiṃ cāgre-
tatas tasmāt samākṛṣya praṇavena tu mantravit ।
tat tejo hṛdaye nyasya cintayed viṣṇum avyayam ।।

kiṃ vā cintana-mātreṇa bhūta-śuddhiṃ vidhāya tām ।
prāṇāyāmāṃś tataḥ kuryāt sampradāyānusarataḥ ।।

atha prāṇāyāmaḥ

recaḥ ṣoḍaśa-mātrābhiḥ pūro dvātriṃśatā bhavet ।
catuḥṣaṣṭhyā bhavet kumbha evaṃ syāt prāṇa-saṃyamaḥ ।।

virecya pavanaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃkocya guda-maṇḍalam ।
pūrayitvā vidhānena sva-śaktyā kumbhake sthitaḥ ।।

tatra praṇavam abhyasyan bījaṃ vā mantram ūrdhvagam ।
ṛṣy-ādi-smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā kuryād dhyānam atandritaḥ ।।

tad dhyānaṃ coktam- 
viṣṇuṃ bhāsvat-kirīṭāṅgada-valaya-kalā-kalpa-hārodarāṅghri-
śroṇībhūṣaṃ savakṣo-maṇi-makara-mahā-kuṇḍalāmṛṣṭa-gaṇḍam ।
hastodyac-chaṅkha-cakrāmbuja-gadam amalaṃ pīta-kauśeya-vāsaṃ
vidyotad-bhāsam udyad-dina-kara-sadṛśaṃ padma-saṃsthaṃ namāmi ।।

kvacic ca-
rudras tu recake brahmā pūrake dhyeya-devatā ।
śrī-viṣṇuḥ kumbhake jñeyo dhyāna-sthānaṃ guror mukhāt ।।

tathā hi-
nābhi-sthāne pūrakeṇa cintayet kamalāsanam ।
brahmāṇaṃ rakta-gaurāṅgaṃ caturvaktraṃ pitāmaham ।।

nīlotpala-dala-śyāmaṃ hṛdi madhye pratiṣṭhitam ।
caturbhujaṃ mahātmānaṃ kumbhakena tu cintayet ।।

recekanaiśvaraṃ dhyānaṃ lalāṭe sarva-pāpaham ।
śuddha-sphaṭika-saṅkāśaṃ kuryād vai nirmalaṃ budhaḥ ।।

iti

ekāntibhiś ca bhagavān sarva-deva-mayaḥ prabhuḥ ।
kṛṣṇaḥ priya-janopetaś cintanīyo hi sarvataḥ ।।

atha prāṇāyāma-māhātmyam

pādme devahūti-vikuṇḍala-saṃvāde-
yama-lokaṃ na paśyanti prāṇāyāma-parāyaṇāḥ ।
api duṣkṛta-karmāṇas tair eva hata-kilbiṣāḥ ।।

divase divase vaiśya prāṇāyāmās tu ṣoḍaśa ।
api brahma-haṇaṃ sākṣāt punanty ahar-ahaḥ kṛtāḥ ।।

tapāṃsi yāni tapyante vratāni niyamāś ca ye ।
go-sahasra-pradānaṃ ca prāṇāyāmas tu tat-samaḥ ।।

ambu-binduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māse māse naraḥ pibet ।
saṃvatsara-śataṃ sāgraṃ prāṇāyāmas tu tat-samaḥ ।।

pātakaṃ tu mahad yac ca tathā kṣudropapātakam ।
prāṇāyāmaiḥ kṣaṇāt sarvaṃ bhasmasāt kurute naraḥ ।।

iti

nyāsān vinā japaṃ prāhur āsuraṃ viphalaṃ budhāḥ ।
ato yathā-sampradāyaṃ nyāsān kuryād yathā-vidhi ।।

tatrādau mātṛkā-nyāsaḥ

ṛṣi-cchando-devatādi smṛtvādau mātṛkā-manoḥ ।
śiro-vaktra-hṛd-ādau ca nyasya tad-dhyānam ācaret ।।

tac coktam- 
pañcāśal-lipibhir vibhakta-mukha-doḥ-pan-madhya-vakṣaḥ-sthalīṃ
bhāvan-mauli-nibaddha-candra-śakalām āpīna-tuṅga-stanīm ।
mudrām akṣa-guṇaṃ sudhāḍhya-kalasaṃ vidyāṃ ca hastāmbujair
bibhrāṇāṃ viśada-prabhāṃ tri-nayanāṃ vāg-devatām āśraye ।।

akārādīn kṣa-kārāntān varṇānādau tu kevalān ।
lalāṭādiṣu cāṅgeṣu nyased vidvān yathā-kramam ।।

tac ca vivicyoktam-
lalāṭa-mukha-bimbākṣi-śruti-ghrāṇeṣu gaṇḍayoḥ ।
oṣṭha-dantottamāṅgāsye doḥ-pat-sandhyagrakeṣu ca ।।

pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhato nābhau jaṭhare hṛdaye'ṃsake ।
kakudyase ca hṛt-pūrvaṃ pāṇi-pāda-yuge tataḥ ।
jaṭharānanayor nyasen mātṛkārṇān yathā-kramam ।।

iti

sānusvārān visargāḍhyān sānusvāra-visargakān ।
nyased bhūyo api tān vidvān evaṃ vāra-catuṣṭayam ।।

atha mātṛkā-nyāsaḥ
