kaṇṭha-hṛn-nābhi-guhyeṣu pāyu-bhrū-mahdyayos tathā ।
sthite ṣoḍaśa-patrābje krameṇa dvādaśa-cchade ।।

daśa-patre ca ṣaṭ-patre catuṣpatre dvipatrake ।
nyased ekaika-patrānte sa-bindv-ekaikam akṣaram ।।

atha keśavādi-nyāsaḥ

smṛtvā ṛṣy-ādikāṃ varṇān mūrtibhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ ।
kīrtyādibhiḥ śaktibhiś ca nyaset tān pūrvavat kramāt ।।

nyasec caturthīn atyantā mūrtīḥ śaktīś ca yādibhiḥ ।
sapta-dhātūn prāṇa-jīvau krodham apy ātmane'ntakān ।।

tatra dhyānam

udyat-pradyotana-śata-ruciṃ tapta-hemāvadānaṃ
pārśva-dvandve jaladhi-sutayā viśva-dhātryā ca juṣṭam ।
nānā-ratnollasita-vividhākalpam āpīta-vastraṃ
viṣṇuṃ vande dara-kamala-kaumodakī-cakra-pāṇim ।।

atha śrī-mūrtayaḥ

prathamaṃ keśavo nārāyaṇaḥ paścāc ca mādhavaḥ ।
govindaś ca tathā viṣṇur madhusūdana eva ca ।।

trivikramo vāmano atha śrīdharaś ca tataḥ param ।
ṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhas tato dāmodaras tathā ।।

vāsudevaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ pradyumno athāniruddhakaḥ ।
cakrī gadī tathā śārṅgī khaḍgī śaṅkhī halī tathā ।।

muṣalī ca tathā śūlī pāśī caivāṅkuśī tathā ।
mukundo nandajaś caiva tathā nandī naras tathā ।।

narakajid dhariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ satyaḥ sātvata eva ca ।
tataḥ śauris tathā śūras tataḥ paścāj janārdanaḥ ।।

bhūdharo viśvamūrtiś ca vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।
balo balānujo bālo vṛṣaghno vṛṣa eva ca ।।
haṃso varāho vimalo nṛsiṃhaś ceti mūrtayaḥ ।।
atha śaktayaḥ

kīrtiḥ kāntis tuṣṭi-puṣṭī dhṛtiḥ śāntiḥ kriyā dayā ।
medhā harṣā tathā śraddhā lajjā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī ।।

prītī ratir jayā durgā prabhā satyā ca caṇḍikā ।
vāṇī vilāsinī caiva vijayā virajā tathā ।।

viśvā ca vinadā caiva sunandā ca smṛtis tathā ।
ṛddhiḥ samṛddhiḥ śuddhiś ca buddhir mūrtir natiḥ kṣamā ।।

ramomā kledinī klinnā vasudā vasudhā parā ।
parāyaṇā ca sūkṣmā ca sandhyā prajñā prabhā niśā ।।

amoghā vidyutety eka-pañcāśat śaktayo matāḥ ।
dadāty ayaṃ keśavādi-nyāso atrākhila-sampadam ।।
amutrācyuta-sārūpyaṃ nayati nyāsa-mātrataḥ ।।
tad uktaṃ- 
dhyātvaivaṃ parama-pumāṃsam akṣarair yo
vinyased dinam anu keśavādi-yuktaiḥ ।
medhāyuḥ-smṛti-dhṛti-kīrti-kānti-lakṣmī-
saubhāgyaiś ciram upabṛṃhito bhavet saḥ ।।

anyatra ca-
keśavādir ayaṃ nyāso nyāsa-mātreṇa dehinaḥ ।
acyutatvaṃ dadāty eva satyaṃ satyaṃna saṃśayaḥ ।।

iti

yaś ca kuryād imaṃ nyāsaṃ lakṣmī-bīja-puraḥsaram ।
bhaktiṃ muktiṃ ca bhuktiṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca labhate'cirāt ।।

tathā coktam- 
amum eva ramā-puraḥ-saraṃ
prabhajed yo manujo vidhiṃ budhaḥ ।
samupetya ramāṃ prathīyasīṃ
punar ante haritāṃ vrajaty asau ।।

atha tattva-nyāsaḥ

ma-kārādi-ka-kārānta-varṇair yuktaṃ sa-bindukaiḥ ।
namaḥ parāyeti pūrvam ātmane nama ity anu ।।

nāma jīvādi-tattvānāṃ nyaset tat-tat-pade kramāt ।
nyāsenānena loko hi bhavet pūjādhikāravān ।।

tatrādau sakale nyasej jīva-prāṇau kalevare ।
hṛdaye maty ahaṅkāra-manāṃsīti trayaṃ tataḥ ।।

śabdaṃ sparśaṃ tato rūpaṃ rasaṃ gandhaṃ ca mastake ।
mukhe hṛdi ca guhye ca pādayoś ca yathā-kramam ।।

śrotraṃ tvacaṃ dṛśaṃ jihvāṃ ghrāṇaṃ sva-sva-pade tataḥ ।
vāk-pāṇi-pāyūpasthāni sva-sva-pade tathā ।।

ākāśa-vāyu-tejāṃsi jalaṃ pṛthvīṃ ca mūrdhani ।
vadane hṛdaye liṅge pādayoś ca yathā-kramam ।।

hṛdi hṛt-puṇḍarīkaṃ ca dviṣaṭ-dvyaṣṭadaśādikam ।
kalā-vyāpteti pūrvaṃ ca sūrya-candrāgni-maṇḍalam ।
varṇaiḥ saha sarephaiś ca kramān nyaset sa-bindukaiḥ ।।

vāsudevaṃ ṣa-kāreṇa parameṣṭhi-yutaṃ ca ke ।
ya-kāreṇa mukhe saṅkarṣaṇaṃ nyaset pumanvitam ।।

hṛdi nyasel la-kāreṇa pradyumnaṃ viśva-saṃyutam ।
aniruddhaṃ nivṛtty-āḍhyaṃ va-kāreṇa ca guhyake ।
nārāyaṇaṃ ca sarvāḍhyaṃ la-kāreṇaiva pādayoḥ ।।

nṛsiṃhaṃ kopa-saṃyuktaṃ tad-bījenākhilātmani ।
tattva-nyāso ayam acirāt kṛṣṇa-sānnidhya-kārakaḥ ।।

tathā coktam-

atattva-vyāptya-rūpasya tat-prāpter hetunā punaḥ ।
tattva-nyāsam iti prāhur nyāsa-tattva-vido budhāḥ ।।

yaḥ kuryāt tattva-vinyāsaṃ sa pūto bhavati dhruvam ।
tad-ātmanānupraviśya bhagavān iha tiṣṭhati ।
yataḥ sa eva tattvāni sarvaṃ tasmin pratiṣṭhitam ।।

atha punaḥ prāṇāyāṃa-viśeṣaḥ

prāṇāyāmāṃs tataḥ kuryān mūla-mantraṃ japan kramāt ।
vārau dvau caturaḥ ṣaṭ ca reca-pūraka-kumbhakaḥ ।।

athavā recakādīṃs tān kuryād vārāṃs tu ṣoḍaśa ।
dvātriṃśac ca catuḥṣaṣṭhiṃ kāma-bījaṃ japan kramāt ।।

o)(o

tathā ca krama-dīpikāyām -

recayen mārutaṃ dakṣayā dakṣiṇaḥ
pūrayed vāmayā madhya-nāḍyā punaḥ ।
dhārayed īritaṃ recakādi-trayaṃ syāt
kalādanta-vidyākhya-mātrācyukam ।।

sanātanaḥ tad eva krama-dīpikoktyā saṃvādayan tatraiva kiṃcid viśeṣaṃ ca darśayati-recayed iti । dakṣayā dakṣiṇa-nāḍyā, dakṣiṇaḥ vidvān janaḥ । madhya-nāḍyā suṣumṇayā dhārayet । evaṃ recaka-pūraka-kumbhakākhyaṃ trayaṃ syāt । recakādiṣu triṣu krameṇāvadhikālam āha-kalāḥ ṣoḍaśa । dantā dvātriṃśat । vidyāś catuḥṣaṣṭhis tat-tat-saṅkhyaka-mātrātmakam ity arthaḥ । mātrā ca-vāmāṅguṣṭhena vāma-kaniṣṭhādy-aṅgulīnāṃ pratyekaṃ parva-traya-samparka-kālaḥ । vāma-hastena vāma-jānu-maṇḍalasya prādakṣiṇyena sparśa-kālo vā । tatrāpy aṅguli-niyamo apy uktaḥ- 
kaniṣṭhānāmikāṅguṣṭhair yan nāsā-puṭa-dhāraṇam ।
prāṇāyāmaḥ sa vijñeyas tarjanī-madhyame vinā ।।

iti
tatra teṣu prāṇāyāmeṣu purvaṃ recakādiṣu saṅkhyoktā । atra ca prāṇāyāmeṣv iti bhedaḥ hbhvc 
tatra kālaḥ saṅkhyādikaṃ ca

tatraiva - 
purato japasya parato api
vihitam atha tat-trayaṃ budhaiḥ ।
ṣoḍaśa ya iha samācared dineśaḥ
paripūyate sa khalu māsato aṃ haṃsaḥ ।।

sanātanaḥ japasya purata ādau parataḥ ante ca iti prāṇāyāmeṣu kālaḥ । tat trayaṃ prāṇāyāma-trayam iti saṅkhyā । yo jano dinaśaḥ pratyahaṃ ṣoḍaśa-prāṇāyāmān ācaret, sa māsataḥ māsenaikena aṃhasaḥ pāpāt paripūyate śuddho bhavatīti sāmānyataḥ phalam । paraṃ ca sarvaṃ purvaṃ likhitam eva hbhvc 

atha pīṭha-nyāsaḥ

tato nija-tanūm eva pūjā-pīṭhaṃ prakalpayet ।
pīṭhasyādhāra-śaktyādīn nyaset svāṅgeṣu tāravat ।।

ādhāra-śaktiṃ prakṛtiṃ kūrmānantau ca tatra tu ।
pṛthivīṃ kṣīra-sindhuṃ ca śvetadvīpaṃ ca bhāsvaram ।।

śrī-ratna-maṇḍapaṃ caiva kalpa-vṛkṣaṃ tathā hṛdi ।
nyaset pradakṣiṇatvena dharma-jñāne tato aṃsayoḥ ।।

ūrvor vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ tathaivādharmam ānane ।
trike'jñānam avairāgyam anaiśvaryaṃ ca pārśvayoḥ ।।

hṛd-abje'nanta-padmaṃ ca sūryendu-śikhinān tathā ।
maṇḍalāni kramād varṇaiḥ praṇavāṃśaiḥ sa-bindukaiḥ ।।

sattva rajas tamaś cātmāntarātmānau ca tatra hi ।
paramātmānam apy ātmādy-ādya-varṇaiḥ sa-bindukaiḥ ।।

jñānātmānaṃ ca bhuvaneśvarī-bījena saṃyutam ।
tasyāṣṭa-dikṣu madhye'pi nava-śaktīś ca dik-kramāt ।।

tāś coktāḥ-
vimalotkarṣiṇī jñānā kriyā yogeti śaktayaḥ ।
prahvī satyā tatheśānānugrahā navam smṛtā ।।

iti

nyaset tad-upariṣṭhāc ca pīṭha-mantraṃ yathoditam ।
ṛṣy-ādikaṃ smared asyāṣṭādaśārṇa-manos tataḥ ।।

jñeyāś caikāntibhiḥ kṣīra-samudrādi-catuṣṭayam ।
kramāc chrī-mathurā-vṛndāvanaṃ tat-kuñja-nīpakāḥ ।।

tato pīṭha-nyāsaḥ

tathā ca brahma-saṃhitāyām ādi-puruṣa-rahasya-stotre -

sa yatra kṣīrābdhiḥ sravati surabhībhyaś ca sumahān
nimeṣārdhākhyo vā vrajati na hi yatrāpi samayaḥ ।
bhaje śvetadvīpaṃ tam aham iha golokam iti yaṃ
vidantas te santaḥ kṣitiviralacārāḥ katipaye ।।

krama-dīpikāyāṃ -
evaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvānvitaś ca bhūtātmā ।
ṅe'ntāḥ sa-vāsudevāḥ sarvātma-yutaṃ ca saṃyogaṃ ।।

yogāvadhaś ca padmaṃ pīṭhāt ṅe-yuto natiś cānte ।
pīṭha-mahā-manur vyaktaḥ paryāpto ayaṃ saparyāsu ।।

sanātanaḥ tāraḥ praṇavaḥ । tato hṛdayaṃ nama iti padam । tataś ca bhagavān iti viṣṇur iti ca । sarvānvitaḥ sarva-śabda-yukto bhūtātmā sarva-bhūtātmeti । ete trayaḥ sa-vāsudevā vāsudeva-sahitāḥ pratyekaṃ ṅe'ntāś caturthy-antāḥ । tataś ca sarvātmanā yutaṃ saṃyogaṃ sarvātma-saṃyogam iti napuṃsakatvam ārṣam । tataś ca yogasyāvadhau ante padmaṃ yoga-padmam iti । tad-ante ṅe-yuktaś caturthy-antaḥ pīṭhātmā । tad-ante ca natiḥ namaḥ-śabdaḥ । evaṃ oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarva-bhūtātmane vāsudevāya sarvātma-saṃyoga-yoga-padma-pīṭhātmane nama iti siddham । tathā ca śāradā-tilake- 
namo bhagavate brūyād viṣṇave ca padaṃ vadet ।
sarva-bhūtātmane vāsudevāyeti vadet tataḥ ।।

sarvātma-saṃyoga-padād yoga-padma-padaṃ punaḥ ।
pīṭhātmane hṛd-anto ayaṃ mantras tārādir īritaḥ ।।

iti

sanat-kumāra-kalpe ca-
oṃ namaḥ padam ābhāṣya tathā bhagavate-padam ।
vāsudevāya ity uktvā sarvātmeti padaṃ tathā ।।

saṃyoga-yogety uktvā ca tathā pīṭhātmane padam ।
vahni-patnī-samāyuktaḥ pīṭha-mantra itīritaḥ ।।

iti ।।

atha ṛṣy-ādi-smaraṇam
oṃ aṣṭādaśākṣara-mantrasya śrī-nārada ṛṣir gāyatrī-cchandaḥ, sakala-loka-maṅgalo nanda-tanayo devatā, hrīṃ bījaṃ, svāhā śaktiḥ, kṛṣṇaḥ prakṛtir, durgādhiṣṭhātrī devatā, abhimatārthe viniyogaḥ ।।
tathā ca saṃmohana-tantre śivomā-saṃvāde-
ṛṣir nārada ity ukto gāyatrī-cchanda ucyate ।
gopa-veśa-dharaḥ kṛṣṇo devatā parikīrtitaḥ ।।

bījaṃ manmatha-saṃjñaṃ tu priyā śaktir havir bhujaḥ ।
tvam eva parameśāni asyādhiṣṭhātṛ-devatā ।
caturvarga-phalāvāptyai viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

athāṅga-nyāsaḥ

catuś caturbhir varṇaiś ca catvāry aṅgāni kalpayet ।
dvābhyām astrākhyam aṅgaṃ ca tasyety aṅgāni pañca vai ।।

nyasyec ca vyāpakatvena tāny aṅgāni kara-dvaye ।
tāny aṅgulīṣu pañcātha kecid varṇān svarān api ।।

te coktāḥ-
drāvaṇa-kṣobhaṇākarṣa-vaśīkṛt-srāvaṇās tathā ।
śoṣaṇo mohanaḥ sandīpanas tāpana-mādanau ।।

iti

kiṃ ca-
namo antaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāṅgaiḥ śiraḥ svāhānvitaṃ śikhām ।
vaṣaḍ-yutaṃ ca kavacaṃ huṃ-yug-astraṃ ca phaḍ-yutam ।।

nyasyanti punar aṅguṣṭhau tarjanyau madhyame tathā ।
anāmike kaniṣṭhe ca kramād aṅgaiś ca pañcabhiḥ ।।

punaś ca hṛdayādīni tathāṅguṣṭhādikāni ca ।
nyasyanti yugapat sarvāṇy aṅgais taiḥ pañcabhiḥ kramāt ।।

nyasyanti ca ṣaḍ-aṅgāni hṛdayādīni tan-manoḥ ।
hṛdayādiṣu caiteṣāṃ pañcaikaṃ dikṣu ca kramāt ।।

ṣaḍ-aṅgāni coktāni sammohana-tantre sanat-kumāra-kalpe-
varrṇenaikena hṛdayaṃ tirbhir eva śiro matam ।
caturbhiś ca śikhā proktā tathaiva kavacaṃ matam ।
netraṃ tathā caturvarṇair astraṃ dvābhyāṃ tathā matam ।।

iti

tataś cāpādam ākeśān nyased dorbhyām imaṃ manum ।
vārāṃs trīn vyāpakatvena nyasec ca praṇavaṃ sakṛt ।।

athākṣara-nyāsaḥ

tato aṣṭādaśa-varṇāṃś ca mantrasyāsya yathā-kramam ।
dante lalāṭe bhrū-madhye karṇayor netrayor dvayoḥ ।।

nāsayor vadane kaṇṭhe hṛdi nābhau kaṭi-dvaye ।
guhye jānu-dvaye caikaṃ nyased ekaṃ ca pādayoḥ ।।

santo nyasyanti tārādi-namo anantāṃs tān sa-bindukān ।
śrī-śakti-kāma-bījaiś ca sṛṣṭy-ādi-kramato apare ।।

atha pada-nyāsaḥ
tāraṃ śirasi vinyasya pañca mantra-padāni ca ।
nyasen netra-dvaye vaktre hṛd-guhyāṅghriṣu ca kramāt ।।

dehe ca vyāpakatvena nyaset tāny akhile punaḥ ।
kecit tāni namo antāni nyasyanty ādyākṣaraiḥ saha ।।

svāhāntāni tathā trīṇi saṃmiśrāṇy uttarottaraiḥ ।
guhyād galān mastakāc ca vyāpayya caraṇāvadhi ।।

nyāso atra jñāna-niṣṭhānāṃ guhyādi-viṣayas tu yaḥ ।
sva-sva-varṇa-tanoḥ kāryas tat-tad-varṇeṣu vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।।

atha ṛṣy-ādi-nyāsaḥ

ṛṣy-ādīn sapta-bhāgāṃś ca nyased asya manoḥ kramāt ।
mūrdhāsya-hṛtsu kucayoḥ punar hṛdi punar hṛdi ।।

atha mudrā-pañcakam

veṇv-ākhyāṃ vana-mālākhyāṃ mudrāṃ sandarśayet tataḥ ।
śrī-vatsākhyāṃ kaustubhākhyāṃ blivākhyāṃ ca manoramām ।।

itthaṃ naysta-śarīraḥ san kṛtvā dig-bandhanaṃ punaḥ ।
kara-kacchapikāṃ kṛtvā dhāyec chrī-nanda-nandanam ।।

atha śrī-nandandana-bhagavad-dhyāna-vidhiḥ

[krama-dīpikā ]

atha prakaṭa-saurabhodgalita-mādhvikotphulla-sat-
prasūna-nava-pallava-prakara-namra-śākhair drumaiḥ ।
praphulla-nava-mañjarī-lalita-vallarī-veṣṭitaiḥ
smarec chiśiritaṃ śivaṃ sita-matis tu vṛndāvanam ।।

athānantaraṃ sita-matiḥ śuddha-manāḥ san vṛndāvanaṃ cintayet । kīdṛśaṃ ? drumaiḥ śiśiritaṃ śītalī-kṛtam । kīdṛśaiḥ ? prakaṭam udbhaṭaṃ saurabhaṃ yasya tac ca । tad udgalita-mādhvīkaṃ ca pracyuta-madhu । utphullaṃ ca vikasitaṃ । sac ca uttamaṃ yat prasūnaṃ puṣpaṃ nava-pallavaṃ ca । tayoḥ prakaraḥ samūhaḥ । tena namrāḥ śākhā yeṣāṃ taiḥ । mādhviketi-hrasvatvaṃ mahā-kavi-nibaddhatvāt soḍhavyam । prakaṭa-saurabhākulita-matta-bhṛṅgollasad iti pāṭhas tu sugama eva । punaḥ kīdṛśaiḥ ? praphullābhir nava-mañjarībhir lalitā manoharā yā vallaryaḥ agra-śākhā latā vā, tabhir veṣṭitaiḥ । śivaṃ maṅgala-rūpaṃ, nirbādhatvāt parama-kalyāṇa-karatvāc ca hbhvc 

vikāsi-sumanorasāsvādana-mañjulaiḥ sañcarac-
chilīmukha-mukhodgatair mukharitāntaraṃ jhaṅkṛtaiḥ ।
kapota-śuka-śārikā-parabhṛtādibhiḥ patribhir
virāṇitam itas tato bhujaga-śatru-nṛtyākulam ।।

kalinda-duhituś calal-lahari-vipruṣāṃ vāhibhir
vinidra-sarasī-ruhodara-rajaś-cayoddhūsaraiḥ ।
pradīpita-manobhava-vraja-vilāsinī-vāsasāṃ
vilolana-vihāribhiḥ satata-sevitaṃ mārutaiḥ ।।

pravāla-nava-pallavaṃ marakata-cchadaṃ vajra-mauktika- prakara-korakaṃ kamala-rāga-nānā-phalam । sthaviṣṭham akhila-rtubhiḥ satata-sevitaṃ kāmadaṃ tad-antar api kalpakāṅghripam udañcitaṃ cintayet ।।

suhema-śikharāvaler udita-bhānuvad bhāsvaram
adho asya kanaka-sthalīm amṛta-śīkarāsāriṇaḥ ।
pradīpta-maṇi-kuṭṭimāṃ kusuma-reṇu-puñjojjvalāṃ
smaret punar atandrito vigata-ṣaṭ-taraṅgāṃ budhaḥ ।।

tad-ratna-kuṭṭima-niviṣṭa-mahiṣṭha-yoga-
pīṭhe'ṣṭa-patram araṇaṃ kamalaṃ vicintya ।
udyad-virocana-sarocir amuṣya madhye
sañcintayet ssukha-niviṣṭam atho mukundam ।।

sūtrāmaratna-dalitāñjana-megha-puñja-
pratyagra-nīla-jalajanma-samāna-bhāsam ।
susnigdha-nīla-ghana-kuñcita-keśa-jālaṃ
rājan-manojña-śiti-kaṇṭha-śikhaṇḍa-cūḍam ।।

rolamba-lālita-sura-druma-sūna-kalpi-
tottaṃsam utkaca-navotpala-karṇa-pūram ।
lolālaka-sphurita-bhāla-tala-pradīpta-
gorocanā-tilakam uccala-cilli-mālam ।।

āpūrṇa-śārada-gatāṅka-śaśāṅka-bimba-
kāntānanaṃ kamala-patra-viśāla-netram ।
ratna-sphuran-makara-kuṇḍala-raśmi-dīpta-
gaṇḍa-sthalī-mukuram unnata-cāru-nāsam ।।

sindūra-sundaratarādharam indu-kunda-
mandāra-manda-hasita-dyuti-dīpitāṅgam ।
vanya-pravāla-kusuma-pracayāvakpta-
graiveyakojjvala-manohara-kambu-kaṣṭham ।।

matta-bhramad-bhramara-juṣṭa-vilambamāna-
santānaka-prasava-dāma-pariṣkṛtāṃsam ।
hārāvalī-bhagaṇa-rājita-pīvaroro-
vyoma-sthalī-lalita-kaustubha-bhānumantam ।।

śrīvatsa-lakṣaṇa-sulakṣitam unnatāṃsa-
ājānu-pīna-parivṛtta-sujāta-bāhum ।
ābandhurodaram udāra-gabhīra-nābhiṃ
bhṛṅgāṅganānikara-vañjula-roma-rājim ।।

nānā-maṇi-praghaṭitāṅgada-kaṅkaṇormi-
graiveya-sāra-sana-nūpura-tunda-bandham ।
divyāṅga-rāga-paripiñjaritāṅga-yaṣṭi-
māpīta-vastra-parivīta-nitamba-bimbam ।।

cārūrujānu-manuvṛtta-manojña-jaṅghaṃ
kāntonnata-prapada-nindita-kūrma-kāntim ।
māṇikya-darāṇa-lasan-nakharājirāja-
dratnāṅguli-cchadana-sundara-pāda-padmam ।।

matsyāṅkuśāradara-ketu-yavābja-vajra-
saṃlakṣitāruṇa-karāṅghri-talābhirāmam ।
lāvaṇya-sāra-samudāya-vinirmitāṅga-
saundarya-nirjita-manobhava-deha-kāntim ।।

āsyāravinda-paripūrita-veṇu-randhra-
lolat-karāṅguli-samīrita-divya-rāgaiḥ ।
śaśvad-ddravīkṛta-vikṛṣṭa-samasta-jantu-
santāna-santatim ananta-sukhāmbu-rāśim ।।

gobhir mukhāmbuja-vilīna-vilocanābhi-
rūdhobhara-skhalita-manthara-mandagābhiḥ ।
dantāgra-daṣṭa-pariśiṣṭa-tṛṇāṅkurābhi-
rālamb-vāladhi-latābhivītam ।।

saprasravastana-vicūṣaṇa-pūrṇa-niśca-
lāsyāvaṭakṣarita-phenila-dugdha-mugdhaiḥ ।
veṇu-pravartita-manohara-mandragīta-
dattocca-karṇa-yugalair api tarṇakaiś ca ।।

pratyagra-śṛṅga-mṛdu-mastaka-samprahāra-
saṃrambha-valgana-vilola-khurāgra-pātaiḥ ।
āmedurair bahula-sāsna-galair udagra-
pucchaiś ca vatsatara-vatsatarī-nikāyaiḥ ।।

hambā-rava-kṣubhita-dig-valayair mahadbhi-
rapy ukṣabhiḥ pṛthu-kakudbhara-bhāra-khinnaiḥ ।
uttambhita-śruti-puṭī-parivīta-vaṃśa-
dhvānāmṛtoddhata-vikāśi-viśāla-ghoṇaiḥ ।।

gopaiḥ samāna-guṇa-śīla-vayo-vilāsa-
veśaiś ca mūrcchita-kala-svana-veṇu-vīṇaiḥ ।
mandroccatāra-paṭa-gāna-parair vilola-
dor-vallarī-lalita-lāsya-vidhāna-dakṣaiḥ ।।

jaṅghānta-pīvara-kaṭīra-taṭī-nibaddha-
vyālola-kiṅkiṇi-ghaṭāraṭitair aṭadbhiḥ ।
mugdhais tarakṣu-nakha-kalpita-kaṇṭha-bhūṣai-
ravyakta-mañju-vacanaiḥ pṛthukaiḥ parītam ।।

atha sulalita-gopa-sundarīṇāṃ
pṛthu-nivivīṣa-nitamba-mantharāṇām ।
guru-kuca-bhara-bhaṅgurāvalagna-
trivali-vijṛmbhita-roma-rāji-bhājām ।।

tad-atimadhura-cāru-veṇu-vādyā-
mṛta-rasa-pallavitāṅgajāṅghripāṇām ।
mukula-visara-ramya-rūḍha-romo-
dgama-samalaṅkṛta-gāna-vallarīṇām ।।

tad-atirucira-manda-hāsa-candrā-
tapa-parijṛmbhita-rāga-vāri-rāśeḥ ।
taralatara-taraṅga-bhaṅga-vipruṭ-
prakara-sama-śrama-bindu-santatānām ।।

tad-atilalita-manda-cilli-cāpa-
cyuta-niśitekṣaṇa-māra-bāṇa-vṛṣṭyā ।
dalita-sakala-marma-vihvalāṅga-
pravisṛta-duḥsaha-vepathu-vyathānām ।।

tad-atisubhaga-kamra-rūpa-śobhā-
mṛta-rasa-pāna-vidhāna-lālasābhyām ।
praṇaya-salila-pūra-vāhinīnā-
malasa-vilola-vilocanāmbujābhyām ।।

visraṃsat-kavarī-kalāpa-vigalat-phulla-prasūna-srava-
n-mādhvī-lampaṭa-cañcarīka-ghaṭayā saṃsevitānāṃ muhuḥ ।
māronmāda-mada-skhalan-mṛdu-girām ālola-kāñcy-ucchvasa-
nnīvī-viślatha-māna-cīna-hicayāntāvir-nitamba-tviṣām ।।

skhalita-lalita-pādāmbhoja-mandābhidhāna-
kvaṇita-maṇi-tulākoṭy-ākulāśāmukhānām ।
calad-adhara-dalānāṃ kuṭ-nala-pakṣmalākṣi-
dvaya-sarasiruhāṇām ullasat-kuṇḍalānām ।।
skhalitasya skhalana-yuktasya lalitasya ca pādāmbhojasya mandābhighātena īṣad bhū-bhāgaa-prahāreṇa kvaṇitaḥ kṛta-śabdo maṇi-mayo yas tulākoṭir nūpuraṃ, tenākulaṃ śabda-vyāptam āśānāṃ diśāṃ mukhaṃ yābhyas tāsām । kuḍmalat mukulāyamānaṃ pakṣmalaṃ ca utkṛṣṭa-pakṣma-yuktam akṣi-dvaya-sarasi-ruhaṃ yāsām hbhvc 
drāghiṣṭha-śvasana-samīraṇābhitāpa-
pramlānībhavad-aruṇoṣṭha-pallavānām ।
nānopāyana-vilasat-karāmbujānā-
mālībhiḥ satata-niṣevitaṃ samantāt ।।

drāghiṣṭho atidīrghaḥ śvāsana-samīraṇaḥ śvāsa-vāyus tena abhitāpaḥ santāpas tena pramlānī-bhavan aruṇoṣṭha-pallavo yāsām hbhvc 

tāsām āyata-lola-nīla-nayana-vyākoṣa-nīlāmbuja-
sragbhiḥ samparipūjitākhila-tanuṃ nānā-vinodāspadam ।
tan-mugdhānana-paṅkaja-pravigalan-mādhvī-rasāsvādinīṃ
vibhrāṇaṃ praṇayonmadākṣi-madhu-kṛn-mālāṃ manohāriṇīm ।।

vyākośaṃ vikasitaṃ, praṇayād unmade udgata-made akṣiṇī eva madhu-kṛn-mālā bhramara-paṅktiḥ । tāṃ bibhrāṇam prakaṭayantam । śrī-locanayor itas tato bahudhā nipatanena sarvato darśanān mālety uktam । kīdṛśīm ? tāsāṃ yan mugdhaṃ manoharam ānana-paṅkajaṃ । tasmāt pravigalito mādhvī-rasasya makarandasya āsvādana- śīlām । ata eva manohāriṇīṃ hbhvc 

gopa-gopī-paśūnāṃ bahiḥ smared
agrato asya gīrvāṇa-ghaṭām ।
vittārthinīṃ viriñci-trinayana-
śatamanyu-pūrvikāṃ stotra-parām ।।
idānīṃ krameṇa vitta-dharma-mokṣa-kāmākhya-puruṣārthacatuṣṭayasya tathā sarvataḥ śreṣṭhasya pañcama-puruṣārtha-rūpāyā bhakteś ca vāñchāyāḥ pradānāṃ devādīnāṃ dhyānam āha-gopeti pañcabhiḥ । asya kṛṣṇasya agrataḥ sammukhe hbhvc 
tad-dakṣiṇato muni-nikaraṃ
dṛḍha-dharma-vāñcham ānāya-param ।
yogīndrān atha pṛṣṭhe mumukṣa-
māṇān samādhinā sanakādyān ।।
dakṣiṇe cāsya muni-nikaraṃ smaret । dṛḍhā dharme vāñchā yasya tam hbhvc 
savye sakāntān atha yakṣa-siddha-
gandharva-vidyādhara-cāraṇāṃś ca ।
sa-kinnarān apsarasaś ca mukhyāḥ
kāmārthino nartana-gīta-vādyaiḥ ।।

sa-kāntān patnī-sahitān yakṣādīṃś ca smaret । katham-bhūtān ? nartanādyaiḥ kāmārthino nija-nijābhīṣṭa-prārthakān । mukhyāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ urvaśy-ādyā apsarasaś ca smaret hbhvc 

śaṅkhendu-kunda-dhavalaṃ sakalāgama-jñaṃ
saudāmanī-tati-piṅga-jaṭā-kalāpam ।
tat-pāda-paṅkaja-gatām acalāṃ ca bhaktiṃ
vāñchantam ujjhitatarānya-samasta-saṅgam ।।
tasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya pāda-paṅka-jagatāṃ tad-viṣayiṇīm ity arthaḥ । ujjhitataro nitarāṃ parityakto anyasmin bhakti-vyatirikte samaste saṅga āsaktir yena tam hbhvc 
nānā-vidha-śruti-gaṇānvita-sapta-rāga-
grāma-trayī-gata-manohara-mūrchanābhiḥ ।
samprīṇayantam uditābhir amuṃ mahatyā
sañcintayen nabhasi dhātṛ-sutaṃ munīndram ।।

ata eva amuṃ śrī-kṛṣṇaṃ mahatyākhyayā kacchapikayā svakīya-vīṇayā prīṇayantam । kābhiḥ ? nānā-vidhaḥ ṣaṭ-triṃśad-bhedātmako yaḥ śruti-gaṇo nāda-samūhas tenānvitā ye sapta rāgāḥ niṣādādi-svarā meghanāda-vasantādi-rāgā vā, teṣu vā grāma-trayī tatra grāmāṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ samāhāras tasyāṃ gatāḥ prāptā yā manoharā mūrchanās tābhiḥ । kimbhūtābhiḥ ? uditābhiḥ svayam eva prākaṭyaṃ prāptābhiḥ । mahatyoditābhir iti vā sambandhaḥ । ata eva munīndraṃ muni-gaṇa-śreṣṭhaṃ dhātṛ-sutaṃ śrī-nāradaṃ nabhasi samyak cintayet hbhvc 

śrī-gautamīya-tantre-
atha dhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarva-pāpa-praṇāśanam ।
pītāmbara-dharaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ puṇḍarīka-nibhekṣaṇam ।।

rakta-netrādharaṃ rakta-pāṇa-pāda-nakhaṃ śubham ।
kaustubhodbhāsitoraskaṃ nānā-ratna-vibhūṣitam ।।

tad-dhāma-vilasan-muktā-baddha-hāropaśobhitam ।
nānā-ratna-prabhodbhāsi-mukuṭaṃ divya-tejasam ।।

hara-keyūra-kaṭaka-kuṇḍalaiḥ parimaṇḍitam ।
śrīvatsa-vakṣasaṃ cāru-nūpurādy-upaśobhitam ।।

nānā-ratna-vicitraiś ca kaṭi-sūtrāṅgulīyakaiḥ ।
barhi-patra-kṛtāpīḍaṃ vanya-puṣpair alaṅkṛtam ।।

kadamba-kusumodbaddha-vana-mālā-vibhūṣitam ।
sa-candra-tārakānandi-vimalāmbara-sannibham ।।

veṇuṃ gṛhītvā hastābhyāṃ mukhe saṃyojya saṃsthitam ।
gāyantaṃ divya-gānaiś ca goṣṭha-madhya-gataṃ harim ।।

svargād iva paribhraṣṭa-kanyakā-śata-veṣṭitam ।
sarva-lakṣaṇa-sampannaṃ saundaryeṇābhiśobhitam ।।

śubhaṃ jagan-maṅgala-rūpaṃ, tasya kaustubhasya dhāmnā tejasā vilasantībhir muktābhir ācchannena saṃveṣṭitena hāreṇa upaśobhitam । muktā-baddheti vā pāṭhaḥ । kaṭi-sūtreṇāṅgulīyakaiś cālaṅkṛtam । sa-candrābhis tārābhir ānandaṃ sukha-karaṃ yad vimalam ambaraṃ vyoma tat sadṛśam । atra candra-sthāne kaustubhaḥ । tārā-sthāne kadamba-mālā । ambara-sthāne śrīmad-vakṣaḥ-sthalam ūhyam । svargād iva paribhraṣṭānāṃ parama-sundarīṇām ity arthaḥ । tadṛśīnāṃ kanyānāṃ śrī-gopa-kumārīṇāṃ śatena veṣṭitam । śata-śabdo atrāsaṅkhyatve hbhvc 

mohanaṃ sarva-gopīnāṃ sarvāsāṃ ca gavām api ।
lelihyamānaṃ vatsaiś ca dhenubhiś ca samantataḥ ।।

siddha-gandharva-yakṣaiś ca apsarobhir vihaṅgamaiḥ ।
surāsura-manuṣyaiś ca sthāvaraiḥ pannagair api ।।

mṛgair vidyādharaiś caiva vīkṣyamāṇaṃ suvismitaiḥ ।
nāradena vaśiṣṭhena viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā ।।

parāśareṇa vyāsena bhṛguṇāṅgirasā tathā ।
dakṣeṇa śaunakātribhyāṃ siddhena kapilena ca ।।

sanakādyir munīndraiś ca brahma-loka-gatair api ।
anyair api ca saṃyuktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyed aharniśam ।।

saṅkṣepeṇa śrī-sanat-kumāra-kalpe'pi- 
avyān mīlat-kalāya-dyutir ahi-ripu-picchollasat keśa-jālo
gopī-netrotsavārādhita-lalita-vapur gopa-go-vṛnda-vītaḥ ।
śrīmad-vaktrāravinda-pratisahit-śaśāṅkākṛtiḥ pīta-vāsā
devo asau veṇu-nāda-kṣapita-jana-dhṛtir devakī-nandano naḥ ।।

iti
asau anirvacanīya-māhātmyaḥ śrī-devakī-nandano devo naḥ asmān avyāt rakṣatu । kalāyasya tat-puṣpasyeva dyutiḥ śyāmā kāntir yasya saḥ hbhvc 
athāntar-yāgaḥ

dhyātvaivaṃ bhagavantaṃ taṃ samprārthya ca yathā-sukham ।
ādau sampūjayet sarvair upacāraiś ca mānasaiḥ ।।

lekhyā ye bahir arcayām upacārā vibhāgaśaḥ ।
te sarve'py antar-arcāyāṃ kalpanīyā yathā-ruci ।।

atha prārthanā-vidhiḥ

śrī-nārada-pañcarātre-
svāgataṃ deva-deveśa sannidhau bhava keśava ।
gṛhāṇa mānasīṃ pūjāṃ yathārtha-paribhāvinām ।।

iti

athopacārair bāhyaiś ca svātmany eva sthitaṃ prabhum ।
pūjayan sthāpayed ādau śaṅkhaṃ sat-sampradāyataḥ ।।

atha śaṅkha-pratiṣṭhā

svasya vāmāgrato bhūmāv ullikhya try-asra-maṇḍalam ।
tatāstra-kṣālitaṃ śaṅkhaṃ sādhāraṃ sthāpayed budhaḥ ।।

śaṅkhe hṛdaya-mantreṇa gandha-puṣpākṣatān kṣipet ।
vyutkrāntair mātṛkārṇais taṃ śiro antaiḥ kena pūrayet ।।

sa-bindunā ma-kāreṇa tad-ādhāre'gni-maṇḍalam ।
sampūjayed a-kāreṇa śaṅkhe cāditya-maṇḍalam ।।

u-kāreṇa jale soma-maṇḍalaṃ ca tathārcayet ।
tīrtha-mantreṇa tīrthāny āvāhayec cārka-maṇḍalam ।।

kṛṣṇaṃ cāvāhya hṛt-padmād gālinīṃ śikhayekṣayet ।
netra-mantreṇa vīkṣyāntaḥ kavacenāvaguṇṭhaet ।।

kuryān nyāsaṃ jale mūla-mantrāṅgānāṃ tato diśaḥ ।
baddhvāstreṇāmṛtīkuṛyād atha tad-dhenu-mudrayā ।।

tac cakra-mudrayā rakṣya salilaṃ matsya-mudrayā ।
ācchādya saṃspṛśan śaṅkhaṃ japen mūlaṃ tato aṣṭaśaḥ ।।

taj jalaṃ prokṣaṇī-pātre kiṃcit kṣiptvā trir ukṣayet ।
tac-cheṣeṇārcana-dravya-jātāni sva-tanūm api ।।

kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhakau saktau karayor itaretaram ।
tarjanī-madhyamānāmāḥ saṃhatā bhugna-sajjitāḥ ।
mudraiṣā gālinī proktā śaṅkhasyopari cālitā ।।

tato apāsyāvaśiṣṭāntaḥ śaṅkhaṃ vardhanikāmbunā ।
punar āpūrya kṛṣṇāgre nyased ācārataḥ satām ।।

atha sva-dehe pīṭha-pūjā

gurūn mūrdhni gaṇeśaṃ ca mūlādhāre'bhipūjya tam ।
pīṭha-nyāsānusāreṇa pīṭhaṃ cātmani pūjayet ।।

atha devāṅgeṣu mantrāṅgādi-nyāsaḥ

tato japan kāma-bījaṃ tri-sthāna-sthaṃ paraṃ mahaḥ ।
mūla-mantrātmakaṃ bījenaikībhūtaṃ vicintayet ।।

tac ca pañcāṅga-nyāsena sākāraṃ sveṣṭa-daivatam ।
vicintya pañcāṅgādīni nyasyet tasmin yathātmani ।।

kuryur bhagavati prādurbhūte kṛṣṇe ca vaiṣṇavāḥ ।
tat-tan-nyāsān abhedāya manor bhagavatā saha ।।

kecin nyasyanti tattvādīnn avyaktāni yathoditam ।
mantrārṇaiḥ svara-haṃsādyair bhūṣaṇeṣu prabhoḥ kramāt ।।

atha bāhyopacārair antaḥ-pūjā

tasmin pīṭhe tam āsīnaṃ bhagavantaṃ vibhāvayan ।
āsanādyais tu puṣpāntair yathā-vidhy arcayed budhaḥ ।।

tato mukhe'rcayed veṇuṃ vanamālāṃ ca vakṣasi ।
dakṣastanordhve śrīvatsaṃ savye tatraiva kaustubham ।।

vaiṣṇavaś candanenāmum ālipyopaka-niṣṭhayā ।
prāgvad dīpa-śikhākāra-tilakāni dviṣaḍ likhet ।।

yathoktaṃ pañcabhiḥ puṣpāñjalibhiś cābhipūjya tam ।
dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ ca naivedyaṃ mukha-vāsādi cārpayet ।।

gītādibhiś ca santoṣya kṛṣṇam asmai tato akhilam ।
aśakto bahir arcāyām arpayej japam ācaret ।।

athāntar-yāga-māhātmyam

vaiṣṇava-tantre-
aśvamedha-sahasrāṇi vājapeya-śatāni ca ।
ekasya dhyāna-yogasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye śrī-vāmana-prādurbhāve-
yan-nāmoccāraṇād eva sarve naśyanty upadravāḥ ।
stotrair vā arhaṇābhir vā kim u dhyānena kathyate ।।

nārada-pañcarātre śrī-bhagavan-nārada-saṃvāde-
ayaṃ yo mānaso yāgo jarā-vyādhi-bhayāpahaḥ ।
sarva-pāpaugha-śamano bhāvābhāva-karo dvija ।
satatābhyāsa-yogena deha-bandhād vimocayet ।।

yaś caivaṃ parayā bhaktyā sakṛt kuryān mahāmate ।
kramoditena vidhinā tasya tuṣyāmy ahaṃ mune ।।

smaraṇa-dhyānayoḥ pūrvaṃ māhātmyaṃ likhitaṃ ca yat ।
jñeyaṃ tad-adhikaṃ cātrāntaryāgāṅgatayā tayoḥ ।।

evaṃ yathā-sampradāyaṃ śaktyā yāvan-manaḥ-sukham ।
antaḥ-pūjāṃ vidhāyādāv ārabheta bahis tataḥ ।।

tathā coktaṃ nāradena-
dhyātvā ṣoḍaśa-saṅkhyātair upacāraiś ca mānasaiḥ ।
samyag ārādhanaṃ kṛtvā bāhya-pūjāṃ samācaret ।।

atha bahiḥ-pūjā
anujñāṃ dehi bhagavan bahir yoge mama prabho ।
śrī-kṛṣṇam ity anujñāpya bahiḥ pūjāṃ samācaret ।।

tatra tv anekaśaḥ santi pūjā-sthānāni tatra ca ।
śrī-mūrtayo bahu-vidhāḥ śālagrāma-śilās tathā ।।

atha pūjā-sthānāni

saṃmohana-tantre-
śālagrāme manau yantre sthaṇḍile pratimādiṣu ।
hareḥ pūjā tu kartavyā kevale bhūtale na tu ।।

ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] śrīmad-uddhava-saṃvāde-
sūryo agnir brāhmaṇā gāvo vaiṣṇavaḥ khaṃ maruj jalam ।
bhūr ātmā sarva-bhūtāni bhadra pūjā-padāni me ।।

sūrye tu vidyayā trayyā haviṣāgnau yajeta mām ।
ātithyena tu viprāgrye goṣv aṅga yavasādinā ।।

vaiṣṇave bandhu-sat-kṛtyā hṛdi khe dhyāna-niṣṭhayā ।
vāyau mukhya-dhiyā toye dravyais toya-puraḥ-saraiḥ ।।

sthaṇḍile mantra-hṛdayair bhogair ātmānam ātmani ।
kṣetra-jñaṃ sarva-bhūteṣu samatvena yajeta mām ।।

dhiṣṇyeṣv ity eṣu mad-rūpaṃ śaṅkha-cakra-gadāmbujaiḥ ।
yuktaṃ catur-bhujaṃ śāntaṃ dhyāyann arcet samāhitaḥ ।।

atha śrī-mūrtayaḥ

tatraiva [bhp ]-
śailī dārumayī lauhī lepyā lekhyā ca saikatī ।
manomayī maṇimayī pratimāṣṭa-vidhā matā ।।

calācaleti dvi-vidhā pratiṣṭhā jīva-mandiram ।
udvāsāvāhane na staḥ sthirāyām uddhavārcane ।।

asthirāyāṃ vikalpaḥ syāt sthaṇḍile tu bhaved dvayam ।
snapanaṃ tv avilepyāyām anyatra parimārjanam ।।

gopāla-mantroddiṣṭatvāt tac-chrī-mūrtir apekṣitā ।
tathāpi vaiṣṇava-prītyai lekhyāḥ śrī-mūrtayo akhilāḥ ।।

atha śrī-mūrti-lakṣaṇāni

śrī-hayaśīrṣa-pañcarātre śrī-bhagavat-śrī-hayaśīrṣa-brahma-saṃvāde-
ādi-mūrtir vāsudevaḥ saṅkarṣaṇam athāsṛjat ।
caturmūrtiḥ paraṃ proktaṃ ekaiko bhidyate tridhā ।
keśavādi-prabhedena mūrti-dvādaśakaṃ smṛtam ।।

paṅkajaṃ dakṣiṇe dadyāt pāñcajanyaṃ tathopari ।
vāmopari gadā yasya cakraṃ cādho vyavasthitam ।
ādi-mūrtes tu bhedo ayaṃ keśaveti parkīrtyate ।।

adharottara-bhāvena kṛtam etat tu yatra vai ।
nārāyaṇākhyā sā mūrtiḥ sthāpitā bhukti-muktidā ।।

savyādhaḥ paṅkajaṃ yasya pāñcajanyaṃ tathopari ।
dakṣiṇordhve gadā yasya cakraṃ cādho vyavasthitam ।
ādimūrtes tu bhedo ayaṃ mādhaveti prakīrtyate ।।

dakṣiṇādhaḥ-sthitaṃ cakraṃ gadā yasyopari sthitā ।
vāmordhva-saṃsthitaṃ padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ cādho vyavasthitam ।
saṅkarṣaṇasya bhedo ayaṃ govindeti prakīrtyate ।।

dakṣiṇopari padmaṃ tu gadā cādho vyavasthitā ।
saṅkarṣaṇasya bhedo ayaṃ viṣṇur ity abhiśabdyate ।।

dakṣiṇopari śaṅkhaṃ ca cakraṃ cādhaḥ pradarśyate ।
vāmopari tathā padmaṃ gadā cādhaḥ pradarśyate ।
madhusūdana-nāmāyaṃ bhedaḥ saṅkarṣaṇasya ca ।।

vāmordhva-saṃsthitaṃ cakram adhaḥ śaṅkhaṃ pradarśyate ।
brahmāṇḍagaṃ vāma-pādaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ śeṣa-pṛṣṭhagam ।।

dakṣiṇordhvaṃ sahasrāraṃ pāñcajanyam adhaḥ-sthitam ।
sapta-tāla-pramāṇena vāmanaṃ kārayet sadā ।।

ūrdhvaṃ dakṣiṇataś cakram adhaḥ padmaṃ vyavasthitam ।
padmā padma-karā vāme pārśve yasya vyavasthitā ।।

sthito vāpy upaviṣṭo vā sānurāgo vilāsavān ।
pradyumnasya hi bhedo ayaṃ śrīdhareti prakīrtyate ।।

dakṣiṇordhvaṃ mahā-cakraṃ kaumudī tad-adhaḥ-sthitā ।
vāmordhve nalinaṃ yasya adhaḥ śaṅkhaṃ virājate ।
hṛṣīkeśeti vijñeyaḥ sthāpitaḥ sarva-kāmadaḥ ।।

dakṣiṇordhve puṇḍarīkaṃ pāñcajanyam adhas tathā ।
vāmordhve saṃsthitaṃ cakraṃ kaumudī tad-adhaḥ-sthitā ।
padmanābheti sā mūrtiḥ sthāpitā mokṣa-dāyinī ।।

dakṣiṇordhve pāñcajanyam adhastāt tu kuśeśayam ।
savordhve kaumudī caiva heti-rājam adhaḥ-sthitam ।
aniruddhasya bhedo ayaṃ dāmodara iti smṛtaḥ ।।
eteṣāṃ tu striyau kārye padma-vīṇādhare śubhe ।।
iti krameṇa mārgādhimāsādhipāḥ keśavādayo dvādaśa । atha caturviṃśati-mūrtayaḥ

siddhārtha-saṃhitāyām-
vāsudevo gadā-śaṅkha-cakra-padma-dharo mataḥ ।
padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ tathā cakraṃ gadāṃ vahati keśavaḥ ।।

śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ gadāṃ cakraṃ dhatte nārāyaṇaḥ sadā ।
gadāṃ cakraṃ tathā śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ vahati mādhavaḥ ।।

cakraṃ padmaṃ tathā śaṅkhaṃ gadāṃ ca puruṣottamaḥ ।
padmaṃ kaumodakīṃ śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ dhatte'py adhokṣajaḥ ।।

saṅkarṣaṇo gadā-śaṅkha-padma-cakra-dharaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
cakraṃ gadāṃ padma-śaṅkhau govindo dharate bhujaiḥ ।।

gadāṃ padmaṃ tathā śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇur bibharti yaḥ ।
cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ tathā padmaṃ gadāṃ ca madhusūdanaḥ ।।

gadāṃ sarojaṃ cakraṃ ca śaṅkhaṃ dhatte'cyutaḥ sadā ।
śaṅkhaṃ kaumodakīṃ cakram upendraḥ padmam udvahet ।।

cakra-śaṅkha-gadā-padma-dharaḥ pradyumna ucyate ।
padmaṃ kaumodakīṃ cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ dhatte trivikramaḥ ।।

śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaṃ vāmano vahate sadā ।
padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ śrīdharo vahate bhujaiḥ ।।

cakraṃ padmaṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ narasiṃho bibharti yaḥ ।
padmaṃ sudarśanaṃ śaṅkhaṃ gadāṃ dhatte janārdanaḥ ।।

aniruddhaś cakra-gadā-śaṅkha-padma-lasad-bhujaḥ ।
hṛṣīkeśo gadāṃ cakraṃ padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca dhārayet ।।

padmanābho vahet śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ tathā ।
padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ dhatte dāmodaraḥ sadā ।।

śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ sarojaṃ ca gadāṃ vahati yo hariḥ ।
śaṅkhaṃ kaumodakīṃ padmaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇur bibharti yaḥ ।।
etāś ca mūrtayo jñeyā dakṣiṇādhaḥ-kara-kramāt ।।
matsya-purāṇe ca-
etad-uddeśataḥ proktaṃ pratimā-lakṣaṇaṃ tathā ।
vistareṇa na śaknoti bṛhaspatir api dvijāḥ ।।

iti

sevā-niṣṭhā hareḥ śrīmad-vaiṣṇavāḥ pāñcarātrikāḥ ।
prākaṭyād akhilāṅgānāṃ śrī-mūrtiṃ bahu manyate ।।

sevyā nija-nijair eva mantraiḥ sva-sveṣṭa-mūrtayaḥ ।
śālagrāmātmake rūpe niyamo naiva vidyate ।।

dvibhujā jalada-śyāmā tribhaṅgī madhurākṛtiḥ ।
sevyā dhyānānurūpaiś ca mūrtiḥ kṛṣṇasya daivataiḥ ।।

anyāś ca vividhā śrīmad-avatārādi-mūrtayaḥ ।
prādurbhāva-vidhāv agre lekhyās tat-tad-viśeṣataḥ ।।

nitya-karma-prasaṅge'tra mūrti-janma-pratiṣṭhayoḥ ।
vidhir na likhituṃ yogyaḥ sa tu lekhiṣyate'grataḥ ।।

atha śālagrāma-śilāḥ

gautamīya-tantre-
gaṇḍakyāś caiva deśe ca śālagrāma-sthalaṃ mahat ।
pāṣāṇaṃ tad-bhavaṃ yat tat śālagrāmam iti smṛtam ।।

skanda-purāṇe-
snigdhā kṛṣṇā pāṇḍarā vā pītā nīlā tathaiva ca ।
vakrā rukṣā ca raktā ca mahā-sthūlā tv alāñchitā ।।

kapilā dardurā bhagnā bahu-cakraika-cakrikā ।
bṛhan-mukhī bṛhac-cakrā lagna-cakrāthavā punaḥ ।
baddha-cakrāthavā kācid bhagna-cakrā tv adhomukhī ।।

atha tāsāṃ varṇādi-bhedena guṇa-doṣau

tatraiva-
snigdhā siddhi-karī mantre kṛṣṇā kīrtiṃ dadāti ca ।
pāṇḍarā pāpa-dahanī pītā putra-phala-pradā ।।

nīlā sandiśate lakṣmīṃ raktā roga-pradāyikā ।
rakṣā codvegadā nityaṃ vakrā dāridrya-dāyikā ।।

sthūlā nihati caivāyur niṣphalā tu alāñchitā ।
kapilā karburā bhagnā bahu-cakraika-cakrikā ।।
bṛhan-mukhī bṛhac-cakrā lagna-cakrāthavā punaḥ ।।
baddha-cakrāthavā yā syād bhagna-cakrā tv adho-mukhī ।
pūjayed yaḥ pramādena duḥkham eva labheta saḥ ।।

agni-purāṇe ca-
tathā vyāla-mukhī bhagnā viṣayā baddha-cakrikā ।
vikārāvartanābhiś ca nārasiṃhī tathaiva ca ।।

kapilā vibhramāvartā rekhāvartā ca yā śilā ।
duḥkhadā sā tu vijñeyā sukhadā na kadācana ।।

snigdhā śyāmā tathā muktāmāyā vā sama-cakrikā ।
ghoṇi-mūrtir anantākhyā gambhīrā sampuṭā tathā ।।

sūkṣma-mūrtir amūrtiś ca sammukhā siddhi-dāyikā ।
dhātrī-phala-pramāṇā yā kareṇobhaya-sampuṭā ।
pūjanīyā prayatnena śilā caitādṛśī śubhā ।।

iṣṭā tu yasya yā mūrtiḥ sa tāṃ yatnena pūjayet ।
pūjite phalam āpnoti iha-loke paratra ca ।।

doṣāś caite sa-kāmārcana-viṣayāḥ

yata uktaṃ śrī-bhagavatā brāhme-
khaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ bhagnaṃ pārśva-bhinnaṃ vibheditam ।
śālagrāma-samudbhūtaṃ śailaṃ doṣāvahaṃ na hi ।।

śrī-rudreṇa ca skānde-
khaṇḍitaṃ truṭitaṃ bhagnaṃ śālagrāme na doṣa-bhāk ।
iṣṭā tu yasya yā mūrtiḥ sa tāṃ yatnena pūjayet ।।

tathā-
cakraṃ vā kevalaṃ tatra padmena saha saṃyutam ।
kevalā vanamālā vā harir lakṣmyā saha sthitaḥ ।।

mukhyāḥ snighdādayas tatrāmukhyā raktādayo matāḥ ।
mukhyābhāve tv amukhyā hi pūjyā ity ucyate paraiḥ ।।

atha tāsām eva lakṣaṇa-viśeṣeṇa saṃjña-viśeṣaḥ

brāhme śrī-bhagavad-brahma-saṃvāde-
nivasāmi sadā brahman śālāgrāmākhya-veśmani ।
tatraiva ratha-cakrāṅka-bheda-nāmāni me śṛṇu ।।

dvāra-deśe same cakre dṛśyate nāntarīyake ।
vāsudevaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ śuklābhaś cātiśobhanaḥ ।।

dve cakre eka-lagne tu pūrva-bhāgas tu puṣkalaḥ ।
saṅkarṣaṇākhyo vijñeyo raktābhiś cātiśobhanaḥ ।।

pradyumnaḥ sūkṣma-cakras tu pīta-dīptis tathaiva ca ।
śuṣiraṃ chidra-bahulaṃ dīrghākāraṃ tu tad bhavet ।।

aniruddhas tu nīlābho vartulaś cātiśobhanaḥ ।
rekhā-trayaṃ tu tad dvāri pṛṣṭhaṃ padmena lāñchitam ।।

saubhāgyaṃ keśavo dadyāt catuṣkoṇo bhavet tu yaḥ ।
śyāmaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ vidyān nābhi-cakraṃ tathonnatam ।।

dīrgha-rekhā-samopetaṃ dakṣiṇe śuṣiraṃ pṛthu ।
ūrdhvaṃ mukhaṃ vijānīyāt dvāre ca hari-rūpiṇam ।।

kāmadaṃ mokṣadaṃ caiva arthadaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
parameṣṭhī lohitabhaḥ padma-cakra-samanvitaḥ ।।

bilvākṛtis tathā pṛṣṭhe śuṣiraṃ cātipuṣkalam ।
kṛṣṇa-varṇas tathā viṣṇuḥ sthūle cakre suśobhanaḥ ।
bramacaryeṇa pūjyo asāv anyathā vighnado bhavet ।।

kvacic ca-
kapilo narasiṃho atha pṛthu-cakre ca śobhane ।
brahmacaryādhikārī syān nānyathā pūjanaṃ bhavet ।।

narasiṃhas tribinduḥ syāt kapilaḥ pañca-bindukaḥ ।
brahmacaryeṇa pūjyaḥ syād anyathā sarva-vighnadaḥ ।।

sthūlaṃ cakra-dvayaṃ madhye guḍa-lākṣā-savarṇakam ।
dvāropari tathā rekhā padmākārā suśobhanā ।।

sphuṭitaṃ viṣamaṃ cakraṃ nārasiṃhaṃ tu kāpilam ।
sampūjya muktim āpnoti saṃgrāme vijayī bhavet ।।

pādme kārttika-māhātmye ca-
yasya dīrghaṃ mukhaṃ pūrva-kathitair lakṣaṇair yutam ।
rekhāś ca keśarākārā nārasiṃho mato hi saḥ ।।

brāhme [padmap ]-
vārāhaṃ śakti-liṅge ca cakre ca viṣame smṛte ।
indranīla-nibhaṃ sthūlaṃ tri-rekhā-lāñchitaṃ śubham ।।

pādme ca tatraiva-
varāhākṛtir ābhugnaś cakra-rekhāsv alaṅkṛtaḥ ।
vārāha iti sa prokto bhukti-mukti-phala-pradaḥ ।।

brāhma eva-
dīrghā kāñcana-varṇā yā bindu-traya-vibhūṣitā ।
matsyākhyā sā śilā jñeyā bhukti-mukti-phala-pradā ।।

kvacic ca-
matsya-rūpaṃ tu deveśaṃ dīrghākāraṃ tu yad bhavet ।
bindu-trayam āyuktaṃ kāsya-varṇaṃ viśobhanam ।।

brāhma [padmap ] eva-
kūrmas tathonnataḥ pṛṣṭhe vartulāvarta-pūritaḥ ।
haritaṃ varṇam ādhatte kaustubhena ca cihnitaḥ ।।

pādme ca tatraiva- kūrmākārā ca cakrāṅkā śilā kūrmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

brāhma [padmap ] eva-
hayagrīvo aṅkuśākāro rekhā cakra-śamīpagāḥ ।
bahu-cakra-samāyuktaṃ pṛṣṭhe nīrada-nīlakam ।।

kvacic ca-
hayagrīvāṅkuśākāre rekhāḥ pañca bhavanti hi ।
bahu-bindu-samākīrṇe dṛśyante nīla-rūpakāḥ ।।

pādme ca tatraiva-
hāyagrīvā yathā lambā rekhāṅkā yā śilā bhavet ।
tathāsau syād dhayagrīvaḥ pūjito jñānado bhavet ।।

kiṃ ca-
aśvākṛti mukhaṃ yasya sākṣamālaṃ śiras tathā ।
padmākṛtir bhaved vāpi hayaśīrṣas tv asau mataḥ ।।

brāhme [padmap ] eva-
vaikuṇṭham maṇi-varṇābhaṃ cakram ekaṃ tathā dhvajam ।
dvāropari tathā rekhā padmākārā suśobhanā ।।

śrīdharas tu tathā devaś cihnito vanamālayā ।
kadamba-kusumākāro rekhā-pañcaka-bhūṣitaḥ ।।

vartulaś cātihrasvaś ca vāmanaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।
atasī-kusuma-prakhyo bindunā pariśobhitaḥ ।।

anyatra ca-
vāmanākhyo bhaved devo hrasvo yaḥ syān mahā-dyutiḥ ।
ūrdhva-cakras tv adhaś cakraḥ so abhīṣṭārtha-prado arcitaḥ ।।

brāhme [padmap ] eva-
sudarśanas tathā devaḥ śyāma-varṇo mahā-dyutiḥ ।
vāma-pārśve gadā-cakre rekhe caiva tu dakṣiṇe ।।

pādme kārttika-māhātmye-
cakrākāreṇa paṅktiḥ sā yatra rekhā-mayī bhavet ।
sa sudarśana ity evaṃ khyātaḥ pūjā-phala-pradaḥ ।।

brāhme [padmap ]-
dāmodaras tathā sthūlo madhye cakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
dūrvābhaṃ dvāra-saṅkīrṇaṃ pītā rekhā tathaiva ca ।।

pādme ca tatraiva-
upary-adhaś ca cakre dve nātidīrghaṃ mukhe bilam ।
cakre ca rekhā lambaikā sa ca dāmodaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

anyatra ca-
sthūlo dāmodaro jñeyaḥ sūkṣma-randhro bhavet tu yaḥ ।
cakre ca madhya-deśa-sthe pūjitaḥ sukhadaḥ sadā ।।

nānā-varṇo hy anantākhyo nāga-bhogena cihnitaḥ ।
anantaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ sarva-pūjā-phala-pradaḥ ।।

pādme ca tatraiva-
ananta-cakro bahubhiś cihnair apy upalakṣitaḥ ।
anantaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ sarva-pūjā-phala-pradaḥ ।।

[padmap ]
dṛśyate śikhare liṅgaṃ śālagrāma-samudbhavam ।
yasya yogeśvaro nāma brahma-hatyāṃ vyapohati ।।

āraktaḥ padmanābhākhyaṃ paṅkaja-cchatra-saṃyutam ।
tulasyā pūjayen nityaṃ daridras tv īśvaro bhavet ।।

candrākṛtiṃ hiraṇyākhyaṃ raśmi-jālaṃ vinirdiśet ।
suvarṇa-rekhā-bahulaṃ sphaṭika-dyuti-śobhitam ।।

kiṃ ca-
ardha-candrākṛtir devo hṛṣīkeśa udāhṛtaḥ ।
tam arcya labhate svargaṃ viṣayāṃś ca samīhitām ।।

vāma-pārśve same cakre kṛṣṇa-varṇaḥ sa bindukaḥ ।
lakṣmī-nṛsiṃho vikhyāto bhukti-mukti-phala-pradaḥ ।।

trivikramas tathā devaḥ śyāma-varṇo mahā-dyutiḥ ।
vāma-pārśve tathā cakre rekhā caiva tu dakṣiṇe ।।

pradakṣiṇāvarta-kṛta-vanamālā-vibhūṣitā ।
yā śilā kṛṣṇa-saṃjñā sā dhana-dhānya-sukha-pradā ।।

gautamīye-
bahubhir janmabhiḥ puṇyair yadi kṛṣṇa-śilāṃ labhet ।
goṣpadena tu cihnena janus tena samāpyate ।।

catasro yatra dṛśyante rekhāḥ pārśva-samīpagāḥ ।
dve cakre madhya-deśe tu sā śilā tu caturmukhā ।।

kiṃ ca, pādme tatraiva-
vajra-kīṭodbhavā rekhāḥ paṅktībhūtāś ca yatra vai ।
śālagrāma-śilā yā sā viṣṇu-pañjara-saṃjñitā ।।

nāgavat kuṇḍalī-bhūta-rekhā-paṅktiḥ sa śeṣakaḥ ।
padmākāre ca paṅktī dve madhye lambā ca rekhikā ।
garuḍaḥ sa tu vijñeyaś catuś cakro janārdanaḥ ।।

catuś cakraḥ sūkṣma-dvāro vanamālāṅkitodaraḥ ।
lakṣmī-nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān bhukti-mukti-phala-pradaḥ ।।

etal lakṣaṇa-yuktās tu śālagrāma-śilāḥ śubhāḥ ।
yāś ca tāsv api sūkṣmāḥ syus tāḥ praśasta-karāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

tathā ca śrī-bhagavad-brahma-saṃvāde tatraiva-
yathā yathā śilā sūkṣmā mahat puṇyaṃ tathā tathā ।
tasmāt tāṃ pūjayen nityaṃ dharma-kāmārtha-siddhaye ।।

tatrāpy āmalakī-tulyā sūkṣmā cātīva yā bhavet ।
tasyām eva sadā brahman śriyā saha vasāmy aham ।।

atha śrī-śālagrāma-śilā-māhātmyam

śālagrāma-śilā-sparśāt koṭi-janmāgha-nāśanam ।
kiṃ punar yajanaṃ tatra hari-sānnidhya-kārakam ।।

pādme māgha-māhātmye tatraiva-
yaḥ pūjayed dhariṃ cakre śālagrāma-śilodbhave ।
rājasūya-sahasreṇa teneṣṭaṃ prativāsaram ।।

yad āmananti vedāntā brahma nirguṇam acyutam ।
tat-prasādo bhaven nṛṇāṃ śālagrāma-śilārcanāt ।।

mahākāṣṭha-sthito vahnir mathyamānaḥ prakāśate ।
yathā tathā harir vyāpī śālagrāme prakāśate ।।

api pāpa-samācārāḥ karmaṇy anadhikāriṇaḥ ।
śālagrāmārcakā vaiśya naiva yānti yamālayam ।।

na tathā ramate lakṣmyāṃ na tathā nija-mandire ।
śālagrām-śilā-cakre yathā sa ramate sadā ।।

agnihotraṃ hutaṃ tena dattā pṛthvī sa-sāgarā ।
yenārcito hariś cakre śālagrāma-śilodbhave ।।

kāmaiḥ krodhaiḥ pralobhaiś ca vyāpto yo atra narādhamaḥ ।
so api yāti harer lokaṃ śālagrāma-śilārcanāt ।।

yaḥ pūjayati govindaṃ śālagrāme sadā naraḥ ।
āhūta-samplavaṃ yāvat na sa pracyavate divaḥ ।।

vinā tīrthair vinā dānair vinā yajñair vinā matim ।
muktiṃ yāti naro vaiśya śālagrāma-śilārcanāt ।।

narakaṃ garbha-vāsaṃ ca tiryaktvaṃ kṛmi-yonitām ।
na yāti vaiśya pāpo api śālagrāme'cyutārcakaḥ ।।

dīkṣā-vidhāna-mantra-jñaś cakre yo balim āharet ।
sa yāti vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma satyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam ।।

naivedyair vividhaiḥ puṣpair dhūpair dīpair vilepanaiḥ ।
gīta-vāditra-stotrādyaiḥ śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।।

kurute mānavo yas tu kalau bhakti-parāyaṇaḥ ।
kalpa-koṭi-sahasrāṇi ramate sannidhau hareḥ ।।

liṅgais tu koṭibhir dṛṣṭair yat phalaṃ pūjitais tu taiḥ ।
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu ekenāpīha tat phalam ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-rūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ ।
tatra devāsurā yakṣā bhuvanāni caturdaśa ।।

śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ ।
pitaras tasya tiṣṭhanti tṛptāḥ kalpa-śataṃ divi ।।

śālagrāma-śilā yatra tat-tīrthaṃ yojana-trayam ।
yatra dānaṃ japo homaḥ sarvaṃ koṭi-guṇaṃ bhavet ।।

śālagrāma-samīpe tu krośa-mātraṃ samantataḥ ।
kīkaṭo api mṛto yāti vaikuṇṭha-bhavanaṃ nara ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-cakraṃ yo dadyād dānam uttamam ।
bhū-cakraṃ tena dattaṃ syāt sa-śaila-vana-kānanam ।।

skānde kārttika-māhātmye [padma ] śrī-śiva-skanda-saṃvāde-
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu trailokyaṃ sa-carācaram ।
mayā saha mahāsena līnaṃ tiṣṭhati sarvadā ।।

dṛṣā praṇamitā yena snāpitā pūjitā tathā ।
yajña-koṭi-samaṃ puṇyaṃ gavāṃ koṭi-phalaṃ labhet ।।

kāmāsakto api yo nityaṃ bhakti-bhāva-vivarjitaḥ ।
śālagrāma-śilāṃ vipra sampūjyaivācyuto bhavet ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-bimbaṃ hatyā-koṭi-vināśanam ।
smṛtaṃ saṅkīrtitaṃ dhyātaṃ pūjitaṃ ca namaskṛtam ।।

śālagrāma-śilāṃ dṛṣṭvā yānti pāpāny anekaśaḥ ।
siṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā yathā yānti vane mṛga-gaṇā bhayāt ।।

namaskaroti manujaḥ śālagrāma-śilārcane ।
pāpāni vilayaṃ yānti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।।

kāmāsakto athavā kruddhaḥ śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।
bhaktyā vā yadi vā'bhaktyā kṛtvā muktim avāpnuyāt ।।

vaivasvataṃ bhayaṃ nāsti tathā maraṇa-janmanoḥ ।
yaḥ kathāṃ kurute viṣṇoḥ śālagrāma-śilāgrataḥ ।।

gītair vādyais tathā stotraiḥ śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।
kurute mānavo yas tu kalau bhakti-parāyaṇaḥ ।
kalpa-koṭi-sahasrāṇi ramate viṣṇu-sadmani ।।

śālagrāma-namaskāre'bhāvenāpi naraiḥ kṛte ।
bhayaṃ naiva kariṣyanti mad-bhaktā ye narā bhuvi ।।

mad-bhakti-bala-darpiṣṭhā mat-prabhuṃ na namanti ye ।
vāsudevaṃ na te jñeyā mad-bhaktāḥ pāpino hi te ।।

śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu sadā putra vasāmy aham ।
dattaṃ devena tuṣṭena sva-sthānaṃ mama bhaktitaḥ ।।

padma-koṭi-sahasrais tu pūjite mayi yat phalam ।
tat phalaṃ koṭi-guṇitaṃ śālagrāma-śilārcane ।।

pūjito æhaṃ na tair martyair namito ahaṃ na tair naraiḥ ।
na kṛtaṃ martya-loke yaiḥ śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।।

śālagrāma-śilāgre tu yaḥ karoti mamārcanam ।
tenārcito ahaṃ satataṃ yugānām ekaviṃśatim ।।

kim arcitair liṅga-śatair viṣṇu-bhakti-vivarjitaiḥ ।
śālagrāma-śilā-bimbaṃ nārcitaṃ yadi putraka ।।

anarhaṃ mama naivedyaṃ patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ jalam ।
śālagrāma-śilā-lagnaṃ sarvaṃ yāti pavitratām ।।

yo hi māheśvaro bhūtvā vaiṣṇava-liṅgam uttamam ।
dveṣṭi vai yāti narakaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।।

sakṛd apy arcite bimbe śālagrāma-śilodbhave ।
muktiṃ prayānti manujā nūnaṃ sāṅkhyena varjitāḥ ।।

mal-liṅgaiḥ koṭibhir dṛṣṭair yat phalaṃ pūjitais tu taiḥ ।
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu ekenāpi hi tad bhavet ।।

tasmād bhaktyā ca mad-bhaktaiḥ prīty-arthe mama putraka ।
kartavyaṃ satataṃ bhaktyā śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-rūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ ।
tatra devāsurā yakṣā bhuvanāni caturdaśa ।।

śālagrāma-śilāgre tu sakṛt piṇḍena tarpitāḥ ।
vasanti pitaras tasya na saṅkhyā tatra vidyate ।।

pramāṇam asti sarvasya sukṛtasya hi putraka ।
phalaṃ pramāṇa-hīnaṃ tu śālagrāma-śilārcane ।।

yo dadāti śilāṃ viṣṇoḥ śālagrāma-samudbhavām ।
viprāya viṣṇu-bhaktāya teneṣṭaṃ bahubhiḥ makhaiḥ ।।

mānuṣye durlabhā loke śālagrāmodbhavā śilā ।
prāpyate na vinā puṇyaiḥ kali-kāle viśeṣataḥ ।।

sa dhanyaḥ puruṣo loke saphalaṃ tasya jīvitam ।
śālagrāma-śilā śuddhā gṛhe yasya ca pūjitā ।।

saṃniyamyendriya-grāmaṃ śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।
yaḥ kuryān mānavo bhaktyā puṣpe puṣpe'śvamedha-bhāk ।।

kāle vā yadi vākāle śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।
bhaktyā vā yadi vābhaktyā yaḥ karoti sa puṇya-bhāk ।।

dveṣeṇāpi ca lobhena dambhena kapaṭena vā ।
śālagrāmodbhavaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpāt pramucyate ।।

aśucir vā durācāraḥ satya-śauca-vivarjitaḥ ।
śālagrāma-śilāṃ spṛṣṭvā sadya eva śucir bhavet ।।

tila-prastha-śataṃ bhaktyā yo dadāti dine dine ।
tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti śālagrāma-śilārcane ।।

patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ mūlaṃ toyaṃ dūrvākṣataṃ suta ।
jāyate meruṇā tulyaṃ śālagrāma-śilārpitam ।।

vidhi-hīno api yaḥ kuryāt kriyā-mantra-vivarjitaḥ ।
cakra-pūjām avāpnoti samyak śāstroditaṃ phalam ।।

tatraiva cānyatra-
skandhe kṛtvā tu yo adhvānaṃ vahate śaila-nāyakam ।
tenoḍhaṃ tu bhavet sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sa-carācaram ।।

brahma-hatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ yat kiñcit kurute naraḥ ।
tat sarvaṃ nirdahaty āśu śālagrāma-śilārcanam ।।

na pūjanaṃ na mantrāś ca na japo na ca bhāvanā ।
na stutir nopacāraś ca śālagrāma-śilārcane ।।

śālagrāma-śilā yatra tat tīrthaṃ yojana-trayam ।
tatra dānaṃ ca homaś ca sarvaṃ koṭi-guṇaṃ bhavet ।।

śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ ।
pitaras tasya tiṣṭhanti tṛptāḥ kalpa-śataṃ divi ।।

śālagrāma-samīpe tu krośa-mātraṃ samantataḥ ।
kīkaṭo api mṛto yāti vaikuṇṭha-bhuvanaṃ naraḥ ।।

pādme ca-
śālagrāma-śilā-cakraṃ yo dadyād dānam uttamam ।
bhū-cakraṃ tena dattaṃ syāt sa-śaila-vana-kānanam ।।

garuḍa-purāṇe- 
tiṣṭhanti nityaṃ pitaro manuṣyās
tīrthāni gaṅgādika-puṣkarāṇi ।
yajñāś ca medhā hy api puṇya-śailāś
cakrāṅkitā yasya vasanti gehe ।।

pādme kārttika-māhātmye śrī-yama-dhūmrakeśa-saṃvāde-
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu yair naraiḥ pūjito hariḥ ।
saṃśodhya teṣāṃ pāpāni muktaye buddhito bhavet ।।

kārttike mathurāyāṃ tu sārūpyaṃ diśate hariḥ ।
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ vai pitṝṇ uddiśya pūjitaḥ ।
kṛṣṇaḥ samuddharet tasya pitṝn etān svalokatām ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye ca yajñadhvajopākhyānānte-
śālagrāma-śilā-rūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ ।
na bādhante'surās tatra bhūta-vetālakādayaḥ ।।

śālagrāma-śilā yatra tat-tīrthaṃ tat tapo-vanam ।
yataḥ sannihitas tatra bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ ।।

śālagrāma-śilās tāś ca yadi dvādaśa pūjitāḥ ।
śataṃ vā pūjitaṃ bhaktyā tadā syād adhikaṃ phalam ।।

atha bāhulye tāsāṃ phala-viśeṣaḥ

pādme māgha-māhātmye devadūta-vikuṇḍala-saṃvāde-
śilā dvādaśa bho vaiśya śālagrāma-śilodbhavāḥ ।
vidhivat pūjitā yena tasya puṇyaṃ vadāmi te ।।

koṭi-dvādaśa-liṅgais tu pūjitaiḥ svarṇa-paṅkajaiḥ ।
yat syād dvādaśa-kāleṣu dinenaikena tad bhavet ।।

yaḥ punaḥ pūjayed bhaktyā śālagrāma-śilāśatam ।
uṣitvā sa harer loke cakravartīha jāyate ।।

skānde kārttika-māhātmye [padma ] śrī-śiva-skanda-saṃvāde-
dvādaśaiva śilā yo vai śālagrāma-samudbhavāḥ ।
arcayed vaiṣṇavo nityaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ nibodha me ।।

koṭi-liṅga-sahasrais tu pūjitair jāhnavī-taṭe ।
kāśī-vāse yugāny aṣṭau dinenaikena tad bhavet ।।

kiṃ punar bahunā yas tu pujayed vaiṣṇavo naraḥ ।
na hi brahmādayo devāḥ saṃkhyāṃ kurvanti puṇyataḥ ।।

atha tat-kraya-vikraya-niṣedhaḥ

tatraiva [padma ]-
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ yo mūlyam udghātayen naraḥ ।
vikretā cānumantā ca yaḥ parīkṣām udīrayet ।।

sarve te narakaṃ yānti yāvad āhūta-samplavam ।
ataḥ saṃvarjayed vipra cakrasya kraya-vikrayam ।।

atha pratiṣṭhā niṣedhaḥ

tatraiva-
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu pratiṣṭhā naiva vidyate ।
mahā-pūjāṃ tu kṛtvādau pūjayet tāṃ tato budhaḥ ।।

iti

ato adhiṣṭhāna-vargeṣu sūryādiṣv iva mūrtiṣu ।
śālagrāma-śilaiva syād adhiṣṭhānottamaṃ hareḥ ।।

atha sarvādhiṣṭhāna-śraiṣṭhyam

pādme tatraiva-
hṛdi sūrye jale vātha pratimā-sthaṇḍileṣu ca ।
samabhyarcya hariṃ yānti narās te vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।।

athavā sarvadā pūjyo vāsudevo mumukṣubhiḥ ।
śālagrāme-śilā-cakre vajra-kīṭa-vinirmite ।।

adhiṣṭhānaṃ hi tad viṣṇoḥ sarva-pāpa-praṇāśanam ।
sarva-puṇya-pradaṃ vaiśya sarveṣām api muktidam ।।

tatraiva kārttika-māhātmye yama-dhūmrakeśa-saṃvāde-
pūjā ca vihitā tasya pratimāyāṃ nṛpātmaja ।
śailī dārumayī lauhī lepyā lekhyā ca saikatā ।
manomayī maṇimayī śrī-mūrtir aṣṭadhā smṛtā ।।

śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu sākṣāt śrī-kṛṣṇa-sevanam ।
nityaṃ saṃnihitas tatra vāsudevo jagad-guruḥ ।।

skānde kārttika-māhātmye śrī-śiva-skanda-saṃvāde-
suvarṇārcā na ratnārcā na śilārcā surottama ।
śālagrāma-śilāyāṃ tu sarvadā vasate hariḥ ।।

ata evoktam- 
hatyāṃ hanti yad-aṅghri-saṅga-tulasī steyaṃ ca toyaṃ pade
naivedyaṃ bahu-madya-pāna-duritaṃ gurv-aṅganā-saṅgajam ।
śrīśādhīna-matiḥ sthitir hari-janais tat-saṅgajaṃ kilbiṣaṃ
śālagrāma-śilā-nṛsiṃha-mahimā ko apy eṣa lokottaraḥ ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-rūpa-bhagavan-mahimāmbudheḥ ।
ūrmīn gaṇayituṃ śakyaḥ śrī-caitanyāśrito api kaḥ ।।

atha śālagrāma-śilā-pūjā-nityatā

pādme-
śālagrāma-śilā-pūjā vinā yo aśnāti kiñcana ।
sa caṇḍālādi-viṣṭhāyām ākalpaṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ ।।

skānde ca-
gauravācala-śṛṅgāgrair bhidyate yasya vai tanuḥ ।
na matir jāyate yasya śālagrāma-śilārcane ।।

iti

evaṃ śrī-bhagavān sarvaiḥ śālagrāma-śilātmakaḥ ।
dvijaiḥ strībhiś ca śūdraiś ca pūjyo bhagavataḥ paraiḥ ।।

tathā skānde śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde cāturmāsya-vrate śālagrāma-śilārcā-prasaṅge-
brāhmaṇa-kṣatriya-viśāṃ sac-chūdrāṇām athāpi vā ।
śālagrāme'dhikāro asti na cānyeṣāṃ kadācana ।।

tatraivānyatra-
striyo vā yadi vā śūdrā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyādayaḥ ।
pūjayitvā śilā-cakraṃ labhante śāśvataṃ padam ।।

iti

ato niṣedhakaṃ yad yad vacanaṃ śrūyate sphuṭam ।
avaiṣṇava-paraṃ tat tad vijñeyaṃ tattva-darśibhiḥ ।।

yathā-
brāhmaṇasyaiva pūjyo ahaṃ śucer apy aśucer api ।
strī-śūdra-kara-saṃsparśo vajrād api suduḥsahaḥ ।।

praṇavoccāraṇārcaiva śālagrāma-śilārcanāt ।
brāhmaṇī-gamanāc caiva śūdraś caṇḍālatām iyāt ।।

sanātanaḥ tad eva śrī-nāradoktyā pramāṇayati-brāhmaṇeti । satāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ, śālagrāme śrī-śālagrāma-śilārcane, anyeṣām asatāṃ śūdrāṇām । ataeva śūdram adhikṛtyoktaṃ vāyu-purāṇe- 
ayācakaḥ pradātā syāt kṛṣiṃ vṛtty-artham ācaret ।
purāṇaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ śālagrāmaṃ ca pūjayet ।।

iti

evaṃ mahā-purāṇānāṃ vacanaiḥ saha-brāhmaṇasyaiva pūjyo aham iti vacanasya virodhān mātsarya-paraiḥ smārtaiḥ kaiścit kalpitam iti mantavyam । yadi ca yuktyā siddhaṃ sa-mūlaṃ syāt tarhi cāvaiṣṇaviḥ śūdrais tādṛśībhiś ca strībhis tat-pūjā na kartavyā, yathā-vidhi gṛhīta-viṣṇu-dīkṣākaiś ca taiḥ kartvyeti vyavasthāpanīyam । yataḥ śūdreṣv antyajeṣv api madhye ye vaiṣṇavās te śūdrādayo na kilocyante । tathā ca nāradīye- śvapaco api mahīpāla viṣṇor bhakto dvijodhikaḥ iti । 
itihāsa-samuccaye-
na śūdrā bhagavad-bhaktaṃ niṣādaṃ śvapacaṃ tathā ।
vīkṣate jāti-sāmānyāt sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam ।।

iti

pādme ca-
na śūdrā bhagavad-bhaktās te tu bhāgavatā narāḥ ।
sarva-varṇeṣu te śūdrā ye na bhaktā janārdane ।।

iti

etad-ādikaṃ cāgre vaiṣṇava-māhātmye vistareṇa vyaktaṃ bhāvi । kiṃ ca, bhagavad-dīkṣā-prabhāvena śūdrādīnām api vipra-sāmyaṃ siddham eva । tathā ca tatra-yathā kāñcanatāṃ yāti ity ādi । etac ca prāg-dīkṣā-māhātmye likhitam eva । ata eva tṛtīya-skandhe devahūti-vākyam [bhp ]- 
yan-nāma-dheya-śravaṇānukīrtanād
yat-prahvaṇād yat-smaraṇād api kvacit ।
śvādo api sadyaḥ savanāya kalpate
kutaḥ punas te bhagavan nu darśanāt ।।

iti

savanāya yajanāya kalpate yogyo bhavatīty arthaḥ । ata eva vipraiḥ saha vaiṣṇavānām ekatraiva gaṇanā । tathā ca hari-bhakti-sudhodaye śrī-bhagavad-brahma-saṃvāde- 
tīrthāny aśvattha-taravo gāvo viprās tathā svayam ।
mad-bhaktāś ceti vijñeyāḥ pañca te tanavo mama ।।

iti

caturtha-skandhe [bhp ] śrī-pṛthu-mahārāja-varṇane-
sarvatrāskhalitādeśaḥ sapta-dvīpaika-daṇḍa-dhṛk ।
anyatra brāhmaṇa-kulād anyatrācyuta-gotrataḥ ।।

iti

īmahārājasyoktau [bhp ] 
mā jātu tejaḥ prabhaven maha-rddhibhis
titikṣayā tapasā vidyayā ca ।
dedīpyamāne ñjita-devatānāṃ
kule svayaṃ rāja-kulād dvijānām ।।

iti

atra śrī-svāmi-pādānāṃ ṭīkā-mahatyaś ca tā ṛddhayaś ca tābhir yad-rāja-kulasya tejas tat tasmāt sakāśād dvijānāṃ viprāṇāṃ kule ajito devatā-pūjyo yeṣāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ, teṣāṃ kule mā jātu prabhavet । kadācid api prabhavaṃ na karotu । kathambhūte ? samṛddhibhir vināpi svayam eva titikṣādibhir dedīpyamāna iti ।

purañjanoktau [bhp ] ca- 
tasmin dadhe damam ahaṃ tava vīra-patni
yo anyatra bhūsura-kulāt kṛta-kilbiṣas tam ।
paśye na vīta-bhayam unmuditaṃ tri-lokyām
anyatra vai mura-ripor itaratra dāsāt ।।

iti

tatrāpi saiva ṭīkā-he vīra-patni ! yas te kṛtāparādhaḥ । tasminn ahaṃ brāhmaṇa-kulād anyatra anyasmin muraripu-dāsād itaratra ca damaṃ dadhe, daṇḍaṃ karomīty adi । īdṛśāni ca vacanāni śrī-bhāgavatādau bahūny eva santi । itthaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha sāmyam eva sidhyati । kiṃ ca-viprād dviṣaḍ-guṇa-yutāt [bhp ] ity ādi-vacanair vaiṣṇava-brāhmaṇebhyo nīca-jāti-jātānām api vaiṣṇavānāṃ śraiṣṭhyaṃ nirdiśyatetarām । ata evoktaṃ śrī-bhagavatā śrī-hayagrīveṇa śrī-hayaśīrṣa-pañcarātre śrī-puruṣottama-pratiṣṭhānte- 
mūrtipānāṃ tu dātavyā deśikārdhena dakṣiṇā ।
tad-ardhaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu tad-ardhaṃ tad-dvijanmanām ।।

iti

ato yuktam eva likhita sarvair bhagavataḥ paraiḥ pūjya iti । tathā ca brahma-vaivarte priyavratopākhyāne dharma-vyādhasyāpi śrī-śālagrāma-śilā-pūjanam uktam- 
tataḥ sa vismitaḥ śrutvā dharma-vyādhasya tad-vacaḥ ।
tasthau sa ca samānīya darśayāmāsa tav ubhau ।।

ninikta-vasanau vṛddhāvāsanasthau nijau gurū ।
śālagrāma-śilāṃ caiva tat-samīpe supūjitam ।।

iti

atrācāraś ca-satāṃ madhya-deśe'smin viśeṣato dakṣiṇa-deśe ca mahattamānāṃ śrī-vaiṣṇavānāṃ pramāṇam iti dik । evaṃ śrī-bhāgavata-pāṭhaādāv apy adhikāro vaiṣṇavānāṃ draṣṭavyaḥ । yato vidhi-niṣedhā bhagavad-bhaktānāṃ na bhavantīti devarṣi-bhūtāpta-nṝṇāṃ pitṝṇām [bhp ] ity ādi-vacanaiḥ । tathā karma-parityāgādināpi na kaścid doṣo ghaṭata iti tāvat karmāṇi kurvīta [bhp ] iti, yadā yasyānugṛhṇāti bhagavān [bhp ] ity ādi vacanaiś ca vyaktaṃ bodhitam evāsti । etat sarvam agre śrī-vaiṣṇava-māhātmye vistareṇa vyaktaṃ bhāvi hbhvc 

śvādatvam atra śva-bhakṣaka-jāti-viśeṣatvam eva śvānam attīti nirukter vartamāna-prayogāt kravyādavat tac-chīlatva-prāpteḥ । kādācitka-bhakṣaṇa-prāyaścitta-vivakṣāyāṃ tv atītaḥ prayogaḥ kriyeta । rūḍhir yogam apaharatīti nyāyena ca tad virudhyate । ataeva śvapaca iti tair vyākhyātam । savanaṃ cātra soma-yāga ucyate । tataś cāsya bhagavan-nāma-śravaṇādy-ekatarāt sadya eva savana-yogyatā-pratikūla-durjātitva-prārambhaka-prārabdha-pāpa-nāśaḥ pratipadyate । uddhavaṃ prati bhagavatā ca - tasmāt bhaktiḥ punāti man-niṣṭhā śvapākān api sambhavāt [bhp ] iti kaimutyārtham eva proktam ity āyāti । kintu yogyatvam atra śvapacatva-prāpaka-prārabdha-pāpa-vicchinnatva-mātram ucyate । savanārthaṃ tu guṇāntarādhānam apekṣata eva । brāhmaṇa-kumārāṇāṃ śaukre janmani yogyatve saty api sāvitra-daiksya-janmāpekṣāvat । sāvitrādi-janmani tu sad-ācāra-prāpter iti savane pravṛttir na yujyate । tasmāt pūjyatva-mātre tātparyam ity abhipretya ṭīkā-kṛdbhir apy uktam anena pūjyatvaṃ lakṣyata iti । tathāpi jāti-doṣa-haratvena prārabdha-hāritvaṃ tu vyaktam evāyātam ।

sandhāryaā vaiṣṇavair yatnāc chālagrāma-śilā'suvat ।
sā cārcyā dvārakā-cakrāṅkitopetaiva sarvadā ।।

brāhme tatraiva-
śālagrāmodbhavo devo devo dvāravatī-bhavaḥ ।
ubhayoḥ saṅgamo yatra muktis tatra na saṃśayaḥ ।।

skānde śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
cakrāṅkitā śilā yatra śālagrāma-śilāgrataḥ ।
tiṣṭhate muni-śārdūla vardhante tatra sampadaḥ ।।

tatraivānyatra-
pratyahaṃ dvādaśa śilāḥ śālagrāmasya yo arcayet ।
dvāravatyāḥ śilā-yuktāḥ sa vaikuṇṭhe mahīyate ।।

atha śrī-dvārakā-cakrāṅka-lakṣaṇāni

śrī-prahlāda-saṃhitāyām-
ekaḥ sudarśano dvābhyāṃ lakṣmī-nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
tribhis trivikramo nāma caturbhiś ca janārdanaḥ ।।

pañcabhir vāsudevas tu ṣaḍbhiḥ pradyumna ucyate ।
saptabhir baladevas tu aṣṭabhiḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।।

navabhiś ca nava-vyūho daśabhir daśa-mūrtikaḥ ।
ekādaśaiś cāniruddho dvādaśair dvādaśātmakaḥ ।
anyeṣū bahu-cakreṣu anantaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।

atha dvādaśa-cakrāṅka-māhātmyam

vārāhe-
ye kecic caiva pāṣāṇā viṣṇu-cakreṇa mudritāḥ ।
teṣāṃ sparśana-mātreṇa mucyate sarva-pātakaiḥ ।।

gāruḍe- sudarśanādyās tu śilāḥ pūjitāḥ sarva-kāmadāḥ ।।

skānde ca-
bhaktyā vā yadi vābhaktyā cakrāṅkaṃ pūjayen naraḥ ।
api cet sudurācāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

dvārakā-māhātmye ca dvārakā-gatānāṃ śrī-brahmādīnām uktau-
etad vai cakra-tīrthaṃ tu yac chilā cakra-cihnitā ।
muktidā pāpināṃ loke mleccha-deśe'pi pūjitā ।।

atha teṣv eva cakra-bhedena phala-bhedaḥ

kapila-pañcarātre-
eka-cakras tu pāṣāṇo dvāravatyāḥ suśobhanaḥ ।
sudarśanābhidho yo asau mokṣaika-phala-dāyakaḥ ।।

lakṣmī-nārāyaṇo dvābhyāṃ bhukti-mukti-phala-pradaḥ ।
ebhiś cācyuta-rūpo asau phalam aindraṃ prayacchati ।।

catur-bhujaś catuś-cakraś catur-varga-phala-pradaḥ ।
pañcabhir vāsudevaś ca janma-mṛtyu-bhayāpahaḥ ।।

ṣaḍbhiḥ pradyumna evāsau lakṣmīṃ kāntiṃ dadāti saḥ ।
saptabhir balabhadro asau gotra-kīrti-vivardhanaḥ ।।

dadāti vāñchitaṃ sarvam aṣṭabhiḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।
nava-cakro nṛsiṃhas tu phalaṃ yacchaty anuttamam ।।

rājya-prado daśabhis tu daśāvatārakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
ekādaśabhir aiśvaryam aniruddhaḥ prayacchati ।।
nirvāṇaṃ dvādaśātmāsau saukhyadaś ca supūjitaḥ ।।
atha varṇādi-bhedena doṣa-guṇāḥ pūjyatvāpūjyatve ca

tatraiva-
kṛṣṇa mṛtyu-prado nityaṃ dhūmraś caiva bhayāvahaḥ ।
asvāsthyaṃ karburo dadyān nīlas tu dhana-hānidaḥ ।।

chidro dāridrya-duḥkhāni dadyāt sampūjito dhruvam ।
pāṇḍaras tu mahad duḥkhaṃ bhagno bhāryā-viyogadaḥ ।।

putra-pautra-dhanaiśvarya-sukham atyantam uttamam ।
dadāti śukla-varṇaś ca tasmād enaṃ samarcayet ।।

śrī-prahlāda-saṃhitāyām-
kṛṣṇā mṛtyu-pradā nityaṃ kapilā ca bhayāvahā ।
rogārtiṃ karburā dadyāt pītā vitta-vināśinī ।।

dhūmrābhā vitta-nāśāya bhagnā bhāryā-vināśikā ।
sac-chidrā ca trikoṇā ca tathā viṣama-cakrikā ।
ardha-candrākṛtir yā ca pūjyās tā na bhavanti hi ।।

gārgya-gālavayoḥ-
sukhadā sama-cakrā tu dvādaśī cottamā śubhā ।
vartulā caturasrā ca narāṇāṃ ca sukha-pradā ।।

trikoṇā viṣamā caiva chidrā bhagnā tathaiva ca ।
ardha-candrākṛtir yā tu pūjārhā na bhavet tu sā ।
phalaṃ notpadyate tatra pūjitāyāṃ kadācana ।।

iti śrī-gopāla-bhaṭṭa-vilikhite śrī-bhagavad-bhakti-vilāse ādhiṣṭhāniko nāma pañcamo vilāsaḥ

snapanika-vilasa

ṣaṣṭha-vilāsaḥ snāpanikaḥ

śrī-caitanya-prasādena tad-rūpaṃ gokulotsavam ।
manojñaṃ yaṣṭu-kāmasya mūrty-arcā-vidhir ucyate ।।

svayaṃ vyaktāḥ sthāpanāś ca mūrtayo dvividhā matāḥ ।
svayaṃ vyaktāḥ svayaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sthāpanās tu pratiṣṭhayā ।।

yathā ca pādmottara-khaṇḍe [padmap ]-
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi tad-arcāvasathaṃ hareḥ ।
sthāpanaṃ ca svayaṃ vyaktaṃ dvividhaṃ tat prakīrtitam ।।

śilā-mṛd-dāru-lohādyaiḥ kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ hareḥ ।
śrauta-smārtāgama-prokta-vidhinā sthāpanaṃ hi yat ।।

tat sthāpanaṃ iti proktaṃ svayaṃ vyaktaṃ hi me śṛṇu ।
yasmin sannihito viṣṇuḥ svam eva nṝṇāṃ bhuvi ।।

pāṣāṇadārvor ātmeśaḥ svayaṃ vyaktaṃ hi tat smṛtam ।
durlabhatvāt svayaṃ vyakta-mūrteḥ śrī-vaiṣṇavottamaḥ ।
yathāvidhi pratiṣṭhāpya sthāpitāṃ mūrtim arcayet ।।

hari-bhakti-sudhodaye-
naikaṃ sva-vaṃśaṃ tu naras tārayaty akhilaṃ jagat ।
arcāyām īpsitaṃ nṝṇāṃ phalaṃ yāgādi-durlabham ।
pratimām āśrito abhīṣṭa-pradāṃ kalpa-latāṃ yathā ।।

atha-śrī-mūrteḥ prasādanam ātmādi-śuddhayaś ca

śrī-mūrtiṃ kṣālanārhāṃ tu śasta-gandha-jalādinā ।
praksālayet tad anyāṃ tu mūla-mantreṇa mārjayet ।।

śrī-mūrti-hṛdayaṃ spṛṣṭvā sva-mantraṃ cāṣṭadhā japet ।
evaṃ prasādanaṃ mūrter ātmanas tat-prasādanāt ।
śuddhir ekā dvitīyā tu syād avyagratayāpi ca ।।

sthāna-śuddhis tathā dravya-śuddhiś ca likhitā purā ।
iti prakāra-bhedena bhavec chuddhi-catuṣṭayam ।।

uktaṃ ca śrī-nāradena-
puṣpeṇāmbu gṛhītvā tu prokṣayete sarva-sādhanam ।
mala-snānaṃ tataḥ kuryāt pātre devaṃ nidhāya ca ।।

anyenāpi-
puṣpākṣatādi-dravyānāṃ kuryān mantrādi-śodhanam ।
kṣālanenāmbu-lepāder mūrti-śuddiṃ samācaret ।
avyagratvenātma-śuddhiṃ ksiti-śuddhiṃ tataś caret ।।

। iti ।।

mantra-śuddhiṃ parāṃ citta-śuddhiṃ cecchanti kecana ।
evaṃ ṣaṭ śuddhayaḥ puṇyāḥ sampradāyānusārataḥ ।।

atha pīṭha-pūjā

tāmrādi-pīṭhe śrī-khaṇḍādyālipte'ṣṭa-dalaṃ likhet ।
sakarṇikaṃ trivṛttāḍhyaṃ padmaṃ ṣoḍaśa-keśaram ।।

sadalāgraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ caturdvāra-vibhūṣitam ।
pūjā-yantraṃ samuddhṛtya pīṭhārcāṃ tatra sādhayet ।।

pīṭhe bhagavato vāme śrī-gurūn guru-pādukām ।
nāradādīn pūrva-siddhān yajed anyāṃś ca vaiṣṇavān ।।

dakṣiṇe cārcayed durgāṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca sarasvatīm ।
tatra prāg-likhita-nyāsasyānusāreṇa pūjayet ।।

madhye ādhāra-śakty-ādīn dharmādīṃś ca vidikṣv atha ।
adharmādīṃś catur-dikṣv anantādīn madhyataḥ punaḥ ।।

śaktīr navāṣṭa-patreṣu karṇikāyāṃ ca pūjayet ।
tathā tad-upariṣṭhāc ca pīṭha-mantraṃ yathoditam ।।

tat-pīṭhe mūla-mantreṇa śrī-mūrtiṃ sthāpayed atha ।
puṣpāñjaliṃ gṛhitveṣṭa-deva-rūpaṃ vicintayet ।।

tataś ca mūla-mantreṇa kṣiptvā puṣpāñjali-trayam ।
nijeṣṭa-deva-mūrteś ca param aikyaṃ vibhāvayet ।।

athāvāhanādīni

tato devārcane prauḍha-pādatāyā niṣedhanāt ।
bhūmai nihita-pādaḥ san kuryād āvāhanādikam ।।

yac cāvāhyam adhiṣṭhānaṃ tatrāvāhanam ācaret ।
śālagrāma-sthāpane ca nāvāhana-visarjane ।।

tathā coktam-
udvāsāvāhane na staḥ sthāvare vai yathā tathā ।
śālagrāmārcane naiva hy āvāhana-visarjane ।।

śālagrāme tu bhagavān āvirbhūto yathā hariḥ ।
na tathānyatra sūryādau vaikuṇṭhe'pi ca sarvagaḥ ।।

athāvāhanādi-vidhiḥ

āvāhanādi-mudrāś ca saṃdarśyāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ ।
tathā saṃsthāpanaṃ sannidhāpanaṃ sannirodhanam ।।

sakalīkaraṇaṃ cāvaguṇṭhanaṃ ca yathāvidhi ।
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt paramīkaraṇaṃ tathā ।।

tathāvāhanādy-arthaḥ

āgame-
āvāhanaṃ cādareṇa sammukhīkaraṇaṃ prabhoḥ ।
bhaktyā niveśanaṃ tasya saṃsthāpana-mudrā-hṛtam ।।

tavāsmīti tvadīyatva-darśanaṃ sannidhāpanam ।
kriyā-samāpti-paryantaṃ sthāpanaṃ sannirodhanam ।।

saklaīkaraṇaṃ coktaṃ tat-sarvāṅga-prakāśanam ।
ānanda-ghanatātyanta-prakāśo hy avaguṭhanam ।।

amṛtīkaraṇaṃ sarvair evāṅgair avaruddhatā ।
paramīkaraṇaṃ nāmābhīṣṭa-sampādanaṃ param ।।

athāvāhana-māhātmyam

nārasiṃhe-
āgaccha narasiṃheti āvāhyākṣata-puṣpakaiḥ ।
etāvatāpi rājendra sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

। iti।

nyased yathā-sampradāyaṃ deve'ṅgādīni pūrvavat ।
śaṅkha-cakrādikāś cātha mudrā vidvān pradarśayet ।।

tathā ca tattva-sāgare-
āvāhanādi-mudrāś ca darśayitvā tataḥ punaḥ ।
aṅga-nyāsaṃ ca devasya kṛtvā mudrāḥ pradarśayet ।।

atha mudrāḥ 
āgame-
āvāhanīṃ sthāpanīṃ ca tathānyāṃ sannidhāpanīm ।
saṃnirodha-karīṃ cānyāṃ sakalīkaraṇīṃ parām ।।

tathāvaguṇṭhanīṃ paścād amṛtīkaraṇīṃ tathā ।
paramīkaraṇaṃ cānyā prāg aṣṭau darśayed imāḥ ।।

śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaṃ muṣalaṃ śārṅgam eva ca ।
khaḍgaṃ pāśāṅkuśī tadvad vainateyaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

śrīvatsa-kaustubhau veṇum abhīti-varadau tathā ।
vanamālāṃ tathā mantrī darśayet kṛṣṇa-pūjane ।।

mudrā cāpi prayoktavyā nitya`abilva-phalākṛtiḥ ।
ity etāś ca punaḥ saptadaśa mudrāḥ pradarśayet ।।

ganda-digdhau karau kṛtvā mudrāḥ sarvatra yojayet ।
yo anyathā kurute mūḍho na siddhaḥ phalabhāg bhavet ।।

atha mudrā-māhātmyam 
agastya-saṃhitāyām-
etābhiḥ saptadaśabhir mudrābhis tu vicaksaṇaḥ ।
yo vai mām arcayen nityaṃ mohayet sa sureśvaram ।
drāpayed api viprendra tataḥ prārthitam āpnuyat ।।

krama-dīpikāyāṃ bilva-mudrām adhikṛtya -

mano-vāṇī-dehair yad iha ca purā vāpi vihitaṃ
tvamatyā matyā vā tad akhilam asau duṣkṛti-cayam ।
imāṃ mudrāṃ jānan kṣapayati naras taṃ sura-gaṇā
namanty asyādhīnā bhavati satataṃ sarva-janatā ।।

athāsanādy-arpaṇam

tato nikṣipya devasyopari puṣpāñjali-trayam ।
dattvāsanārthaṃ puspaṃ ca svāgataṃ vidhinācaret ।।

āsanādy-upacāreṣu mudrāḥ ṣoḍaśa darśayet ।
prasiddhāḥ padma-svasty-ādyā vidvān ṣoḍaśasu kramāt ।।

śrī-kṛṣṇāyārpayed arghyaṃ pādyam ācamanīyakam ।
madhuparkaṃ punaś cācamanīyaṃ ca vidhir yathā ।।

tathā ca smṛty-artha-sāre -
āvāhanāsanaṃ pādyam arghyam ācamanīyakam ।
snānam ācamanaṃ vastrācamanaṃ copavītakam ।।

ācamanaṃ gandha-puṣpaṃ dhūpa-dīpaṃ prakalpayet ।
naivedyaṃ punar ācāmaṃ natvā stutvā visarjayet ।।

anyatra ca -
ādau puṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā pādārcanam ataḥ param ।
pādyam arghaṃ tv ācamanaṃ madhuparkaṃ yathoditam ।।

abhyaṅgodvartane kṛtvā mahā-snānaṃ samācaret ।
abhiṣekāṅga-vastraṃ ca dattvā nīrājayed dharim ।।

। iti।

śrī-mūrtau tu śirasy arghyaṃ dadyāt pādyaṃ ca pādayoḥ ।
mukhe cācamanīyaṃ trir madhuparkaṃ ca tatra hi ।।

sarveṣv apy upacāreṣu pādyādiṣu pṛthak pṛthak ।
ādau puṣpāñjaliṃ kecid icchanti bhagavat-parāḥ ।।

athāsanādy-arpaṇa-māhātmyam

narasiṃha-purāṇe -
dattvāsanam athārghyaṃ ca pādyam ācamanīyakam ।
devadevasya vidhinā sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare -
āsanānāṃ pradānena sthānaṃ sarvatra vindati ।
godāna-phalam āpnoti tathā pādya-prado naraḥ ।।

tatas tv arhaṇa-dānena sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।
tathaivācamaīyasya dātā brāhamaṇa-sattamāḥ ।।

tīrtha-toyaṃ tathā dattvā devasyācamanaṃ punaḥ ।
svarga-lokam avāpnoti sarva-pāpa-vivarjitaḥ ।
naras tv ācamanīyasya dātā bhavati nirmalaḥ ।।
madhuparkasya dānena paraṃ padam ihāśnute ।।
viṣṇu-purāṇe ca -
madhuparka-vidhiṃ kṛtvā madhuparkaṃ prayacchati ।
brahman sa yāti paramaṃ sthānam etan na saṃśayaḥ ।।

atha snānam

vijñāpya devaṃ snānārthaṃ pāduke purato arpayet ।
mahā-vidyādinā taṃ ca snāna-sthānaṃ tato nayet ।।

prāgvat tatrāsanaṃ pādyaṃ tatraivācamanīyakam ।
nivedya darśayen mudrām amṛtīkaraṇīṃ budhaḥ ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-rūpaṃ tato devaṃ niveśayet ।
snāna-pātre nijābhīṣṭāṃ calāṃ śrī-mūrtim eva vā ।।

atha snāna-pātram

skanda-purāṇe -
kṛtvā tāmra-maye pātre yo arcayen madhusūdanam ।
phalam āpnoti pūjāyāḥ pratyahaṃ śatvārṣikam ।।

yo arcayen mādhavaṃ bhaktyā aśvattha-dala-saṃsthitam ।
pratyahaṃ labhate puṇyaṃ padma-yuta-samudbhavam ।।

rambhā-dalopari hariṃ kṛtvā yo abhyarcayen naraḥ ।
varṣāyutaṃ bhavet pītaḥ keśavaḥ priyayā saha ।।

ye paśyanti sakṛd bhaktyā padma-patropari sthitam ।
bhaktyā padmālayā-kāntaṃ tair āptaṃ durlabha-phalam ।।

। iti।

tataḥ śaṅkhenābhiṣekaṃ kuryād ghaṇṭādi-niḥsvanaiḥ ।
mūlenāṣṭākṣareṇāpi dhūpayann antarāntarā ।।

tatra tu prathamaṃ bhaktyā vidadhīta sugandhibhiḥ ।
divyais tailādibhir dravyair abhyaṅgaṃ śrī-hareḥ śanaiḥ ।।

athābhyaṅga-dravyāṇi tan-māhātmyaṃ ca

skande - mālatī-jātim ādāya sugandhānāṃ tu vā punaḥ ।।

tathānya-puṣpa-jātīnāṃ gṛhītvā bhaktito narāḥ ।
ye snāpayanti deveśam utsave vai harer dine ।।

medinī-dāna-tulyaṃ hi phalam uktaṃ svayambhuvā ।
yaḥ punaḥ puṣpa-tailena divyauṣadhi-yutena hi ।।

abhyaṅgaṃ kurute viṣṇor madhye kṣiptvā tu kuṅkumam ।
romāñcita-tanur bhūtvā priyayā saha mādhavaḥ ।
prītyā bibharti svotsaṅge manvantara-śataṃ hariḥ ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare ca -
gandha-tailāni divyāni sugandhīni śucīni ca ।
keśavāya naro dattvā gandharvaiḥ saha modate ।।

atha pañcāmṛta-snapanam

tataḥ śaṅkha-bhṛtenaiva kṣīreṇa snāpayet kramāt ।
dadhnā ghṛtena madhunā khaṇḍena ca pṛthak pṛthak ।।

pañcāmṛtādyaiḥ snapanaṃ sadā necchanti tat priyāḥ ।
kintu taiḥ kāla-deśādi-viśeṣe kārayanti tat ।।

atha tat-parimāṇam

brahma-purāṇe 
devānāṃ pratimā yatra ghṛtābhyaṅgas tato bhavet ।
palāni tasya deyāni śraddhayā pañcaviṃśatiḥ ।।

aṣṭottara-pala-śataṃ deyaṃ ca sarvadā ।
dve sahasre palānāṃ tu mahā-snāne ca saṅkhyayā ।।
dātavye yena sarvāsu dikṣu niryāti tad-ghṛtam ।।
। iti।

dugdhādāv api saṅkhyeyam evaṃ jñeyā manīṣibhiḥ ।
pala-saṅkhyā ca vijñeyā yājñavalkyādi-vākyataḥ ।।

tathā hi -
pañca-kṛṣṇalako māṣas te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa ।
suvarṇānāṃ ca catvāraḥ palam ity abhidhīyate ।।

। iti।

kiṃ ca - snānārthaṃ surabhī-kṣīraṃ mahiṣyādyās tu kutsitāḥ ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare ca -
śarīra-duḥkha-śamanaṃ mano-duḥkha-vināśanam ।
kṣīreṇa snapanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kṣīrābhodhi-pradaṃ tathā ।।

agni-purāṇe -
gavāṃ śatasya viprebhyaḥ samyag-dattasya yat phalam ।
ghṛta-prasthena tad viṣṇor labhet snānān na saṃśayaḥ ।।

indradyumnena samprāptā sapta-dvīpā vasundharā ।
ghṛtodakena saṃyuktā pratimā snāpitā kila ।।

pratimāsaṃ sitāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtena jagatāṃ patim ।
snāpayitvā samabhyarcya sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

jñānato ajñānato vāpi yat pāpaṃ kurute naraḥ ।
tat kṣālayati sandhyāyāṃ ghṛta-snapana-toṣitaḥ ।।

yeṣu kṣīravahā nadyo pāyasa-kardamāḥ ।
tān lokān puruṣā yānti kṣīra-snapanakā hareḥ ।।

viṣṇu-dharme śrī-pulastya-prahlāda-saṃvāde ca -
dvādaśyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ ca gavyena havisā hareḥ ।
snāpanaṃ daitya-śārdūla mahā-pātaka-nāśanam ।।

dadhy-ādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīrataḥ sambhavo yathā ।
tathaivāśeṣa-kāmānāṃ kṣīra-snānaṃ tato hareḥ ।।

nārasiṃhe -
payasā yas tu deveśaṃ snāpayed garuḍa-dhvajam ।
sarva-pāpa-viśuddhātmā viṣṇu-loke mahīyate ।।

snāpya dadhnā sakṛd viṣṇuṃ nirmalaṃ priya-darśanam ।
viṣṇu-lokam avāpnoti sevyamānaḥ surottamaḥ ।।

duḥsvapna-śamanaṃ jñeyam amaṅgalya-vināśanam ।
māṅgalya-vṛddhi-daṃ dadhnā snapanaṃ nara-puṅgava ।।

yaḥ karoti harer arcāṃ madhunā snāpitāṃ naraḥ ।
agni-loke sa moditvā punar viṣṇu-pure vaset ।।

madhunā snapanaṃ kṛtvā saubhāgyam adhigacchati ।
loka-mitrāṇy avāpnoti tathaivekṣu-rasena ca ।।

śrī-dvārakā-māhātmye ca śrī-mārkaṇḍeyendradyumna-saṃvāde -
kṣīra-snānaṃ prakurvanti ye narā viṣṇu-mūrdhani ।
tenāśva-medhajaṃ puṇyaṃ bindunā bindunā smṛtam ।।

kṣīrād daśa-guṇaṃ dadhnā ghṛtaṃ tasmād daśottaram ।
ghṛtād daśa-guṇaṃ kṣaudraṃ khaṇḍaṃ tasmād daśottaram ।।

puṣpodakaṃ ca gandhodaṃ vardhate ca daśottaram ।
mantrodakaṃ ca darbhodaṃ tathaiva nṛpa-sattama ।।

drākṣā-rasaṃ cūta-rasaṃ śata-vāji-makhaiḥ samam ।
tathaiva tīrtha-nīraṃ ca phalaṃ yacchati bhūmipa ।।

snāpanaṃ kṛṣṇa-devasya yaḥ karoti sva-śaktitaḥ ।
phalam āpnoti tat proktaṃ niṣkāmo muktim āpnuyāt ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare-
tīrthodakāni puṇyāni svayam ānīya mānavaḥ ।
tailasya snapanaṃ dattvā sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

atha snapane dhūpane dhūpana-māhātmyam

skānde -
snāna-kāle tu kṛṣṇasya aguruṃ dahate tu yaḥ ।
praviṣṭo nāsikā-randhraṃ pāpaṃ janmāyutaṃ dahet ।।

udvartanaṃ ca tailāder apasāraṇa-kāraṇam ।
devasya kārayed dravyair upayuktyair anantaram ।।

athodvartanaṃ tan-māhātmyaṃ ca

nārasiṃhe -
yava-godhūmaiś cūrṇair udvartyoṣṇena vāriṇā ।
prakṣālya deva-deveśaṃ vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnuyāt ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare ca -
go-dhūma-yava-cūrṇais tu tam utsādya janārdanam ।
lodhra-cūrṇaka-saṅkīrṇair bala-rūpaṃ tathāpnuyāt ।।

masūra-māsa-cūrṇaṃ ca kuṅkuma-kṣoda-saṃyutam ।
nivedya deva-devāya gandharvaiḥ saha modate ।।

vārāhe -
kalāyakasya cūrṇena piṣṭa-cūrṇena vā punaḥ ।
tenaivodvartanaṃ kuryād gandha-puṣpaiś ca saṃyutam ।
yadīcchet paramāṃ siddhiṃ mama karma-parāyaṇaḥ ।।

। iti।

tataḥ samarpayet kūrcam uṣīrādi-vinirmitam ।
malāpakarṣaṇādy-arthaṃ śrīman-mūrty-aṅga-sandhitaḥ ।।

atha kūrcaṃ tan-māhātmyam

viṣṇu-dharmottare -
uṣīra-kūrcakaṃ dattvā sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।
dattvā go-bāla-jaṃ kūrcaṃ sarvāṃs tāpān vyapohati ।
dattvā cāmarakaṃ kūrcaṃ śriyam āpnoty anuttamam ।।

atha śuddha-jala-snapanam

tataḥ koṣṇena saṃsnāpya saṃskṛtena sugandhinā ।
śītalenāmbunā śaṅkha-bhṛtena snāpayet punaḥ ।।

tad uktam ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] -
candanośīra-karpūra- kuṅkumāguru-vāsitaiḥ ।
salilaiḥ snāpayen mantrair nityadā vibhave sati ।।

atha jala-parimāṇam

bhaviṣye -
snāne pala-śataṃ deyam abhyaṅge pañca-viṃśatiḥ ।
palānāṃ dve sahasre tu mahā-snānaṃ prakīrtitam ।।

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ- na naktodaka-puṣpādyair arcanaṃ snānam arhati ।।

viṣṇuḥ- na naktaṃ gṛhītodakena daiva-karma kuryāt ।।

hārītaḥ-
rātrāv etā āpo varuṇaṃ prāviśanta
tasmān na rātrau gṛhṇīyāt ।।

atha snapana-māhātmyam 
nārasiṃhe-
nirmālaym apanīyātha toyena snāpya keśavam ।
narasiṃhākṛtiṃ rājan sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

go-dāna-jaṃ phalaṃ prāpya yānenāmbara-śobhinā ।
narasiṃha-puraṃ prāpya modate kālam akṣayam ।।

kiṃ ca-
snāpya toyena bhaktyā tu narasiṃhaṃ narādhipa ।
sarva-pāpa-vinirmukto viṣṇu-lokaṃ mahīyate ।।

narasiṃhaṃ tu saṃsnāpya karpūrāguru-vāriṇā ।
canddra-loke sa moditvā paścād viṣṇu-puraṃ vaset ।।

kiṃ ca-
kuśa-puṣpodakenāpi viṣṇu-lokam avāpnuyāt ।
ratnodakena sāvitraṃ kauveraṃ hema-vāriṇā ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare -
ratnodaka-pradānena śriyam āpnoty anuttamām ।
bījodaka-pradānena kriyā-sāphalyam āpnuyāt ।।

puṣpa-toya-pradānena śrīmān bhavati mānavaḥ ।
phala-toya-pradānena saphalāṃ vindate kriyām ।।

hayaśīrṣa-pañcarātre-
sugandhinā yas toyena snāpayej jala-śāyinam ।
brahma-lokam avāpnoti yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।।

gāruḍe - tulasī-miśra-toyena snāpayanti janārdanam । pūjayanti ca bhāvena dhanyās te bhuvi mānavāḥ ।। ।

agni-purāṇe-
mahā-snānena govindaṃ samyak saṃsnāpya mānavaḥ ।
yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate kāmaṃ taṃ taṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayaḥ ।।

pādme śrī-pulastya-bhagīratha-saṃvāde-
snānam abhyarcanaṃ yas tu kurute keśave sadā ।
tasya puṇyasya yā saṅkhyā nāsti sā jñāne gocarā ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare -
snānārthaṃ devadevasya yas tu gandhaṃ prayacchati ।
bhavanti vaśagās tasya nāryaḥ sarvatra sarvadā ।।

puṣpa-dānāt tathā loke bhavatīha phalānvitaḥ ।
dattvā mṛgamada-snānaṃ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt ।।

sarvauṣadhi-pradānena vājimedha-phalaṃ labhet ।
dattvā jātī-phalaṃ mukhyaṃ saphalāṃ vindati kriyām ।।

atha sarvauṣadhiḥ

murā māsī vacā kuṣṭhaṃ śaileyaṃ rajanī-dvayam ।
śaṭī campaka-mustaṃ ca sarvauṣadhi-gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

gandhaś cāgame- gandhaś candana-karpūra-kālāgurubhir īritaḥ ।।

atha śaṅkha-māhātmyam

skānde śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
śaṅkha-sthitena toyena yaḥ snāpayati keśavam ।
kapilā-śata-dānasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।।

śaṅke tīrthodakaṃ kṛtvā yaḥ snāpayati mādhavam ।
dvādaśyāṃ bindu-mātreṇa kulānāṃ tārayec chatam ।।

kapilā-kṣīram ādāya śaṅkhe kṛtvā janārdanam ।
yaḥ snāpayati dharmātmā yajñāyuta-phalaṃ labhet ।।

anya-go-sambhavaṃ kṣīraṃ śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu nārada ।
yaḥ snāpayati deveśaṃ rājasūya-phalaṃ labheet ।।

śaṅkhe kṛtvā ca pānīyaṃ sākṣataṃ kusumānvitam ।
snāpayed devadeveśaṃ hanyāt pāpaṃ cirārjitam ।।

sākṣataṃ kusumopetaṃ śaṅkhe toyaṃ sa-candanam ।
yaḥ kṛtvā snāpayed devaṃ mama loke vasec ciram ।।

kṣiptvā gandhodakaṃ śaṅkhe yaḥ snāpayati keśavam ।
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mucyate yoni-saṅkaṭān ।।

nādyaṃ taḍāgajaṃ vāri vāpī-kūpa-hradādijam ।
gāṅgeyaṃ ca bhavet sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ śaṅkhe kali-priya ।।

trailokye yāni tīrthāni vāsudevasya cājñayā ।
śaṅkhe tiṣṭhanti viprendra tasmāt śaṅkhaṃ sadārcayet ।।

śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu pānīyaṃ sa-puṣpaṃ satilākṣatam ।
arghyaṃ dadāti devasya sa-sāgara-dharā-phalam ।।

arghyaṃ dattvā tu śaṅkhena yaḥ karoti pradakṣiṇam ।
pradakṣiṇī-kṛtā tena sapta-dvīpā vasundharā ।।

darśanenāpi śaṅkhasya kiṃ punaḥ sparśane kṛte ।
vilayaṃ yānti pāpāni himaṃ sūryodaye yathā ।।

nitye naimittike kāmye snānārcana-vilepane ।
śaṅkham udvahate yas tu śvetadvīpe vasec ciram ।।

natvā śaṅkhaṃ kare dhṛtvā mantreṇānena vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
yaḥ snāpayati govindaṃ tasya puṇyam anantakam ।।

mantraḥ

tvaṃ purā sāgarotpanno viṣṇunā vidhṛtaḥ kare ।
mānitaḥ sarva-devaiś ca pāñcajanya namo astu te ।।

tava nādena jīmūtā vitrasyanti surāsurāḥ ।
śaśāṅkāyuta-dīptābha pāñcajanya namo astu te ।।

garbhā devāri-nārīṇāṃ vilīyante sahasradhā ।
tava nādena pātāle pāñcajanya namo astu te ।।

vārāhe ca-
dakṣiṇāvarta-śaṅkhena tila-miśrodakena ca ।
udake nābhimātre tu yaḥ kuryād abhiṣecanam ।।

prāk srotasi ca nadyāṃ vai naras tv ekāgra-mānasaḥ ।
yāvaj jīva-kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat-kṣaṇād eva naśyati ।।

dakṣiṇāvarta-śaṅkhena pātre auḍumbare sthitam ।
udakaṃ yaḥ pratīccheta śirasā kṛṣṇa-mānasaḥ ।
tasya janma-kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat-kṣaṇād eva naśyati ।।

āgame- bṛhattvaṃ snigdhatācchatvaṃ śaṅkhasyeti guṇa-trayam ।।

āvarta-bhaṅga-doṣas tu hema-yogān na jāyate ।
nālikāyāṃ svabhāvena yadi chidraṃ bhaven nahi ।।

। iti।

ghaṇṭāvādyaṃ ca nitarāṃ snāna-kāle praśasyate ।
yato bhagavato viṣṇos tat sadā paramaṃ priyam ।।

āvāhanārghye dhūpe ca puṣpa-naivedya-yojane ।
nityam etāṃ prayuñjīta tan-mantreṇābhimantritām ।।

tan-mantraḥ

jaya-dhvaniṃ tato mantramātaḥ svāhety udīrya ca ।
abhyarcya vādayan ghaṇṭāṃ dhūpaṃ nīcaiḥ pradāpayet ।।

pūjā-kālaṃ vinānyatra hitaṃ nāsyāḥ pracālanam ।
na tayā ca vinā kuryāt pūjanaṃ siddhi-lālasaḥ ।।

atha ghaṇṭā-māhātmyam

uktaṃ ca skānde śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
snānārcana-kriyā-kāle ghaṇṭā-nādaṃ karoti yaḥ ।
purato vāsudevasya tasya puṇya-phalaṃ śṛṇu ।।

varṣa-koṭi-sahasrāṇi varṣa-koṭi-śatāni ca ।
vasate deva-loke tu apsaro-gaṇa-sevitaḥ ।।

sarva-vādya-mayī ghaṇṭā keśavasya sadā priyā ।
vādanāl labhate puṇyaṃ yajña-koṭi-samudbhavam ।।

vāditra-ninadais tūrya-gīta-maṅgala-nisvanaiḥ ।
yaḥ snāpayati govindaṃ jīvan-mukto bhaved dhi saḥ ।।

vāditrāṇām abhāve tu pūjā-kāle hi sarvadā ।
ghaṇṭā-śabdo naraiḥ kāryaḥ sarva-vādya-mayī yataḥ ।।

sarva-vādya-mayī ghaṇṭā devadevasya vallabhā ।
tasmāt sarva-prayatnena ghaṇṭā-nādaṃ tu kārayet ।।

manvantara-sahasrāṇi manvantara-śatāni ca ।
ghaṇṭā-nādena deveśaḥ prīto bhavati keśavaḥ ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare śrī-bhagavat-prahlāda-saṃvāde-
śṛṇu daityendra vakṣyāmi ghaṇṭā-māhātmyam uttamam ।
prahlāda tvat-samo nāsti mad-bhakto bhuvana-traye ।।

mama nāmāṅkitā ghaṇṭā purato mama tiṣṭhati ।
arcitā vaiṣṇava-gṛhe tatra māṃ viddhi daityaja ।।

vainateyāṅkitāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ sudarśana-yutāṃ yadi ।
mamāgre sthāpayed yas tu dehe tasya vasāmy aham ।।

yas tu vādayate ghaṇṭā vainateyena cihnitām ।
dhūpe nīrājanae snāne pūjā-kāle vilepane ।।

mamāgre pratyahaṃ vatsa pratyekaṃ labhate phalam ।
mamāyutaṃ go-yutaṃ ca cāndrāyaṇa-śatodbhavam ।।

vidhi-bāhya-kṛtā pūjā saphalā jāyate nṝṇām ।
ghaṇṭā-nādena tusṭo ahaṃ prayacchāmi svakaṃ padam ।।

nāgāri-cihnitā ghaṇṭā rathāṅgena samanvitā ।
vādanāt kurute nāśaṃ janma-mṛtyu-bhayasya ca ।।

garuḍenāṅktāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ dṛṣṭvāhaṃ pratyahaṃ sadā ।
prītiṃ karoti daityendra lakṣmīṃ prāpya yathādhanaḥ ।।

dṛṣṭvāmṛtaṃ yathā devāḥ prītiṃ kurvanty aharniśam ।
suparṇe ca tathā prītiṃ ghaṇṭā-śikhara-saṃsthite ।।

sva-kareṇa prakurvanti ghaṇṭā-nādaṃ sva-bhaktitaḥ ।
madīyārcana-kāle tu phalaṃ koṭy-aindavaṃ kalau ।।

anyatra ca-
ghaṇṭā-daṇḍasya śikhare sa-cakraṃ sthāpayet tu yaḥ ।
garuḍaṃ vai priyaṃ viṣṇoḥ sthāpitaṃ bhuvana-trayam ।।

sa-cakra- ghaṇṭā-nādaṃ tu mṛtyu-kāle śṛṇoti yaḥ ।
pāpa-koṭi-yutasyāpi naśyanti yama-kiṅkarāḥ ।।

sarve doṣāḥ pralīyante ghaṇṭā-nāde kṛte harau ।
devatānāṃ munīndrāṇāṃ pitṝṇām utsavo bhavet ।।

abhāve vainateyasya cakrasyāpi na saṃśayaḥ ।
ghaṇṭā-nādena bhaktānāṃ prasādaṃ kurute hariḥ ।।

gṛhe yasmin bhaven nityaṃ ghaṇṭā nāgāri-saṃyutā ।
na sarpāṇāṃ bhayaṃ tatra nāgni-vidyut-samudbhavam ।।

yasya ghaṇṭā gṛhe nāsti śaṅkhaś ca purato hareḥ ।
kathaṃ bhāgavataṃ nāma gīyate tasya dehinaḥ ।।

। iti।

ato bhagavataḥ prītyai ghaṇṭā śrī-garuḍānvitā ।
saṅgṛhyā vaiṣṇavair yatnāc cakreṇopari maṇḍitā ।।

snāne śaṅkhādi-vādyāṃ tu nāma-saṅkīrtanaṃ hareḥ ।
gītaṃ nṛtyaṃ purāṇādi-paṭhanaṃ ca praśasyate ।।

atha snāne vādyādi-māhātmyam

skanda-purāṇe-
snāna-kāle tu kṛṣṇasya śaṅkhādīnāṃ tu vādanam ।
kurute brahma-loke tu vasate brahma-vāsaram ।।

snāna-kāle tu samprāpte kṛṣṇasyāgre tu nartanam ।
gītaṃ caiva punāty atra ṛcoktaṃ vadanena hi ।।

tatraiva śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
mṛdaṅga-vādyena yutaṃ paṇavena samanvitam ।
arcanaṃ vāsudevasya sa-nṛtyaṃ mokṣadaṃ nṝṇām ।।

gītaṃ vādyaṃ ca nṛtyaṃ ca tathā pustaka-vācanam ।
pūjā-kāle tu kṛṣṇasya sarvadā keśava-priyam ।।

nṛtya-vādyādy-abhāve tu kuryāt pustaka-vācanam । pūjā-kāle tv idaṃ putra sarvadā prīti-dāyakam ।। । 
pustakasyāpy abhāve tu viṣṇu-nāma-sahasrakam ।
stava-rājaṃ mini-śreṣṭha gajendrasya ca mokṣaṇam ।।

pūjā-kāle tu devasya gītā-stotram anusmṛtiḥ ।
pañca-staavā mahā-bhāga mahā-prīti-karā hareḥ ।।

vihāya gīta-vādyāni pūjā-kāle sadā hareḥ ।
paṭhanīyaṃ mahā-bhaktyā viṣṇor nāma-sahasrakam ।।

dvārakā-māhātmye-
snāna-kāle tu kṛṣṇasya jaya-śabdaṃ karoti yaḥ ।
kara-tāḍana-saṃyuktaṃ gītaṃ nṛtyaṃ prakurvate ।।

unmatta-ceṣṭāṃ kurvāṇo hasan jalpan yathecchayā ।
nottāna-śāyī bhavati mātur aṅke nareśvara ।।

atha sahasra-nāma-māhātmyam

tatraiva-
snāna-kāle tu devasya paṭhen nāma-sahasrakam ।
pratyaksaraṃ labhet puṇyaṃ kapilā-go-śatodbhavam ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare-
kṛtvā nāma-sahasreṇa stutiṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ ।
viyogam āpnoti naraḥ sarvānarthair na saṃśayaḥ ।।

skānde śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
viṣṇor nāma-sahasraṃ tu pūjā-kāle paṭhanti ye ।
vedānāṃ caiva puṇyānāṃ phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ ।।

ślokenaikena devarṣe sahasra-nāmakasya yat ।
paṭhitena phalaṃ proktaṃ na tat kratu-śatair api ।।

mantra-hīnaṃ kriyā-hīnaṃ yat kṛtaṃ pūjanaṃ hareḥ ।
paripūrṇaṃ bhavet sarvaṃ sahasra-nāma-kīrtanāt ।।

kiṃ ca-
jñānājñāna-kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paṭhitvā viṣṇu-sannidhau ।
nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ viṣṇos tu prajahāti mahā-rujam ।।

brahma-hatyādi-pāpāni kāma-cāra-kṛtāny api ।
vilayaṃ yānti vai nūnam anya-pāpe tu kā kathā ।।

siddhyanti sarva-kāryāṇi manasā cintitāni ca ।
yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya viṣṇor nāma-sahasrakam ।।

tatraiva śrī-kṛṣṇārjuna-saṃvāde-
adhītās tena vai vedāḥ surāḥ sarva-samarcitāḥ ।
nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ yo adhīte muktis tasya kare sthitā ।।

kurvat pāpa-sahasrāṇi bhuñjāno api yatas tataḥ ।
paṭhen nāma-sahasras tu durgandhaṃ na sa paśyati ।।

muktvā nāma-sahasras tu nānyo dharmo asti kaścana ।
kalau prāpte guḍākeśa satyam etan mayeritam ।।

yajñair dānais tapabhiś ca stavaiḥ prītir na me'rjuna ।
santuṣṭis tu na cānyena vinā nāma-sahasrakam ।।

stavaṃ nāma-sahasrākhyaṃ ye na jānanti vai kalau ।
bhramanti te narī̀a loke sarva-dharma-bahiṣkṛtāḥ ।।

stavaṃ nāma-sahasrākhyaṃ likhitaṃ yasya veśmani ।
pūjyate mama sānnidhye pūjāṃ gṛhṇāmi tasya vai ।।

yasmin nāma-sahasraṃ me gṛhe tiṣṭhati sarvadā ।
likhitaṃ pāṇḍava-śreṣṭha tatra no viśate kaliḥ ।।

tasmāt tvam api kaunteya mad-bhakto man-manā bhava ।
paṭhan nāma-sahasraṃ me sarvān kāmān avāpsyasi ।।

aham ārādhitaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā loka-kartṛṇā ।
tato nāma-sahasraṃ me prāptaṃ loka-hitaṃ param ।।

nāradena tataḥ pūrvaṃ prāptaṃ ca parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
nāradena tataḥ prokta-vṛṣīṇām ūrdhva-retasām ।।

ṛṣibhis tu mahābāho devaloke prakāśitam ।
martya-loke manuṣyāṇāṃ vyāsena paribhāṣitam ।।

tapasogreṇa mahatā śaṅkareṇa mahātmanā ।
mat-prasādād anuprāptaṃ guhyānām uttamottamam ।।

dattaṃ bhavānyai rudreṇa nāmnāṃ me hi sahasrakam ।
viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu mayā te parikīrtitam ।।

aśeṣārtiharaṃ pārtha mama nāma-sahasrakam ।
sadyaḥ prīti-karaṃ puṇyaṃ surāṇām amṛtaṃ yathā ।।

aṣṭādaśa-purāṇānāṃ sārem etad dhanañjaya ।
mayoddhṛtya samākhyātaṃ tava nāma-sahasrakam ।।

sahasra-nāma-māhātmyaṃ devo jānāti śaṅkaraḥ ।
sahasra-nāma-māhātmyaṃ yaḥ paṭhec chṛṇuyād api ।
aparādha-sahasreṇa na sa lipyet kadācana ।।

atha śrī-bhagavad-gītā-māhātmyam

skānde avantī-khaṇḍe śrī-vyāsoktau -
gītā sugītā kartavyā kim anyaiḥ śāstra-vistaraiḥ ।
yā svayaṃ padma-nābhasya mukha-padmād viniḥsṛtā ।।

sarva-śāstra-mayī gītā sarva-deva-mayī yataḥ ।
sarva-dharma-mayī yasmāt tasmād etāṃ samabhyaset ।।

śālagrāma-śilāgre tu gītādhyāyaṃ paṭhet tu yaḥ ।
manvantara-sahasrāṇi vasate brahmaṇaḥ pure ।।

hatvā hatvā jagat sarvaṃ muṣitvā sa-carācaram ।
pāpair na lipyate caiva gītādhyāyī kathañcana ।।
