pañca-gavya-sahasrais tu prāśitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam ।।

prāyaścitte samutpanne kiṃ dānaiḥ kim upoṣañaiḥ ।
cāndrāyañaiś ca tṛrthaiś ca pṛtvā pādodakaṃ śuci ।।

bṛhan-nāradiye lubdhakopākhyānārambhe-
hari-pādodakaṃ yas tu kṣaña-mātraṃ ca dhārayet ।
sa snātaḥ sarva-tṛrthesu viṣñoḥ priyataras tathā ।।

akāla-mṛtyu-śamanaṃ sarva-vyādhi-vināśanam ।
sarva-duḥkhopaśamanaṃ hari-pādodakaṃ śubham ।।

tatraiva tad-upākhyānānte-
hari-pādodaka-sparśāl lubdhako vṛta-kalmaṣaḥ ।
divyaṃ vimānam āruhya munim enam athābravṛt ।।

hari-pādodakaṃ yasmān mayi tvaṃ kṣiptavān mune ।
prāpito asmi tvayā tasmāt tad viṣñoḥ paramaṃ padam ।।

hari-bhakti-sudhodaye-
pādaṃ pūrvaṃ kila spṛṣṭvā gaśgābhūt smartṛ-mokṣa-dā ।
viṣñoḥ sadyas tu sat-saśgi pādāmbu katham ṛḍyate ।।

tāpa-trayānalo yo asau na śāmyet sakalābdhibhiḥ ।
drutaṃ śāmyati so alpena śrṛmad-viṣñu-padāmbunā ।।

yuddhāstrābhedya-kavacaṃ bhavāgni-stambhanauṣadham ।
sarvāśgaiḥ sarvathā dhāryaṃ pādyaṃ śuci-padaḥ sadā ।।

amṛtatvāvahaṃ nityaṃ viṣñu-pādāmbu yaḥ pibet ।
sa pibaty amṛtaṃ nityaṃ māse māse tu devatāḥ ।।

māhātmyam iyad ity asya vaktā yo api sa nirbhayaḥ ।
nanv anargha-mañer mūlyaṃ kalpayann agham aśnute ।।

anyatrapi-
sa brahmacārṛ sa vratṛ āśramṛ ca sadā-śuciḥ ।
viṣñu-pādodakaṃ yasya mukhe śirasi vigrahe ।।

janma-prabhṛti-pāpānāṃ prāyaścittaṃ yadṛcchati ।
śālagrāma-śilā-vari pāpa-hāri niṣevyatām ।।

ata eva tejodravina-pañcaratre śrṛ-brahmañoktam- pṛṭha-prañālād udakaṃ pṛthag ādāya putraka । siñcayen mūrdhni bhaktānāṃ sarva-tṛrtha-mayaṃ hi tat ।। iti ।

pādodakasya māhātmyaṃ vikhyātaṃ sarva-śāstrataḥ ।
likhituṃ śaknuyat ko hi sindhūrmṛn gañayann api ।।

viśeṣataś ca pādodaṃ tulasṛ-dala-saṃyutam ।
śaśkhe kṛtvā vaiṣñavebhyo dattvā prāgvat pibet svayam ।।

atha śaśkha-kṛta-pādodaka-māhātmyaṃ

skānde śrṛ-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
kṛtvā pādodakaṃ śaśkhe vaiṣñavānāṃ mahātmanām ।
yo dadyāt tulasṛ-miśraṃ cāndrāyaña-śataṃ labhet ।।

gṛhṛtvā kṛṣña-pādāmbu śaśkhe kṛtvā tu vaiṣñavaḥ ।
yo vahet śirasā nityaṃ sa munis tapasottamaḥ ।।

pādme devadūta-vikuñḍala-saṃvāde-
śālagrāma-śilā-toyaṃ yadi śaśkha-bhṛtaṃ pibet ।
hatyā-koṭi-vināśaṃ ca kurute nātra saṃsayaḥ ।।

agastya-saṃhitāyām- śālagrāma-śilā-toyaṃ tulasṛ-dala-vāsitam । ye pibanti punas teṣāṃ stanya-pānaṃ na vidyate ।। iti । 
śrṛ-viṣñor vaiṣñavānāṃ ca pāvanaṃ carañodakam ।
sarva-tṛrtha-mayaṃ pṛtvā kuryād ācamanaṃ na hi ।।

tad uktaṃ skānde śivena-
viṣñoḥ pādodakaṃ pṛtvā paścād aśuci-śaśkayā ।
ācamati ca yo mohād brahma-hā sa nigadyate ।।

srutiś ca- bhagavān pavitraṃ bhagavat-pādau pavitraṃ, bhagavat-pādodakaṃ pavitraṃ, na tat-pāna ācamanṛyam । yathā hi soma iti ।।

sauparñe ca- viṣñu-pādodakaṃ pṛtvā bhakta-pādodakaṃ tathā । ya ācamati saṃmohād brahma-hā sa nigadyate ।। iti ।

tataḥ śuddhaṃ payaḥ-pūrñaṃ gandha-puṣpākṣatānvitam ।
adharopari sannyasec chaśkhaṃ bhagavad-agrataḥ ।।

atha śrṛ-bhagavad-agrataḥ śaśkha-sthapana-mahatamyaṃ

skānde brahma-nārada-saṃvāde śaśkha-māhātmye-
purato vāsudevasya sa-puṣpaṃ sa-jalākṣatam ।
śaśkham abhyarcitaṃ paśyet tasya lakṣmṛr na durlabhā ।।

sa-puṣpaṃ vāri-jaṃ yasya durvākṣata-samanvitam । purato vāsudevasya tasya śrṛḥ sarvato-mukhṛ ।। iti ।

bhūtvātha bhaktimān śrṛmat-tulasyā kānane prabhum ।
sampūjyābhyarcayet taṃ ca śrṛ-kṛṣña-caraña-priyam ।।

atha śrṛ-tulasṛ-vana-pūjā

prāg dattvārghyaṃ tato avyarcya gandha-puṣpākṣatādinā ।
stutvā bhagavatṛṃ tāṃ ca prañamet prārhtya dañḍavat ।।

athārghya-mantraḥ

śriyaḥ śriye śriyāvāse nityaṃ śrṛdhārā-satkṛte ।
bhaktyā dattaṃ mayā devi arghyaṃ gṛhña namo astu te ।।

pūjā mantraḥ

nirmitā tvaṃ purā devair arcitā tvaṃ surāsuraiḥ ।
tulasṛ hara me pāpaṃ pūjāṃ gṛhña namo astu te ।।

stutiś ca

mahā-prasāda-jananṛ sarva-saubhāgya-vardhinṛ ।
ādhi-vyādhi-haro nityaṃ tulasṛ tvaṃ namo astu te ।।

prārthanā

śrṛyaṃ dehi yaśo dehi kṛrtim āyus tathā sukham ।
balaṃ puṣṭiṃ tathā dharmaṃ tulasṛ tvaṃ prasṛda me ।।

prañāma-vākyam

avantṛ-khañḍe- 
yā dṛṣṭā nikhilāgha-saśgha-śamanṛ spṛṣṭā vapuḥ-pāvanṛ
rogāñām abhivanditā nirasinṛ siktāntaka-trāsinṛ ।
pratyāsatti-vidhāyinṛ bhagavataḥ kṛṣñasya saṃropitā
nyastā tac-carañe vimukti-phaladā tasyai tulasyai namaḥ ।।

bhagavatyās tulasyās tu māhātmyāmṛta-sāgare ।
lobhāt kūrditum icchāmi kṣudras tat kṣamyatāṃ tvayā ।।

atha tulasi-vana-puja-mahatmyam 
skānde-
śrāvaña-dvādaśṛ-yoge śālagrāma-śilārcane ।
yat phalaṃ saśgame proktaṃ tulasṛ-pūjanena tat ।।

gāruḍe-
dhātrṛ-phalena yat puñyaṃ jayantyāṃ samupoṣañe ।
khagendra bhavate nṛñāṃ tulasṛ-pūjanena tat ।।

prayāga-snāna-niratau kasyāṃ prāña-vimokṣañe ।
yat phalaṃ vihitaṃ devais tulasṛ-pūjanena tat ।।

agastya-saṃhitāyām
caturñām api varñānām āśramāñām viśeṣataḥ ।
strṛñāṃ ca puruṣāñāṃ ca pūjiteṣṭaṃ dadāti hi ।।

tulasṛ ropitā siktā dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā ca pāvayet ।
ārādhitā prayatnena sarva-kāma-phala-pradā ।।

atha tulasṛ-vana-pūja-māhātmyaṃ

pradakṣiñaṃ bhramitvā ye namaskurvanti nityaśaḥ ।
na teṣāṃ duritaṃ kiñcid akṣṛñam avaśiṣyate ।।

bṛhan-nāradiye yajñadhvajopākhyānānte-
pūjyamānā ca tulasṛ yasya veśmani tiṣṭhati ।
tasya sarvāñi śreyāṃsi vardhante ahar-ahar dvijāḥ ।।

ata eva pādme devadūta-vikuñḍala-saṃvāde-
pakṣe pakṣe tu samprāpte dvādaśyāṃ vaiśya-sattama ।
brahmādayo api kurvanti tulasṛ-vana-pūjanam ।।

ata eva śrṛ-tulasṛ-stuti-mahimā

ananya-manasā nityaṃ tulasṛṃ stauti yo naraḥ ।
pitṛ-deva-manuṣyāñāṃ priyo bhavati sarvadā ।।

atha tulasṛ-vana-māhātmyaṃ

skānde-
ratiṃ badhnāti nānyatra tulasṛ-kānanam vinā ।
deva-devo jagat-svāmṛ kali-kāle viśeṣataḥ ।।

hitvā tṛrtha-sahasrāñi sarvān api śiloccayan ।
tulasṛ-kānane nityaṃ kalau tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ ।।

nirṛkṣitā narair yais tu tulasṛ-vana-vāṭikā ।
ropitā yaiś ca vidhinā samprāptaṃ paramaṃ padam ।।

na dhātrṛ sa-phalā yatra na viṣñus tulasṛ-vanam ।
tat śmaśāna-samaṃ sthānaṃ santi yatra na vaiṣñavāḥ ।।

keśavārthe kalau ye tu ropayantṛha bhū-tale ।
kiṃ kariṣyaty asantuṣṭo yamo api saha kiśkaraiḥ ।।

tulasyā ropañaṃ kāryaṃ śravañena viśeṣataḥ ।
aparādha-sahasrāñi kṣamate puruṣottamaḥ ।।

devālayeṣu sarveṣu puñya-kṣetreṣu yo naraḥ ।
vāpayet tulasṛṃ puñyāṃ tat tṛrthaṃ cakra-pāñinaḥ ।।

ghaṭair yantra-ghaṭṛbhiś ca siñcitaṃ tulasṛ-vanam ।
jala-dhārābhir viprendra prṛñitaṃ bhuvana-trayam ।।

tatraiva śrṛ-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
tulasṛ-gandham ādāya yatra gacchati mārutaḥ ।
diśo daśa ca pūtāḥ syur bhūta-grāmāś catur-vidhāḥ ।।

tulasṛ-kānanodbhūtā chāyā yatra bhaved dvija ।
tatra śrāddhaṃ pradātavyam pitṅñāṃ tṛpti-hetave ।।

tulasṛ-bṛja-nikarāḥ patate yatra nārada ।
piñḍa-dānaṃ kṛtaṃ tatra pitṅñāṃ dattam akṣayam ।।

tatraivāgre-
dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā tathā dhyātā kṛrtitā namitā śrutā ।
ropitā sevitā nityaṃ pūjitā tulasṛ śubhā ।।

navadhā tulasṛṃ nityaṃ ye bhajanti dine dine ।
yuga-koṭi-sahasrāñi te vasanti harer gṛhe ।।

ropitā tulasṛ yāvat kurute mūla-vistaraṃ ।
tāvat koṭi-sahasraṃ tu tanoti sukṛtaṃ kalau ।।

yāvac chākhā-praśākhābhir bṛja-puṣpaiḥ phalair mune ।
ropitā tulasṛ pumbhir vardhate vasudhā-tale ।।

kule teṣāṃ tu ye jātā ye bhaviṣyanti ye mṛtaḥ ।
ākalpaṃ yuga-sāhasraṃ teṣāṃ vāso harer gṛhe ।।

tatraiva cāvantṛ-khañḍe-
tulasṛṃ ye vicinvanti dhanyās tat-kara-pallavāḥ ।
keśavārthe kalau ye ca ropayantṛha bhū-tale ।।

snāne dāne tathā dhyāne prāśane keśavārcane ।
tulasṛ dahate pāpaṃ ropañe kṛrtane kalau ।।

kāśṛ-khañḍe sva-dūtān prati śrṛ-yamānuśāsane-
tulasy-alaśkṛtā ye ye tulasṛ-nāma-jāpakāḥ ।
tulasṛ-vana-pālā ye te tyājyā dūrato bhaṭāḥ ।।

tatraiva dhruva-carite-
tulasṛ yasya bhavane praty-ahaṃ paripūjyate ।
tad-gṛhe nopasarpanti kadācid yama-kiśkarāḥ ।।

pādme devadūta-vikuñḍala-saṃvāde-
na paśyanti yamaṃ vaiśya tulasṛ-vana-ropañāt ।
sarva-pāpa-haraṃ sarva-kāmadaṃ tulasṛ-vanam ।।

tulasṛ-kānanaṃ vaiśya gṛhe yasmiṃs tu tiṣṭhate ।
tad-gṛhaṃ tṛrthṛ-bhūtaṃ hi no yānti yama-kiśkarāḥ ।।

tāvad varṣa-sahasrāñi yāvad bṛja-dalāni ca ।
vasanti deva-loke tu tulasṛṃ ropayanti ye ।।

tulasṛ-gandham āghrāya pitaras tuṣṭa-mānasāḥ ।
prayānti garuḍārūḍhās tat padaṃ cakra-pāñinaḥ ।।

darśanaṃ narmadāyās tu gaśgā-snānaṃ viśāṃ vara ।
tulasṛ-dala-saṃsparsaḥ samam etat trayaṃ smṛtam ।।

ropañāt pālanāt sekād darśanāt sparśanān nṛñām ।
tulasṛ dahate pāpaṃ vāś-manaḥ-kāya-sañcitam ।।

āmra-vṛkṣa-sahasreña pippalānāṃ śatena ca ।
yat phalaṃ hi tad ekena tulasṛ-vitapena tu ।।

viṣñu-pūjana-saṃyuktas tulasṛṃ yas tu ropayet ।
yugāyuta-daśaikaṃ sa ropako ramate divi ।।

tatraiva vaiśākha-māhātmye-
puṣkarādṛni tṛrthāni gaśgādyāḥ saritas tathā ।
vāsudevādayo devā vasanti tulasṛ-dale ।।

dāridrya-duḥkha-rogārti-pāpāni su-bahūny api ।
tulasṛ harati kṣipraṃ rogān iva harṛtakṛ ।।

tatraiva kārttika-māhātmye-
yad-gṛhe tulasṛ bhāti rakṣābhir jala-secanaiḥ ।
tad-gṛhe yama-dūtāś ca dūrato varjayanti hi ।।

tulasyās tarpañaṃ ye ca pitṅn uddiśya mānavāḥ ।
kurvanti teṣāṃ pitaras tṛptā varṣayutaṃ jalaiḥ ।।

paricaryāṃ ca ye tasya rakṣayābāla-bandhanaiḥ ।
śuśrūṣito haris tais tu nātra kāryā vicārañā ।।

nāvajñā jātu kāryāsyā vṛkṣa-bhāvān manṛṣibhiḥ ।
yathā hi vāsudevasya vaikuñṭha-bhoga-vigrahaḥ ।।

śālagrāma-śilā-rūpam sthāvaraṃ bhuvi dṛśyate ।
tathā lakṣmy-aikyam āpannā tulasṛ bhoga-vigrahā ।।

aparaṃ sthāvaraṃ rūpaṃ bhuvi loka-hitāya vai ।
spṛṣṭā dṛṣṭā rakṣitā ca mahā-pātaka-nāśinṛ ।।

agastya-saṃhitāyām
viṣños trailokya-nāthasya rāmasya janakātmajā ।
priyā tathaiva tulasṛ sarva-lokaika-pāvanṛ ।।

tulasṛ-vāṭikā yatra puṣpāntara-śatāvṛtā ।
śobhate rāghavas tatra sṛtayā sahitaṃ svayam ।।

tulasṛ-vipinasyāpi samantāt pāvanaṃ sthalam ।
krośa-mātraṃ bhavaty eva gāśgeyasyaiva pāthasaḥ ।।

tulasṛ-sannidhau prāñān ye tyajanti munṛśvara ।
na teṣāṃ naraka-kleśah prayānti paramaṃ padam ।।

kiṃ ca-
ananya-darśanāḥ prātar ye paśyanti tapo-dhana ।
aho-rātra-kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat-kṣañāt praharanti te ।।

gāruḍe-
kṛtaṃ yena mahā-bhāga tulasṛ-vana-ropañam ।
muktis tena bhaved dattā prāñināṃ vinatā-suta ।।

tulasṛ vāpitā yena puñyārāme vane gṛhe ।
pakṣṛndra tena satyoktaṃ lokāḥ sapta pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।

tulasṛ-kānane yas tu muhūrtam api viśramet ।
janma-koṭi-kṛtāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

pradakṣiñāṃ yaḥ kurute paṭhan nāma-sahasrakam ।
tulasṛ-kānane nityaṃ yajñāyuta-phalaṃ labhet ।।

hari-bhakti-sudhodaye-
nityaṃ sannihito viṣñuḥ sa-spṛhas tulasṛ-vane ।
api me'kṣata-patraikaṃ kaścid dhanyo arpayed iti ।।

bṛhan-nāradṛye gaśgā-prasaśge-
saṃsāra-pāpa-vicchedi gaśgā-nāma prakṛrtitam ।
tathā tulasyā bhaktiś ca hari-kṛrti-pravaktari ।।

tulasṛ-kānanaṃ yatra yatra padma-vanāni ca ।
purāña-paṭhanaṃ yatra tatra sannihito hariḥ ।।

tatraiva śrṛ-yama-bhagṛratha-saṃvāde-
tulasṛ-ropañaṃ ye tu kurvate manujeśvara ।
teṣāṃ puñya-phalaṃ vakṣye vadatas tvaṃ niśāmaya ।।

sapta-koṭi-kulair yukto mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tathā ।
vaset kalpa-śataṃ sāgraṃ nārāyaña-samṛpagaḥ ।।

tṛñāni tulasṛ-mūlāt yāvanty apahinoti vai ।
tāvatṛr brahma-hatyā hi chinnatty eva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tulasyā siñcayed yas tu culukodaka-mātrakam ।
kṣṛrodaśāyinā sārdhaṃ vased ācandra-tārakam ।।

kañṭakāvarañaṃ vāpi vṛtiṃ kāṣṭhaiḥ karoti yaḥ ।
tulasyāḥ śṛñu rājendra tasya puñya-phalaṃ mahat ।।

yāvad dināni santiṣṭhet kañṭakāvarañaṃ prabho ।
kula-traya-yutas tāvat tiṣṭhed brahma-pade yugam ।।

prākāra-kalpako yas tu tulasyā manujeśvara ।
kula-trayeña sahito viṣñoḥ sārūpyatāṃ vrajet ।।

ataiva tatraiva yajñadhvajopākhyānānte-
durlabhā tulasṛ-sevā durlabhā saśgatiḥ satām ।
durlabhā hari-bhaktiś ca saṃsārārñava-pātinām ।।

purāñāntareṣu-
yat phalaṃ kratubhiḥ sviṣṭaiḥ samāpta-vara-dakṣiñaiḥ ।
tat phalaṃ koṭi-guñitaṃ ropayitvā hareḥ priyām ।।

tulasṛṃ ye prayacchanti surāñām arcanāya vai ।
ropayanti śucau deśe teṣāṃ loko akṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

ropitāṃ tulasṛṃ dṛṣṭvā nareña bhuvi bhūmipa ।
vivarña-vadano bhūtvā tal-lipiṃ mārjayed yamaḥ ।।

tulasṛti ca yo brūyāt tri-kālaṃ vadane yadi ।
nityaṃ sa go-sahasrasya phalam āpnoti bhūsura ।।

tena dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ kṛtaṃ śrāddhaṃ gayāśire ।
tapas taptaṃ khaga-śreṣṭha tulasṛ yena ropitā ।।

śrutābhilaṣitā dṛṣṭā ropitā siñcitā natā ।
tulasṛ dahate pāpaṃ yugāntāgnir ivākhilam ।।

keśavāyatane yas tu kārayet tulasṛ-vanam ।
labhate cākṣayaṃ sthānaṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha vaiṣñavaḥ ।।

anyatrāpi-
tulasṛ-kānane śrāddhaṃ pitṅñāṃ kurute tu yaḥ ।
gayā-śrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena bhāṣitaṃ viṣñunā purā ।।

tulasṛ-gahanaṃ dṛṣṭvā vimukto yāti pātakāt ।
sarvathā muni-śārdūla brahmahā puñya-bhāg bhavet ।।

kiṃ ca, skānde vaśiṣṭha-māndhātṛ-saṃvāde- śukla-pakṣe yadā rājan tṛtṛyā budha-saṃyutā । śravañena mahābhāga tulasṛ cātipuñyadā ।। iti ।

prasaśgāt śrṛ-tulasyā hi mṛdaḥ kāṣṭhasya cādhunā ।
māhātmyaṃ likhyate kṛṣñe arpitasya dalasya ca ।।

atha śrṛ-tulasṛ-mṛttikā-kāṣṭhādi-māhātmyam

skānde śrṛ-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
bhūgatais tulasṛ-mūlair mṛttikā sparśitā tu yā ।
tṛrtha-koṭi-samā jñeyā dhāryā yatnena sā gṛhe ।।

yasmin gṛhe dvija-śreṣṭha tulasṛ-mūla-mṛttikā ।
sarvadā tiṣṭhate dehe devatā na sa mānuṣaḥ ।।

tulasṛ-mṛttikā-lipto yadi prāñān parityajet ।
yamena nekṣituṃ śakto yuktaḥ pāpa-śatair api ।।

śirasi kriyate yais tu tulasṛ-mūla-mṛttikā ।
vighnāni tasya naśyanti sānukūlā grahās tathā ।।

tulasṛ-mṛttikā yatra kāṣṭhaṃ patraṃ ca veśmani ।
tiṣṭhate muni-śārdūla niścalaṃ vaiṣñavaṃ padam ।।

atha vṛtti-sampadānaṃ

tatraivānyatra-
maśgalārthaṃ ca doṣa-ghnaṃ pavitrārthaṃ dvijottama ।
tulasṛ-mūla-saṃlagnāṃ mṛttikām āvahed budhaḥ ।।

tan-mūla-mṛttikāṃ yo vai dhārayiṣyati mastake ।
tasya tuṣṭo varān kāmān pradadāti janārdanaḥ ।।

bṛhan-nāradiye gaśgā-prasaśge-
tulasṛ-mūla-sambhūtā hari-bhakta-padodbhavā ।
gaśgodbhavā ca mṛl-lekhā nayaty acyuta-rūpatām ।।

gāruḍe
yad-gṛhe tulasṛ-kāṣṭham patraṃ śuṣkam athārdrakam ।
bhavate naiva pāpaṃ tad-gṛhe saśkramate kalau ।।

śrṛ-prahlāda-saṃhitāyāṃ tathā viṣñu-dharmottare'pi-
patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ tvak-śākhā-pallavāśkuram ।
tulasṛ-sambhavaṃ mūlaṃ pāvanaṃ mṛttikādy api ।।

homaṃ kurvanti ye viprās tulasṛ-kāṣṭha-vahninā ।
lave lave bhavet puñyam agniṣṭoma-śatodbhavam ।।

naivedyaṃ pacate yas tu tulasṛ-kāṣṭha-vahninā ।
meru-tulyaṃ bhaved annaṃ tad dattaṃ keśavāya hi ।।

śarṛraṃ dahyate yeṣāṃ tulasṛ-kāṣṭha-vahninā ।
na teṣāṃ punar āvṛttir viṣñu-lokāt kathañcana ।।

grasto yadi mahā-pāpair agamyāgamanādikaiḥ ।
mṛtaḥ śudhyati dāhena tulasṛ-kāṣṭha-vahninā ।।

tṛrthaṃ yadi na samprāptaṃ smṛtir vā kṛrtanam hareḥ ।
tulasṛ-kāṣṭha-dagdhasya mṛtasya na punar bhavaḥ ।।

yady ekaṃ tulasṛ-kāṣṭhaṃ madhye kāṣṭha-cayasya hi ।
daha-kāle bhaven muktih pāpa-koṭi-yutasya ca ।।

janma-koṭi-sahasrais tu toṣito yair janārdanaḥ ।
dahyante te janā loke tulasṛ-kāṣṭha-vahninā ।।

agastya-saṃhitāyām-
yaḥ kuryāt tulasṛ-kāṣṭhair akṣa-mālāṃ su-rūpiñṛm ।
kañṭha-mālāṃ ca yatnena kṛtaṃ tasyākṣayaṃ bhavet ।।

atha tulasṛ-patra-dhāraña-māhātmyam 
skānde śrṛ-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
yasya nābhi-sthitaṃ patraṃ mukhe śirasi karñayoḥ ।
tulasṛ-sambhavaṃ nityaṃ tṛrthais tasya makhaiś ca kim ।।

tatraivānyatra-
śatrughnaṃ ca supuñyaṃ ca śrṛ-karaṃ roga-nāśanam ।
kṛtvā dharmam avāpnoti śirasā tulasṛ-dalam ।।

yaḥ kaścid vaiṣñavo loke mithyācāro apy anāśramṛ ।
punāti sakalān lokān śirasā tulasṛṃ vahan ।।

bṛhan-nāradiye śrṛ-yama-bhagṛratha-saṃvāde-
karñena dhārayed yas tu tulasṛṃ satataṃ naraḥ ।
tat-kāṣṭhaṃ vāpi rājendra tasya nāsty upapātakam ।।

hari-bhakti-sudhodaye vaiṣñava-vipraṃ prati yamadūtanam uktau-
kasmād iti na jānṛmas tulasyā hi priyo hariḥ ।
gacchantaṃ tulasṛ-hastam rakṣañn evanugacchati ।।

purāñāntare ca-
yaḥ kṛtvā tulasṛ-patram śirasā viṣñu-tat-paraḥ ।
karoti dharma-kāryāñi phalam āpnoti cākṣayam ।।

garuḍa-purāñe-
mukhe tu tulasṛ-patram dṛṣṭvā śirasi karñayoḥ ।
kurute bhaskaris tasya duṣkṛtasya tu mārjanam ।।

tri-kālaṃ vinatā-putra prāśayet tulasṛṃ yadi viśiṣyate ।
kāya-śuddhiś cāndrāyaña-śataṃ vinā ।।

skānde śrṛ-vaśiṣtha-mandhatṛ-saṃvāde-
cāndrāyañat tapta-kṛcchrāt brahma-kūrcāt kuśodakāt ।
viśiṣyate kāya-śuddhis tulasṛ-patra-bhakṣañāt ।।

tathā ca tulasṛ-patra-bhakṣañād bhāva-varjitaḥ ।
pāpo api sad-gatiṃ prāpta ity etad api viśrutam ।।

tathā ca skānde śrṛ-brahma nāradaṃ prati kathite amṛta-saroddhare lubdhakopākhyānānte yamadūtan prati śrṛ-viṣñudūtanaṃ vacanaṃ-
kṣṛrābdhau mathyamāne hi tulasṛ kāma-rūpiñṛ ।
utpāditā mahā-bhāga lokoddhāraña-hetave ।।

yasyāḥ smaraña-mātreña darśanāt kṛrtanād api ।
vilayaṃ yānti pāpāni kiṃ punar viṣñu-pūjanāt ।।

jāta-rūpa-mayaṃ puṣpam padmarāga-mayaṃ śubham ।
hitvā tu ratna-jātāni gṛhñāti tulasṛ-dalam ।।

bhakṣitaṃ lubdhakenāpi patraṃ tulasṛ-sambhavam ।
paścād diṣṭāntam āpanno bhasmṛbhūtaṃ kalevaram ।।

sitāsitaṃ yathā nṛraṃ sarva-pāpa-kṣayāvaham ।
tathā ca tulasṛ-patram prāśitaṃ sarva-kāma-dam ।।

yathā jāta-balo vahnir dahate kānanādikam ।
prāśitaṃ tulasṛ-patraṃ yathā dahati pātakam ।।

yathā bhakti-rato nityaṃ naro dahati pātakam ।
tulasṛ-bhakṣañāt tat tad dahate pāpa-sañcayam ।।

cāndrāyaña-sahasrasya parakāñāṃ śatasya ca ।
na tulyaṃ jāyate puñyaṃ tulasṛ-patra-bhakṣañāt ।।

kṛtvā pāpa-sahasrāñi pūrve vayasi mānavaḥ ।
tulasṛ-bhakṣañān mucyet śrutam etat purā hareḥ ।।

tāvat tiṣṭhanti pāpāni dehināṃ yama-kiśkarāḥ ।
yāvan na tulasṛ-patraṃ mukhe śirasi tiṣṭhati ।।

amṛtād utthitā dhātrṛ tulasṛ viṣñu-vallabhā ।
smṛtā saśkṛrtitā dhyātā prāśitā sarva-kāma-dā ।।

tatraiva śrṛ-yamaṃ prati śrṛ-bhagavad-vakyaṃ-
dhātrṛ-phalaṃ ca tulasṛ mṛtyu-kāle bhaved yadi ।
mukhe yasya śire dehe durgatir nāsti tasya vai ।।

yukto yadi mahā-pāpaiḥ sukṛtaṃ nārjitaṃ kvacit ।
tathāpi dṛyate mokṣas tulasṛ bhakṣitā yadi ।।

lubdhakenātma-dehena bhakṣitaṃ tulasṛ-dalam ।
samprāpto mat-padaṃ nūnaṃ kṛtvā prāñasya saṃkṣayam ।।

purāñāntare ca- upoṣya dvādaśṛṃ śuddhāṃ parāñe tulasṛ-dalam । prāśayed yadi viprendra aśvamedhāṣṭakaṃ labhet ।। iti ।

tathaiva tulasṛ-sparsat kṛṣña-cakreña rakṣitaḥ ।
brahma-bandhur iti khyāto hari-bhakti-sudhodaye ।।

ata evoktam- kiṃ citram asyāḥ patitaṃ tulasyā dalaṃ jalaṃ vā patitaṃ punṛte । lagnādhibhāla-sthalam ālavāla- mṛtsnāpi kṛtsnāgha-vināśanāya ।। iti ।

śrṛmat-tulasyāḥ patrasya māhātmyaṃ yady apṛdṛśam ।
tathāpi vaiṣñavais tan na grāhyaṃ kṛṣñārpañaṃ vinā ।।

kṛṣña-priyatvāt sarvatra śrṛ-tulasyāḥ prasaśgataḥ ।
saśkṛrtyamānaṃ dhātryāś ca māhātmyaṃ likhyate adhunā ।।

atha dhātrṛ-māhātmyaṃ skānde brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
dhātrṛ-cchāyāṃ samāśritya yo arcayec cakra-pāñinām ।
puṣpe puṣpe aśvamedhasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।।

tatraivāgre-
dhātrṛ-cchāyāṃ tu saṃspṛśya kuryāt piñḍaṃ tu yo mune ।
muktiṃ prayānti pitaraḥ prasādān mādhavasya ca ।।

mūrdhni ghrāñe mukhe caiva dehe ca muni-sattama ।
dhatte dhātrṛ-phalaṃ yas tu sa mahātmā su-durlabhaḥ ।।

dhātrṛ-phala-viliptāśgo dhātrṛ-phala-vibhūṣitaḥ ।
dhātrṛ-phala-kṛtāhāro naro nārāyaño bhavet ।।

yaḥ kaścid vaiṣñavo loke dhatte dhātrṛ-phalaṃ mune ।
priyo bhavati devānāṃ manuṣyāñāṃ tu kā kathā ।।

yaḥ kaścid vaiṣñavo loke mithyācāro api duṣṭa-dhṛḥ ।
punāti sakalān lokān dhātrṛ-phala-dalānvitaḥ ।।

dhātrṛ-phalāni yo nityaṃ vahate kara-sampuṭe ।
tasya nārāyaño devo varam ekaṃ prayacchati ।।

dhatrṛ-phalaṃ ca bhoktavyaṃ kadācit kara-sampuṭāt ।
yaśaḥ śriyam avāpnoti prasādāc cakra-pāñinaḥ ।।

dhātrṛ-phalaṃ ca tulasṛ mṛttikā dvārakodbhavā ।
saphalaṃ jṛvitaṃ tasya tritayaṃ yasya veśmani ।।

dhātrṛ-phalais tu saṃmiśraṃ tulasṛ-dala-vāsitam ।
pibate vahate yas tu tṛrtha-koṭi-phalaṃ labhet ।।

yasmin gṛhe bhavet toyaṃ tulasṛ-dala-vāsitam ।
dhātrṛ-phalaiś ca viprendra gāśgeyaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam ।।

tulasṛ-dala-naivedyaṃ dhātryā yasya phalaṃ gṛhe ।
kavacaṃ vaiṣñavaṃ tasya sarva-pāpa-vināśanam ।।

brahma-purāñe ca-
dhātrṛ-phalāni tulasṛ hy anta-kāle bhaved yadi ।
mukhe caiva śirasy aśge pātakaṃ nāsti tasya vai ।।

kṛtvā tu bhagavat-pūjāṃ na tṛrthaṃ snānam ācaret ।
na ca devālayopetāspṛśya-saṃsparśanādinā ।।

atha snāna-viśeṣa-kalaḥ 
smṛty-artha-sāre-
na snāyād utsave tṛrthe māśgalyaṃ vinivartya ca ।
anuvrajya suhṛd-bandhūn arcayitveṣṭa-devatām ।।

viṣñu-smṛtau ca-
viṣñv-ālaya-samṛpa-sthān viṣñu-sevārtham āgatān ।
cāñḍālān patitān vāpi spṛṣṭvā na snānam ācaret ।।

deva-yatra-vivāheṣu yajñopakarañeṣu ca ।
utsaveṣu ca sarveṣu spṛṣṭāspṛṣṭir na vidyate ।।

evaṃ prātaḥ samabhyarcya śrṛ-kṛṣñaṃ tad-anantaram ।
śāstrābhyāsaṃ dvijaḥ śaktyā kuryād vipro viśeṣataḥ ।।

yad uktam-
śruti-smṛtṛ ubhe netre viprāñaṃ parikṛrtite ।
ekena vikalaḥ kāño dvābhyām andhaḥ prakṛrtitaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca kaurme vyasa-gṛtāyām-
yo anyatra kurute yatnaṃ anādhṛtya śrutiṃ dvijaḥ ।
sa samūḍho na sambhāṣyo veda-bāhyo dvijātibhiḥ ।।

na veda-patha-mātreña santusyed esa vai dvijaḥ ।
yathoktācāra-hinas tu paśke gaur iva sidati ।।

yo adhṛtya vidhivad vedaṃ vedārthaṃ na vicārayet । sa cāndhaḥ śūdra-kalpas tu padārthaṃ na prapadyate ।। iti ।

ato adhṛtyānvahaṃ vidvān athādhyāpya ca vaiṣñavaḥ ।
samarpya tac ca kṛṣñāya yateta nija-vṛttaye ।।
vṛttau satyāṃ ca śṛñuyāt sādhūn saśgatya sat-kathām ।।
saptama-skandhe [bhp ]-
ṛtāmṛtābhyāṃ jṛveta mṛtena pramṛtena vā ।
satyānrtābhyām api vā na sva-vṛttyā kadācana ।।

ṛtam uñcha-śilaṃ proktaṃ amṛtaṃ syād ayācitam ।
mṛtaṃ tu nityaṃ yācñā syāt pramṛtaṃ karṣañaṃ smṛtam ।।
satyānṛtaṃ tu vāñijyaṃ śva-vṛttir nṛca-sevanam ।।
ātmano nṛca-lokānāṃ sevanaṃ vṛtti-siddhaye ।
nitarāṃ nindyate sadbhir vaiṣñavasya viśeṣataḥ ।।

tad uktaṃ-
sevā śva-vṛttir yair uktā na samyak tair udāhṛtam ।
svacchanda-caritaḥ kva śvā vikrṛtāsuḥ kva sevakaḥ ।।

pañṛ-kṛtyātmanaḥ prāñān ye vartante dvijādhamāḥ । teṣāṃ durātmanām annaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyañaṃ caret ।। iti ।

śukla-vṛtter asiddhau ca bhojyānnān śūdra-vargataḥ ।
tathaiva grāhyāgrāhyāñi jānṛyāc chāstrato budhaḥ ।।

śukla-vṛttiś ca

śrṛ-viṣñu-dharmottare trtiya-khañḍe-
pratigraheña yal labdhaṃ yajyataḥ śiṣyatas tathā ।
gunānvitebhyo viprasya śuklaṃ tat tri-vidhaṃ smṛtam ।।

yuddhopakārāl labdhaṃ ca dañḍāc ca vyavahārataḥ ।
kṣatriyasya dhanaṃ śuklaṃ tri-vidhaṃ parikṛrtitam ।।

kṛṣi-vāñijya-go-rakṣaḥ kṛtvā śuklaṃ tathā viśaḥ ।
dvija-śuśrūṣayā labdhaṃ śuklaṃ śūdrasya kṛrtitam ।।

kramāgataṃ prṛti-dānaṃ prāptaṃ ca saha bhāryayā ।
aviśeṣena sarveṣāṃ dhanaṃ śuklaṃ prakṛrtitam ।।

atha grāhyāgrāhyāñi

kaurme tatraiva-
nādyāc chūdrasya vipro annaṃ mohād vā yadi kāmataḥ ।
na śūdra-yoniṃ vrajati yas tu bhuśkte hy anāpadi ।।

duṣkṛtaṃ hi manuṣyasya sarvam anne pratiṣṭhitam ।
yo yasyānnaṃ samaśnāti sa tasyāśnāti kilbiṣam ।।

ārdhikaḥ kula-mitraś ca sva-gopālaś ca nāpitaḥ ।
ete śūdreṣu bhojyānnā dattvā svalpa-pañaṃ budhaiḥ ।।

pāyasaṃ sneha-pakvaṃ yad go-rasaṃ caiva śaktavaḥ ।
piñyākaṃ caiva tailaṃ ca śūdrād grāhyaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

aśgirāḥ-
go-rasaṃ caiva śaktūṃś ca taila-piñyākam eva ca ।
apūpān bhakṣayec chūdrāt yat kiñcit payasā kṛtam ।।

atri-smṛtau-
sva-sutāyāś ca yo bhuśkte sa bhuśkte pṛthivṛ-malam ।
narendra-bhavane bhuktvā viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ ।।

dāsa-nāpita-gopāla- kula-mitrārdha-sṛriñaḥ ।
bhojyānnāḥ śūdra-varge amṛ tathātma-vinivedakaḥ ।।

madhūdakaṃ phalaṃ mūlam edhāṃsy-abhaya-dakṣiñā ।
abhyudyatāni tv etāni grāhyāñy api nikṛṣṭataḥ ।।

khala-kṣetra-gataṃ dhanyaṃ kūpa-vāpisu yaj jalam ।
agrāhyād api tad-grāhyaṃ yac ca goṣṭha-gataṃ payaḥ ।।

pānṛyaṃ pāyasaṃ bhakṣyaṃ ghṛtaṃ lavañam eva ca ।
hasta-dattaṃ na gṛhñṛyāt tulyaṃ go-māṃsa-bhakṣañaiḥ ।।

manu-smṛtau-
samudraṃ saindhavaṃ caiva lavañe paramādbhute ।
pratyakṣe api tu grāhye niṣedhas tv anya-gocaraḥ ।।

āyasenaiva pātreña yad annam upanṛyate ।
bhoktā tad viṭ-samaṃ bhuśkte dātā ca narakaṃ vrajet ।।

go-rakṣakān vāñijakān tathā kāruka-śṛlinaḥ ।
proṣyān vārdhūṣikāṃś caiva viprān śūdravad ācaret ।।

kaurme ca tatraiva-
tṛñaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ prakāśaṃ vai harer budhaḥ ।
dharmārthaṃ kevalaṃ vipra hy anyathā patito bhavet ।।

tila-mudga-yavādṛnāṃ muṣṭir grāhyā pathi sthitaiḥ ।
kṣudhārthair nānyathā vipra dharma-vidbhir iti sthitiḥ ।।

vaiṣñavānāṃ hi bhoktavyaṃ prārthyānnaṃ vaiṣñavaiḥ sadā ।
avaiṣñavānām annaṃ tu parivarjyam amedhyavat ।।

tathā ca pādme devadūta-vikuñḍala-saṃvāde-
prārthayed vaiṣñavād annaṃ prayatnena vicakṣañaḥ ।
sarva-pāpa-viśudhy-arthaṃ tad-abhāve jalaṃ pibet ।।

nāradiye-
mahā-pātaka-saṃyukto vrajed vaiṣñava-mandiram ।
yācayed annam amṛtaṃ tad-abhāve jalaṃ pibet ।।

viṣñu-smṛtau-
śrotriyānnaṃ vaiṣñavānnaṃ huta-śeṣaṃ ca yad-dhaviḥ ।
ānakhāt śodhayet pāpaṃ tuṣāgniḥ kanakaṃ yathā ।।

skānde mārkañḍeya-bhagṛratha-saṃvāde-
śuddhaṃ bhāgavatasyānnaṃ śuddhaṃ bhagṛrathi-jalam ।
śuddhaṃ viṣñu-paraṃ cittaṃ śuddham ekādaśṛ-vratam ।।

avaiṣñava-gṛhe bhuktvā pṛtvā vā jānato api vā ।
śuddhiś cāndrāyañe prokta iṣṭāpūrtaṃ vṛthā sadā ।।

śrṛ-prahlāda-vākye ca-
keśavārcā gṛhe yasya na tiṣṭhati mahṛ-pate ।
tasyānnaṃ naiva bhoktavyam abhakṣyeña samaṃ smṛtam ।।

kecid vṛtty-anapekṣasya japa-śraddhāvataḥ prabho ।
viśvastasyādiśanty asmin kāle api kṛtino japam ।।

atha madhyāhnika-kṛtyāni

madhyāhne snānataḥ pūrvaṃ puṣpādy āhṛtya vā svayam ।
bhṛtyādinā vā sampādya kuryān madhyāhnikṛḥ kriyāḥ ।।

snānāśaktau ca madhyāhne snānam ācārya māntrikam ।
yathoktaṃ bhagavat-pūjāṃ śaktaś cet prāgvad ācaret ।।

atha vaiṣñava-vaisvadevadi-vidhiḥ

tataḥ kṛṣñārpitenaiva śuddhenānena vaiṣñavaḥ ।
vaiśvadevādikaṃ daivaṃ karma paitraṃ ca sādhayet ।।

tad uktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe dina-vibhāge tu kuryāt pañca mahā-makhān ।
daivo homena yajñaḥ syāt bhautas tu bali-dānatah ।।

paitro viprānna-dānena paitreña balināthavā ।
kiñcid anna-pradānād vā tarpañād vā catur-vidhaḥ ।।

nṛ-yajño atithi-satkārāt hanta-kāreña cāmbunā ।
brahma-yajño veda-japāt purāña-paṭhanena vā ।।

tan-nityatā

kaurme-
akṛtvā tu dvijaḥ pañca mahā-yajñān dvijottamaḥ ।
bhuñjṛta cet su-mūḍhātmā tiryag-yoniṃ sa gacchati ।।

atha vaiṣñava-śrāddha-vidhiḥ

prāpte śrāddha-dine api prāg annaṃ bhagavate arpayet ।
tac-cheṣeñaiva kurvṛta śrāddhaṃ bhāgavato narah ।।

yac ca smṛtau- gṛhāgni-śiṣu-devānāṃ yatṛnāṃ brahmācāriñām । pitṛ-pāko na dātavyo yāvat piñḍān na nirvapet ।। iti ।

ṛdṛñ sāmānya-vacanam viśeṣa-vacana-vrajaih ।
śruti-smṛti-purāñādi- varttibhir bādhyate dhruvam ।।

tathā ca pādme-
viṣñor niveditānnena yaṣṭavyaṃ devatāntaram ।
pitṛbhyaś cāpi tad deyam tad ānantyāya kalpate ।।

mokṣa-dharme nāradoktau-
sātvataṃ vidhim āsthāya prāñ sūrya-mukha-nisṛtam ।
pūjāyām āsa deveśaṃ tac-cheṣeña pitāmahān ।।

brahmāñḍa-purāñe- 
yaḥ śrāddha-kāle hari-bhukta-śeṣam
dadāti bhaktyā pitṛ-devatānām ।
tenaiva piñḍāṃs tulasṛ-vimiśrān
ākalpa-koṭiṃ pitaraḥ su-tṛptāḥ ।।

skānde-
devān pitṅn samuddiśya yad viṣñor viniveditam ।
tān uddiśya tathā kuryāt pradānaṃ tasya caiva hi ।।

prayānti tṛptim atulāṃ sodakena tu tena vai ।
mukunda-gātra-lagnena brāhmañānāṃ vilepanam ।।

candanena tu piñḍanam kartavyaṃ pitṛ-tṛptaye ।
devānāṃ ca pitṅñāṃ ca jāyate tṛpti-rakṣayā ।।
evaṃ kṛte mahṛ-pala mā bhavet saṃśayaḥ kvacit ।।
tatraiva śrṛ-purusottama-khañḍe-
annādyaṃ śrāddha-kāle tu patitādyair nirṛkṣitam ।
tulasṛ-dala-miśreña salilenābhiṣiñcayet ।।

tad-annaṃ śuddhatām eti viṣñor naivedya-miśritam ।
viṣñor naivedya-śeṣaṃ tu tasmād deyaṃ dvijātmanām ।
piñḍe caiva viśeṣena pitṅñāṃ tṛptim icchatā ।।

tatraiva śrṛ-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
pitṅn uddiśya yaiḥ pūjā keśavasya kṛtā naraih ।
tyaktvā te nārakṛṃ pṛḍāṃ muktiṃ yānti mahā-mune ।।

dhanyās te mānavā loke kali-kāle viśeṣatah ।
ye kurvanti harer nityaṃ pitr-arthaṃ pūjanaṃ mune ।।

kiṃ dattair bahubhir piñḍair gayā-śrāddhādibhir mune ।
yair arcito harir bhaktyā pitr-arthaṃ ca dine dine ।।

yam uddiśya hareḥ pūjā kriyate muni-puśgava ।
uddhṛtya narakāvāsāt taṃ nayet paramaṃ padam ।।

yo dadāti hareḥ sthānaṃ pitṅn uddiśya nārada ।
kartavyaṃ hi pitṅñāṃ yat tat kṛtaṃ tena bho dvija ।।

śrutau ca- eka eva nārāyaña āsṛt, na brahmā, neme dyāvā-pṛthivyau, sarve devāḥ, sarve pitaraḥ, sarve manusyāḥ । viṣñunā aśitam aśnanti viṣñunāghrātaṃ jighranti, viṣñunā pṛtaṃ pibanti, tasmād vidhvaṃso viṣñūpāhṛtaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ ।। iti ।

ata evoktaṃ śrṛ-bhagavatā viṣñu-dharme-
prāñebhyo juhuyād annaṃ man-niveditam uttamam ।
tṛpyanti sarvadā prāñā man-nivedita-bhakṣañāt ।।

tasmāt sarva-prayatnena pradeyaṃ man-niveditam ।
mamāpi hṛdaya-sthasya pitṅñāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

kiṃ ca tatraivānyatra-
bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca yat kiñcid anivedyāgra-bhoktari ।
na deyaṃ pitṛ-devebhyaḥ prāyaścittṛ yato bhavet ।।

svargādau kathito devair agra-bhug bhagavān hariḥ ।
yajña-bhāga-bhujo devās tatas tena prakalpitāḥ ।।

skānde śrṛ-mārkañḍeya-bhagṛratha-saṃvāde-
yas tu vidyā-vinirmuktaṃ mūrkhaṃ matvā tu vaiṣñavam ।
vedavidbhyo avadād vipraḥ śrāddhaṃ tad rākṣasaṃ bhavet ।।

siktha-mātraṃ tu yad bhuśkte jalaṃ gañḍūṣa-mātrakam ।
tad-annaṃ meruñā tulyaṃ taj jalaṃ sāgaropamam ।।

brahma-purāñe śrṛ-brahma-vacanam-
śaśkhāśkita-tanur vipro bhuśkte yasya ca veśmani ।
tad-annaṃ svayam aśnāti pitṛbhiḥ saha keśavaḥ ।।

smṛtiś ca-
surābhāñḍastha-pṛyūṣaṃ yathā naśyati tat-kṣañāt ।
cakrāśka-rahitaṃ śrāddhaṃ tathā śātātapo abravṛt ।।

kiṃ ca, śrṛ-viṣñu-rahasye-
niveśayen naro mohād anya-paśktau hareḥ priyam ।
sa paten niraye ghore paśkti-bhedṛ narādhamaḥ ।।

atha śrṛ-bhagavad-arpañe niṣiddham

niveditaṃ yad anyasmai tad ucchiṣṭaṃ hi kathyate ।
ataḥ kathañcid api tan na śrṛ-bhagavate'rpayet ।।

tathā caikādaśa-skandhe śrṛ-bhagavad-uktau [bhp ]- api dṛpāvalokaṃ me nopayuñjyān niveditam ।।

nāradṛye-
pitṛ-śeṣaṃ tu you dadyād dharaye paramātmane ।
retodāḥ pitaras tasya bhavanti kleśa-bhāginaḥ ।।

śrṛ- viṣñu-dharme-
hari-śeṣaṃ havir dadyāt pitṅñām akṣayaṃ bhavet ।
na punaḥ pitṛ-śeṣaṃ tu harer brahmādi-sad-guroḥ ।।

anyatra ca- dakṣādayaś ca pitaro bhṛtyā indrādayaḥ surāḥ । atas tad-bhakta-śeṣaṃ tu viṣñor naiva nivedayet ।। iti ।

evam āvaśyakaṃ kṛtvā vaiṣñavebhyo vibhajya ca ।
śrṛman-mahā-prasādānnaṃ bhuñjṛta saha bandhubhiḥ ।।

tathā ca prahlāda-pañcarātre-
svabhāvasthaiḥ karma-jaḍān vañcayan draviñādibhiḥ ।
harer naivedya-sambhārān vaiṣñavebhyaḥ samarpayet ।।

ataiva vaiṣñava-tantre-
harer niveditaṃ kiñccin na dadyāt karhicid budhaḥ ।
abhaktebhyaḥ saśalyebhyo yad davan niraye vrajet ।।

viṣñu-dharmottare- avaiṣñave deva-dhṛtaṃ nirmālyaṃ na prayacchati । naivedyaṃ vā mahābhāga tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ ।। iti ।

kathañcid api nāśnṛyād akṛtvā kṛṣña-pūjanam ।
na cāsamarpya govinde kiñcid bhuñjṛta vaiṣñavaḥ ।।

atha pūjā-vyatirikta-bhojana-doṣāḥ

śrṛ-kūrma-purāñe-
anarcayitvā govindaṃ yair bhuktaṃ dharma-varjitaiḥ ।
śvāna-viṣṭhā-samaṃ cānnaṃ nṛraṃ ca surayā samam ।।

kiṃ ca-
yo mohād athavālasyād akṛtvā devatārcanam ।
bhuśkte sa yāti narakaṃ śūkareṣv iha jāyate ।।

viṣñu-dharmottare-
eka-kālaṃ dvikālaṃ vā tri-kālaṃ pūjayed dharim ।
apūjya bhojanaṃ kurvan narakāñi vrajen naraḥ ।।

nāradṛye ca-
prātar madhyandinaṃ sāyaṃ viṣñu-pūjā smṛtā budhaiḥ ।
aśakto vistareñaiva prātaḥ sampūjya keśavam ।।

madhyāhne caiva sāyaṃ ca puṣpāñjalim api kṣipet ।
madhyāhne vā vistareña saṃkṣepeñāthavā harim ।।
sambhojya bhojanaṃ kuryād anyathā narakaṃ vrajet ।।
athānarpita-bhoga-niṣedhaḥ

hāyaśṛrṣa-pañcarātre-
na tv evāpūjya bhuñjṛta bhagavantaṃ janārdanam ।
na tat svayaṃ samaśnṛyāt yad viṣñau na nivedayet ।।

brahmāñḍa-purāñe -
patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyam anna-pānādyam auṣadham ।
anivedya ca bhuñjṛta yad āhārāya kalpitam ।।

anivedyaṃ tu bhuñjānaḥ prāyaścittṛ bhaven naraḥ ।
tasmāt sarvaṃ nivedyaiva viṣñor bhuñjṛta sarvadā ।।

pādme gautamāmbarṛṣa-saṃvāde-
ambarṛṣa gṛhe pakvaṃ yad abhṛṣṭaṃ sadātmanaḥ ।
anivedya harer bhuñjan sapta-kalpāni nārakṛ ।।

tatraivottara-kāñḍe śivomā-saṃvāde -
avaiṣñavānāṃ yac cānnaṃ patitānāṃ tathaiva ca ।
anarpitaṃ tathā viṣñau śva-māṃsa-sadṛśaṃ bhavet ।।

viṣñu-smṛtau-
anivedya tu yo bhuśkte haraye paramātmane ।
majjanti pitaras tasya narake śāśvatṛḥ samāḥ ।।

ataiva gautmāmbarṛṣa-saṃvāde-
ambarṛṣa navaṃ vastraṃ phalam annaṃ rasādikam ।
kṛtvā viṣñūpabhuktaṃ tu sadā sevyaṃ hi vaiṣñavaiḥ ।।

viṣñu-dharmāgnipurāñayoḥ-
gandhānna-vara-bhakṣyāṃś ca srajo vāsāṃsi bhūṣañam ।
dattvā tu devadevāya tac-cheṣāñy upabhuñjate ।।

gāruḍe-
pādodakaṃ piben nityaṃ naivedyaṃ bhakṣayed dhareḥ ।
śeṣāś ca mastake dhāryā iti vedānuśāsanam ।।

ṣaṣṭha-skandhe puṃsavana-vrata-prasaśge [bhp ]-
udvāsya devaṃ sve dhāmni tan niveditam agrataḥ ।
adyād ātma-viśuddhy-arthaṃ sarva-kāmārtha-siddhaye ।।

aṣṭama-skandhe ca payo-vrata-prasaśge [bhp ]- niveditaṃ tad-bhaktāya dadyād bhuñjṛta vā svayam ।।

gautamṛya-tantre-
śuklopacāra-sambhārair nityaśo harim arcayet ।
nivedya kṛṣñāya vidhivad annaṃ bhuñjṛta tat svayam ।
athavā sātvate dadyād yadi labhyate bhaktitaḥ ।।

śarat-pradṛpe ca-
bhakta-kṣaña-kṣaño devaḥ smṛtiḥ sevā sva-veśmani ।
sva-bhojyasyārpañaṃ dānaṃ phalam indrādi-durlabham ।।

atha naivedya-bhakṣaña-vidhiḥ

dṛṣṭvā mahā-prasādānnaṃ tat prāś natvābhimantrayet ।
sveṣṭa-nāmnā tato mūla-manunā vāra-saptakam ।।

dharmarājādi-bhāgaṃ cāpāsya śrṛ-carañāmṛtam ।
tulasṛṃ cātra nikṣipya ślokān saśkṛrtayed imān ।।

yasyocchiṣṭaṃ hi vāñchanti brahmādyā ṛṣayo amalāḥ ।
siddhādyāś ca hares tasya vayam ucchiṣṭa-bhojinaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
yasya nāmnā vinaśyanti mahāpātaka-rāśayaḥ ।
tasya śrṛ-kṛṣña-devasya vayam ucchiṣṭa-bhojinaḥ ।।

ucchiṣṭa-bhojinas tasya vayam adbhuta-karmañaḥ ।
yo bālya-lṛlayā tāṃs tān pūtanādṛn apātayat ।।

ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ]-
tvayopabhukta-srag-gandha-vāso alaśkāra-carcitāḥ ।
ucchiṣṭa-bhojino dāsās tava māyāṃ jayemahi ।।

yato amṛtopastarañam asṛty uktvā yathā-vidhi ।
pañca prāñāhutṛḥ kṛtvā bhuñjṛta purataḥ prabhoḥ ।।

śrṛ-viṣñu-purāñe [vip ] aurva-sagara-saṃvāde- praśasta-ratna-pāñis tu bhuñjṛta prayato gṛhṛ ।।

puñya-gandhau śasta-mālya-dhārṛ caiva nareśvara ।
naika-vastra-dharo athārdra-pāñi-pādo mahṛpate ।।

viśuddha-vadanaḥ prṛto bhuñjṛta na vidiś-mukhaḥ ।
prāś-mukhodaś-mukho vāpi na caivānya-manā naraḥ ।।

dattvā tu bhaktaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ kṣudhitebhyas tathā gṛhṛ ।
praśasta-śuddha-pātre tu bhuñjṛtākupito dvijaḥ ।।

nāsandi-saṃsthite pātre nādeśe ca nareśvara ।
nākāle nātisaśkṛrñe dattvāgraṃ ca naro agnaye ।
nāśeṣaṃ puruṣo aśnṛyād anyatra jagatṛ-pate ।।

madhvambhu-dadhi-sarpibhyaḥ saktubhyaś ca vivekavān ।
aśnṛyāt tan-mayo bhūtvā pūrvaṃ tu madhuraṃ rasam ।।

lavañāmle tathā madhye kaṭu-tiktādikāṃs tataḥ ।
prāg dravaṃ puruṣo aśnṛyān madhye kaṭhināśanam ।।

ante punar dravāśṛ tu balārogye na muñcati ।
pañca-grāsaṃ mahā-maunaṃ prāñādyāpyāyanāya tat ।।

bhuktvā samyag athācamya prāś-mukhodaśmukho api vā ।
yathāvat punar ācāmet pāñṛ prakṣālya mūlataḥ ।।

svasthaḥ praśānta-cittas tu kṛtāsana-parigrahaḥ ।
abhṛṣṭa-devatānāṃ tu kurvṛta smarañaṃ naraḥ ।।

agastir agnir baḍavānalaś ca
bhuktaṃ mayānnaṃ jarayatv aśeṣam ।
sukhaṃ ca me tat-pariñāma-sambhavaṃ
yacchantv arogo mama cāstu dehe ।।

viṣñuḥ samastendriya-deha-dehṛ
pradhāna-bhūto bhagavān yathaikaḥ ।
satyena tenāttam aśeṣam annam
ārogyadaṃ me pariñāmam etu ।।

ity uccārya sva-hastena parimṛjya tathodaram ।
anāyāsa-pradāyṛni kuryāt karmāñy atandritaḥ ।।

kaurme vyāsa-gṛtāyām-
prāś-mukho annāni bhuñjṛta sūryābhimukham eva vā ।
āsṛnaḥ svāsane siddhe bhūmyāṃ pādau nidhāya ca ।।

āyuṣyaṃ prāś-mukho bhuśkte yaśasyaṃ dakṣiñāmukhaḥ ।
śriyaṃ pratyaś-mukho bhuśkte ṛtaṃ bhuśkte udaś-mukhaḥ ।।

pañcārdro bhojanaṃ kuryād bhūmau pātraṃ nidhāya ca ।
upavāsena tat tulyaṃ manur āha prajāpatiḥ ।।

upalipte śucau deśe pādau prakṣālya vai karau ।
ācamyārdrānano akrodhaḥ pañcārdro bhojanaṃ caret ।।

mahā-vyāhṛtibhis tv annaṃ parivāryodakena tu ।
amṛtopastarañam asṛtyapośāna-kriyāṃ caret ।।

svāhā-prañava-saṃyuktāṃ prāñāyety āhutiṃ tataḥ ।
apānāya tato hutvā vyānāya tad-anantaram ।।

udānāya tataḥ kuryāt samānāyeti pañcamṛm ।
vijñāya tattvam eteṣāṃ juhuyād ātmani dvijāḥ ।।

śeṣam annaṃ yathākāmaṃ bhuñjṛta vyañjanair yutam ।
dhyātvā tan-manasā devam ātmānaṃ vai prajāpatim ।।
amṛtāpidhānam asṛty upariṣṭād apaḥ pibet ।।
kiṃ ca, tatraiva-
yad bhuśkte veṣṭita-śirā yac ca bhuśkte vidiś-mukhaḥ ।
sopānatkaś ca yad bhuśkte sarvaṃ vidyāt tad āsuram ।।

nārdha-rātre na madhyāhne nājṛrñaṃ nārdra-vastra-dhṛk ।
na ca bhinnāsana-gato na yāne saṃsthito api vā ।।

na bhinna-bhājane caiva na bhūmyāṃ na ca pāñiṣu ।
anārogyam anāyuṣyam asvargyaṃ cātibhojanam ।
apuñyaṃ loka-vidviṣṭaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।।

kiṃ ca- na vāma-hastenoddhṛtya pibed vaktreña vā jalam ।।

viṣñu-smṛtau-
pibataḥ patate toyaṃ bhājane mukha-nirgayam ।
abhojyaṃ tad bhaved annaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyañaṃ caret ।।

mārkañḍeye-
bhuñjṛtānnaṃ ca tac-citto hy antarjāsu sadā naraḥ ।
upaghātād ṛte doṣānnānnasyodṛrayed budhaḥ ।।

anyatra ca-
hastādṛte'mbunānyenān aśnan pātrād ṛte pibet ।
dakṣiñaṃ tu parityajya vāme nṛraṃ nighāpayet ।
abhojyaṃ tad bhaved annaṃ pānṛyaṃ ca surā-samam ।।
tṛpto dadyād dhi tad-annaṃ śeṣaṃ durgata-tṛptaye ।।samyag ācamya dakṣāśghrer aśguṣṭhe vāri nikṣipet ।।
tataḥ saṃsmṛtya santuṣṭaḥ puṣṭidām iṣṭa-devatām । sannikṛṣṭair vṛtaḥ śiṣṭair japed anna-pater manūn । annapate'nnasya no dehi ।। ity ādi ।

bhakṣayed atha tāmbūlaṃ prasādaṃ vallavṛ-prabhoḥ ।
śiṣṭair iṣṭair japed divyaṃ bhagavan nāma-maśgalam ।।

atha naivedya-māhātmyam 
vārāhe-
yo mamaivārcanaṃ kṛtvā tatra prāpañam uttamam ।
śeṣam annaṃ śam aśnāti tataḥ saukhyataraṃ nu kim ।।

skānde-
tavopahāraṃ bhuktvā yaḥ sevate yajña-pūruṣam ।
sevitaṃ tena niyataṃ puroḍāśo mahādhiyā ।।

kiṃ ca tatraiva- 
śaśkhodakaṃ tṛrtha-varād variṣṭhaṃ
pādodakaṃ tṛrtha-gañād gariṣṭham ।
naivedya-śeṣaṃ kratu-koṭi-puñyaṃ
nirmālya-śeṣaṃ vrata-dāna-tulyam ।।

naivedya-śeṣaṃ tula-sṛvi-miśraṃ
viśeṣataḥ pāda-jalena siktam ।
yo aśnāti nityaṃ purato murāreḥ
prāpnoti yajñāyuta-koṭi-puñyam ।।

ṣaḍbhir māsopavāsais tu yat phalaṃ parikṛrtitam ।
viṣñor naivedya-śeṣe yat phalaṃ tad bhuñjatāṃ kalau ।।

kiṃ ca, tatra śrṛ-śālagrāma-śilā-māhātmye-
bhaktyā bhunakti naivedyaṃ śālagrāma-śilārpitam ।
koṭiṃ makhasya labhate phalaṃ śata-sahasraśaḥ ।।

brahma-vāri-gṛhasthaiś ca vānaprasthaiś ca bhikṣubhiḥ ।
bhoktavyaṃ viṣñu-naivedyaṃ nātra kāryā vicārañā ।।

bhuktvānya-deva-naivedyaṃ dvijaś cāndrāyañaṃ caret ।
bhuktvā keśava-naivedyaṃ yajña-koṭi-phalaṃ labhet ।।

tatraiva śrṛ-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde-
agniṣṭoma-sahasrais tu vājapeya-śatair api ।
tat phalaṃ prāpyate nūnaṃ viṣñor naivedya-bhakṣañāt ।।

hṛdi rūpaṃ mukhe nāma naivedyam udare hareḥ ।
pādodakaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ mastake yasya so acyutaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca-
pāvanaṃ viṣñu-naivedyaṃ sura-siddharṣibhiḥ smṛtam ।
anya-devasya naivedyaṃ bhuvattvācāndrāyañaṃ caret ।।

koṭi-yajñais tu yat puñyaṃ māsopoṣaña-koṭibhiḥ ।
tat phalaṃ prāpyate pumbhir viṣñor naivedya-bhakṣañāt ।।

tulasyāś ca rajo-juṣṭaṃ naivedyasya ca bhakṣañam ।
nirmālyaṃ ca dhṛtaṃ yena mahā-pātaka-nāśanam ।।

bṛhad-viṣñu-purāñe 
naivedyaṃ jagadṛśasya anna-pānādikaṃ ca yat ।
brahmavan nirvikāraṃ hi yathā viṣñus tathaiva tat ।।
vikāraṃ ye prakurvanti bhakṣañe tad dvijātayaḥ ।।
kuṣṭha-vyādhi-samāyuktāḥ putra-dāra-vivarjitāḥ ।
nirayaṃ yānti te viprā yasmān nāvartate punaḥ ।।

viṣñudharmottare-
navam annaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ nivedya madhusūdane ।
paścād bhuśkte svayaṃ yaś ca tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ ।।

brahmāñḍa-purāñe-
mukundāśana-śeṣaṃ tu yo hi bhuśkte dine dine ।
sikthe sikthe bhavet puñyaṃ cāndrāyaña-śatādhikam ।।

anyatrāpi- ekādaśṛ-sahasrais tu māsopoṣaña-koṭibhiḥ । tat phalaṃ prāpyate pumbhir viṣñor naivedya-bhakṣañāt ।। iti ।

tato yathoktam ācamya tāmbūlādi vibhajya ca ।
mahā-prasādaṃ dāsyena gṛhñṛyāt prayataḥ svayam ।।

tathā ca navama-skandhe śrṛmad-ambarṛṣa-carite [bhp ]-
kāmaṃ ca dāsye na tu kāma-kāmyayā
yathottamaśloka-janāśrayā ratiḥ ।।

naivedya-bhakṣañe yac ca nirmālya-grahañe ca yat ।
māhātmyam ādau likhitaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvam ihāpi tat ।।

iti śrṛ-gopāla-bhaṭṭa-vilikhite śrṛ-bhagavad-bhakti-vilāse mahā-prasādo nāma navamo vilāsaḥ ।

satsamgama-vilasa

daśama-vilāsaḥ

śrī-kṛṣṇa-caraṇāmbhoja-madhupebhyo namo namaḥ ।
kathañcid āśrayād yeṣāṃ śvāpi tad-gandha-bhāg bhavet ।।

atha śrī-kṛṣṇa-bhaktānāṃ sabhāṃ sa-vinayaṃ śubhām ।
gacched vaiṣṇava-cihnāḍhyaḥ pātuṃ kṛṣṇa-kathā-sudhām ।।

tathā ca smṛtiḥ - itihāsa-purāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭha-saptamakau nayet ।।

atha śrī-bhagavad-bhaktānāṃ lakṣaṇāni -
sāmānyataḥ laiṅge -
viṣṇur eva hi yasyaiṣa devatā vaiṣṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

atra viśeṣaḥ -
vrata-karma-guṇa-jñāna-bhoga-janmādimatsv api ।
śaiveṣv api ca kṛṣṇasya bhaktāḥ santi tathā tathā ।।

atra vratiṣu madhye bhagavad-bhakti-hetu-vrata-paratā bhagavad-bhakta-lakṣaṇam

tathā skānde śrī-mārkaṇḍeya-bhagīratha-saṃvāde -
daśamī-śeṣa-saṃyuktaṃ dinaṃ vaiṣṇava-vallabham ।
nopāsate mahīpāla te vai bhāgavatā narāḥ ।।

prāṇātyaye na cāśnanti dinaṃ prāpya harer narāḥ ।
kurvanti jāgaraṃ rātrau sadā bhāgavatā hi te ।।

upoṣya dvādaśīṃ śuddhāṃ rātrau jāgaraṇānvitām ।
alpāṃ tu sādhayed yas tu sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ ।।

bhaktir na vicyutā yeṣāṃ na cyutāni vratāni ca ।
supriyaḥ śrīpatir yeṣāṃ te syur bhāgavatā narāḥ ।।

karmiṣu bhagavad-arpaṇādinā tad-ājñā-buddhyā vā bhakti-hetuḥ sadācāra-paratā ।
dharmārthaṃ jīvitaṃ yeṣāṃ santānārthaṃ ca maithunam ।
pacanaṃ vipramukhyārthaṃ jñeyās te vaiṣṇavā narāḥ ।।

adhvagaṃ tu pathi śrāntaṃ kāle'tra gṛham āgatam ।
yo atithiṃ pūjayed bhaktyā vaiṣṇavaḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ ।।

sadācāra-ratāḥ śiṣṭāḥ sarva-bhūtānukampakāḥ ।
śucayas tyakta-rāgā ye sadā bhāgavatā hi te ।।

pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye śrī-nāradāmbarīṣa-saṃvāde -
jīvitaṃ yasya dharmārthaṃ dharmo hary-artham eva ca ।
aho-rātrāṇi puṇyārthaṃ taṃ manye vaiṣṇavaṃ bhuvi ।।

laiṅge ca -
viṣṇu-bhakti-samāyuktān śrauta-smārta-pravartakān ।
prīto bhavati yo dṛṣṭvā vaiṣṇavo asau prakīrtitaḥ ।।

guṇavatsu bhakti-hetuḥ kṛpālutvādi-sad-guṇa-śīlatā ।

skānde tatraiva -
para-duḥkhenātma-duḥkhaṃ manyante ye nṛpottama ।
bhagavad-dharma-niratās te narā vaiṣṇavā nṛpa ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe śrī-kapila-devahūti-saṃvāde -
titikṣavaḥ kāruṇikāḥ suhṛdaḥ sarva-dehinām ।
ajāta-śatravaḥ śāntāḥ sādhavaḥ sādhu-bhūṣaṇāḥ ।।

pañcama-skandhe ṛṣabhadevasya putrānuśāsane 
mahat-sevāṃ dvāram āhur vimuktes
tamo-dvāraṃ yoṣitāṃ saṅgi-saṅgam ।
mahāntas te sama-cittāḥ praśāntā
vimanyavaḥ suhṛdaḥ sādhavo ye ।।

ekādaśa-skandhe bhagavat-pradattoddhava-praśnottare -
kṛpālur akṛta-drohas titikṣuḥ sarva-dehinām ।
satya-sāro anavadyātmā samaḥ sarvopakārakaḥ ।।

kāmair ahata-dhīr dānto mṛduḥ śucir akiñcanaḥ ।
anīho mita-bhuk śāntaḥ sthiro mac-charaṇo muniḥ ।।

apramatto gabhīrātmā dhṛti-māñ jita-ṣaḍ-guṇaḥ ।
amānī māna-daḥ kalyo maitraḥ kāruṇikaḥ kaviḥ ।।

viṣṇu-purāṇe yama-tad-bhaṭa-saṃvāde [vip ] - 
na calati nija-varṇa-dharmato yaḥ
sama-matir ātma-suhṛd-vipakṣa-pakṣe ।
na harati na hanti kiñcid uccaiḥ
sthita-manasaṃ tam avehi viṣṇu-bhaktam ।।

jñāniṣu bhakti-hetur jñānavattā । ekādaśe havi-yogeśvarottare [bhp ] -
sarva-bhūteṣu yaḥ paśyed bhagavad-bhāvam ātmanaḥ ।
bhūtāni bhagavaty ātmany eṣa bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

na yasya svaḥ para iti vitteṣv ātmani vā bhidā ।
sarva-bhūta-samaḥ śāntaḥ sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

ekādaśe śrī-bhagavad-uktau [bhp ] -
jñātvājñātvātha ye vai māṃ yāvān yaś cāsmi yādṛśaḥ ।
bhajanty ananya-bhāvena te me bhakta-tamā matāḥ ।।

tatraiva havi-yogeśvarottare [bhp ]
īśvare tad-adhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca ।
prema-maitrī-kṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ ।।

arcāyām eva haraye pūjāṃ yaḥ śraddhayehate ।
na tad-bhakteṣu cānyeṣu sa bhaktaḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
bhogavatsu bhakti-hetur bhogānāsaktatā । havi-yogeśvarottare [bhp ]
gṛhītvāpīndriyair arthān yo na dveṣṭi na hṛṣyati ।
viṣṇor māyām idaṃ paśyan sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।
sajjanma-vidyādimatsu bhakti-hetur nirabhimānitā । tatraiva [bhp ] 
na yasya janma-karmabhyāṃ na varṇāśrama-jātibhiḥ ।
sajjate asminn aham-bhāvo dehe vai sa hareḥ priyaḥ ।।

bhāvāḥ kathañcid bhaktaiva jñānānāsakty-amānitā ।
bhakti-niṣṭhāpakā jātās tato hy uttamatoditā ।।
śaiveṣu śrīśiva-kṛṣṇa-bhedakāḥ । bṛhan-nāradīye [nārp ] -
śive ca parameśāne viṣṇau ca paramātmani ।
samabuddhyā pravarttante te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ ।।

anyac ca teṣāṃ bhagavac-chāstrārtha-paratādikam ।
sākṣād-bhakty-ātmakaṃ mukhyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ likhyate'dhunā ।।

skānde -
yeṣāṃ bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ sadā tiṣṭhati sannidhau ।
pūjayanti ca ye nityaṃ te syur bhāgavatā narāḥ ।।

yeṣāṃ bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ jīvitād adhikaṃ bhavet ।
mahā-bhāgavatāḥ śreṣṭhā viṣṇunā kathitā narāḥ ।।

vaiṣṇava-sammāna-niṣṭhā । laiṅge - 
viṣṇu-bhaktam athāyātaṃ yo dṛṣṭvā sumukhaḥ priyaḥ ।
praṇāmādi karoty eva vāsudeve yathā tathā ।
sa vai bhakta iti jñeyaḥ sa punāti jagat trayam ।।

rukṣākṣarā giraḥ śṛṇvan tathā bhāgavateritāḥ ।
praṇāma-pūrvakaṃ kṣāntvā yo vaded vaiṣṇavo hi saḥ ।।

bhojanācchādanaṃ sarvaṃ yathā-śaktyā karoti yaḥ ।
viṣṇu-bhaktasya satataṃ sa vai bhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

gāruḍe -
yena sarvātmanā viṣṇu-bhaktyā bhāvo niveśitaḥ ।
vaiṣṇaveṣu kṛtātmatvān mahā-bhāgavato hi saḥ ।।

śrī-tulasī-sevā-niṣṭhā [nārp ] -
tulasī-kānanaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye namaskurvate narāḥ ।
tat-kāṣṭhāṅkita-karṇā ye te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ ।।

tulasī-gandham āghrāya santoṣaṃ kurvate tu ye ।
tan-mūlam ṛddhūtā yaiś ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ ।।

śrī-bhagavataḥ kathā-paratā

bṛhan-nāradīye śrī-bhagavan-mārkaṇḍeya-saṃvāde -
mat-kathā-śravaṇe yeṣāṃ vartate sāttvikī matiḥ ।
tad-bhakta-viṣṇu-bhaktāś ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ ।।

skānde śrī-bhagavad-arjuna-saṃvāde -
mat-kathāṃ kurute yas tu mat-kathāṃ ca śṛṇoti yaḥ ।
hṛṣyate mat-kathāyāṃ ca sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe [bhp ] tatraiva -
mad-āśrayāḥ kathā mṛṣṭāḥ śṛṇvanti kathayanti ca ।
tapanti vividhās tāpā naitān mad-gata-cetasaḥ ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye tatraiva -
man-mānasāś ca mad-bhaktā mad-bhakta-jana-lolupāḥ ।
man-nāma-śravaṇāsaktās te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ ।।

ye'bhinandanti nāmāni hareḥ śrutvā'tiharṣitāḥ ।
romāñcitaśarīrāśca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ ।।

tatraivānyatra -
anyeṣām udayaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye'bhinandanti mānavāḥ ।
hari-nāma-parā ye ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ ।।

smaraṇa-paratā tatra sva-dharma-niṣṭhayā rāga-dveṣa-nivṛttyā smaraṇam

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe yama-tad-bhaṭa-saṃvāde [vip ] -
na calati ya uccaiḥ śrī-bhagavat-padāravinde ।
sitamanās tam avehi viṣṇu-bhaktam ।।

kali-kaluṣa-malena yasya nātmā
vimala-mater malinīkṛtas tam enam ।
manasi kṛta-janārdanaṃ manuṣyaṃ
satatam avehi harer atīva-bhaktam ।।

kanakam api rahasy avekṣya buddhyā
tṛṇam iva yaḥ samavaiti para-svam ।
bhavati ca bhagavaty ananya-cetāḥ
puruṣa-varaṃ tam avehi viṣṇu-bhaktam ।।

sphaṭika-giri-śilāmalaḥ kva viṣṇur
manasi nṝṇāṃ kva ca matsarādi-doṣaḥ ।
na hi tuhina-mayūkha-raśmi-puñje
bhavati hutāśana-dīptijaḥ pratāpaḥ ।।

vimala-matir amatsaraḥ praśāntaḥ
śuci-carito akhila-sattva-mitra-bhūtaḥ ।
priya-hita-vacano astumānamāyo
vasati sadā hṛdi tasya vāsudevaḥ ।।

vasati hṛdi sanātane ca tasmin
bhavati pumān jagato asya saukhya-rūpaḥ ।
kṣiti-rasam atiramyam ātmano antaḥ
kathayati cārutayaiva śālapotaḥ ।।

anya-vijaye vairāgyādinā ca smaraṇam

ekādaśa-skandhe havi-yogeśvarottare [bhp ] 
dehendriya-prāṇa-mano-dhiyāṃ yo
janmāpyaya-kṣud-bhaya-tarṣa-kṛcchraiḥ ।
saṃsāra-dharmair avimuhyamānaḥ
smṛtyā harer bhāgavata-pradhānaḥ ।।

tri-bhuvana-vibhava-hetave apy akuṇṭha-
smṛtir ajitātma-surādibhir vimṛgyāt ।
na calati bhagavat-padāravindāl
lava-nimiṣārdham api yaḥ sa vaiṣṇavāgryaḥ ।।

bhagavata uru-vikramāṅghri-śākhā-
nakha-maṇi-candrikayā nirasta-tāpe ।
hṛdi katham upasīdatāṃ punaḥ sa
prabhavati candra ivodite arka-tāpaḥ ।।

skānde tatraiva -
ye'rcayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ yajñeśaṃ varadaṃ harim ।
dehinaḥ puṇya-karmāṇaḥ sadā bhāgavatā hi te ।।

laiṅge -
viṣṇu-kṣetre śubhāny eva karoti sneha-saṃyutaḥ ।
pratimāṃ ca harer nityaṃ pūjayet pratayāmavān ।।

viṣṇu-bhaktaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ karmaṇā manasā girā ।
nārāyaṇa-paro nityaṃ bhūpa bhāgavato hi saḥ ।।

atha vaiṣṇava-dharma-niṣṭhādi

pādmottara-khaṇḍe -
tāpādi-pañca-saṃskārī navejyākarma-kārakaḥ ।
artha-pañcaka-vid vipro mahā-bhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

ekāntikatā 
gāruḍe -
ekāntena sadā viṣṇau yasmād deve parāyaṇāḥ ।
tasmād ekāntinaḥ proktās tad-bhāgavata-cetasaḥ ।।

tad-vijñānenānanya-paratā

ekādaśe [bhp ] uddhava-praśnottare -
jñātvājñātvātha ye vai mām yāvān yaś cāsmi yādṛśaḥ ।
bhajanty ananya-bhāvena te vai bhāgavatā matāḥ ।।

ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] -
na kāma-karma-bījānāṃ yasya cetasi sambhavaḥ ।
vāsudevaika-nilayaḥ sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

sā ca ekāntitā caturdhā

tatra dharmānādareṇa śrīmad-uddhava-praśnottara eva [bhp ] -
ājñāyaivaṃ guṇān doṣān mayādiṣṭān api svakān ।
dharmān santyajya yaḥ sarvān māṃ bhajeta sa tu sattamaḥ ।।

śrī-bhagavad-gītāyām [gītā ] 
sarva-dharmān parityajya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।
ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ ।।

caturtha-skandhe [bhp ] -
yadā yasyānugṛhṇāti bhagavān atma-bhāvitaḥ ।
na jahāti matiṃ loke vede ca pariniṣṭhitām ।।

anya-sarva-nirapekṣatā

śrī-bhagavad-uddhava-saṃvāde [bhp ] ailopākhyāne -
santo anapekṣā mac-cittāḥ praśāntāḥ sama-darśinaḥ ।
nirmamā nirahaṅkārā nirdvandvā niṣparigrahāḥ ।।

ataeva śrī-kapila-devahūti-saṃvāde -
ta ete sādhavaḥ sādhvi sarva-saṅga-vivarjitāḥ ।
saṅgas teṣv atha te prārthyaḥ saṅga-doṣa-harā hi te ।।

vighnākulatve'pi mano-rati-paratā ।

skānde tatraiva 
yasya kṛcchra-gatasyāpi keśave ramate manaḥ ।
na vicyutā ca bhaktir vai sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ ।।

āpad-gatasya yasyeha bhakir avyabhicāriṇī ।
nānyatra ramate cittaṃ sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ ।।

premaika-rasatā ।

śrī-ṛṣabhadevasya putrānuśāsane [bhp ] 
ye vā mayīśe kṛta-sauhṛdārthā; janeṣu dehambhara-vārtikeṣu ।
gṛheṣu jāyātmaja-rātimatsu; na prīti-yuktā yāvad-arthāś ca loke ।।

tridhā premaika-paratā premṇaḥ syāt tāratamyataḥ ।
uttamā madhyamā cāsau kaniṣṭhā ceti bhedataḥ ।।

tatrottamā ।

yathā ekādaśe havi-yogeśvarottare [bhp ] 
sarva-bhūteṣu yaḥ paśyed bhagavad-bhāvam ātmanaḥ ।
bhūtāni bhagavaty ātmany eṣa bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

sveṣṭa-devasya bhāvaṃ yaḥ sarva-bhūteṣu paśyati ।
bhāvayanti ca tāny asminn ity arthaḥ sammataḥ satām ।।

śrī-kapila-devahūti-saṃvāde -
mayy ananyena bhāvena bhaktiṃ kurvanti ye dṛḍhām ।
mat-kṛte tyakta-karmāṇas tyakta-svajana-bāndhavāḥ ।।

śrī-havi-yogeśvarottare [bhp ] 
visṛjati hṛdayaṃ na yasya sākṣād
dharir avaśābhihito apy aghaugha-nāśaḥ ।
praṇaya-rasanayā dhṛtāṅghri-padmaḥ
sa bhavati bhāgavata-pradhāna uktaḥ ।।

tatra madhyamā ।

śrī-havi-yogeśvarottare [bhp ] 
īśvare tad-adhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca ।
prema-maitrī-kṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ ।।

tatra kaniṣṭhā ।

tatraiva [bhp ] 
arcāyām eva haraye pūjāṃ yaḥ śraddhayehate ।
na tad-bhakteṣu cānyeṣu sa bhaktaḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

śraddhayā pūjanaṃ prema-bodhakaṃ bhakta ity api ।
lakṣaṇāni ca yāny agre bhakter lekhyāni tāny api ।।

vandanādīni vidyante yeṣu bhāgavatā hi te ।
etāni lakṣaṇānītthaṃ gauṇa-mukhyādi-bhedataḥ ।।
ūhyāni lakṣaṇāny evaṃ vivecyāni parāṇy api ।।
īdṛg-lakṣaṇavantaḥ syur durlabhā bahavo janāḥ ।
divyā hi maṇayo vyaktaṃ na varterann itas tataḥ ।।

ataevoktaṃ mokṣa-dharme nārāyaṇīye [mbh ] -
jāyamānaṃ hi puruṣaṃ yaṃ paśyen madhusūdanaḥ ।
sāttvikas tu sa vijñeyo bhaven mokṣe ca niścitaḥ ।।

evaṃ saṅkṣipya likhitād vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu lakṣaṇāt ।
māhātmyam api vijñeyaṃ likhyate'nyac ca tat kiyat ।।

atha bhagavad-bhaktānāṃ māhātmyam ।

sauparṇe śrī-śakroktau -
kalau bhāgavataṃ nāma yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate ।
jananī putriṇī tena pitṝṇāṃ tu dhurandharaḥ ।।

kalau bhāgavataṃ nāma durlabhaṃ naiva labhyate ।
brahma-rudra-padotkṛṣṭaṃ guruṇā kathitaṃ mama ।।

yasya bhāgavataṃ cihnaṃ dṛśyate tu harir mune ।
gīyate ca kalau devā jñeyās te nāsti saṃśayaḥ ।।

śrī-mārkaṇḍeyoktau -
samīpe tiṣṭhate yasya ha anta-kāle'pi vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
gacchate paramaṃ sthānaṃ yadyapi brahmahā bhavet ।।

nāradīye śrī-vāmadeva-rukmāṅgada-saṃvāde [nārp ] -
śvapaco api mahī-pāla viṣṇu-bhakto dvijādhikaḥ ।
viṣṇu-bhakti-vihīnas tu dvijo api śvapacādhikaḥ ।।

skānde revā-khaṇḍe śrī-brahmoktau -
indro maheśvaro brahmā paraṃ brahma tadaiva hi ।
śvapaco api bhavaty eva yadā tuṣṭā'si keśava ।।

śvapacād api kaṣṭatvaṃ brahmeśānādayaḥ surāḥ ।
tadaivācyuta yānty ete yadaiva tvaṃ parāṅmukhaḥ ।।

sa kartā sarva-dharmāṇāṃ bhakto yas tava keśava ।
sa kartā sarva-pāpānāṃ yo na bhaktas tavācyuta ।।

dharmo bhavaty adharmo api kṛto bhaktais tavācyuta ।
pāpaṃ bhavati dharmo api tavābhaktaiḥ kṛto hareḥ ।।

niḥśeṣa-dharma-kartā vāpy abhakto narake hare ।
sadā tiṣṭhati bhaktas te brahmahāpi viśudhyati ।।

niścalā tvayi bhaktir yā saiva muktir janārdana ।
muktā eva hi bhaktās te tava viṣṇo yato hare ।।

tatraiva durvāso-nārada-saṃvāde -
nūnaṃ bhāgavatā loke loka-rakṣā-viśāradāḥ ।
vrajanti viṣṇunādiṣṭā hṛdisthena mahāmune ।।

bhagavān eva sarvatra bhūtānāṃ kṛpayā hariḥ ।
rakṣaṇāya caran lokān bhakta-rūpeṇa nārada ।।

tatraiva śrī-brahma-nārada-saṃvāde -
yas tu viṣṇu-paro nityaṃ dṛḍha-bhaktir jitendriyaḥ ।
sva-gṛhe'pi vasan yāti tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।।

aśvamedha-sahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ yaḥ karoti vai ।
nāsau tat-phalam āpnoti tad-bhaktair yad avāpyate ।।

tatraivāmṛta-sāroddhāre śrī-yama-tad-bhaṭa-saṃvāde -
sarvatra vaiṣṇavāḥ pūjyāḥ svarge martye rasātale ।
devatānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tathaivoraga-rakṣasām ।।

yeṣāṃ smaraṇa-mātreṇa pāpa-lakṣa-śatāni ca ।
dahyante nātra sandeho vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām ।।

yeṣāṃ pāda-rajenaiva prāpyate jāhnavī-jalam ।
nārmadaṃ yāmunaṃ caiva kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam ।।

yeṣāṃ vākya-jalaughena vinā gaṅgā-jalair api ।
vinā tīrtha-sahasreṇa snāto bhavati mānavaḥ ।।

tatraiva cāturmāsya-māhātmye -
tāvad bhramanti saṃsāre pitaraḥ piṇḍa-tat-paraḥ ।
yāvat kule bhakti-yuktaḥ suto naiva prajāyate ।।

sa eva jñānavān loke yogināṃ prathamo hi saḥ ।
mahā-kratūnām āhartā hari-bhakti-yuto hi yaḥ ।।

kāśī-khaṇḍe dhruva-carite -
na cyavante hi yad-bhaktyā mahatyāṃ pralayāpadi ।
ato acyuto akhile loke sa ekaḥ sarvago avyayaḥ ।।

na tasmād bhagavad-bhaktād bhetavyaṃ kenacit kvacit ।
niyataṃ viṣṇu-bhaktā yena te syuḥ para-tāpinaḥ ।।

tatraivāgre 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā yadi vetaraḥ ।
viṣṇu-bhakti-samāyukto jñeyaḥ sarvottamottamaḥ ।।

śaṅkha-cakrāṅkita-tanuḥ śirasā mañjarī-dharaḥ ।
gopī-candana-liptāṅgo dṛṣṭaś ced tad-aghaṃ kutaḥ ।।

mahābhārate rāja-dharme-
īśvaraṃ sarva-bhūtānāṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam ।
bhaktā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ durgāṇy atitaranti te ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare-
śayanād utthito yas tu kīrtayen madhusūdanam ।
kīrtanāt tasya pāpāni nāśam āyānty aśeṣataḥ ।।

tatraiva- 
yasyāpy anante jagatām adhīśe
bhaktiḥ parā yādava-deva-deve ।
tasmāt paraṃ nāparam asti kiñcit
pātraṃ triloke puruṣa-pravīra ।।

dvārakā-māhātmye śrī-prahlāda-bali-saṃvāde-
nityaṃ ye prātar utthāya vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu kīrtanam ।
kurvanti te bhāgavatāḥ kṛṣṇa-tulyāḥ kalau bale ।।

hari-bhakti-sudhodaye- 
sva-darśana-sparśana-pūjanaiḥ kṛtī
tamāṃsi viṣṇu-pratimeva vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
dhunvan vasaty atra janasya yan na tat
svārthaṃ paraṃ loka-hitāya dīpavat ।।

itihāsa-samuccaye śrī-lomaśa-vākye-
ye bhajanti jagad-yoniṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam ।
na tebhyo vidyate tīrtham adhikaṃ rāja-sattama ।।

yatra bhāgavatāḥ snānaṃ kurvanti vimalāśrayāḥ ।
tat-tīrtham adhikaṃ viddhi sarva-pāpa-viśodhanam ।।

yatra rāgādi-rahitā vāsudeva-parāyaṇāḥ ।
tatra sannihito viṣṇur nṛpate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

na gandhair na tathā toyair na puṣpaiś ca manoharaiḥ ।
sānnidhyaṃ kurute devo yatra santi na vaiṣṇavāḥ ।।

balibhiś copavāsaiś ca nṛtya-gītādibhis tathā ।
nityam ārādhyamāno api tatra viṣṇur na tṛpyati ।।

tasmād ete mahābhāgā vaiṣṇavā vīta-kalmaṣāḥ ।
punanti sakalān lokāṃs tat tīrtham adhikaṃ tataḥ ।।

śūdraṃ vā bhagavad-bhaktaṃ niṣādaṃ śvapacaṃ tathā ।
vīkṣataṃ jāti-sāmānyāt sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam ।।

tasmād viṣṇu-prasādāya vaiṣṇavān paritoṣayet ।
prasāda-sumukho viṣṇus tenaiva syān na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tatraiva śrī-nārada-puṇḍarīka-saṃvāde -
ye nṛśaṃsā durātmānaḥ pāpācāra-ratāḥ sadā ।
te'pi yānti paraṃ dhāma nārāyaṇa-parāśrayāḥ ।।

lipyante na ca pāpena vaiṣṇavā viṣṇu-tat-parāḥ ।
punanti sakalān lokān sahasrāṃśur ivoditaḥ ।।

janmāntara-sahasreṣu yasya syād buddhir īdṛśī ।
dāso ahaṃ vāsudevasya sarvān lokān samuddharet ।।

sa yāti viṣṇu-sālokyaṃ puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
kiṃ punas tad-gata-prāṇāḥ puruṣāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ ।।

smṛtaḥ sambhāṣito vāpi pūjito vā dvijottamāḥ ।
punāti bhagavad-bhaktaś cāṇḍālo api yadṛcchayā ।।

śrī-vyāsa-vākye -
janmāntara-sahasreṣu viṣṇu-bhakto na lipyate ।
yasya sandarśanād eva bhasmībhavati pātakam ।।

itihāsa-samuccaye śrī-bhagavad-vākye -
na me priyaś caturvedī mad-bhaktaḥ śvapacaḥ priyaḥ ।
tasmai deyaṃ tato grāhyaṃ sa ca pūjyo yathā hy aham ।।

tatraiva brahma-vākye -
sabhartṛkā vā vidhavā viṣṇu-bhaktiṃ karoti yā ।
samuddharati cātmānaṃ kulam ekottaraṃ śatam ।।

dvārakā-māhātmye prahlāda-bali-saṃvāde -
saṅkīrṇa-yonayaḥ pūtā ye bhaktā madhusūdane ।
mleccha-tulyāḥ kulīnās te ye na bhaktā janārdane ।।

ādi-purāṇe śrī-kṛṣṇārjuna-saṃvāde -
vaiṣṇavān bhaja kaunteya mā bhajasvānya-devatāḥ ।
punanti vaiṣṇavāḥ sarve sarva-devam idaṃ jagat ।
mad-bhakto durlabho yasya sa eva mama durlabhaḥ ।।

tat-paro durlabho nāsti satyaṃ satyaṃ dhanañjaya ।
jagatāṃ guravo bhaktā bhaktānāṃ guravo vayam ।
sarvatra guravo bhaktā vayaṃ ca guravo yathā ।
asmākaṃ bāndhavā bhaktā bhaktānāṃ bāndhavā vayam ।।

asmākaṃ guravo bhaktā bhaktānāṃ guravo vayam ।
mad-bhaktā yatra gacchanti tatra gacchāmi pārthiva ।
bhaktānām anugacchanti muktayaḥ śrutibhiḥ saha ।।

ye me bhakta-janāḥ pārtha na me bhaktāś ca te janāḥ ।
mad-bhaktānāṃ ca ye bhaktās te me bhaktatamā matāḥ ।।

ye kecit prāṇino bhaktā mad-arthe tyakta-bāndhavāḥ ।
teṣām ahaṃ parikrīto nānya-krīto dhanañjaya ।।

eṣāṃ bhakṣyaṃ sunirṇītaṃ śrūyatāṃ niścitaṃ mama ।
ucchiṣṭam avaśiṣṭaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhojana-dvayam ।।

nāma-yukta-janāḥ kecij jāty-antara-samanvitāḥ ।
kurvanti me yathā prītiṃ na tathā veda-pāragāḥ ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye mārkaṇḍeyaṃ prati śrī-bhagavad-uktau -
viṣṇur bhakta-kuṭumbīti vadanti vibudhāḥ sadā ।
tad eva pālayiṣyāmi majjano nānṛtaṃ vadet ।।

mama janma kule yasya tat kulaṃ mokṣagāmi vai ।
mayi tuṣṭe muni-śreṣṭha kim asādhyaṃ jagat-traye ।।

mayi bhakti-paro yas tu mad-yājī mat-kathā-paraḥ ।
mad-dhyānī sva-kulaṃ sarvaṃ nayaty acyuta-rūpatām ।।

mad-arthaṃ karma kurvāṇo mat-praṇāma-paro naraḥ ।
man-manāḥ sva-kulaṃ sarvaṃ nayaty acyuta-rūpatām ।।

aham eva dvija-śreṣṭha nityaṃ pracchanna-vigrahaḥ ।
bhagavad-bhakta-rūpeṇa lokān rakṣāmi sarvadā ।।

tatraivāditi-māhātmye śrī-sūtoktau -
viprāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ māhātmyaṃ hari-bhakti-ratātmanām ।
hari-dhyāna-parāṇāṃ tu kaḥ samarthaḥ prabādhitum ।।

hari-bhakti-paro yatra tatra brahmā hariḥ śivaḥ ।
tatra devāś ca siddhādyā nityaṃ tiṣṭhanti sattamāḥ ।।

nimiṣaṃ nimṣārdhaṃ vā yatra tiṣṭhanti sattamāḥ ।
tatraiva sarva-śreyāṃsi tat tīrthaṃ tat tapo-vanam ।।

tatraivāditiṃ prati śrī-bhagavad-uttare [nārp ]-
rāga-dveṣa-vihīnā ye mad-bhaktā mat-parāyaṇāḥ ।
vadanti satataṃ te māṃ gatāsūyā adāmbhikāḥ ।।

paropatāpa-vimukhāḥ śiva-bhakti-parāyaṇāḥ ।
mat-kathā-śravaṇāsaktā vahanti satataṃ hi mām ।।

tatraiva dhvajāropaṇa-māhātmye śrī-viṣṇu-dūtoktau [nārp ] -
yatīnāṃ viṣṇu-bhaktānāṃ paricaryā-parāyaṇāḥ ।
īkṣitā api gacchanti pāpino api parāṃ gatim ।।

tatraiva śrī-bhagavat-toṣa-prakāra-praśnottare [nārp ] -
ripavas taṃ na hiṃsanti na bādhante grahāś ca tam ।
rākṣasāś ca na cekṣante naraṃ viṣṇu-parāyaṇam ।।

bhaktir dṛḍhā bhaved yasya deva-deve janārdane ।
śreyāṃsi tasya sidhyanti bhaktimanto adhikās tataḥ ।।

tatraivāgre [nārp ] 
adyāpi ca muni-śreṣṭha brahmādyā api devatāḥ ।
prabhāvaṃ na vijānanti viṣṇu-bhakti-ratātmanām ।।

kiṃ ca [nārp ] -
dharmārtha-kāma-mokṣākhyāḥ puruṣārthā dvijottamāḥ ।
hari-bhakti-parāṇāṃ vai sampadyante na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tatraiva lubdhakopākhyānasyādau [nārp ] 
ye viṣṇu-niratāḥ śāntā lokānugraha-tat-parāḥ ।
sarva-bhūta-dayā-yuktā viṣṇu-rūpāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

viṣṇu-bhakti-vihīnā ye caṇḍālāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
caṇḍālā api vai śreṣṭhā hari-bhakti-parāyaṇāḥ ।।

tatraiva yajña-dhvajopākhyānasyādau śrī-sūta-vākyam [nārp ] 
hari-bhakti-rasāsvāda-muditā ye narottamāḥ ।
namaskaromy ahaṃ tebhyo yat-saṅgān mukti-bhāg naraḥ ।।

hari-bhakti-parā ye tu hari-nāma-parāyaṇāḥ ।
durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā tebhyo nityaṃ namo namaḥ ।।

aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ viṣṇu-bhakti-ratātmanām ।
yasmān muktiḥ karasthaiva yoginām api durlabhā ।।

tatraiva kali-prasaṅge [nārp ?]
ghore kali-yuge prāpte sarva-dharma-vivarjite ।
vāsudeva-parā martyāḥ kṛtārthā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

asty antar durlabhā proktā hari-bhaktiḥ kalau yuge ।
hari-bhakti-ratānāṃ vai pāpa-bandho na jāyate ।।

veda-vāda-ratāḥ sarve tathā tīrtha-niṣeviṇaḥ ।
hari-bhakti-rataiḥ sārdhaṃ kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।।

ataevoktaṃ devais tatraiva bhāratavarṣa-prasaṅge [nārp ] -
hari-kīrtana-śīlo vā tad-bhaktānāṃ priyo api vā ।
śuśrūṣur vāpi mahatāṃ sa vandyo asmābhir uttamaḥ ।।

pādme śrī-bhagavad-brahma-saṃvāde -
darśana-dhyāna-saṃsparśair martya-kūrma-vihaṅgamāḥ ।
puṣṇanti svāny apatyāni tathāham api padmaja ।।

muhūrtenāpi saṃhartuṃ śaktau yadyapi dānavāt ।
mad-bhaktānāṃ vinodārthaṃ karomi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

tatraiva māgha-māhātmye devadūta-vikuṇḍala-saṃvāde -
na vayaṃ yamaṃ yama-lokaṃ na na dūtān ghora-darśanāt ।
paśyanti vaiṣṇavā nūnaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam ।।

śvapākam iva nekṣeta loke vipram avaiṣṇavam ।
vaiṣṇavo varṇa-bāhyo api punāti bhuvana-trayam ।।

na śūdrā bhagavad-bhaktās te tu bhāvanā matāḥ ।
sarva-varṇeṣu te śūdrā ye na bhaktā janārdana ।।

viṣṇu-bhaktasya ye dāsā vaiṣṇavānna-bhujaś ca ye ।
te'pi kratu-bhujāṃ gvaiśya gatiṃ yānti nirākulāḥ ।।

tatraiva vaiśākha-māhātmye pañca-puruṣāṇām uktau -
bhavyāni bhūtāni janārdanasya
paropakārāya caranti viśvam ।।

tathā 
santaḥ pratiṣṭhā dīnānāṃ daivād udbhūta-pāpmanām ।
ārtānām ārtihantāro darśanād eva sādhavaḥ ।।

tatraivottara-khaṇḍe śiva-pārvatī-saṃvāde [padmap ]
na karma-bandhanaṃ janma vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vidyate ।
viṣṇor anucaratvaṃ hi mokṣayāhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

na dāsyam amareśasya bandhanaṃ parikīrtitam ।
sarva-bandhana-nirmuktā hari-dāsā nirāmayāḥ ।।

brahmāṇḍa-purāṇe janmāṣṭamī-vrata-māhātmye śrī-citraguptoktau -
darśana-sparśanālāpa-sahavāsādibhiḥ kṣaṇāt ।
bhaktāḥ punanti kṛṣṇasya sākṣād api ca pukkaśam ।।

tyakta-sarva-kulācāro mahā-pātakavān api ।
viṣṇor bhaktaṃ samāśritya naro nārhati yātanām ।।

vāśiṣṭhe -
yasmin deśe marau taj-jño nāsti sajjana-pādapaḥ ।
saphalaḥ śītalac-chāyo na tatra divasaṃ vaset ।।

sadā santo abhigantavyā yadyapy upadiśanti na ।
yā hi svaira-kathās teṣām upadeśā bhavanti te ।।

gāruḍe -
satrayāji-sahasrebhyaḥ sarva-vedānta-pāragaḥ ।
sarva-vedānta-vit-koṭyā viṣṇu-bhakto viśiṣyate ।।

vaiṣṇavānāṃ sahasrebhya ekānty eko viśiṣyate ।
ekāntinas tu puruṣā gacchanti paramaṃ padam ।।

śrī-bhagavad-gītāsu [gītā ] -
api cet sudurācāro bhajate mām ananyabhāk ।
sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥ ।।

kṣipraṃ bhavati dharmātmā śaśvacchāntiṃ nigacchati ।
kaunteya pratijānīhi na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati ।।

māṃ hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye api syuḥ pāpayonayaḥ ।
striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te api yānti parāṃ gatim ।
kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayas tathā ।।

kiṃ ca tatraiva [gītā ] -
yoginām api sarveṣāṃ mad-gatenāntarātmanā ।
śraddhāvān bhajate yo māṃ sa me yuktatamo mataḥ ।।

śrī-bhāgavatasya prathama-skandhe śrī-parīkṣitoktau [bhp ] -
yeṣāṃ saṃsmaraṇāt puṃsāṃ sadyaḥ śuddhyanti vai gṛhāḥ ।
kiṃ punar darśana-sparśa- pāda-śaucāsanādibhiḥ ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe śrī-vidurasya [bhp ] - 
śrutasya puṃsāṃ sucira-śramasya
nanv añjasā sūribhir īḍito arthaḥ ।
tat-tad-guṇānuśravaṇaṃ mukunda-
pādāravindaṃ hṛdayeṣu yeṣām ।।

devahūtiṃ prati kapila-devasya [bhp ] - 
na karhicin mat-parāḥ śānta-rūpe
naṅkṣyanti no me animiṣo leḍhi hetiḥ ।
yeṣām ahaṃ priya ātmā sutaś ca
sakhā guruḥ suhṛdo daivam iṣṭam ।।

caturthe śrī-dhruvasya [bhp ] - 
yā nirvṛtis tanu-bhṛtāṃ tava pāda-padma-
dhyānād bhavaj-jana-kathā-śravaṇena vā syāt ।
sā brahmaṇi sva-mahimany api nātha mā bhūt
kiṃ tv antakāsi-lulitāt patatāṃ vimānāt ।।

śrī-rudrasya [bhp ] 
sva-dharma-niṣṭhaḥ śata-janmabhiḥ pumān
viriñcatām eti tataḥ paraṃ hi mām ।
avyākṛtaṃ bhāgavato atha vaiṣṇavaṃ
padaṃ yathāhaṃ vibudhāḥ kalātyaye ।।

pañcame śrī-jaḍa-bharatasya [bhp ] - 
rahūgaṇaitat tapasā na yāti
na cejyayā nirvapaṇād gṛhād vā ।
na cchandasā naiva jalāgni-sūryair
vinā mahat-pāda-rajo-'bhiṣekam ।।

ṣaṣṭhe śrī-parīkṣitaḥ [bhp ] -
rajobhiḥ sama-saṅkhyātāḥ pārthivair iha jantavaḥ ।
teṣāṃ ye kecanehante śreyo vai manujādayaḥ ।।

prāyo mumukṣavas teṣāṃ kecanaiva dvijottama ।
mumukṣūṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaścin mucyeta sidhyati ।।

muktānām api siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇa-parāyaṇaḥ ।
sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣv api mahāmune ।।

śrī-śivasya [bhp ] -
nārāyaṇa-parāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati ।
svargāpavarga-narakeṣv api tulyārtha-darśinaḥ ।।

saptame śrī-prahlādasya [bhp ] - 
naiṣāṃ matis tāvad urukramāṅghriṃ
spṛśaty anarthāpagamo yad-arthaḥ ।
mahīyasāṃ pāda-rajo-'bhiṣekaṃ
niṣkiñcanānāṃ na vṛṇīta yāvat ।।

kiṃ ca [bhp ] - 
viprād dvi-ṣaḍ-guṇa-yutād aravinda-nābha-
pādāravinda-vimukhāt śvapacaṃ variṣṭham ।
manye tad-arpita-mano-vacanehitārtha-
prāṇaṃ punāti sa kulaṃ na tu bhūrimānaḥ ।।

aṣṭame śrī-gajendrasya [bhp ] - 
ekāntino yasya na kañcanārthaṃ
vāñchanti ye vai bhagavat-prapannāḥ ।
aty-adbhutaṃ tac-caritaṃ sumaṅgalaṃ
gāyanta ānanda-samudra-magnāḥ ।।

navame śrī-bhagavataḥ [bhp ] -
ahaṃ bhakta-parādhīno hy asvatantra iva dvija ।
sādhubhir grasta-hṛdayo bhaktair bhakta-jana-priyaḥ ।।

nāham ātmānam āśāse mad-bhaktaiḥ sādhubhir vinā ।
śriyaṃ cātyantikīṃ brahman yeṣāṃ gatir ahaṃ parā ।।

ye dārāgāra-putrāpta- prāṇān vittam imaṃ param ।
hitvā māṃ śaraṇaṃ yātāḥ kathaṃ tāṃs tyaktum utsahe ।।

mayi nirbaddha-hṛdayāḥ sādhavaḥ sama-darśanāḥ ।
vaśe kurvanti māṃ bhaktyā sat-striyaḥ sat-patiṃ yathā ।।

sādhavo hṛdayaṃ mahyaṃ sādhūnāṃ hṛdayaṃ tv aham ।
mad-anyat te na jānanti nāhaṃ tebhyo manāg api ।।

tatraiva śrī-durvāsasaḥ [bhp ] -
duṣkaraḥ ko nu sādhūnāṃ dustyajo vā mahātmanām ।
yaiḥ saṅgṛhīto bhagavān sātvatām ṛṣabho hariḥ ।।

yan-nāma-śruti-mātreṇa pumān bhavati nirmalaḥ ।
tasya tīrtha-padaḥ kiṃ vā dāsānām avaśiṣyate ।।

daśame deva-stutau [bhp ] - 
tathā na te mādhava tāvakāḥ kvacid
bhraśyanti mārgāt tvayi baddha-sauhṛdāḥ ।
tvayābhiguptā vicaranti nirbhayā
vināyakānīkapa-mūrdhasu prabho ।।

śrī-bādarāyaṇeḥ [bhp ] -
nāyaṃ sukhāpo bhagavān dehināṃ gopikā-sutaḥ ।
jñānināṃ cātma-bhūtānāṃ yathā bhaktimatām iha ।।

tatraiva śrī-bhagavataḥ [bhp ] -
sādhūnāṃ sama-cittānāṃ mukunda-caraṇaiṣiṇām ।
upekṣyaiḥ kiṃ dhana-stambhair asadbhir asad-āśrayaiḥ ।।

kiṃ ca [bhp ] -
na hy am-mayāni tīrthāni na devā mṛc-chilā-mayāḥ ।
te punanty uru-kālena darśanād eva sādhavaḥ ।।

api ca [bhp ] - 
nāgnir na sūryo na ca candra-tārakā
na bhūr jalaṃ khaṃ śvasano atha vāṅ manaḥ ।
upāsitā bheda-kṛto haranty aghaṃ
vipaścito ghnanti muhūrta-sevayā ।।

yasyātma-buddhiḥ kuṇape tri-dhātuke
sva-dhīḥ kalatrādiṣu bhauma ijya-dhīḥ ।
yat-tīrtha-buddhiḥ salile na karhicij
janeṣv abhijñeṣu sa eva go-kharaḥ ।।

śruti-stutau [bhp ] - 
tava pari ye caranty akhila-sattva-niketatayā
ta uta padākramanty avigaṇayya śiro nirṛteḥ ।
parivayase paśūn iva girā vibudhān api tāṃs
tvayi kṛta-sauhṛdāḥ khalu punanti na ye vimukhāḥ ।।

ekādaśe śrī-vasudevasya [bhp ] -
bhūtānāṃ deva-caritaṃ duḥkhāya ca sukhāya ca ।
sukhāyaiva hi sādhūnāṃ tvādṛśām acyutātmanām ।।

bhajanti ye yathā devān devā api tathaiva tān ।
chāyeva karma-sacivāḥ sādhavo dīna-vatsalāḥ ।।

tatraiva śrī-bhagavataḥ [bhp ] -
na mayy ekānta-bhaktānāṃ guṇa-doṣodbhavā guṇāḥ ।
sādhūnāṃ sama-cittānāṃ buddheḥ param upeyuṣām ।।

evam etān mayā diṣṭān anutiṣṭhanti me pathaḥ ।
kṣemaṃ vindanti mat-sthānaṃ yad brahma paramaṃ viduḥ ।।

nimajjyonmajjatāṃ ghore bhavābdhau paramāyaṇam ।
santo brahma-vidaḥ śāntā nor dṛḍhevāpsu majjatām ।।

annaṃ hi prāṇināṃ prāṇā ārtānāṃ śaraṇaṃ tv aham ।
dharmā vittaṃ nṝṇāṃ pretya santo arvāg-bibhyato araṇam ।।

santo diśanti cakṣūṃṣi bahir arkaḥ samutthitaḥ ।
devatā bāndhavāḥ santaḥ santa ātmāham eva ca ।।

kiṃ ca [bhp ] 
na kiñcit sādhavo dhīrā bhaktā hy ekāntino mama ।
vāñchanty api mayā dattaṃ kaivalyam apunar-bhavam ।।

dvādaśe ca śrī-parīkṣitaḥ [bhp ] 
nāty-adbhutam ahaṃ manye mahatām acyutātmanām ।
ajñeṣu tāpa-tapteṣu bhūteṣu yad anugrahaḥ ।।

śrī-rudrasya ca mārkaṇḍeyam adhikṛtya [bhp ] 
śravaṇād darśanād vāpi mahā-pātakino api vaḥ ।
śudhyerann antyajāś cāpi kim u sambhāṣaṇādibhiḥ ।।

ataeva śrī-dharma-rājasya sva-dūtānuśāsane ṣaṣṭha-skandhe [bhp ] 
te deva-siddha-parigīta-pavitra-gāthā
ye sādhavaḥ samadṛśo bhagavat-prapannāḥ ।
tān nopasīdata harer gadayābhiguptān
naiṣāṃ vayaṃ na ca vayaḥ prabhavāma daṇḍe ।।

tathā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe [vip ] 
yama-niyama-vidhūta-kalmaṣāṇām
anudinam acyuta-sakta-mānasānām ।
apagatam adamāna-matsarāṇāṃ
vraja bhaṭa dūratareṇa mānavānām ।।

sakalam idam ahaṃ ca vāsudevaḥ
parama-pumān parameśvaraḥ sa ekaḥ ।
iti matir acalā bhavaty anante
hṛdaya-gate vraja tān vihāya dūrāt ।।

kamala-nayana vāsudeva viṣṇo
dharaṇidharācyuta śaṅkha-cakra-pāṇe ।
bhava śaraṇam itīrayanti ye vai
tyaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa tān apāpān ।।

vasati manasi yasya so avyayātmā ।
puruṣa-varasya na tasya dṛṣṭi-pāte ।
tava gatir atha vā mamāsti cakra-
pratihata-vīrya-balasya so anya-lokyaḥ ।।

nārasiṃhe, viṣṇu-purāṇe ca [vip ] 
aham amarārcitena dhātrā
yama iti loka-hitāhite niyuktaḥ ।
hari-guru-vaśago asmi na svatantraḥ
prabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi viṣṇuḥ ।।

sugatim abhilaṣāmi vāsudevā-
vaham api bhāgavata-sthitāntarātmā ।
madhuvara vaśago asmi na svatantraḥ
prabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi kṛṣṇaḥ ।।

na hi śaśakaluṣa-cchaviḥ kadācit
timira-parābhavatām upaiti candraḥ ।
bhagavati ca harāv ananya-cetā
bhṛśa-malino api virājate manuṣyaḥ ।।

pādme devadyūti-vikuṇḍala-saṃvāde [padmap ]
prāhāsmān yamunā bhrātā sadaiva hi punaḥ punaḥ ।
bhavadbhir vaiṣṇavās tyājyā na te syur mama gocarāḥ ।।

durācāro duṣkṛto api sadācāra-rato api yaḥ ।
bhavadbhiḥ sa sadā tyājyo viṣṇuṃ ca bhajate naraḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavo yad-gṛhe bhuṅkte yeṣāṃ vaiṣṇava-saṅgatiḥ ।
te'pi vaḥ parivāryāḥ syus tat-saṅga-hata-kilbiṣāḥ ।।

skānde amṛta-sāroddhāre -
ekādaśyām abhuñjānā yuktāḥ pāpa-śatair api ।
bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyā hitā me yadi sarvadā ।।

ye smaranti jagannāthaṃ mṛtyu-kāle janārdanam ।
pāpa-koṭi-śatair yuktā na te grāhyā mamājñayā ।।

na brahmā na śivāgnīndrā nāhaṃ nānye divaukasaḥ ।
śaktā na nigrahaṃ kartuṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām ।।

ato ahaṃ sarva-kālaṃ ca vaiṣṇavānāṃ bibhemi vai ।
bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyā vaiṣṇavā ye sadaiva hi ।।

vaiṣṇavā viṣṇuvat pūjyā mama mānyā viśeṣataḥ ।
teṣāṃ kṛte'pamāne'pi vināśo jāyate dhruvam ।।

kiṃ ca -
yeṣāṃ smaraṇa-mātreṇa pāpa-lakṣa-śatāni ca ।
dahyante nātra sandeho vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām ।।

yeṣāṃ pāda-rajenaiva prāpyate jāhnavī-jalam ।
nārmadaṃ yāmunaṃ caiva kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam ।।

yeṣāṃ vākya-jalaughena vinā gaṅgā-jalair api ।
vinā tīrtha-sahasreṇa snāto bhavati mānavaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca -
brahma-loke na me vāso na me vāso harālaye ।
nālaye loka-pālānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ parābhave ।।

na devā na ca gandharvā na yakṣoraga-rākṣasāḥ ।
trātuṃ samarthā ṛṣayo vaiṣṇavānāṃ parābhave ।।

karomi karmaṇā vācā manasāpi na vipriyam ।
vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahābhāgāḥ sudarśana-bhayād api ।।

ekato dhāvate cakram ekato hari-vāhanam ।
ekato viṣṇu-dūtāś ca vaiṣṇave cārdite mayā ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye caikādaśī-māhātmye [nārp ] - 
ye viṣṇu-pūjana-ratāḥ prayatāḥ kṛtajñāś
caikādaśī-vrata-parā vijitendriyāś ca ।
nārāyaṇācyuta hare śaraṇaṃ bhaveti
śāntā vadanti satataṃ tarasā tyajadhvam ।।

nārāyaṇārpita-dhiyo hari-bhakta-bhaktān
svācāra-mārga-niratān guru-sevakāṃś ca ।
sat-pātra-dāna-niratān hari-kīrti-bhaktān
dūtās tyajadhvam aniśaṃ hari-nāma-saktān ।।

pāṣaṇḍa-saṅga-rahitān hari-bhakti-tuṣṭān
sat-saṅga-lolupa-tarāṃś ca tathātipuṇyān ।
śambhor hareś ca sama-buddhi-matas tathaiva
dūtās tyajadhvam upakāra-parāñ narāṇām ।।

ye vīkṣitā hari-kathāmṛta-sevakaiś ca
nārāyaṇa-smṛti-parāyaṇa-mānasaiś ca ।
viprendra-pāda-jala-sevana-samprahṛṣṭais
tān pāpino api ca bhaṭā satataṃ tyajadhvam ।।

ataevoktaṃ śrī-nāradena caturtha-skandha-śeṣe [bhp ] 
śriyam anucaratīṃ tad-arthinaś ca
dvipada-patīn vibudhāṃś ca yat sva-pūrṇaḥ ।
na bhajati nija-bhṛtya-varga-tantraḥ
katham amum udvisṛjet pumān kṛta-jñaḥ ।।

ataeva prārthanam । nārāyaṇa-vyūha-stave - 
nāhaṃ brahmāpi bhuyāsaṃ tvad-bhakti-rahito hare ।
tvayi bhaktas tu kīṭo api bhūyāsaṃ janma-janmasu ।।

śrī-brahma-stutau ca daśama-skandhe [bhp ] - 
tad astu me nātha sa bhūri-bhāgo
bhave'tra vānyatra tu vā tiraścām ।
yenāham eko api bhavaj-janānāṃ
bhūtvā niṣeve tava pāda-pallavam ।।

ataevoktaṃ śrī-nārāyaṇa-vyūha-stave -
ye tyakta-loka-dharmārthā viṣṇu-bhakti-vaśaṃ gatāḥ ।
bhajanti paramātmānaṃ tebhyo nityaṃ namo namaḥ ।।

evaṃ śrī-bhagavad-bhakta-māhātmyāmṛta-vāridheḥ ।
vicitra-bhaṅga-lekhārho lobha-lolaṃ vināsti kaḥ ।।

ataḥ śrī-bhagavad-bhakta-janānāṃ saṅgatiḥ sadā ।
kāryā sarva-prayatnena dvau lokau vijigīṣubhiḥ ।।

atha śrī-bhagavad-bhakta-saṅga-māhātmyam

bhagavad-bhakta-pādābja-pādukābhyo namo astu me ।
yat-saṅgamaḥ sādhanaṃ ca sādhyaṃ cākhilam uttamam ।।

tatra sarva-pātaka-mocakatā

bṛhan-nāradīye [nārp ] yajña-māly-upākhyānānte ।
hari-bhakti-parāṇāṃ tu saṅgināṃ saṅga-mātrataḥ ।
mucyate sarva-pāpebhyo mahā-pātakavān api ।।

sāmānyato anartha-nivartakatāartha-prāpakatā ca ।

pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye [padmap ] śrī-muni-śarmāṇaṃ prati pretānām uktau -
vināśayaty apayaśo buddhiṃ viśadayaty api ।
pratiṣṭhāpayati prāyo nṛṇāṃ vaiṣṇava-darśanam ।।

tatra śrī-yama-brāhmaṇa-saṃvāde mahāratha-nṛpoktau -
yathā prapadyamānasya bhagavantaṃ vibhāvasum ।
śītaṃ bhayaṃ tamo apy eti sādhūn saṃsevataḥ sadā ।।

tatraiva pretopākhyāne pretoktau [padmap ] -
apākaroti duritaṃ śreyaḥ saṃyojayaty api ।
yaśo vistārayaty āśu nṝṇāṃ vaiṣṇava-saṅgamaḥ ।।

atha sarva-tīrthādhikatā

tatraiva [padmap ] -
gaṅgādi-puṇya-tīrtheṣu yo naraḥ snātum icchati ।
yaḥ karoti satāṃ saṅgāṃ tayoḥ sat-saṅgamo varaḥ ।।

tatraiva bhagīratha-nṛpoktau [padmap ] -
yaḥ snātaḥ śānti-sitayā sādhu-saṅgati-gaṅgayā ।
kiṃ tasya dānaiḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ ।।

atha sarveṣṭa-sādhakatā

yāni yāni durāpāṇi vāñchitāni mahī-tale ।
prāpyante tāni tāny eva sādhūnām eva saṅgamāt ।।

atha anarthasyāpy arthatvāpādakatā

vāśiṣṭhe -
śūnyam āpūrṇatām eti mṛtir apy amṛtāyate ।
āpat sampad iva bhāti vidvaj-jana-samāgame ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe [bhp ] 
saṅgo yaḥ saṃsṛter hetur asatsu vihito adhiyā ।
sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto niḥsaṅgatvāya kalpate ।।

śrī-kapila-devoktau [bhp ] 
prasaṅgam ajaraṃ pāśam ātmanaḥ kavayo viduḥ ।
sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto mokṣa-dvāram apāvṛtam ।।

yataḥ -
arir mitraṃ viṣaṃ pathyam adharmo dharmatāṃ vrajet ।
prasanne puṇḍarīkākṣe viparīte viparyayaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca śrī-bhagavad-vākyaṃ [bhaktis attributed to padmap] -
man-nimittaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpam api dharmāya kalpate ।
mām anādṛtya dharmo api pāpaṃ syān mat-prabhāvataḥ ।।

caturtha-skandhe śrī-dhruvoktau [bhp ] 
te na smaranty atitarāṃ priyam īśa martyaṃ
ye cānv adaḥ suta-suhṛd-gṛha-vitta-dārāḥ ।
ye tv abja-nābha bhavadīya-padāravinda-
saugandhya-lubdha-hṛdayeṣu kṛta-prasaṅgāḥ ।।

pādme tatraiva pretoktau [padmap ] -
rasāyana-mayī śītā paramānanda-dāyinī ।
nānandayati kaṃ nāma vaiṣṇavāśraya-candrikā ।।
atha mokṣadatvam । daśama-skandhe śrī-mucukunda-stutau [bhp ] 
bhavāpavargo bhramato yadā bhavej
janasya tarhy acuta sat-samāgamaḥ ।
sat-saṅgamo yarhi tadaiva sad-gatau
parāvareśe tvayi jāyate matiḥ ।।

ataevoktaṃ śrī-pracetobhiś caturtha-skandhe [bhp ]
yatreḍyante kathā mṛṣṭās tṛṣṇāyāḥ praśamo yataḥ ।
nirvairaṃ yatra bhūteṣu nodvego yatra kaścana ।।

yatra nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣād bhagavān nyāsināṃ gatiḥ ।
saṃstūyate sat-kathāsu mukta-saṅgaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ vicaratāṃ padbhyāṃ tīrthānāṃ pāvanecchayā ।
bhītasya kiṃ na roceta tāvakānāṃ samāgamaḥ ।।
atha sarva-sāratā । bṛhan-nāradīye śrī-nārada-sanatkumāra-saṃvāde [nārp ] -
asāra-bhūte saṃsāre sāram etad ajātmaja ।
bhagavad-bhakta-saṅgaś ca hari-bhaktis titikṣutā ।।

pādme tatraiva mahāratha-nṛpoktau -
asāgarotthaṃ pīyūṣam adravyaṃ vyasanauṣadham ।
harṣaś cāloka-paryantaḥ satāṃ kila samāgamaḥ ।।
atha bhagavat-kathāmṛta-pānaika-hetutā । pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye śrī-nāradoktau [padmap ]
prasaṅgena satām ātma-manaḥ śruti-rasāyanāḥ ।
bhavanti kīrtanīyasya kathāḥ kṛṣṇasya nirmalāḥ ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe [bhp ] śrī-kapila-devoktau - 
satāṃ prasaṅgān mama vīrya-saṃvido
bhavanti hṛt-karṇa-rasāyanāḥ kathāḥ ।
taj-joṣaṇād āśv apavarga-vartmani
śraddhā ratir bhaktir anukramiṣyati ।।

caturthe śrī-nāradoktau [bhp ] 
yatra bhāgavatā rājan sādhavo viśadāśayāḥ ।
bhagavad-guṇānukathana- śravaṇa-vyagra-cetasaḥ ।।

tasmin mahan-mukharitā madhubhic-
caritra-pīyūṣa-śeṣa-saritaḥ paritaḥ sravanti ।
tā ye pibanty avitṛṣo nṛpa gāḍha-karṇais
tān na spṛśanty aśana-tṛḍ-bhaya-śoka-mohāḥ ।।

pañcame [bhp ] śrī-brāhmaṇa-rahūgaṇa-saṃvāde - 
yatrottamaśloka-guṇānuvādaḥ
prastūyate grāmya-kathā-vighātaḥ ।
niṣevyamāṇo anudinaṃ mumukṣor
matiṃ satīṃ yacchati vāsudeve ।।

ekādaśe śrī-bhagavad-uddhava-saṃvāde śrī-ailopākhyānānte [bhp ] -
teṣu nityaṃ mahā-bhāga mahā-bhāgeṣu mat-kathāḥ ।
sambhavanti hi tā nṇāṃ juṣatāṃ prapunanty agham ।।

tā ye śṛṇvanti gāyanti hy anumodanti cādṛtāḥ ।
mat-parāḥ śraddadhānāś ca bhaktiṃ vindanti te mayi ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye tatraiva 
bhaktis tu bhagavad-bhakta-saṅgena parijāyate ।
sat-saṅgaḥ prāpyate pumbhiḥ sukṛtaiḥ pūrva-sañcitaiḥ ।।

ekādaśe śrī-bhagavad-uddhava-saṃvāde [bhp ] 
athaitat paramaṃ guhyaṃ śṛṇvato yadu-nandana
su-gopyam api vakṣyāmi tvaṃ me bhṛtyaḥ suhṛt sakhā ।।

no rodhayati māṃ yogo na sāṅkhyaṃ dharma eva ca ।
na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo neṣṭā-pūrtaṃ na dakṣiṇā ।।

vratāni yajñaś chandāṃsi tīrthāni niyamā yamāḥ ।
yathāvarundhe sat-saṅgaḥ sarva-saṅgāpaho hi mām ।।

ataevoktaṃ vidureṇa tṛtīya-skandhe [bhp ] 
yat-sevayā bhagavataḥ kūṭa-sthasya madhu-dviṣaḥ ।
rati-rāso bhavet tīvraḥ pādayor vyasanārdanaḥ ।।

prathama-skandhe śrī-śaunakādīnāṃ [bhp ], caturthe ca śrī-pracetasām uktau [bhp ] 
tulayāma lavenāpi na svargaṃ nāpunar-bhavam ।
bhagavat-saṅgi-saṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ ।।

caturthe ca śrī-pracetasaḥ prati śrī-śivopadeśaḥ [bhp ] 
kṣaṇārdhenāpi tulaye na svargaṃ nāpunar-bhavam ।
bhagavat-saṅgi-saṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ ।।

dvādaśe śrī-mārkaṇḍeyopākhyāne śrī-śivasya [bhp ] 
athāpi saṃvadiṣyāmo bhavāny etena sādhunā ।
ayaṃ hi paramo lābho nṛṇāṃ sādhu-samāgamaḥ ।।

ataeva śrī-prahlādaṃ prati śrī-dharaṇyoktaṃ hari-bhakti-sudhodaye - 
akṣṇoḥ phalaṃ tvādṛśa-darśanaṃ hi
tanvāḥ phalaṃ tvādṛśa-gātra-saṅgaḥ ।
jihvā-phalaṃ tvādṛśa-kīrtanaṃ hi
sudurlabhā bhāgavatā hi loke ।।

ataeva vidureṇa tṛtīya-skandhe [bhp ] 
durāpā hy alpa-tapasaḥ sevā vaikuṇṭha-vartmasu ।
yatropagīyate nityaṃ deva-devo janārdanaḥ ।।

śrī-videhenāpy ekādaśa-skandhe [bhp ] 
durlabho mānuṣo deho dehināṃ kṣaṇa-bhaṅguraḥ ।
tatrāpi durlabhaṃ manye vaikuṇṭha-priya-darśanam ।।

ataeva hi prārthitaṃ śrī-dhruveṇa caturtha-skandhe [bhp ] 
bhaktiṃ muhuḥ pravahatāṃ tvayi me prasaṅgo
bhūyād ananta mahatām amalāśayānām ।
yenāñjasolbaṇam uru-vyasanaṃ bhavābdhiṃ
neṣye bhavad-guṇa-kathāmṛta-pāna-mattaḥ ।।

pracetasaḥ pratyupadeśe śrī-śivena ca [bhp ] 
athānaghāṅghres tava kīrti-tīrthayor
antar-bahiḥ-snāna-vidhūta-pāpmanām ।
bhūteṣv anukrośa-susattva-śīlināṃ
syāt saṅgamo anugraha eṣa nas tava ।।

śrī-pracetobhiś ca [bhp ] 
yāvat te māyayā spṛṣṭā bhramāma iha karmabhiḥ ।
tāvad bhavat-prasaṅgānāṃ saṅgaḥ syān no bhave bhave ।।

śrī-prahlādenāpi saptama-skandhe [bhp ] tasmād amūs tanu-bhṛtām aham āśiṣo æjña āyuḥ śriyaṃ vibhavam aindriyam āviriñcyāt । necchāmi te vilulitān uruvikrameṇa kālātmanopanaya māṃ nija-bhṛtya-pārśvam ।। iti ।

athāsat-saṅga-doṣāḥ । śrī-kātyāyana-vākye 
varaṃ huta-vaha-jvālā-pañjarāntar-vyavasthitiḥ ।
na śauri-cintā-vimukha-jana-saṃvāsa-vaiśasam ।।

pādme uttara-khaṇḍe śrī-umā-maheśvara-saṃvāde -
avaiṣṇavās tu ye viprāś cāṇḍālād adhamāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
teṣāṃ sambhāṣaṇaṃ sparśaṃ soma-pānādi varjayet ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe śrī-kapila-devahūti-saṃvāde [bhp ]
satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā maunaṃ buddhiḥ śrīr hrīr yaśaḥ kṣamā ।
śamo damo bhagaś ceti yat-saṅgād yāti saṅkṣayam ।।

teṣv aśānteṣu mūḍheṣu khaṇḍitātmasv asādhuṣu ।
saṅgaṃ na kuryāc chocyeṣu yoṣit-krīḍā-mṛgeṣu ca ।।

na tathāsya bhaven moho bandhaś cānya-prasaṅgataḥ ।
yoṣit-saṅgād yathā puṃso yathā tat-saṅgi-saṅgataḥ ।।

ekādaśe ca śrī-bhagavad-uddhava-saṃvāde [bhp ] -
saṅgaṃ na kuryād asatāṃ śiśnodara-tṛpāṃ kvacit ।
tasyānugas tamasy andhe pataty andhānugāndha-vat ।।

bhagavad-bhakti-hīnā ye mukhyā'santas ta eva hi ।
teṣāṃ niṣṭhā śubhā kvāpi na syāt sac-caritair api ।।

bṛhan-nāradīye prāyaścitta-prakaraṇānte -
kiṃ vedaiḥ kim u vā śāstraiḥ kim u tīrtha-niṣevaṇaiḥ ।
viṣṇu-bhakti-vihīnānāṃ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ ।।

śrī-gāruḍe -
antaṃ gato api vedānāṃ sarva-śāstrārtha-vedy api ।
yo na sarveśvare bhaktas taṃ vidyāt puruṣādhamam ।।

tṛtīya-skandhe [bhp ] 
ahny āpṛtārta-karaṇā niśi niḥśayānā
nānā-manoratha-dhiyā kṣaṇa-bhagna-nidrāḥ ।
daivāhatārtha-racanā ṛṣayo api deva
yuṣmat-prasaṅga-vimukhā iha saṃsaranti ।।

ataevoktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe [bhp ] 
prāyaścittāni cīrṇāni nārāyaṇa-parāṅmukham ।
na niṣpunanti rājendra surā-kumbham ivāpagāḥ ।।

viṣṇu-dharmottare -
kutaḥ pāpa-kṣayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ ca maṅgalam ।
yeṣāṃ naiva hṛdistho ayaṃ maṅgalāyatano hariḥ ।।

ataeva bṛhan-nāradīye lubdhakopākhyānārambhe -
hari-pūjā-vihīnāś ca veda-vidveṣiṇas tathā ।
dvija-go-dveṣiṇaś cāpi rākṣasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

ataeva nija-dūtān prati dharma-rājasyānuśāsanaṃ ṣaṣṭha-skandhe [bhp ] 
tān ānayadhvam asato vimukhān mukunda-
pādāravinda-makaranda-rasād ajasram ।
niṣkiñcanaiḥ paramahaṃsa-kulair asaṅgair
juṣṭād gṛhe niraya-vartmani baddha-tṛṣṇān ।।

jihvā na vakti bhagavad-guṇa-nāma-dheyaṃ
cetaś ca na smarati tac-caraṇāravindam ।
kṛṣṇāya no namati yac-chira ekadāpi
tān ānayadhvam asato akṛta-viṣṇu-kṛtyān ।।

skānde mārkaṇḍeya-bhagīratha-saṃvāde -
yo hi bhāgavataṃ lokam upahāsaṃ nṛpottama ।
karoti tasya naśyanti artha-dharma-yaśaḥ-sutā ।।

nindāṃ kurvanti ye mūḍhā vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām ।
patanti pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ mahā-raurava-saṃjñite ।।

hanti nindati vai dveṣṭi vaiṣṇavān nābhinandati ।
krudhyate yāti no harṣaṃ darśane patanāni ṣaṭ ।।

tatraivāmṛtasāroddhāre śrī-yamoktau -
janma-prabhṛti yat kiñcit sukṛtaṃ samupārjitam ।
nāśam āyāti tat sarvaṃ pīḍayed yadi vaiṣṇavān ।।

dvārakā-māhātmye prahlāda-bali-saṃvāde -
kara-patraiś ca phālyante sutīvrair yama-śāsanaiḥ ।
nindāṃ kurvanti ye pāpā vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām ।।

pūjito bhagavān viṣṇur janmāntara-śatair api ।
prasīdati na viśvātmā vaiṣṇave cāpamānite ।।

daśama-skandhe ca [bhp ] -
nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śṛṇvaṃs tat-parasya janasya vā ।
tato nāpaiti yaḥ so api yāty adhaḥ sukṛtāc cyutaḥ ।।

ataevoktaṃ viṣṇu-dharmottare -
jīvitaṃ viṣṇu-bhaktasya varaṃ pañca-dināni ca ।
na tu kalpa-sahasrāṇi bhakti-hīnasya keśave ।।

ataevoktaṃ śrī-bhāgavate ailopākhyānānte [bhp ] 
tato duḥsaṅgam utsṛjya satsu sajjeta buddhimān ।
santa evāsya chindanti mano-vyāsaṅgam uktibhiḥ ।।

atha śrī-vaiṣṇava-samāgama-vidhiḥ

atha śrī-bhagavad-bhaktān sal-lakṣaṇa-vibhūṣitān ।
